UKUBA nomuzwa wokuphila kahle, ukuthula nokukhululeka emoyeni, ngezinye zezinto eseziseqhulwini lezivakashi uma zihlela amaholidi nezindawo ezizozihambela.Yikho lokhu okwenza ukuthi sande isitayela sokuthi izivakashi uma zibheka izindawo ezizovakashela kuzo, ziqikelele ukuthi zinaso iSpa noma sisondelene yini naleyo ndawo.Izindawo eziningi zokuvakasha sezidlisa ngazo izindawo zokubhucunga nokwelapha umzimba.Sikuhlanganisele uhlu lwezindawo ezinhlanu ezineSpa esihamba phambili, okumele uhlele ukuzivakashela maduze.1. Brahman Hills Spa and Healing EarthSiyiklelise eqhulwini ngenhloso le ndawo njengoba nozokuthola kuyo kusezingeni eliphezulu.Uphuma uwuzwa umehluko hhayi emzimbeni kuphela kepha nasemoyeni uma uqeda ukubhucungwa nezinye izinto ezenziwa kulesi Spa njengeFacial, Yoga, iBody Detox neBody Polish.Kulesi Spa kunanechibi elinamanzi afudumele anezithako ezenza umzimba unethezeke. Ukuba sendaweni enokuthula nakho kukodwa kukunika umuzwa opholile.Lesi Spa singaphakathi endaweni yezivakashi iBrahman Hills phakathi kweHowick neMooi River, edlisa kakhulu ngokuba yindawo yemishado. Nakhona eSpa zikhona izipesheli ezenzelwa omakoti, izimpelesi nezithandani.2. Sanctuary SpaLesi Spa siseSani Pass Premier Resort, ese-Underberg. Kukude impela uma kuthiwa usuka eThekwini kepha kuphela ukukhathala kulesi Spa. Ihhotela esikuso lidume nangokuba yindawo ekahle ukuhlela izingqungquthela nemihlangano yomsebenzi.Kulesi Spa beluleka ngokuthi abasuke beze ehhotela ngokomsebenzi, bangaziphuthiseli ngokuvakashela le ndawo yokuzibhucunga, okungabasiza nasekwehliseni ingcindezi yomsebenzi.Ukubhucungwa nokucwalwa kwezandla nezinyawo, kuthola amaphuzu aphelele kule ndawo. Eceleni kwayo kune-swimming pool ne-hot tub.3. Nibela SpaUsuke ubuka isidakadaka sechibi elingenela eSimangaliso Wetlands Park, uma useSpa esiseNibela Lake Lodge. Leli chibi lilodwa likunika umuzwa wokuphumula nokuthula.Uyadideka uma usungene ngaphakathi sekufanele ukhethe ukuthi uzowujabulisa kanjani umzimba wakho njengoba kunezinhlobonhlobo zezindlela zokuwubhucunga nokuwucwala njengoba kukhona oSwedish massage, Indian head massage ne-Anti stress massage. 4. The Spa Oyster BoxNgeyomntakabani le ndawo esehhotela iThe Oyster Box, eMhlanga. Yize incinza ephaketheni kodwa ngeke uyikhalele imali yakho ngoba ‘imigilingwane’ eyenziwa kulesiya Spa, ikushiya ‘uzelwe kabusha’ uzizwa sengathi unamandla amasha okubhekana nempilo.Indlela yokukhuculula nokwelapha umzimba eyayenziwa eTurkey emandulo iHammam, iyenziwa kulesi Spa esisehhotela eligudle ulwandle nelidume ngokuvakashelwa ngosaziwayo bamazwe omhlaba.5. Mangwanani SpaKuke kwakhona isikhathi lapho bekudlisa yona yodwa iMangwanani emkhakheni wezindawo zokubhucunga nokwelapha umzimba. Okuhle wukuthi le ndawo isalibambile izinga eliphezulu.Kuyibhonasi nokuthi iMangwanani Spa isitholakala emahhotela ehlukene nakwezinye izikhungo nezinxanxathela. IFacial yakhona ihamba phambili, uphuma ubuso buntofontofo futhi bukhazimula.Ungaya eMangwanani ekwezinye izindawo kodwa isahamba phambili eseSibaya Casino, eThekwini.IZITSHUDENI ezine zakuleli  ezifundela ubunesi  zizomela iNingizimu Afrika emqhudelwaneni wezitshudeni ezisemkhakheni ofanayo emhlabeni i-46th International WorldSkills Competition, ezobe iseChina ngo-Okthoba.Zingu-20 izitshudeni ebeziqhudelana ngesikhathi zisaqhathwe kuleli kwi-South Africa WorldSkills National Competion lapho kuwine khona ezine okuyizona ezizohamba.Lo mncintiswano wenziwa isikhungo sokuqeqeshelwa ezempilo nenhlalakahle, Health and Welfare Sector Education and TrainingAuthority (HWSETA) ngokubambisana neWorldSkills.Lezi zitshudeni bekumele ziveze ukuthi ulwazi lwazo lomsebenzi wokunakelela nolwezempilo esezilufundile lungakanani.Abane abazomela leli eChina nabanye ebebeyingxenye yalo mqhudelwano bahlomule ngomfundaze abazowusebenzisela ukuthuthukisa ulwazi lwabo ngokuthi bafunde ezinye iziqu emkhakhakheni wezempilo.USabelo Mazibuko owenza unyaka wesine eCharles Johnson Memorial Campus eNquthu,  uthe wenze konke okusemandleni  ukuze aphumelele kulo mncintiswano futhi kuyamjabulisa ukuthi uphumelele." Lo mqhudelwano awulula kodwa ngenze konke ebengingakwazi ukuthi ngikwenze, ngiyajabula ukuthi ukusebenza kwami kanzima kube nemiphumela emihle. Okungijabulisa kakhulu ukuthi ngizothola umfundaze engizowusebenzisela ukuqhubeka nezifundo zami,"  kusho uMazibuko.UDalisu Khumalo waseMtubatuba ofunda ekolishi labahlengikazi elisesibhedlela eMshiyeni, uthe umfundaze wakhe uzowusebenzisela ukuthi afunde i-Advanced Diploma in Midwifery.USakhile Ngcobo waseSoweto uthe yena uzowusebenzisela ukuthi afunde kabanzi ngePrimary Health Care.UNkk Elaine Brass isikhulu esiphezulu seHWSETA CEO, uthe lo mqhudelwano ubuyise ithemba ngobuhlengikazi. Abaphumelele lesi isiqalo sohambo oluzobasiza ekutheni bathole olunye ulwazi baphinde bahlangane nezinye izitshudeni zakwamanye amazwe lapho zizofunda khona okuningi. UTshiamo Mokgoetsi waseRustenberg, uthe ngaphezu kwakho konke okuhle azokuthola okuwumhlomulo womncintiswano uzophinde akwazi ukufaka kwiCV yakhe ukuthi uke waba yingxenye yomncintiswano omkhulu kangaka.Inhlangano ebhekele umdlavuza wesikhumba kuleli, iNational Cancer Association of SA, ithi abantu abasezindaweni ezishisa kakhulu zakuleli basengozini yokuhlaselwa wumdlavuza wesikhumba.Lesi sifo bathi siya ngokwanda emhlabeni ngenxa yokushintsha kwesimo sezulu.Njengoba uJanuwari ngokwekhalenda lezempilo uyinyanga yokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza wesikhumba, i-International Journal of Women Dermatology, ithe umoya ongcolile ngenxa yezimboni ezikhafula isisi esingcolile, imisebe yelanga eyingozi edalwa wukushintsha kwesimo sezulu, ngesinye sezizathu eziholela ekutheni senyuke isibalo sabanalesi sifo.IMelanoma bathi iwuhlobo oluyingozi lomdlavuza wesikhumba, oluvamise ukuhlasela ingxenye yesikhumba ejwayele ukutholwa yilanga.Ngokombhalo wezibalo zabahaqwe wumdlavuza, iNational Cancer Registry (NCR) ka-2019, iMelamona iwumdlavuza wesihlanu ohlasela abantu besilisa, ube ngowesithupha ohlasela abantu besifazane  kuleli.Ongoti besikhumba bathi nakuba ukuhlolwa ngongoti ukuthi kawunawo yini umdlavuza kungenye yezinto eziyingxenye yokuhlolwa okwenziwayo,  kodwa kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu azibheke isikhumba sakhe ukuthi asinalo yini ushintsho okungaba amachashazi noma amabala angafani nesikhumba sakhe.Uma ubuvele unamachachazi hlala ubheka ukuthi awashintshi umbala wawo, noma kube nokuqinile kuleyo ngxenye yesikhumba.Ukuvumbuka kwezinsumpa ekade ungenazo.Ukuba nemihuzuko kodwa ungazange ulimaleUkuba nezinyawo ezimnyama ezithendeni naseduze kwezinzipho. UNkk Lorraine Govender we-Cansa,  uthe inhloso enkulu yayo wukuthi ibe nezinhlelo zokufundisa abantu ngalo mdlavuza ukuze bawazi  bawuqonde."Uma sebewuqonda kuzoba lula ukuthi abantu abanawo basheshe babonwe, belashwe kusenesikhathi, okuyinto engakenzeki manje. Kuyenzeka umuntu eyedwa abe namabala okungenzeka ukuthi anomdlavuza angaphezulu kuka-100 kodwa angasukumi ngoba usuke engaqondi ukuthi la mabala noma ukushintsha kwesikhumba kwesinye isikhathi kungasho ukuthi unomdlavuza wesikhumba, " kusho uNkk Govender.ABACWANINGI bakhathazekile ngemiphumela yocwaningo olubheka ukuthi kwenzekani emzimbeni weziguli ezike zahlaselwa yiCorona ngokuhamba kwesikhathi.Ucwaningo lwenziwe e-UK kusetshenziswa imininingwane yocwaningo oluke lwenziwa phambilini olubheka ukuthi ingqondo ishintsha kanjani ngesikhathi umuntu ekhula. Abacwaningi bebethatha izithombe zabake bahaqwa yiCovid-19 beminyaka ehlukene bese beqhathanisa nemiphumela yalolu cwaningo olwaphothulwa ngo-2014.Abacwaningi  kulolu cwaningo oluqhubekayo bebebheka ukuthi umzimba ushintsha kanjani kumuntu oke wahaqwa yiCorona. Imiphumela yesikhashana ekhishwe ngenyanga edlule iveza ukuthi  bathole ukuthi liyehla izinga lokusebenza kobuchopho kumuntu oke wahaqwa yiCovid-19 uma eqhathaniswa nalingana naye ongazange ahaqwe yileli gciwane. Ngokocwaningo kuphela izinyanga oke wahaqeka izinga lokusebenza kobuchopho bakhe lehlile okwamanje abacwaningi abakwazi ukuthola ukuthi kuba  yisikhathi esingakanani ngoba ucwaningo lunezinyanga eziwu-18 .Okukhathaza abacwaningi ukuthi lokhu kuzoba nomthelela omubi ongenza ukuthi abantu baguge ngokushesha kanti sikhona isikhathi esithile esaziwayo sokuthi ubuchopho  bomuntu behlelwe izinga lokusebenza  ngoba esekhulile..Abacwaningi bathi uma beqhubeka nalolu cwaningo lwabo babheka ukuthi ngabe  kusho ukuthi abantu abasesigabeni esiphakathi  sokukhula nasebekhulile bangazithola kuphazamiseka ukusebenza kobuchopho babo bafane nabantu abadala kunabo.Lolu cwaningo luveze ukuthi  ingaphambili lobuchopho nengxenye ebizwa nge-temporal lobes iyancipha kubantu abake bahaqwa iCovid-19 kanti kubantu abangazange bahaqeke ayinciphi ize inciphe uma sebesesigabeni esithile seminyaka okuhambisana nokukhula kwabo.UDkt Mike Dow ongomunye wabacwaningi uthe njengamanje abacwaningi babheka ukuthi ngabe le miphumela ichaza ukuthi abake bahaqwa yiCorona bazophathwa isifo sabantu abadala i-Alzheimer ngoba lesi sifo senza ukuthi umuntu omdala akhohlwe masinyane futhi angabuzwa ubumnandi bento ayidlayo okuthiwa kwenzeka uma kuncipha lezi zingxenye zobuchopho kanti zingezinye zezimpawu zeCorona.“ Lokhu kusho ukuthi kwabanye noma ingasekho iCorona emzimbeni kodwa bayaqhubeka bakhohlwe futhi bangezwa ukuthi into abayidlayo injani,”  kusho yena.U-71% wabantu bakuleli uzimisele ngokugomela iCovid-19 ukuze uphephe kulesi sifo. Lokhu kusho ukuthi abayisikhombisa kwabawu-10 abanankinga nokugoma. Lezi zindaba zivezwe wucwaningo lwakamuva olubizwa ngeNational Income Dynamics Study (Nids) Coronavirus Rapid Mobile Survey (Cram) olwethulwe ngokusemthethweni kwi-webinar yayizolo.UMnuz Nic Spaul ongumcwaningi ozinze eNyuvesi yaseStellenbosch uveze ukuthi bawu-29% abantu abangathandi ukugomela iCovid-19 kanti basaba ukuthi umgomo uzobadalela ezinye izifo.Uthe iningi lalabo abasaba ukugoma lifunda kakhulu izindaba ezingaqinisekisiwe ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.Ucwaningo luveze ukuthi abantu abasha abaneminyaka ewu-18 kuya ku-25 abathandi ukugoma uma kuqhathaniswa nabadala abaneminyaka engaphezu kuka-25.U-73% wabadala abaneminyaka ewu-35 kuya ku-59 bazwakalise ukuthi bazimisele ngokugoma.“Sithole ukuthi abantu abanezifo ezingalapheki bazimisele ngokugoma kanjalo nabadala. Ucwaningo lwethu luveze ukuthi abakhuluma isibhunu (42%) bayasaba ukugomela iCovid-19. U-25% kuphela wabantu abasaba ukugoma abakhuluma isiZulu, isiXhosa, isiPedi nezinye izilimi. Abantu abangasabi ukugoma yilabo abakhuluma iTshiVenda njengoba sithole ukuthi wu-18% kuphela omanqika,” kusho uSpaul.UMnuz Reza Daniels ongumcwaningi eNyuvesi yaseCape Town, uveze ukuthi ukuqubuka kweCovid-19 kushintshe indlela yokufunda ezikoleni.Abafundi bamabanga aphansi ezikoleni okungakhokhwa kuzo balahlekelwe wu-75% wezifundo zabo.Uthe izingane ezifunda kulezi zikole aziyi njalo esikoleni futhi azikwazi ukwenza umsebenzi emakhaya uma kuqhathaniswa nalezo ezifunda ezikoleni ezikhokhayo, ezinezinsiza zobuchwepheshe besimanje.Uveze nokuthi izingane bezingakutholi ukudla kahle njengoba bezisemakhaya kanti namanje u-43% kuphela okwazi ukuphakelwa ezikoleni.“Sithole ukuthi isibalo sezingane ezilala zingadlile sehlile njengoba izikole zivuliwe sasuka ku-16% saya ku-14% ngoFebhuwari noMashi walo nyaka uma siliqhathanisa noNovemba noDisemba wonyaka odlule. U-67% wabantu esikhulume nabo uveze ukuthi awunayo imali yokuthenga ukudla yingakho izingane zilala zingadlile. Lokhu kukhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi izingane kufanele zidle esikoleni,” kusho uDaniels.Uthe othisha ababulawa yiCovid-19 abavamisile ukuyithola esikoleni ngoba abanye bebeshona nangesikhathi izikole zivaliwe.Ucwaningo lweNIDS-CRAM lwenziwa abacwaningi abawu-30 bamanyuvesi amahlanu aseNingizimu Afrika okungeyaseCape Town, Stellenbosch,Wits, Rhodes neyaseJohannesburg.Ucwaningo oluphelele lutholakala ngokuvakashela u-cramsurvey.org.WONKE ama-medical aid kuleli azokukhokhela ukugonywelwa kweCovid-19 kwamalungu awo.Umkhandlu wama-medical aid kuleli uthi ukugonyelwa kweCovid-19, sekufakiwe ngaphansi kwezinto ezikhokhelwa yi-medical, iPrescribed Minimum Benefits (PMB).UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt  Zweli Mkhize, wamukele indlela ahlelwe ngayo ama-PMB kuwo okukhona nokuthi i-medical aid ikhokhele nokwelashwa okuphuthumayo, kuhlanganisa nezifo ezingu-25 ezingamahlalakhona kanye nezinye izifo ezingu-271.Ukuhlolelwa iCovid-19, ukulawulwa kwayo nokuphefumula ngomshini konke kufakwe ohlwini olusha lwama-PMB, azokhokhelwa ama-medical aid kungakhathalekile ukuthi ilungu likuluphi uhlelo lwe-medical aid.Uhulumeni wakuleli kulindeleke ukuthi uqale uhlelo lokugonywa kwabasebenzi bezempilo njengoba umgomo ongenela abangu-1 million,  okhiqizwe yi-AstraZeneca, usufikile kuleli.Isikhulu esiphezulu kwaMomentum Health Solutions, uMnuz Damian McHugh, sithe ikhava yeCovid-19 izozimela, ayizuthathwa emalini ebhekelele ukugula kwelungu eyaziwa ngama-savings.UMnuz Lee Callakopen waKwaBonitas Medical Aid, uthe bazokhokhela nokugoma kwamanye amalungu abhaliswe ngumnikazi we-medical aid ngaphansi kwakhe.Uthe basohlelweni lokuhlanganisa ulwazi lwamalungu abo ukuze akwazi ukubhalisa esebenzisa i-online ukuze akwazi ukuyogoma."Lo mgomo uphindwa kabili, ukubhalisa ngalolu hlelo kuzokwenza ukuthi umuntu azi ukuthi kuzomele abuyele nini futhi ukuyogoma," kusho uCallakopen.UMkhize uthe amalungu omphakathi angenayo i-medical aid azokhokhelwa uhulumeni."Wonke umuntu osengcupheni yokuthola iCovid-19 uzogonywa. I-medical aid izokhokha, uma usuphumile kuyona uhulumeni uzokukhokhela," kusho yenaIziguli ezinesifo sikashukela nesokwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi zinamathuba amaningi okuthi zihlaselwe isifo esithinta ukungasebenzi ngendlela kwezinso.Lokhu kushiwo isikhulu esiphezulu esikhungweni esibhekele izifo ezithinta izinso, iNational Renal Care(NRC), uDkt Chevon Clark edlulisa umyalezo ohambisana nokuthi leli sonto ngokwekhalenda lezempilo elokuqwashisa ngezifo zezinso.Uthe ulwazi  olugcinwe esikhungweni iNational Kidney Foundation of South Africa (NKFSA), lukhombisa ukuthi u-60 kuya ku-65% weziguli ezinesifo sokwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi zinenkinga yezinso ezingasebenzi kahle, kanti 25% weziguli ezinesifo sikashukela esidalwa indlela umuntu aphila  ngayo, utype 2 zinenkinga yezinso ezingasebenzi kahle.“Ukhiye wokulawuleka kwalesi sifo ukuthi sisheshe sitholakale ngoba aselapheki kodwa abezempilo bayakwazi ukwenza uhlelo lokusilawula olukahle uma sisheshe satholakala.  Iziguli ezinesifo sikashukela nezinesifo sokwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi zinamathuba engeziwe okuthi zihlaselwe ilesi sifo, ngakho kubalulekile ukuthi zihlale zihlola ukuthi izinso zazo zisasebenza kahle yini.  Into ebaluleke kakhulu ukuthi kwandiswe imikhankaso yokuqwashisa ngalesi sifo, ngoba usuku oludlulayo onesifo sezinso engaluqalile uhlelo lokwelashwa, isifo siyaqhubeka egazini okwenza ukuthi kube nzima ukuthi silawulwe agcine esethembele ekuhlanzweni izinso ngomshini okusuke sekuyisigaba esibucayi,” kusho yena.Uqhube wathi umsebenzi wezinso ukusefa uketshezi olusuke lungasadingwa umzimba nalolo olunobuthi zilukhiphe emzimbeni, ngomchamo. Uma lokhu kungenzekanga umzimba uhlala nokungcola okumele ngabe sekuphumile kuwo okudala ezinye izinkinga zempilo.Uthe ukulawulwa ngendlela kwesifo sokwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi nesikashukela kwehlisa amathuba okuhlaselwa isifo senhliziyo nesezinso ngo-70 kuya ku-80%.Uthe enye into esizayo ukuthi uma isiguli sesitsheliwe ukuthi izinso zaso zithwele kanzima,  sishintshe indlela esiphila ngayo. Sizivocavoce, siphuze kakhulu amanzi ukuze umzimba ungaphelelwa ngamanzi, sizame ukusebenzisa izinto ezizohlanza uketshezi olungubuthi olusemzimbeni, sinciphise ekuphuzeni utshwala nokubhema. Sidle ukudla okunempilo okuyimifino nezithelo.ABANGABONI KwaZulu-Natal bafuna ukuthi uhulumeni ababhekelele, babe ngabanye babantu abazogoma kuqala njengengoba kuqala isigaba sesibili sokugomela iCovid-19 namhlanje.NgoLwesihlanu, inhlangano ebhekelela abakhubazekile, iGezephi Foundation, ibe nesigcawu sokubonisana  sabangaboni ebesiseThekwini lapho beveze khona izinkinga ezibenza babe sengcupheni yokuthola iCovid-19.UNksz Slindile Makhaye, weBlind Youth Organisation, uthe bayafisa ukuthi uhulumeni nabo ababeke eqhulwini ngoba basengcupheni yokutheleleka ngaleli gciwane."Njengoba singaboni nje, sibambelela endololwaneni yomuntu ukuze sikwazi ukuzwa umzimba wakhe ukuthi wenzenjani. Indololwane njengoba kuneCovid-19 kuthiwa abantu abakhwehlelele kuyo, okwenza ukuthi thina sibe sengcupheni ngoba sibambelela kuyo singazi ukuthi kuke kwakhwehlelelwa kuyo. Njengamanje sibambelela esandleni kodwa lokho akuphephile ngoba awawuzwa umzimba womuntu," kuchaza uNksz MakhayeUqhube wathi ngaphandle kwalokho, njengoba bengaboni basebenzisa izandla zabo bathinte ukuze bezwe ukuthi abukho yini ubungozi."Sibona ukuthi kwasekuqaleni ngesikhathi uhulumeni ebheka izindlela zokunqanda ukusabalala kwaleli gciwane, akazange amcabangele umuntu ongaboni. Sifisa ukuthi lokho akulungise ngokuthi sibe ngabanye abantu abazogoma kulesi sigaba sesibili,"  kusho yena.Usihlalo weGezephi Foundation, uMnuz Siya Zondi, uthe lesi siphakamiso basidlulisele kubaphathi bophiko lwabakhubazekile ehhovisi likaNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal naseMnyangweni wezeMpilo kulesi sifundazwe banethemba lokuthi sizofinyelela kuNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo, uDkt Zweli Mkhize.UMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli uthunyelelwe imibuzo  mayelana nokuthi abangaboni ngabe bayingxenye yini yabazogonywa kulesi sigaba. Kuze kwashaya isikhathi sokushicilela ungakaphenduli. ABENHLANGANO yabathandana nabobulili obufanayo KwaZulu-Natal, iLesbian and Gay Community and Health Centre, bathi iyize imikhankaso yabo yokugubha inyanga yesifo sofuba ababambisene kuyo noMnyango wezeMpilo ngenxa yokungcola kweTheku.USbo Khumalo omele le nhlangano KwaZulu-Natal, uthe babona zizokwanda izibalo zabahlaselwe yisifo sofuba ngenxa yokungcola okuseThekwini nezindawo ezilakhele ngenxa yesiteleka sakamuva.“Akukhona ukuthi asizwelani nabasebenzi bakamasipala weTheku abafuna izimfuno zabo. Inkinga wukuthi noMnyango wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal awenzi okwanele ukulekelela ukuthi siqhube kahle imikhankaso yokulwa nesifo sofuba njengoba uMashi kuyinyanga yofuba.“Ikhona imizamo abangayenza njengokukhipha amaphoyisa ukuphelezela abaletha amanzi nabaqoqa udoti ezitaladini. Uma siqhuba le mikhankaso sigqugquzela inhlanzeko ukuze kugwemeke isifo sofuba.“Inkinga ukuthi uyigqugquzela kanjani inhlanzeko ube uqhuba umkhankaso endaweni engcolile? Kumanje kuxake nesifo sophenyane esidinga ukuthi kube nenhlanzeko ukuze singabhebhetheki,” kusho uSbo.Uthe kumanje balungiselela iNational TB Day ezoba seGoli ngoMashi 24 kodwa bazofika khona bengayilungele njengoba imikhankaso yaKwaZulu-Natal iphazanyiswa ukungcola okuseThekwini.Uveze ukuthi ngisho nesiqubulo salo nyaka semikhankaso yesifo sofuba sithi: “Sithi mina nawe singasiqeda isifo sofuba”  kodwa babona kuyinto engelula ukwenzeka njengoba kugcole ngalolu hlobo eThekwini.Uqhube wathi njengamanje akulula ukuthi bangakhuluma nomasipala weTheku njengoba inkinga kungabasebenzi bakhona abalwela izimfuno zabo, kodwa uMnyango wezeMpilo kumele kube yiwona ongenelelayo.INHLANGANO i-World Health Organisation (WHO) isinxenxe abesifazane abazithwele kanye nabesifazane abaneminyaka ebavumela ukuba bathole abantwana ukuba bazithibe otshwaleni.Lokhu kuvela njengoba iphakamisa izincomo ngaphansi kohlelo lwayo lwe-Global Alcohol Action Plan, nokuyilapho ifuna ukulusebenzisa emazweni ahlukene ukuzama ukwehlisa izinga lotshwala.Kulezi zincomo abasaziphakamisa, kuvele ukuthi utshwala buba nemithelela emibi empilweni yabantu, kube nemithelela engemihle ngokuthola izifo.Konina bezingane abazithwele, kuthiwa bangasondelani nhlobo notshwala. Bese kuthi abesifazane abasazimisele ukuba nabantwana banciphise otshwaleni.Phakathi kwezinye izinto ezivela kulo mqulu we-WHO ukuthi izingane ziqala zisencane ukuphuza, cishe zineminyaka engu-15, nokuyinto abayihlabile.Kube nemvunge ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngalezi ziphakamiso ezishicilelwe ngoLwesithathu kwi-website ye-WHO, abanye bethi zicwasa abesifazane abasafuna ukuba nezingane kodwa kungashiwo lutho ngabesilisa.NJENGOBA kuyinyanga yabesifazane, inkampani ekhiqiza imithi iphinde igqugquzele ukuthi abantu bazinakekele ngokuzihlola ukuthi abanazo yini izifo ukuze bathole ukwelashwa kusenesikhathi iPharma Dynamics, ikhuthaza abesifazane ukuthi bangakhohlwa ukuya ezikhungweni zezempilo bayohlolwa izifo ezibahluphayo ukuze baphile kahle.UNkk Nicole Jennings, okhulumela le nkampani, uthe ukuhlolwa kubalulekile noma kungathiwa uzizwa uphile kahle.“Ukuhlolwa kwezempilo ngokuvamile kumele ukwenze uphilile ungalindi uze ugule. Inhloso yakho wukuthola isifo kusenesikhathi - zingakabonakali izimpawu. Ezimeni eziningi, ukwelapha isifo kusenesikhathi kukhipha imiphumela engcono. Ukuzihlola kungasiza ngokuthi isifo esiyingozi singabhebhetheki ngokushesha ngoba sisheshe sabonakala noma sinqandwe uma kuyisifo eselaphekayo.” usho kanje.Uqhube wathi abantu besifazane basemakhaya bajwayele ukuya emitholampilo izifo sezingene zagxila egazini okwenza ukuthi kubukeke sengathi izifo zidlanga kakhulu kubona. Uthe lokhu kwenziwa ukuthi kunezinto eziyizinkoleloze abazikholwayo njengokuthi izifo ezithile ziphatha abantu abadala.“Kuyinganekwane ukuthi umfutho wegazi ophezulu ngokujwayelekile uphatha amadoda noma abantu abadala. Ucwaningo olwenziwe eNingizimu Afrika lukhomba ukuthi isifo sezinga lomfutho wegazi ophezulu kubantu besifazane linyukile kule minyaka engu-20 edlule,” kusho yena.Ucwaningo olwenziwe kuleli kubantu besilisa abangu-5 477 nabesifazane abangu-7 740 luveze ukwanda kwesifo somfutho wegazi ophezulu esinyuke sisuka ku-27% saya ku-45% kwabesilisa kwabesifazane sisuke ku-31% saya ku-48%."Umfutho wegazi ophezulu ubizwa ngokuthi umbulali ocashile ngoba ngokuvamile awunazo izimpawu kodwa unomthelela omubi empilweni yakho. Ngokujwayelekile zonke izifo ezidalwa umfutho wegazi ophezulu nokukhubazeka okudalwa yiwo kungagwemeka uma usheshe wabonakala. Ngakho kubalulekile ukuthi uhlale uya esikhungweni sezempilo uyohlola umfutho wegazi."UNkk Jennings uthe ukuhlolwa umfutho wegazi kumele abantu abaqale ukukwenza beneminyaka engu-18.Okunye athe kubalulekile ukuthi abantu besifazane bakwenze ukuhlola izinga le-cholesterol.Uthe imiphumela yokuhlolwa i-cholesterol iyona eshoyo ukuthi usemathubeni angakanani okuthi uhlaselwe yisifo senhliziyo nesohlangothi. Uthe kona kumele umuntu aqale ukukwenza uma eseneminyaka engu-20 bese ekwenza njalo ngemuva kweminyaka emihlanu kodwa uma ekhaya kunomlando wabantu abake baxakwa yiyo kumele kwenziwe njalo.Uthe izinga likashukela egazini ngesinye sezimo okumele abantu besifazane bazijwayeze ukusihlola.Uthe abantu besifazane abaneminyaka engu-45 kuya phezulu kumele njalo ngemuva kweminyaka emithathu bahlolwe ukuthi banoshukela ongakanani egazini labo.Uthe ukuhlolwa ukuthi awunalo yini igciwane lengculazi kubaluleke kakhulu njengoba izinga lokusabalala kwaleli gciwane kuleli liphezulu. Uthe okungenani umuntu wesifazane kumele ahlole kanye ngonyaka ukuthi akanalo yini igciwane lengculazi.Ukuhlolwa ukuthi awunawo yini umdlavuza wesibeletho, wenze i-pap smear, uthe ngenye yezinto ezibalulekile kubantu besifazane."Udokotela uhlola uketshezi olusemlonyeni wesibeletho kusetshenziswa ubuchwepheshe obukhombayo uma kunoshintsho olungasho ukuthi unomdlavuza wesibeletho," kusho yena.Uthe umuntu wesifazane kumele aqale ukwenza i-pap smear eneminyaka engu-25.Ngaphandle komdlavuza wesibeletho omunye umdlavuza ophatha abantu besifazane umdlavuza webele. Uthe abantu besifazane abaneminyaka ewu-40 kuya phezulu kumele bazijwayeze ukuzihlola bona ngokuzithinta, babuye benze ukuhlolwa okubizwa ngemammogram.Okunye ukuhlolwa athe kubalulekile ukubheka ukuthi amathambo akho aqine ngokwanele yini okwaziwa ngebone density ukuze bangaphuki kalula. Uthe lokhu kuhlolwa kunconywa ukuthi kwenziwe ngabesifazane abaneminyaka engu-60 kuya ku-65.ABACWANINGI abahlola umgomo wesandulela ngculazi bathi nakuba lo mgomo okhiqizwe ngobuchwepheshe imNRA, ohlolwa emhlabeni wonke, uthembisa uma uhlolwa ezilwaneni kodwa ngeke baqale bawuhlole kubantu okwamanje.Bekulindeleke ukuthi kuphele unyaka lo mgomo ususesigabeni sokuhlolwa kubantu. Ososayensi besikhungo iNational Institute of Allergy and Infectious Diseases (NIAID) sase-United States of America (USA) bathi kusekuningi okusamele bakubhekisise ngaphambi kokuthi baqale ucwaningo olwenziwa kubantu njengoba olwenziwe emagundaneni, luthembisa.UPaolo Lusso ongomunye wabacwaningi futhi ongumbhali walolu cwaningo olushicilelwe emqingweni i-Journal Nurture Medicines eshicilelwe ngeledlule, uthe balwenza ngemigomo eyenziwa ngobuchwepheshe i-mRNA. Uthe lobu wubuchwepheshe obusetshenziswe ngesikhathi kwenziwa imigomo yeCovid-19, buyethembisa kodwa bekumele bangaqhubekeli esigabeni esilandelayo kuze kube babhekisisa ezinye izinto. Uthe yingakho besimisile isigaba eslilandelayo sokuhlola umgomo kubantu obekumele siqale uma sekuphele esokuhlolwa kwawo ezilwaneni."Njengoba besenza ucwaningo ezilwaneni, sibonile ukuthi kudingeka ukuthi amagundane ajove izikhawu eziningi okungacishe kube wunyaka ngaphambi kokuthi kube nokuvikeleka okukhona futhi kwenziwe isikali esithe xaxa. Lokhu kusitshela ukuthi akumele siqhubekele phambili senze isigaba esilandelayo socwaningo ngoba sisafuna ukugculiseka kahle,“  usho yena.Uthe lokhu akusho ukuthi sebephonse ithawula kodwa basafuna ukuthi benyuse izinga lokuvikela kulo mgomo, okusho ukuthi bazokwenza omunye ozobe namandla athe xaxa abazophinde bawuhlole ezilwaneni futhi ngaphambi kokuthi bawuhlole ngabantu."Uma kubonakala ukuthi kunomehluko ezilwaneni sizoqhubeka senze ucwaningo lwesigaba sokuqala ngabantu, siqale ngabantu abadala,"  kusho yena.Ngo-Agasti, abakhiqizi bemigomo, iJohnson&Johnson, balumisa ucwaningo i-Imbokodo obelwenziwa ngabantu besifazane abangu-2 600 e-Afrika, ngoba bethi lolu cwaningo ebese luqhubeke iminyaka emibili, lukhombise ukuthi lo mgomo uvikela ngo-25% kuphela.Umgomo weJ&J wona wenziwe ngohlelo lokwenza imigomo olwaziwa nge-viral vector vaccine.Abacwaningi be-NIAID bathi ulwazi olutholakale kulolu cwaningo olwamiswa ngo-Agasti, bazolusebenzisa njengoba beqhubeka besebenzisa umgomo owenziwe ngobuchwepheshe, i-mNRA.Ucwaningo lweJ&J bekumele luphele ngo-2023 olwemigomo ekhiqizwe nge-mNRA luzophela ngo-2024.USolwazi Lynn Morris owungoti wamagciwane ocwaninga ngesandulela ngculazi kuleli, uthe ucwaningo olwenziwayo ngeHIV alukakwazi ukukhanda amasosha avikelayo adingekayo."Lokho akufani nokukhanda uketshezi oluvikelayo olwaziwa ngama-spike protein esibona kwenzeka. Inkinga esibhekene nayo ukuthi kusenzima ukwenza into efana ncamashi ne-HIV ukuze kuzothi uma i-HIV yangempela isihlasela emzimbeni, ifice umzimba sewakhe amasosha afana ncamashi. Amasosha adingeka ukuze azokwenza ukuthi ingangeni," kusho uSolwazi Morris. ISIKHUNGO esibhekelele izifo ezithathelanayo, iNational Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD), sithi izibalo zakamuva ezikhomba ukuthi abantu abasha abahaqwe yiCovid-19 ezithi bangu-37,857 zidalwe ubuhixihixi bamakhompyutha, njengoba izibalo zangempela ziwuhhafu walezi.Isitatimende esithunyelwe yilesi sikhungo sithe izibalo eziyizo zabantu abasha abahaqekile zithi bangu-18 035."Izinga lokutheleleka kwabantu ngeCovid-19 liku-28.9%," kusho isitatimende.Lezi zibalo bezithusa ngoba ezinkulu ezike zaba khona ezikaJulayi ezathi bangu-26, 645 abantu abahaqekile. Abantu abahaqwe yiCovid-19 kuleli selokhu yafika kuleli bangu-3,167,497Abantu abasha ababulelwe yileli gciwane bangu-21, okuholele ekutheni izibalo zababulelwe yileli gciwane zibe ngu-90,137.“Sibikelwe ngesonto eledlule ukuthi kunezinkinga zokwedluliselwa kolwazi lwabantu abahaqekile kumakhompyutha ezikhungweni zezempilo zikahulumeni. Kuthiwa abengakwazi ukudlulisa ulwazi lwabantu okutholakale ukuthi bahaqekile, okuholele ekutheni nathi singakwazi ukubika ngokushesha izibalo zaze zabikwa sekudlule isikhathi. Lesi sikhungo senza isiqiniseko sokuthi imibiko mayelana nabantu abasha abahaqekile siyikhipha injengoba injalo, akukho obekufihlwa. Sizoqhubeka senze njalo," kusho isitatimende.Siqhube sathi abantu abasha abalaliswe ezibhedlela ngenxa yezifo ezidalwa yiCovid-19 bangu-96, osekuholele ekutheni abantu abalaliswe ezibhedlela ngenxa yeleli gciwane babe ngu-5,563.ABANTU besifazane abaningi kuyabakhathaza ukubona izimpahla zangaphansi zishintsha umbala, okungaba ukuthi zibukeke sengathi zishile noma kube sengathi zifakwe izinsiza zokususa amabala, ibleach.Ongoti bezempilo bathi nakuba lokhu kubukeka kabi futhi kubakhathaza abesifazane nabesilisa abaye babone izimpahla zabo zangasese sezimoshekile,  kodwa lokhu akuyona ingozi nakancane ngoba kusho ukuthi isitho sangasese sisuke sizihlanza sona bese sikhipha uketshezi olusasawotshana abadala ukuthi izingubo zangaphansi zishintshe umbala wazo. UDkt Kim Sonntag ongudokotela wezifo zabesifazane obelethisayo obuye abhale ebhukwini lezempilo, iWomen's Health South Africa uthe: “Isitho sangasese sowesifazane ngokwemvelo sinendawo enokusasawotshana (acid), ene-pH ephansi.Amagciwane amahle adingekayo emzimbeni abizwa nge-Lactobacilli, atholakala esithweni sangasese sowesifazane, ayasiza ekugcineni i-pH ihlale isezingeni elifanele ukuze owesifazane angangenwa yizifo.Lama gciwane iwona asiza ekutheni isitho sangasese sizihlanze. Uma isitho sangasese sikhipha uketshezi olungenalo iphunga futhi lungewona umbala ongajwayelekile okungaba ophuzi, oluhlaza okotshani noma onsundu kusho ukuthi isitho sangasese siyazihlanza."Uqhube wathi kujwayelekile ukuthi abesifazane babone izingubo zabo zangasese zimoshekile ngenxa yoketshezi oluphumayo. Lokhu kwenzeka kubantu besifazane abaningi emhlabeni.Ongakwenza ukuthi uma ubona lawo mabala uwabuke njengamabala achaza ukuthi isitho sakho sangasese senza lokho okumele sikwenze, hhayi njengento eyihlazo noma echaza ukuthi awuhlanzekile," kusho yena.Okunye athe ungakwenza ukuthi ugqoke izingubo zangaphansi ezingagqamile ukuze amabala angabonakali kalula.UDkt Annie Frenkel, owungoti wezifo zabantu besifazane obuye abeluleke  enkundleni yezokuxhumana uTik Tok, uthe baningi abangaqondi ngokusebenza kwesitho sabo,Abanye uthe baye basebenzise ama-panty liners ngenhloso yokuthi uketshezi okungenzeka lonakalise umbala wezingubo zangaphansi, lungene kuyona."Ipanty liner ilimaza isikhumba sesitho sangasese esibucayi,  uma uyigqoka nsuku zonke. Uma uzwa sengathi kukhona uketshezi oseluphumile ongakwenza, wukushintsha  izingubo zakho zangaphansi ngoba ukufaka ipanty liner njalo kulimaza isikhumba esibucayi.“Sigcina sesiluma ngoba ipanty liner uma ithintana naso lesi sikhumba igcina isiklwebha okungadala ukuthi amagciwane angene kalula," kusho yena.UKUSABALALA ngokushesha kwegciwane leCorona elitholakale kamuva e-India kuzoba nomthelela ohlelweni lokuusatshalaliswa kwemigomo yeCovid-19 emazweni ase-Afrika.UMqondisi Jikelele weNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO),  uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus uthe ukusabalala ngendlela engalawuleki kwegciwane elitholakale e-India, kuyayithinta i-Afrika njengoba kuzomele yonke imigomo eyikhiqizayo, iyikhiqizele izwe layo ngaphambi kokuthi kudayiselwe amanye amazwe."Maningi amazwe ase-Afrika anesivumelwano sokuthenga imigomo yeCovid-19 e-India, okumanje alinde imigomo yawo. Ukubhebhetheka ngokwedlulele kweCorona kuleliya lizwe kuzofaka ingcindezi kubakhiqizi  bemigomo, okuzodingeka ukuthi  bakhiqizele ekhaya ngaphambi kokuthi bacabange ngokudayisa. Zikhona izinhlelo esezenziwe zokuthi imigomo ithengwe kwamanye amazwe ngenxa yokuthi i-India nayo ibhekene negcindezi yayo. Lokho kuzosho ukuthi lawo mazwe asezoba sekugcineni ohlelweni lwabazokhiqizelwa imigomo kulezo zinkampani ngoba nazo bezivele zinohla lwazo, lwamazwe ebezihlele ukuwakhiqizela," kusho uGhebreyesus.UGhebreyesus wubekhuluma nabaholi bezempilo e-Afrika emhlanganweni wabo muva nje.Uthe e-Afrika bangu-2% abantu abagonyelwe iCovid-19 uma beqhathaniswa nasebegome emhlabeni wonke.Usho kanjena nje kuleli kutholakale ukuthi bane abantu abanegciwane elitholakale e-India, okudale uvalo olukhulu kubantu. Abanye bagxeka uhulumeni ngokuthi akazange ayivale imingcele namachweba, ukuze leli gciwane lingafinyeleli kuleli.USolwazi Barry Schoub, osekomitini eleluleka ongqongqoshe ababhekele iCovid-19 kuleli, iMinisterial Advisory Committee (MAC), uthe ukuvala imingcele namachweba bekungaba yisona sisombululo, ebesingasebenza kodwa ngenxa yesimo somnotho esintengayo kuleli ukwenza lokho kakusona isisombululo okwamanje. “Okwamanje akusona isinqumo okumele sithathwe wuhulumeni uma sibheka isimo somnotho kuleli. Mhlawumbe uma isimo siya ngokuya siqina lokho kungacatshangwa,” kusho uSchoub. UNHLANGOTHI yisifo esihlasela ubuchopho sibone sekuzwela ohlangothini olulawulwa yileyo ngxenye yobuchopho.Ubuchopho bulawula ukusebenza komzimba ngokwehlukana kwako, asithi nje kunengxenye yobuchopho elawula ukunyakaza, kunenye ezothi hamba uye kochama isinye sesiyakuthuma.Igazi lidlala indima enkulu ekuxhumaniseni lo msebenzi obucayi kangaka, yilesi sizathu kubalulekile ukufinyelela njalo kwegazi ebuchosheni futhi libe ngesikalo nangezithako ezifanele.Igazi eliya ebuchosheni lisuke lithwele umoya onamandla nohlanzekile, lifike liwushiye lo moya bese licosha umoya omdala osungcolile libuyele nawo emuva uyohlanzwa emaphashini. Ngiyaphinda, ngale ndlela siyakwazi ukuhamba ngezinyaw ozethu, sigijime, sikhulume ngemilomo, sixhawule abantu ngezandla, umzimba usithume endlini encane siyozikhulula, kubenjeya. Ngifisa sibone ukuthi kubaluleke kangakanani ukuthi igazi leli eligijima ngemithambo, lifike liseyilo ebuchosheni. Ngisho noma ngabe yini ezokwehlisa umumatho nengathikameza amakhemikhali amumethwe yigazi, kusho ukuqala kwezinkinga.Ake sithi imigwaqan aebuchosheni ehambisa leligazi isiyashintsha ayisabi uthela wayeka njengenjwayelo, lokhu kusho ukuthi leya ndawo okumele ihlale ithola umumatho ongakaya, ayisawutholi. Nakanjani kuzoqala ukuzwela emzimbeni; mhlawumbe uzozwa isiyezi, kuthi zibaba, kokunye yikhanjana, inkwantshu kuleyo ngxenye yomzimba elawulwa yileyo ngxenye yobuchopho.Kwesinye isikhathi umgwaqwana awunciphi nje kodwa uvaleke thaqa kuthiwe akudluli lutho. Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi leyo ngxenye yobuchopho ebilinde lelo gazi ayizukuthola lutho. Okunye okungenzeka, imithanjana ehambisa leli gazi ivele igqashuke ebuchosheni, siyayibona inkinga? Nalapho kuleyo ngxenye yobuchopho elindele lelo gazi ayizukuthola lutho. Emizimbeni umphumela yini?Usushaywe wuhlangothi, uhlangothi luyavendlenzeka, usuwe phansi akusahambeki, uyehluleka ukukhuluma, intamo ibheka eceleni, amathe ayajuza, uyazichamela nendle iyaziphumela. Isifo unhlangothi senzeka ngale ndlela!Ngiyafisa ukukuveza ukuthi kwabaningi ziba khona izinto ezenzeka emzimbeni eziba ngamabika, njenganje: ikhanda ongalijwayele, isiyezi, kuthi zibaba, inkwantshu engxenyeni yohlangothi, ulwimi lushwabane, intamo ijijeke, unkwankwaze ulwimi lugoqane ushwashwade amazwi angaphimiseleki, abanye babenamalimi into ongayijwayele.Abantu bakithi bakhetha ukunganaki bazibe nje, okanye baye kubantu abathile, kungaba umelaphi wendabuko, umthandazi, abanye bahambe bayofuna umhlola? Unhlangothi usuqalile la, angithi? Ukulima kuya phambili. Anginankinga nokuya kumelaphi wendabuko.Engifisa kwenzeke wukuthi uma unqume ukuyokwelashwa ngaleyo ndlela yini ungahlali kuye akwelaphe uze usinde? Sifikelani kudokotela okanye emtholampilo sekudlule isikhathi unhlangothi ukushayile sewuze wendlaleka wajula?Unhlangothi ufuna ukwelashwa usaqala, ngiyaphinda abantu bakithi mabeze nakithi lapha ekuqaleni singakajiyi isifo!Okujwayele ukwenzeka ukuzak udokotela emuva kwesikhathi eside seziziningi izindawo esezilimele emzimbeni. Ekugcineni kusishiya nebala elithi siyehluleka ukwelapha unhlangothi. Uma uqoke ukuyoqala ndawondawo isiguli sivinjwa yini ukuhlala selashwe khona kuze kube sekugcineni?Sifunelani ukuhlala njalo sidlaliseka injeje kuzekwakheke isithombe esibi esithi uma esengene lapha ngeke abuye! Sekwaze kwabanenkoleloze ethi uma ushaywe wunhlangothi awusindi uma ungaqalanga kuphikuphi ngaphambi kokuthi uye kudokotela. Amanga aluhlaza lawa, ayikho into enjalo.Ngicela ukuphinda ngithi oshaywe wunhlangothi makasondele ngokushesha kudokotela. Isifo sohlangothi siyaphindana, ngokulandelayo siba sibi kakhulu kunesangaphambilini futhi uma ungelashwa ngokuphelele kuyakwazi ukulandelana ngokushesha.Nakhu okunye okubaluleke kakhulu, lesi sifo senza kuncisheke umoya onamandla ebuchosheni, uma ogulayo ezojikeleza angasheshi ukuza kudokotela wenza ukuthi athi noma esesindile kodwa abenalokho nje ukungathi zasha emqondweni okanye agcine esenesifo sokuwa.Uma ushaywe wunhlangothi fika kudokotela ngokushesha, uzothola ukwelashwa okuphephile, okuphelele nokungena njeje.Mpilonde!NGABE uphoqelekile ukutshela umqashi ukuthi uhlushwa yisifo esithile sengqondo?Lona ngumbuzo ohlupha abantu abaningi abanokhwantalala nezinye izifo zengqondo. NgoLwesihlanu iSouth African Depression and Anxiety Group (Sadag), ibinenkundla yokucobelelana ngolwazi kwiFacebook, lapho abantu bebekhululekile bebuza nangezinkinga ababhekana nazo uma benezifo zengqondo emsebenzini.Izazi zeSadag, ziveze ukuthi yize abantu abaningi benazo izifo zengqondo kodwa bakuthola kunzima ukuziveza obala emsebenzini ngenxa yokusaba ukucwaswa, ngozakwabo abasebenza nabo noma ukubeka itoho labo engcupheni.UMnuz Peter Strasheim ongumnikazi weDLM Labour, oyisazi ngezifo zengqondo, ukukhubazeka nomthetho othinta ezabasebenzi, uthi kubalulekile ukuthi umsebenzi abheke imithetho ethinta ezempilo emsebenzini, ngaphambi kokudalula isifo esimphethe.“Uma ukhetha ukuphumela obala ngokuthi unesifo sengqondo akubalulekile ukuthi usisho igama laso kodwa kufanele ucacise ukuthi sikuthikameza kanjani. Abaqashi abanemithetho emihle yezempilo bayazwelana nawe, bese bekunikeza usizo olufanele. Kubalulekile ukutshela umqashi ngoba kwesinye isikhathi uzodinga ukuyobonana nodokotela wezifo zengqondo noma ukuhlaba ikhefu kancane emsebenzini,” kusho uStrasheim.Uthe uma kwenzeka umsebenzi exoshwa emuva kokuthi ephumele obala ngesifo sengqondo, kufanele abikele umnyango wezabaSebenzi , ummeli neCCMA.UDkt Nkateko Ndala-Magoro oyiClinical Psychologist, uthe kubalulekile nokuthi umsebenzi angavele nje aphumele obala ngesifo sengqondo kodwa asiveze uma siphazamisa indlela asebenza ngayo.UMENGAMELI Cyril Ramaphosa uthe iNingizimu Afrika ihlela ukusheshisa uhlelo lokukhiqiza imigomo yeCovid-19, uma amalungelo obunikazi bempahla (Intellectual property) exegiswa yiziphathimandla zokuhweba zamazwe omhlaba (World Trade Organisation).Uthe uhulumeni wakhe ufuna ukuthi  kuhoxiswe okwesikhashana amalungelo obunikazi bempahla athinta ukukhiqizwa kwemigomo yeCovid-19 (Trade-Related Aspects of Intellectual Property Rights (TRIPS).Usho lokhu encwadini ayibhalela umphakathi masonto onke, izolo.Ukumiswa okwesikhashana kwamalungelo uthe kuzosiza amazwe ampofu ukuze azikhiqizele imigomo azoyisabalalisa emazweni awo, njengoba umhlaba wonke ubhekene nenkinga yokuthi izinkampani ezinamalungelo okukhiqiza imigomo imvamisa okungezasemazweni anothile, ziyehluleka ukukhiqiza umthamo ozokwanela wonke  amazwe kanti futhi imigomo iyabiza."Lesi simo senza ukuthi amazwe anothile aqhubeke nohlelo lwawo lokugoma, antulayo ahlale elinde ukuthenga umgomo kwacebile.  Abantu emazweni antulayo bayafa kusalindiwe ngoba kunohlu olude lwabalinde ukuthenga,"   kusho uRamaphosa.Uthe ngenxa yokuthi imigomo idingeka kuwo  wonke amazwe kuholela ekutheni abakhokha kakhulu kube ibona abayithola kuqala."Imigomo kufanele itholwe yibo bonke abantu hhayi abakhokha kakhulu," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi u-55%  wemigomo yeCovid-19 ukhiqizwa eMpumalanga ye-Asia, u-40% ukhiqizwa e-Europe naseNorth America,  i- Afrika ne-South America bakhiqiza imigomo engaphansi kuka-5%.Uthe iNingizimu Afrika ingelinye lamazwe amahlanu e-Afrika  akwaziyo ukukhiqiza umgomo weCovid-19."Yize iNingizimu Afrika isiyithengile imigomo okuzogonywa ngayo iningi labantu  bese kuvikeleka abanye, kodwa sisesikhulu isidingo sokuthi nathi sikhiqize imigomo ukuze sizivikele,"  kusho yena.Isiphakamiso sikaRamaphosa sokuthi kumiswe okwesikhashana amalungelo obunikazi bempahla sesekwa nawumengameli wase-America uMnuz Joe Biden nenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO). INHLANGANO yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithi ukusabalala kukapokisi wezinkawu, i-monkeypox kuyakhathaza kodwa okwamanje akukakafinyeleli esigabeni lapho kungathiwa ukuhlasela kwayo kuyisimo esiphuthumayo emhlabeni.Umqondisi wale nhlangano uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus, uthe ongoti abehlukene ngaphansi kwale nhlangano bebehlangene bedingida udaba lokubheduka kwalesi sifo bebonisana ngokuthi ngabe sekungamele kuthiwe kumele ukubheduka kwaso kubekwe ngaphansi kwesimo esiphuthumayo yini kwavunyelwana ngokuthi kuyakhathaza kakhulu ukuqubuka kwaso kodwa izikhungo zezempilo emhlabeni ngeke kuthiwe azibe nezinhlelo zaso eziphuthumayo okwamanje."Okwamanje lesi sifo sisasiqaphe ngeso lokhozi ukuthi ngabe sizofaka ingcindezi yini ezikhungweni zezempilo," kusho uGhebreyesus.Uqhube wathi izinkomba abazisebenzisayo zokukala ukuthi sekumele isifo sifakwe ngaphansi kohlu lwezifo okumele kube nezinhlelo eziphuthumayo ngaso, azihambisani nokuthi lesi sifo sifakwe ngaphansi kwalolu hlelo.Uqhube wathi okwamanje abantu okubikwa ukuthi banaso bangu-3 000, basemazweni angu50 abengakaze abe nomuntu ohlaselwe yilesi sifo phambilini."Okwamanje munye umuntu okusabikwe ukuthi ubulawe yilesi sifo, lowo muntu ubenesifo esimenza ukuthi amasosha omzimba abe ntekenteke," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi lesi sifo sekunesikhathi sikhona emazweni ase-Afrika kodwa asinakiwe, azikho izinhlelo eziqondile zokusilawula futhi alukaze lwenziwe ucwaningo olusibheka kabanzi luveze namasu okusilawula."Kumele lokhu kuphele, lesi sifo kumele sibhekwe kabanzi, kungabhekwa sona kuphela kodwa kubhekwe nezinye izifo ezihlasele abantu abahlala emazweni antulayo ezinganakiwe."Udaba lwezempilo kumele kubanjiswane ngalo ngoba luthinta wonke umhlaba," kusho yena.Lesi sifo kuthiwa sithelelana ngokuthi uthintane nomuntu onaso noma ulunywe isinambuzane esinaso noma uthinte igazi noma uketshezi oluphuma kuleso sinambuzane.Ongoti bezempilo bathi akuvamisile ukuthi umuntu athole lesi sifo ngokusondelana nomuntu onaso kodwa kuyenzeka uma bezothintana ngomzimba okuhlanganisa ukuya ocansini, ukuthinta izingubo zokugqoka nezokulala ezisetshenziswa wumuntu onaso.Okunye okuthiwa kungenza ukuthi kube lula ukuthi utheleleke ukuthi usondelane nomuntu onaso uma ekhwehlela.Izifo ezike zangena ohlwinini lwezifo okumele zibhekwe ngokushesha, iCovid-19, Swine flu, Ebola, Polio nezinye.Ikomiti longoti bezifo kwiWHO lithe okwamanje kusamele leli gciwane liqashwe amanye amasonto kubhekwe ukuthi lizoziphatha kanjani."Sisafuna ukuthi sithole ulwazi oluthe xaxa ngaso, sithole nolunye ulwazi esingakabi nalo. Uma sesilutholile lolo lwazi kungenzeka isinqumo esithathiwe sishintshe,” kusho uGhebreyesus.INDODA eyodwa kwangu-17 isengcupheni yokuhlaselwa wumdlavuza wendlala yesinye, i-prostate cancer.Lokhu kuvezwe yiCancer Association of South Africa (Cansa), njengoba kuyinyanga yokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza wendlala yesinye kubantu besilisa.Lezi zibalo iCansa izithathe emqulwini oqukethe yizibalo zabahlaselwe yilo mdlavuza, iCancer Registry yango-2017.UNkk Gerda Strauss oyisikhulu esiphezulu kule nhlangano, uthe ucwaningo olwenziwe kuleli nasemazweni aphesheya, luveza ukuthi umdlavuza uya ngokuya uba mandla kubantu besilisa abamnyama base-Afrika."Okumele sikuqaphele ukuthi umdlavuza uyathanda ukugadla uphindelela emindenini eyodwa. Kubalulekile ukuthi uma uyindoda wazi ukuthi emndenini wakho bakhona yini asebeke baphathwa umdlavuza? Uma bekhona kumele ubheke ukuthi babe naziphi izimpawu? Amadoda awakukhuthaleli ukuhlola imidlavuza ehambisana nokukhula yingakho amanye amadoda abulawa umdlavuza obungeke uwabulale ukube asheshe ahlolwa kwaqinisekiswa ukuthi anawo," kusho yena.Umdlavuza wendlala yesinye utholwa ngokuthi kuhlolwe igazi kubhekwe iProstate Specific Antigen (PSA). Kubalulekile ukuthi amadoda aqale ukuzihlola eneminyaka ewu-40.Uma kukhona ilungu lomndeni elike laba nomdlavuza owesilisa oyilungu lalowo mndeni usengcupheni yokuthi naye ahlaselwe umdlavuza.UNkk Strauss uthe kunobudlelwano obukhona phakathi kwadoda adla ukudla onamafutha amaningi ezilwane okufana nenyama ebomvu enonile.Ucwaningo olwenziwe yiCleaveland Clinic olwethulwe kule nyanga luveza ukuthi inyama ebomvu, isikhuphasha seqanda, imikhiqizo yobisi enamafutha amaningi, kungenza amadoda abe ne-prostate cancer enenkani.UDkt Nima Shaffi ongomunye wabacwaningi uthe okwamanje lolu cwaningo luveze lokho, kusafuneka ukuthi baphinde benze olunye oluzocacisa kabanzi ukuthi yini ekulokhu kudla eyenza ukuthi umdlavuza ube nenkani uma sewelashwa? USolwazi Riana Bornman, wophiko lweSayensi ethinta ezempilo eNyuvesi yasePretoria, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi indoda njalo ngonyaka izihlole ukuthi ayinayo yini i-prostate cancer ukuze itholakale isasesigabeni esiphansi.“Ukuzihlola kumele amadoda akuqale eneminyaka ewu-45 kodwa amadoda ase-Afrika amnyama noma anamalungu omndeni aseke aba nomdlavuza kumele aqale eneminyaka ewu-40 ukuzihlola," kusho yena.Umdlavuza wendlala yesinye ungumdlavuza wesibili ohlasela amadoda, umdlavuza wamaphaphu yiwo ohamba phambili.UKUDLANGA kweCoronavirus kuleli okufaka ingcindezi ezikhungweni zezempilo kuholele ekutheni abantu abaningi babe nezinto abazisebenzisayo emakhaya ngethemba lokuthi zizokwenza ukuthi bangangenwa yileli gciwane, uma libangena bangaguli baze bafinyelele esigabeni sokuthi badinge ukuya esibhedlela.Lokhu bakwenza ngokuthi baphuze imithi ethile abayiphuzayo emakhaya, abanye bayagquma,abanye basebenzisa izinto ezizokwenza ukuthi amasosha  omzimba aqine ukuze uma lifika i gciwane libafice bengekho ntekenteke.Ongoti bezempilo bathi zikhona izinto abantu abangazenza emakhaya eziyizaba. Namhlanje sibheka ukuthi yiziphi lezi zinto abangazisebenzisa futhi kumele bazisebenzise kanjani ukuze zingaphenduki ushevu kubona.Ongoti bazempilo bathi ukuzelapha ekhaya akulula ngoba  amakhambi amaningi alukho ulwazi lwesayensi olukhomba ukuthi ayayelapha iCoronavirus.Amakhambi ahlale ekhona emakhaya amanye awo asetshenziselwa ukupheka  aziwayo ukuthi ayawukhathaza umkhuhlane owejwayelekile nawo abukho ubufakazi bokuthi ayayikhathaza iCoronavirus ngakho kuba nzima ukwazi ukuthi kumele ufake isikali esingakanani.Izinto ezihamba phambili abantu abaziphuzayo izinto ezaziwayo ukuthi ziyawukhathaza umkhuhlane ojwaylekile  ezifana noginger, ugarlic, ulamula  ukugquma zenziwa kakhulu ngalesi sikhathi ngoba kunenkolelo yokuthi kuyasiza nakwiCovid-19.Ongoti bathi lamakhambi asekhaya anakho ukusiza kodwa kumele ungalinge uyeke imithi oynikwe udokotela uma unaleli gciwanwe   nakuba  nayo ingayelaphi iCovid-19 kodwa eyelapha izimpawu ezidalwa ukuthi isiguli sinaleli gciwaneUDkt Atiya Mosam owungoti okwelashweni kwezifo ezijwayelekile uthe  ukugquma kuyasiza ekwehliseni ukucinana."Nakuba  kungalelaphi igciwane kodwa kuyasiza ekwehliseni ukucinana abantu abaningi ababanakho uma bephethwe yiCovid-19.  Kodwa abantu kumele baqaphele uma ukuthi basebenzisa isibulali magciwane  ngoba umjuluko usuke unaleli gciwane ngakho akumele uthintwe ngomunye umuntu, ngoba naye angalithola leli gciwane," kusho uDkt Mosam.UDkt   Indira Govender uthe ukugquma kusiza uma unezimpawu ezingatheni kodwa akulelapheki igciwane.Ukuphuza amanzi anolamula nane-ginger bayakuncoma ngoba  bathi ano-vitaminC onikeza umzimba amandla okulwa namagciwane.UDkt Mosan uthe amanzi anolamula naneginger ayasiza ukupholisa ubuhlungu bomphimbo nakho okujwayele ukuphatha iziguli ezineCovid-19.“ Kulula ukuphuza ukuphuza amanzi anolamula nanoginger kumuntu okhishwa yisisu nomuntu ozizwa  engakuthandi ukudla futhi uginger uyakuqeda ukucanuzela kwenhliziyo,"  kusho uDkt Govender.Okunye okusizayo kumuntu onezinga lokushisa okuphezulu ukumbeka indwangu emanziswe ngamanzi antukuntuku.UDkt Mosama uthe amanzi abandayo aphuma efrijini  namanaqhwa awasetshenziswa.AMAKHEMIKHALI amabili atholakala emikhiqizweni evamile yasendlini njengezibulali magciwane kanye nasetshenziswa kwifenisha anomthelela ekuphazamisekeni kwemizwa okudala i-autism ne-multiple sclerosis.Lokhu kuvezwe ucwaningo olulwenziwe iCase Western Reserve University School of Medicine, ese-Ohio olushicilelwe kwiJournal Nature Neurology muva nje. Ukushicilelwa kwalolu cwaningo kuqondaniswe nokuthi namhlanje, iWorld Autism Awareness Day.Abacwaningi bahlole imikhiqizo yasendlini yokuhlanza engu-1 800  esetshenziswa e-Unites States bathola ukuthi inamakhemikhali anomthelela ekuphazamisekeni kwemizwa. Amakhemikhali amabili ayizithako zeminye imikhiqizo aziwa ngama-quaternary ammonium compounds (quats) ne-organophosphate. abaretardants, angase abe nomthelela omubi empilweni yobuchopho bomuntu.Ama-quats atholakala emikhiqizweni yokugeza umzimba, eyokuthambisa izindwangu, ama-shampoos, imikhiqizo yokuvikela ilanga, kuma-baby wipes, okhilimu bokushefa, ama-nail polish, okhaphethi nezibulala-magciwane.I-Organophosphate itholakala ezintweni zikagesi, ezokwakha, ifenisha nakucwazi.Ngokwalolu cwaningo, ama-quats abangela ama-oligodendrocyte okungamagqamuzana obuchopho akhiqiza ulwelwesi oluvikelayo ukuba afe, i-organophosphate flame retardants iwavimbela avuthwe noma akhule ngokwenele.Omunye wababhali balolu cwaningo uDkt Paul Tesar we-Case Western Reserve University School of Medicine uthe ucwaningo luveza ukuthi ukukhiqizwa kwama-oligodendrocyte, okuphazamisekile kuhlobene nokuphazamiseka kwemizwa njenge-multiple sclerosis ne-autism.Ngakho-ke abacwaningi bakholwa ukuthi bathole 'ubungozi' obungasiza ekuhlonzweni nasekuvikelweni kwalesi sifo."Sithemba ukuthi umsebenzi wethu uzoba nomthelela ezinqumweni ezinolwazi mayelana nezinyathelo zokulawulwa kwala makhemikhali," kusho uTesar.Bangu-1.8 million abantu emhlabeni jikelele abane-multiple sclerosis, ngokusho kweWorld Health Organisation (WHO). Ngokwale nhlangano ingane eyodwa kwezingu-100 emhlabeni ine-autism.UDkt Erin Cohn ongumbhali kulolu cwaningo uthe isibalo sezingane ezine-Autism e-US siphindaphindeke kathathu eminyakeni engu-16Lokhu kwenza ukuthi kube nemibuzo yokuthi akukho yini okunye okunomthelela ekutheni lesi sifo sande ngaphandle kwalokho okwaziwayo  kokuthi kusuke kunenkinga yama-genes nokuthi nemvelo ingaba nomthelela.Ama-quats kwaziwa ukuthi ayasebenza ekubulaleni amagciwane kanye nesikhunta."Ukusetshenziswa kwemikhiqizo yokuhlanza, izibulala-magciwane kanye namakhemikhali kunomthelela empilweni yomphakathi emakhaya, ezikoleni, ezindaweni zokunakekelwa kwempilo nasemiphakathini nsuku zonke.“Ngemuva kokuhlasela kweCovid-19 kwenyukile ukusetshenziswa kwezibulali magciwane ezihlanza izandla," kusho uDkt Teaser.Ucwaningo olwenziwe ngo-2022 olwenziwe emagundaneni luveze ukuthi i-organophosphate flame retardants iguqula ukukhula kobuchopho enganeni esasesibelethweni.I-American Osteopathic Association yabheka imiphumela yamakhemikhali emagundaneni yathola ukuthi abangela ukwehla kwezinga lesidoda emagundaneni esilisa, awesifazane abe namaqanda amancane okudala ukuthi azale amagundane akhubazekile noma anezimo zempilo ezikhomba ukuphazamiseka.INHLANGANO eqwashisa futhi ilekelele imiphakathi entula amanzi yeluleka abantu ngokuthi baqaphele uma besebenzisa amanzi ngoba uma engcolile, angabagulisa. Bathi amanzi angahlanzekile ayimbangela yesifo sohudo esibulala u-19%, wezingane ezineminyaka engaphansi kwemihlanu  kuleli njalo ngonyaka.AbeSanofi, inhlangano elekelela imiphakathi ngezinsiza zokuthola amanzi ahlanzekile, ithe izingane ezihlala ezindaweni ezingenawo amanzi ahlanzekile zivamise ukuba sengcupheni yokuhlaselwa yisifo sokuhudo, esinganawo amandla kwesinye isikhathi zihlaselwe esinamandla esigcina sidlule nemiphefumulo yazo.Ucwaningo olushicilwe emqingweni wezempilo iSouth African Medical Journal, ngo-2018 lukhomba ukuthi ezinganeni ezingu-1000 ezizelwe, ezingu-27 kuya kwezingu-33, ziyashona ngaphambi kokuthi zibe neminyaka emihlanu. Ngokocwaningo ingxenye yezingane ishona ngesikhathi ibelethwa. Isifo sohudo, ipneumonia nesandulela ngculazi zihlonzwe njengezifo ezihamba phambili ngokubulala izingane ezingazange zishone ngesikhathi zibelethwa. Ngombiko wocwaningo ezinye izifo ezibulala izingane yizinhlekelele, izifo ezingena ezinganeni ngesikhathi onina besazikhulelwe, okuvame ukuba yinhlliziyo engekho esimeni esifanele, ukungakhuli kwezitho zengane ngendlela elindelekile iDown Syndrome, nezinye.Ongoti bezempilo bathi isifo sohudo esinganqamuki sidala izinkinga emzimbeni. Ezinye izinkinga kungaba ukuphelelwa ngamanzi emzimbeni futhi uma umuntu engalutholanga usizo ngokushesha angashona. Bathi okunye okwenzekayo ngesikhathi umuntu ekhishwa yisisu, umzimba awukwazi ukuthola imisoco okumele ngabe uyithola ekudleni ngoba kusuke sekuphazamiseke nomgudu wokugayeka kokudla.Inhloko yophiko lwesayensi enhlanganweni iSanofi, uNkk  Momeena Omarjee, ithe: “Izingane ezihlala ezindaweni ezikhungethwe ubuphofu zisemathubeni aphindwe kayishumi okubulawa yisifo sohudo, uma kuqhathaniswa nezingane ezihlala ezindaweni ezisezingenabo ubuphofu,"UNkk Omarjee usho kanje ngempelasonto ngesikhathi kugujwa usuku lwezingane, iNational Children Day.Uthe bakhethe ukuthi usuku balugube ngokubheka ukunakekelwa komgudu ohambisa ukudla ezinganeni. Uthe eNingizimu Afrika ukubheduka kwesifo sohudo kuvamise ukudalwa indawo engahlanzekile izingane ezihlala kuyo, ukungabikhona kwamanzi ahlanzeke ngokwenele, ukungahanjiswa ngendlela kwendle nezinye izinto ezithinta inhlanzeko.Ezinye izinkinga zokungahlanzeki kwamanzi kuleli uthe zidalwa ukucishwa kugesi ngenhloso yokuwonga, ukuhlasela kwesimo zezulu esilimaza ingqalasizinda yokuhanjiswa kwamanzi,  okuyizikhukhula, ukuguguleka kwenhlabathi okusanda kwenzeka KwaZulu-Natal, nase-Eastern Cape.Uthe inhlangano yakhe ngokubambisana neSave Children SA, izibekele ukuthi isize abantu abangu-2 million ukuthi bathole amanzi ahlanzekile  ngaphambi kuka-2025, okwamanje basazize abantu abangu-54 000 bakuleli.INTSHA namadoda kuthiwa bayadembesela ukuya ezikhungweni zezempilo ngoba besaba ukucwaswa noma ukungaphatheki kahle kulezi zikhungo.Ngenxa yalokhu kwasungulwa amasu azolekelela uMnyango wezeMpilo ukuze basondele ezikhungweni zezempilo, iSouth African National Intergrated Men's Health Strategy (SANINH) 2020-2025.  Nge-SANINH kunohlu lokuhlolwa olubhaliwe ukuze lulandelwe izingane ezineminyaka ephakathi  kuka 10 kuya ku 19, abesilisa abaphakathi kuka-20 kuya ku-34 namadoda aneminyaka engu-50 kuya phezulu basizakale.Ngala masu kukhuthazwa abafana namadoda ukuthi bajwayele ukuhlolwa ezifo ezifana nesifo sikashukela, umdlavuza, isifuba somoya nesifo senhliziyo nezifo zamaphaphu njalo ngonyaka.Kukhuthazwa abafana namadoda ukuthi baphile impilo ezobasiza ekutheni bangabi sengcupheni yokungenwa izifo eziyingozi okungaba ukugwema ukubhema, ukuzijwayeza ukudla ukudla okunempilo, ukugwema ukuba nesisindo esikhulu somzimba,  ukunyakazisa umzimba ngokuzivocavoca noma ukwenza imisebenzi enyakazisa umzimba.UMnuz Lesego Mateme we-SA Tobacco Free Youth Forum, uthe iningi lentsha liqala ukubhema ugwayi lisafunda ezikoleni zamabanga aphansi."Ucwaningo lwakamuva olwenziwe umkhandlu wezempilo kuleli, iSouth African Medical Reseach Council (SAMRC), luveza ukuthi u-26% wentsha esemanyuvesi ubhema  isibhawubhawu, ama-e cigarettes, i-vaping nezinye izinhlobo zikagwayi abacabanga ukuthi zinobungozi kancane kunogwayi ojwayelekile,  kanti bayazikhohlisa. Ama-e-cigarretes  ayingozi, iningi lentsha lingeniswa ezibhedlela lihaqwe izifo zamaphaphu ezidalwa ukuwabhema," kusho uMateme.Unxuse uhulumeni ukuthi ashaye imithetho ezovikela intsha ukuze  ingangeni ogibeni lokubhema lo gwayi.UDkt  Padaruth (Prithy) Ramlachan, owudokotela owungoti wezifo zocansi, oke waba umengameli we-African Society for Sexual Medicine, uthe izingane ezineminyaka ephakathi kwewu-10 kuya ku-19 kubalulekile ukuthi zihlolwe ukuthi zizwa kahle, zihlolwe amazinyo nomlomo, zihlolwe ukuthi zibona kahle  nokuthi imizimba yazo isebenza kahle yini. Ngaphezu kwalokho zilandele uhlelo lokugomela izifo. UDkt Ramlachan uthe amadoda aneminyaka ephakathi kuka-20 kuya ku-34 kumele ungapheli unyaka engazange ahlole ukuthi izinhlamvu zamankwahla azinazo yini izimila noma izigaxa ezingajwayelekile, ahlolwe ukuthi umfutho wegazi usezingeni elikahle yini,   izifo zocansi nokuthi inhliziyo ishaya kahle yini.“Ukuhlolwa okujwayelekile okubalwa umfutho wegazi, ushukela egazini, isisindo somuntu kubaluleke ngendlela eyisimanga yize kungabukeka kuyinto encane ongayenza uma unesikhathi,” kugcizelela uDkt Ramlachan. ABALELWA ku-38 amazwe abike ukuthi kunabantu emazweni awo okubikwe ukuthi banegciwane elizishintshile leCovid-19 i-Omicron.Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithe nakuba emaningi amazwe okubikwe ukuthi anabantu abanaleli gciwane kodwa akukabi khona umuntu okubikwe ukuthi ushonile ngenxa yalo. UDkt Maria Van Kerkhove weWHO uthe ngokubona kwabo leli gciwane lisabalala ngokushesha kodwa abakazi ukuthi ubungozi balo bungakanani.Uthe kusazothatha amasonto ngaphambi kokuthi bazi kabanzi ngokuthi ngabe lithelelana ngokushesha ukwedlula amanye yini nokuthi imigomo ekhona njengoba kusenziwa ucwaningo ngalo izoqhubeka isebenze ngendlela ebisebenzza ngayo yini noma izokwehla.Umengameli wase-USA uMnuz Joe Biden, uthe  leli gciwane kumele bakhathazeke ngalo kodwa akumele okwamanje batatazele kuze kube baneminingwane ephelele ngalo.Izibalo zakamuva zabahaqwe yileli gciwane kuleli zikhomba ukuthi bangu-11 125 abantu abasha abahaqwe yilona ngeSonto.IGauteng iyona ehamba phambili ngezibalo zabahaqwe yigciwane,  bangu-7 929 khona.Ongoti bezempilo bakuqinisekisile ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika isisesiwombeni sesine sokuhlalela kweCovid-19.Uhulumeni unxusa abantu ukuthi bagome ukuze bazivikele kuleli gciwane ngoba imigomo kuseyiyona kuphela engakuvikela kuleli gciwane.Bathe nakuba leli gciwane kubonakala sengathi lizosabalala ngokushesha kuneDelta yaphambilini kodwa bathi noma kungehla ukuvikeleka kodwa ukugoma kusasiza ngokugwema  ukuthi  abantu bagule kakhulu badinge ukulaliswa ezibhedlela.UmbuzoNGINGOWESIFAZANE, ngihlala nengane yami enonyaka. Asisathandani nobaba wayo ngoba selokhu kwabakhona ingane izinto aziphindanga zahamba kahle phakathi kwethu. Sasixabana njalo, ngathola ukuthi useqonyiwe, sahlukana. Yize ngangisamthanda kodwa ngasamukela isimo.Inkinga wukuthi uyafika ezobona ingane futhi ayilethele nezinto, yilapho uthando luvele luvuke kimi lume ngezinyawo. Ngiyabona ukuthi usangithanda ngoba sesike salala. Ngelinye ilanga efikile wangitshela nokuthi uyazisola ngesenzo sakhe, usefuna ukubuya. Ngiyamthanda.  Angifuni ukuqamba amanga, manje angazi noma ngimbuyise yini? Ngizokwazi kanjani ukuthi ngeke yini futhi esangishiya nengane?ImpenduloKuyacaca ukuthi, ukuhlukana kwakho naye, awuzange ukwamukele kodwa wawudinwe ukuthi useqonyiwe. Okuyiphutha elikhulu! Akumele uhlukane nomuntu usamthanda ngoba leyo nto ihlukumeza wena, nomuntu ozama ukuthandana naye. Lokhu kungenxa yokuthi inhliziyo yakho isasele kulona ozitshela ukuthi usuhlukene naye. Njengoba usamthanda futhi senike naya nasocansini, ekubeni nithi nihlukene, ngibona kungcono nihlale phansi. Nizame ukulungisa izinto ngoba kungenjalo nizolokhu nidlala umdlalo kamalalana, ozobe uxhaphaza wena. Akuhlukanwa nomuntu usamthanda dadewethu, ngoba inhliziyo isuke ingaxolile.KUSENZIMA ukuthi kusungulwe izinsiza eziningi ezakhelwe amadoda afuna ukuhlela umndeni.Lokhu kushiwo uDkt Zozo Nene oyinhloko yophiko olwelapha izinkinga ezithinta inzalo esibhedlela iSteve Biko obuye asebenze eNyuvesi yasePretoria. Ukusho lokhu ngesikhathi kunomhlangano wokucobelelana ngolwazi ngezinto ezenza ukuthi abantu bangakuthandi ukuhlela umndeni nokukhulelwa kwamantombazane asemancane. Lo mhlangano ubuhlelwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli obewenziwe ngezobuchwepheshe, izolo.UDkt Nene uthe ukuhlela umndeni nakuba kunganele, kube yinto eyenziwa ngumuntu wesifazane kuphela kodwa okwamanje zisembalwa izinto ezikhona zabantu besilisa.Uthe uma kucwaningwa ngokuhlela umndeni ngokwendoda, kusuke kubhekwa umkhiqizo ongaba yiphilisi okulula ukuthi iphinde ikhulelise uma isiyekile ukuhlela, elingeke liphazamise imizwa yocansi futhi elingabizi kakhulu."Okwenza ukuthi zingabi ziningi izinto ezikhona emakethe zokuhlela kwamadoda ukuthi umzimba wendoda kawufani nomuntu wesifazane. Umuntu wesifazane uneqanda elilodwa eliphumayo kuye ngenyanga kanti endodeni imbewu ekhiqizekayo ngosuku ingu-290 million. Ngesikhathi indoda ichitha imbewu isuke iphakathi kuka-20 kuya-40  million. Indoda ikhiqiza imbewu engu-1 500 ngomzuzwana, ngakho umkhiqizo okhona kumele ukwazi ukwenza zonke lezi zinto," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi abantu abaningi besifazane bayesaba ukusebenzisa imikhiqizo yokuhlela ngoba besaba ukuthi izokwenza ukuthi bangabatholi abantwana."Lokhu kwenziwa ukuthi kunabantu abantu abasabalalisa ulwazi olungelona bese abanye abantu balukholwe. Ikhona eminye imikhiqizo eyenza ukuthi uma umuntu esebenzisa yona kube nenkinga," kusho yena.UDkt Manala Makua woMnyango wezeMpilo uthe ukukhulelwa kwamantombazane asemancane aneminyaka ephakathi kuka-10 no14, kuyethusa."Ngo-2018, amantombazane anale minyaka akhulelelwa, ayengaphezulu kuka-2 000 nyakenye. Lesi sibalo sesiphindaphindeke kabili. Akufanele ngabe sikhuluma ngamantombazane anale minyaka akhulelwayo. Izingane ezingaka akumele ngabe ziyakhulelwa," kusho yena.UDkt Alex Maisoto uthe lesi sibalo kungenzeka ukuthi singaphezulu ngoba amantombazane okukhulunywa ngawo aye ezikhungweni zezempilo,  kawabelethelanga emakhaya noma azihushulele wona izisu."Lolu daba ludinga ukusukunyelwa ngoba amantombazane akhulelwe esamancane aba nezinkinga eziningi ezinye zazo eziwaholela ekutheni abelethe izingane ezinesisindo esincane. Enye yezinkinga, aba nokhwantalala olwenziwa ukuthi aye azibone ekhishwa inyumbazana, ngakolunye uhlangothi, enenkinga yokukhulisa ingane edinga ukuthi abe ngomama ngokuphelele, kungakhathalekile ukuthi uneminyaka emingaki. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, umuntu kusuke kusafanele aye esikoleni. Uba sengcupheni yokuthi agcine eyekile ukufunda," kusho yena.Uthe kusamele ukuthi kusungulwe imitholampilo noma izinhlelo ezizobhekana ngqo namantombazane amancane ukuze angesabi ukuya emitholampilo ayohlela umndeni ngoba kuze kufinyelele esigabeni sokuthi akhulelwe nje, ayesaba ukuya emitholampilo ngoba abahlengikazi kwabona abakafundiseki."Kudingeka ukuthi sibe nabahlengikazi abangeke babehlulele ngokuthi sebefuna ukuhlela umndeni besabancane. Abahlengikazi abangeke basho uma bebone intombazane encane emtholampilo indaba igcine ifinyelele ekhaya, ingane ingabe isabuyela ngoba isaba," kusho yena.KUNEZINTO eziyizinkolelo-ze, ezikhulunywa ngabantu, ikakhulu ezinkundleni zokuxhumana nezigcina sezididisa abantu ngoba uma kuxoxwa ngazo, bazitshela ukuthi  ziyiqiniso ekubeni zingamanga.Kunenkulumo ethi umuntu wesifazane ompofu noma okhanyayo ngebala, akamnandi embhedeni kodwa omnandi kakhulu yiloyo onebala elizothile.Bakwethu, akulona iqiniso lokho. Kangisho ngoba nakhu ngikhanya ngebala kodwa ngisho ngoba ngiyalwenza ucwaningo.Akugcini kwabesifazane kuphela kodwa nabesilisa abakhanyayo ngebala, bachazwa njengabantu abangakwazi ukwanelisa owesifazane embhedeni. Ngisho noma osisi bekhuluma ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, bakubeka kucace ukuthi indoda empofu abayifuni.Nginombuzo owodwa kulaba abakholelwa kule nto wokuthi,  ngabe ibala lomuntu lihlangana kanjani nokuya ocansini? Kwesinye isikhathi kufanele siyeke ukufafaza amanga ngenhloso yokucindezela nokuzwisa abanye abantu ubuhlungu.Ngenxa yala manga, kunabantu asebenqena nokuzibandakanya nezothando ngoba nakhu bona bayakhanya ngebala.Omunye uze ayeke ukuqoma indoda ayithandayo ngoba nakhu impofu ngoba  yena ukholwa ukuthi indoda empofu ishaya udaka embhedeni.Ngifisa ukwazi ukuthi la manga aqhamuka namuphi ungqeqe, owayenesikhathi sokuhamba ezwa bonke abantu abampofu, waze wezwa nokuthi abamnandi? Ngifisa siyilungise le nto ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi singabantu asithandi izinto ezifanayo.Wena uma ungathandi ukuthandana nomuntu okhanyayo ngebala, yeka labo abathandayo babaqome.Nikhumbule futhi ukuthi akuthina sonke esithanda ukujola nabantu abanebala elizothile.Mina ngikholwa ukuthi umuntu nomuntu unohlobo lwakhe lomuntu aluthandayo nolumchazayo. Akekho futhi umuntu ophoqwayo ukuthi athandane nomuntu angamthandi.Uma singakwazi ukuhlukanisa izinto eziyizinkolelo-ze nezinto zangempela singaphila kahle. Ngoba abantu abampofu abamnandi embhedeni pho bagana/baganwa kanjani?  Bashada/bashadelwa kanjani? Kufanele engabe phela bangumgodi onganukwanja ngoba ayikho indaba yabo.Le nto nje yaziqhamukela nomuntu thizeni, owaba nebhadi lokuzithokozisa nomuntu ompofu, igazi labo langahlangana kahle nokuyinto eyenzekayo nakumuntu onebala elizothile.Abantu abaningi bazithola bedidiseka ngenxa yokulalela zonke izinto ezikhulunywa ngabantu ezingelona iqiniso.Asikho isidingo sokuyeka ukuthanda umuntu omthandayo ngoba nakhu uthi uyakhanya ngebala.Akekho umuntu owuchwepheshe wocansi, ngabe umpofu noma unebala elizothile.Yekani nje ukufaka izimendlela zamanga ngabantu abanebala elizothile. Mina ngazi indoda enebala elizothile kodwa engeve ifathuza embhedeni nokufakazela khona ngempela ukuthi embhedeni akuyi ngabala kodwa kuya ngomuntu ukuthi yena umdlalo uwudlala kanjani.Ngicela nje abantu abampofu bayeke ukuzizwa bengelutho ngenxa yala manga akhulunywa ngabo.Kumele nazi ukuthi ezinye izinto zisuke zikhulunyelwa ukuqhuba usuku nje hhayi ngoba ziyiqiniso.Ngakho-ke nani ningavumi ukudidiseka. Umuntu akathandane nenhlobo yakhe ayithandayo, niyeke ukufafaza amanga.Alukho uhlobo lomuntu okuqinisekisiwe ukuthi lo muntu onjena umnandi kodwa zikhona lezo zinkolelo-ze, ezenza umuntu ashele nomuntu angamthandi ngoba embona enale nto okuthiwa abantu abanayo bamnandi.Omunye uke ashele umuntu wesifazane onezindebe ezinkulu ngoba ekholelwa ukuthi unenkomo enkulu.Omunye aqome owesilisa onamagwegwe ngoba ekholwa ukuthi embhedeni bangojikelele.Umuntu uma esefika kungasenjalo bese eyaphoxeka kanti uyena othanda izinto.Asibeke eceleni ukuthanda izinto nokuya ngezinto esizizwa zishiwo ngabantu kodwa iya kumuntu ngoba umthanda.ONGOTI bezempilo bathi amavithamini afakwa egazini ngomjovo noma ngama-drip adlisayo kubantu abadumile kulezi zinsuku kumele bawasebenzise ngokuqaphela.Iningi losaziwayo, nabantu abasebenza imisebenzi ebenza bazizwe benengcindezi, sekuvamile ukuthi ubezwe bethi basebenzisa imijovo yamavithamini eyaziwa nge-Intravenous Vitamin (IV) therapy.Le mijovo isetshenziswa ngabantu abaningi emhlabeni wonke ngoba kunenkolelo yokuthi ukujova ngala mavithamini kuhlanza isikhumba,  kususe imibimbi, kunikeze amasosha omzimba amandla, kwehlise ukhwantalala, kukwenze ube nomfutho, eminye kuthiwa ihlanza igazi uma kade uphuze utshwala.Kubantu abaningi le ndlela ibonakala iyindlela esizayo ekutheni bakwazi ukubhekana nezinselelo ezikhona esikhathini samanje kodwa odokotela bathi abayisebenzisayo le mijovo kumele bayisebenzise ngokuqaphela futhi benze isiqiniseko sokuthi izindawo abajova kuzo zibhalisiwe.Ulwazi olutholakala emqulwini wezempilo, i-American Journal of Infection Control, ekhuluma ngakho ukusetshenziswa kwe-IV therapy, ithi kunemibiko yokuthi kuyenzeka abajove ngale mijovo bazithole sebenamagciwane emgudwini wegazi angene ngesikhathi bejova.Lo mqulu uthi okuyinkinga kakhulu nge-IV therapy ukuthi amanye amazwe awanalo uhlelo lokuyilawula ngoba ayingeni ngaphansi kohlelo lwemithi elawulwa yilezi zikhungo, njengakhona e-America, i-US Food and Drug Administration (FDA) ayikulawuli ukusetshenziswa kwale mijovo uma isetshenziselwa ukuzigcina usesimeni esikahle sempilo. Ilawula imijovo engama-IV esetshenziselwa ukwelapha ngakho akekho umuntu oqaphe ukuthi aphephile nokuthi kulandelwa imigomo uma abantu bejova ngawo.Ongoti bazempilo bathi uma ungumuntu obona ukuthi udinga ukwengeza umsoco emzimbeni, kungakuhle ukuthi usebenzise indlela ejwayelekile yokuphuza amavithamini elawulekayo noma uqale ubonisane nodokotela wakho ngokuthi kukulungele yini ukuthi ungasebenzisa le ndlela yokufaka amavithamini egazini lakho.USolwazi Alan Shenkin, weNyuvesi yaseLiverpool, emqingweni wezempilo iNutritional Journal, uthe kumele abantu bangabheki imiphumela ebonakala ngamehlo bese beba nethemba lokuthi le mijovo iyasebenza, bengazi ukuthi ngesikhathi ifakwa egazini yini eyilimazile."Abanye abantu basebenzisa le  mijovo ngoba bethi bazoba nomfutho wokusebenza kodwa lo womfutho kuba owesikhashana, ngemuva kwalokho umuntu akhathale ngaphezulu kwalokhu akade eyikho ngaphambi kokujova. Abanye kusuke sekudingeka ukuthi bangaphumeli elangeni ngoba isikhumba sabo sigcina sesizwela," kusho uSolwazi Shenkin.Uthe okunye ngala mavithamini ukuthi axutshwe ngendlela engefani kuya ngodokotela wakulowo mtholampilo ukuthi yena usebenzisa maphi. Amavithamini ajwayele ukuba kule ngxube yiB12, iZinc namanye."Uma ubuza ukuthi umehluko ukuphi kunokusebenzisa amavithamini ngendlela ejwayelekile, uthola impendulo ethi uma ujova amavithamini angena ngqo egazini kanti lawa angamaphilisi kusuke kusamele ancibilike kuqala. Inkinga ezinye iziguli ezibhekana nayo ukuthi odokotela abazijovayo beqisa isikali ngoba bayazixubela, abalawulwa," kusho uShenkin.UZOKWETHULWA ngonyaka ozayo umqulu wamasu amasha okwelapha isifo sofuba nezifo zocansi ezithathelanayo kuleli.UMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli usuqalile ukudweba kabusha amasu okubhekana nesifo sofuba (TB) nezifo zocansi ezithathelanayo, iNew TB and Sexually Transmitted Infections (STI) National Strategic Plan, abanethemba lokuthi azosiza ekutheni lezi zifo zibe sezigobekile ngo-2030.Lokhu kushiwo nguNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuzwelonke, uDkt Joe Phaahla, sekuvalwa ingqungquthela ebidingida izinto ezithinta isifo sofuba kuleli, ebibanjelwe eThekwini ngeledlule.Uvumile ukuthi imikhankaso nezinhlelo zokulwa nalesi sifo zike zasilela emuva ngesikhathi kuhlasele iCovid-19 kuleli.Ucwaningo luveza ukuthi ngo-2020 nje kuphela bangu-328 000 abantu abasha abahaqwe yisifo sofuba kuleli, u-60% wabo bekungabantu abangculazi. UPhaahla uthe la masu azosiza ekutheni izwe likwazi ukulwa nalesi sifo futhi.“La masu njengamanje asesigabeni esibalulekile sokudwetshwa kwawo lapho kusahlanganiswa khona amaphepha akhona. Engqungqutheleni yalesi sifo ngonyaka ozayo sizowethula la masu esibheke ukuthi sisebenze ngawo kuze kube u-2030," kusho uPhaahla.Uqhube wathi luningi ucwaningo olwenziwayo mayelana nemigomo yokuvimbela lesi sifo kanye nemishanguzo esetshenziswa isikhathi esifishane yokuselapha. Uthe okwamanje imiphumela iyethembisa kodwa njengoba kungakaphothulwa, kusasetshenziswa umgomo, iBCG, onikezwa izingane.Uthe imiphumela yocwaningo olwenziwayo ibanikeza ithemba lokuthi singase sehle isikhathi sokudla imishanguzo yokwelapha lesi sifo kuhlanganisa nokwelashwa kweTB engezweli emakhanjini, iMulti-Drug Resistant TB.KUHLUKENE imibono ngomthethosivivinywa ohlongozwayo, olawula ugwayi. UMnyango wezeMpilo ubuvule uhlelo lokuthi kuphawulwe ngawo, kuxhunywana ngokusebenzisa ubuchwepheshe.Ngeledlule uMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli uvule ithuba lokuthi abathintekayo kulo mkhakha baphawule ngokuthi ngabe ezomnotho zizothinteka kanjani, iSocio-Economic Impact Assessment System (SEIAS), uma umthetho ohlongozwayo, iControl of Tobacco and Electronic Delivery Systems Bill, iphasiswa ube wumthetho ngokugcwele.Lokhu kwenziwe kwaqondaniswa nenyanga uMeyi, ngokwekhalenda lezempilo ehlelelwe ukuthi kwenziwe ngayo imikhankaso yokulwa nokubhenywa kukagwayi kuleli, i-Anti-tobacco Campaign.ISouth Africa Tobacco Transformation Alliance (Satta), iyakuchitha ukuthi lo mthethosivivinywa wenziwe ube ngumthetho.Phakathi kwezinye izinto eziqukethwe wumthethosivivinywa wukulawula ukubhenywa kukagwayi, ukudayiswa kwawo, ukukhangiswa kwawo, yizinto okumele zibhalwe emaphaketheni awo nokuthi kumele abukeke kanjani.USihlalo weSatta, uMnuz Ntando Shadrack Sibisi, ephawula ngokuqukethwe wumthethosivivinywa, uthe kuyingozi nobudedengu ukuthi umnyango ucabanga ukugunyaza umthetho ozokwenza ukuthi kuqine imithetho, ekubeni vele le mboni idonsa kanzima ngenxa yokuthi ilahlekelwe yinzuzo, okuholele ekutheni idilize abasebenzi ngenxa yeCovid-19.“Kuyinto eyaziwayo ukuthi le mboni ikhinyabezekile ngenxa yokuthi uhulumeni uke wakumisa ukudayiswa kukagwayi kuleli, ngesikhathi ukuvalwa kwezwe kusesesigabeni sesihlanu. Ukuhlasela kweCovid-19 kuleli kusifundisile ukuthi kumele kulandelwe uphenyo lwesayensi. Nakulokhu sithi ucwaningo lwesayensi yilo okumele lusho ukuthi yini okumele yenziwe ngalolu daba,"  kusho uSibisi.Abadayisa ugwayi ezimakethe ezincane, abeSouth African Informal Traders Alliance (Saita), bathi bayakwemukela ukuthi lolu daba luke lubekwe ezithebeni kudingidwe ngalo.UNobhala weSaita, uMnuz Michael Mokgoja, uthe ukubekwa kwemibono ngalolu daba kufike ngesikhathi esikahle njengoba sekunolwazi olukhomba ukuthi eminye imikhiqizo kagwayi, engashiswa uma ubhema inobungozi obuncane kuneshiswayo."Lolu lwazi lukhomba ukuthi ngempela sidinga ukuholwa wucwaningo lwesayensi, oluzosinika ubufakazi obuyibo ngalolu daba,"  kusho uMokgoja.INHLANGANO egqugquzela ukuthi abantu ukuthi badle ukudla okunempilo ukuze bagweme izifo, ifuna inyuselwe ku-20% intela kashukela kuleli. Njengamanje intela kashukela kuleli ingu-11%, iHealthy Living Alliance (HEALA) ithi ushukela otholakala eziphuzweni  ezinoshukela ungaphezulu kwalokho okumele ngabe uyikho yingakho kumele izinkampani ezikhiqiza lezo ziphuzo zikhokhe intela. UMnuz Lawrence Mbalati ohola lo mkhankaso kwi-HEALA, uthe ushukela otholakala kuzo  unomthelela wokuthi abantu bakhuluphale ngokweqile, okubenza ukuthi bangenwe isifo sikashukela,  babe nezinkinga zenhliziyo neminye imidlavuza.Uqhube wathi ngo-2016  uhulumeni  wafaka umthetho wokulawula usawoti ofakwa ngesikhathi kukhiqizwa ukudla ngenhloso yokuthi abantu bangadli ukudla okunosawoti omningi ngoba usawoti unomthelela omubi empilweni yomuntu nakushukela kumele kwenziwe okufanayo."Umuntu kumele adle ushukela ongamathisipuni ayisithupha kuya kwayisishiyagalombili ngosuku.  Abakhiqizi beziphuzo bafaka ushukela omningi ngakho yibo okumele bakhokhe intela, asifuni  ukuthi le ntela ikhokhwe umphakathi ngoba uvele uphila ngaphansi kwengcindezi. Ukwenyuka kwentela kuzokwenza ukuthi abakhiqizi balezi ziphuzo babuyekeze izithako zabo behlise njengoba sibona sekukhona iziphuzo okuthiwa zinoshukela owehlisiwe  noma ezingenawo ushukela njengamanje,  kodwa emlonyeni ushukela uzwakala ngendlela efanayo," kusho yena.Uthe ngalo mkhankaso wabo bafisa ukuthi ungqongqoshe wezezimali kuleli   le ntela ayifake kwibhajethi yalo nyaka kodwa uyazi ukuthi kungenzeka kungenzeki ngoba kuningi okubhekwayo."Ushukela awunayo intela ngoba ngumuntu  olawula ukuthi uwufaka kangakanani  kodwa abakhiqiza beziphuzo ezinoshukela bona kumele bakhokhe intela ngoba yibo abafaka ushukela omningi umthengi akakwazi ukukulawula lokho. Njengamanje uhulumeni wenza imithetho elawula ukufakwa kukasawoti emikhiqizweni yakuleli ngenhloso yokwehlisa izifo. Lo-20% esiwushoyo awusuki  kithina kodwa ubekwe inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWord Health Organisation (WHO), sifuna ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika ilandele okubekwe yile nhlangano,“ kusho uMbalati.Uthe kuleli le ntela iyingxenye  yamasu omnyango wezempilo okulwa nezinga eliphezulu labantu abakhuluphele ngokweqile kanye nokulawulwa kwezifo.Uqhube wathi  selokhu le ntela  yasungulwa ngo-2018 kuleli uhulumeni useqoqe R3.29 billion."Le mali  iwusizo kuhulumeni isetshenziselwa ukwenza ucwaningo  lwezempilo nakwezinye izinto. Njengoba sibhekene neCovid-19 kudingeka imali eningi, uma le ntela ingenyuka ibe ngu-20%, uhulumeni uzoqoqa imali eningi  engasiza nasezinhlelweni zokuthengwa komgomo weCovid-19,"  kusho yena. PHILI MJOLISIPHINDAPHINDEKE kathathu isibalo sabantu ababulewe yiCovid-19 emhlabeni  kunaleso esisaziyo.Lokhu kuvezwe yinhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni  iWorld Health Organisation (WHO) esithangamini nabezindaba sakamuva.Izibalo ezikhona njengamanje zithi bangu-3.4 million abantu ababulewe yileli gciwane emhlabeni selokhu sabheduka eChina ekupheleni kuka-2019 kodwa iWHO ithi izibalo eziyizona ziphindaphindeke kathathu kulezi.UDkt Samira Asma, osophikweni olucubungula ulwazi kwi-WHO, uthe nakuba abanye abantu bengabulawanga yiCovid-19 ngqo kodwa bebengeke bashone ukube belungekho ubhubhane oluholele ekutheni bangakutholi ukwelashelwa isifo abanaso  base beyashona."Izibalo zabashone ngenxa yaleli gciwane luphindaphindeke kabili noma kathathu kunokubikwe ngokusemthethweni,"  kusho uDkt Asma.Uthe ngokombiko owenziwe yile nhlangano ngo-2020, kuvela ukuthi okungenani bangaphezulu kuka-3 million abanye abantu abashonile ukufa kwabo okweyamaniswa neCovid-19 ngqo. Ngaleso sikhathi izibalo ezisemthethweni zababulewe yigciwane uthe zazikhomba ukuthi bangu- 1.8 million abashonile.Ebuzwa ukuthi ngabe izibalo zababulewe wubhubhane uma ehlanganisa nalabo bantu manje zithini, uphendule ngokuthi: "Ngicabanga ukuthi kuphephile ukuthi ngithi isilinganiso esiyiso kungaba ngabantu abaphakathi kuka-6 kuya ku-8 million".Uthe iWHO ibisebenzisana namazwe ukuze iqonde izibalo zangempela zabantu ababulewe wubhubhane. Uthe lokhu bebekwenzela ukuthi bazihlinzekele ezinye izimo eziphuthumayo ezingavela ngesikhathi esizayoUqhube wathi:" Ukungafani kolwazi kudalwe yizinto eziningi phakathi kwazo ukusilela emuva  kokushicilelwa kwababulewe yigciwane kwamanye amazwe. Elinye iqiniso ukuthi  abanye abantu abazange bahlolwe ukuthi babulewe yigciwane noma cha, abanye  baze bashona bengazange belashelwe lona ngoba abazange bakwazi nokufinyelela ezikhungweni zezempilo ukuze bahlolwe ngenxa yemigomo yomvalelandlini ebikhona. Abanye babulewe ezinye izifo ngenxa yokuthi abakwazanga ukuthola ukwelashwa ngoba kubhekenwe nobhubhane."UKWENYUKA komfutho wegazi  i-Hypertension ebuye ibizwe ngeBlood Pressure  kuyimbangela  cishe  ngo-50% yazo zonke izifo zenhliziyo nesifo sohlangothi emhlabeni jikelele.Lokhu kushiwo inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO)  njengoba kusasa (17 Meyi 2023) kuwusuku lokuqwashisa nokufundisa ngalesi sifo emhlabeni wonke iWorld Hypertension Day. Ithe kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu ngamunye asazi isimo sakhe ngalesi sifo uma kutholakale ukuthi unaso azinakekele.Isikhulu esiphezulu kwaDischem Baby City Clinic uNksz Lizeth Kruger, sithe umfutho wegazi ophezulu ungumabulala buthule njengoba u46% weziguli ezinalesi sifo ungenalo ulwazi lokuthi unaso kuze kube lesi sifo sesingene sagxila." Kukhathaza kakhulu ukuthi abesifazane abakhulelwe basengozini enkulu njengoba umfutho wegazi ophezulu uyimbangela cishe ngo-15% yokushona komama eNingizimu Afrika. Lalela isiqubulo salo nyaka  bheka umfutho wegazi lakho, uwulawule, uphile isikhathi eside," kusho uNksz  UKruger .IWHO ithe babalelwa ku1.28 billion abantu  abadala abaneminyaka  engu-30-79 emhlabeni wonke abanomfutho wegazi ophezulu, iningi labo lihlala emazweni antulayo  nasathuthuka. Ithe u-46% wabantu abadala abanomfutho wegazi ophezulu abazi ukuthi banalesi simo. U-42% wabantu  abanesifo somfutho wegazi ophezulu bayaxilongwa futhi belashwe. Cishe umuntu oyedwa, kwabangu-5 abadala (21%) abanomfutho wegazi ophezulu, uyawulawula.Le nhlangano ithe iHypertension iyimbangela enkulu yokufa ngaphambi kwesikhathi emhlabeni wonke.Iqhuba ithe ifuna ukuthi kwehliswe izifo ezingathathelani  ngokwehlisa isibalo sabantu abahlaselwa umfutho wegazi ophezulu ngo-33% phakathi kuka-2010 no2030.Ithe  lesi sifo  sibizwa ngomabulala buthule ngoba kwabanye abantu asibi nazo izimpawu,  yingakho kufanele abantu bahlale behlola izinga lomfutho wegazi ukuze babone ukuthi asikabahlaseli yini."I-hypertension kwabesifazane abakhulelwe ingathinta nempilo yengane. Ingaholela ekuzalweni kwengane enesisindo esincane , ukubeletha ngaphambi kwesikhathi  kwezinye izikhathi iholela ekushoneni kukamama . Kubalulekile ukuthi owesifazane ozithwele azinakekele uma enalesi sifo,"  kusho uNksz Kruger.Uqhube wathi ezinye izinkinga ezenzeka kwabesifazane abakhulelwe zingaholela ekutheni unyuke kakhulu umfutho wegazi.
