Ezinye zalezi zinkinga zihlanganisa ukukhuluphala ngokweqile, isifo sikashukela abazalwa emindenini enomlando weHypertension ."Abesifazane abakhulelwe abanalezi zinkinga eziyingozi kufanele bathathe izinyathelo zokuphepha ezengeziwe futhi bafune iseluleko sezokwelashwa ukuze balawule umfutho wegazi labo ngesikhathi sokukhulelwa," kusho uNksz Kruger.UMnuz Murray Hewlett isikhulu esiphezulu kwi- Affinity Health , uthe  ukudla okunempilo, ukuzivocavoca noma ukunyakazisa umzimba njalo,  ukunciphisa uphuzo oludakayo, nokuyeka ukubhema konke kungasiza ekwehliseni umfutho wegazi futhi kunciphise ingozi yesifo senhliziyo kukhululeke nemithambo yegazi.BABALELWA ku-970 million abantu abanezifo ezithinta ukuphazamiseka kwengqondo emhlabeni. Lokhu kuvezwe wumbiko wezempilo othinta ukuphazamiseka kwengqondo owenziwe yiWorld Health Organisation, osanda kwethulwa ngokusemthethweni iMental Health Report ka-2022.Lo mbiko uveza ukuthi ngo-2019 ezigulini ezinokuphazamiseka kwengqondo ezingu-970 million, u-14% ngabantu abasha.Ngokwalo mbiko kubantu abangu-100 abashonayo oyedwa usuke ezibulele ngenxa yokuthi ubenengcindezi ethile. Uphinde uveze ukuthi u-58% wabantu abazibulalayo bakwenza lokhu ngaphambi kokuthi babeneminyaka engu-50. Ukuzibulala kuyimbangela yesine kwezihamba phambili eziholela ekufeni kwentsha eminyaka ephakathikuka-15 kuya ku-29 ubudala emhlabeni.U-82% wabantu abaphila nokuphazamiseka kwengqondo kubikwa ukuthi bahlala emazweni antulayo nasathuthuka kuwo okubalwa neNingizimu Afrika. INingizimu Afrika ngokwalo mbiko inezinga eliphansi lokunakekelwa kwesifo sengqondo lokhu kungenxa yokuthi leli lizwe likhungethwe yizimo zokuphila ezibhebhezela ukuntengantenga komqondo, kuko okunye kugqugquzela inhlalo, izinga eliphezulu lodlame, ububha,ukwentuleka kwemisebenzi nokungalingani.Ngeledlule iNingizimu Afrika ibenengqungquthela yezifo ezithinta ukuphazamiseka kwengqondo lapho bekubhekwa kabanzi lesi sifo nebanga eselihanjwe yiNingizimu Afrika ekwelashweni kwalesi sifo kanjalo nezinselelo ezisekhona.USihlalo womkhandlu wengculazi kuleli, iSouth African National Aids Council (SANAC), uMnuz Paul Mashatile, uthe: "Zihlangenelezi zinkinga ziyimbangela yokuphazamiseka kwengqondo, ukucindezeleka, ukungakwazi ukugxilisa ingqondo, ukukhathazeka, ukuzibulala, ukuphelelwa ithemba kanye nemizwa yokuzizwa ungelutho.“Umlando waseNingizimu Afrika wobandlululo, okuhlanganisa nezibonelo zayo zabasebenzi abavela kwamanye amazwe ezacekela phansi isakhiwo somndeni kubantu base-Afrika, uyaqhubeka nokuba nomthelela omubi empilweni yengqondo yabesifazane nezingane," kusho uMashatile.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleliuDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe eminyakeni emine edlule umnyango wenzekangcono ekuhleleni izinhlelo zokwelapha lesi sifo."Emkhakheni wezokuphathwa kwalolu hlelo siyelulekwa futhi sesekwa ikomitii elelulekao ngqongqoshe ngezempilo ezithinta ukuphazamiseka. Ezifundazweni amabhodi azimele eluleka ngezifo zengqondo nokuvikelwa kwamalungelo abantu abanalesi sifo akhona," kusho uPhaahla.Uqhube wathi umnyango wenzakahle ekudwebeni ingqubomgomo okumele ilandelwe kodwa kusadingeka ukuthi uqinise umkhankaso wokuqwashisa ngalesi sifo, ukuvimbela ukugula ngengqondo, ukunciphisa ukucwaswa kwabanalesi sifo."Ukucwaswa kwabanalesi sifo kusaqhubeka futhi kubhebhethekiswa wukuntuleka kolwazi ngaso," kusho uPhaahla.KULELI sonto eliphelile, ngibone ubuhlungu ongazi ungabuthini ngenxa yesimo ebesingaphezu kokwenza. Udabuka ufikephi uma ubona umuntu osemncane, osanda kuqeda izifundo zemfundo ephakeme, esedlavazwe wukwelashwa umdlavuza ngokushiswa nangamakhemikhali? Engani phela konke kufakwe emzimbeni ngendlela yokuthi indle igcina isizijuzela kudalwe ukunqamuka kwefindo lombhobho yawo, bese kukhumuzeka untwentwesi oluhlukanisa umgudu wendle nowentombazane.Ngaleso sikhathi udadewethu ulala uma bufikile ubuthongo ngesayidi elilodwa ngenxa yezinhlungu azichaza njengezihambayo zimmemezise abe wuqanduqandu. Ngokuhlala, usizwa ngugogo wakamakhelwane ofika ezobalalisa ngoba ebona usizi lodwa. Ubaba wengane kade amshiya. Uma ulandela okwenzekile, uyathola ukuthi udadewethu wayengenjena ngaphambi kokuqala kohlelo lokushiswa nekhimo. Bebethi bamelapha umdlavuza kodwa emuva kokuwelashwa izinto zivele zadlulele phambili, wagcina esenkinga enjena.Akasakwazi ukuzihambela. Njengoba enqunyelwe usuku lokubuya ukuze bamhlelele iphoyinti lokuyohlizwa ukuze afakelwe isigujana sokuthululela indle, kumele aqashelwe imoto.Awukwazi ukungazibuzi ukuthi uma kuwukumhlelela ukuya kwesinye isibhedlela kuphela, yini eyenza udokotela angamhleleli iphoyinti nesibhedlela leso bese eshayelwa ucingo esekhaya? Njalo sizolokhu sihlangana nezimo ezifana nalezi ngenxa yokwanda kokusetshenziswa kokushiswa nekhimo uma kwelashwa umdlavuza.Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje, ikhona indlela elula engadingi mishini etheni, ukwelashwa kuphela okulandela ukudla okudliwa imidlavuza. Yonke imidlavuza idla ushukela iGlucose neprotheyini iGlutamine. Esikwenzayo ukuncisha umdlavuza izibiliboco zayo imidlavuza. Konke lokhu kulimala komzimba ukuphalaza, ukuqothuka kwezinwele, ukungakuthandi ukudla, ngeke ukuthole. Kubalulekile ukuthi ogulayo aze kudokotela engakamosheki ingaphakathi ngoba liyadingeka ukuze elapheke.Asingamvumeli onomdlavuza aququdeke umzimba wonke ngenxa yokusha namakhemikhali, kuba nzima kwesinye isikhathi ukulungisa osekushisiwe ngapha nangapha ukwenze kusebenze.Angikwazi ukungakhulumi ngomdlavuza osebeleni nalowo osobendeni, esibindini, usinyaka nasomhlehlweni olugubuzele ingaphakathi. Kunabafowethu abangene kuleli sonto esisuka kulo. Ngokushesha, sesehlile isigaxa sobende, nejondisi ebisibakhungathile, kwehla nobuhlungu obebungabekezeleleki ezinhlangothini nokukhathala komzimba. Umzimba usubuyele esimeni obukuso ngaphambili. Esikwenzayo ukuncisha umdlavuza ukudla kwawo, sikorobhe isibindi amafutha ayizinqwabanqwaba okuyiwona adala abhebhezele umdlavuza.Obekuhlukile ngodadewethu onomdlavuza wamabele ukuthi ubusuhambe wafika emaphashini, entanyeni nakhona sekonakele ngenxa yendlela osabalala ngayo. Lokhu bekusabalala kuhambisana nezinhlungu ezingabekezeleleki. Zonke izinhlungu azisekho emuva kwesikhashana simqalile. Ngizama ukukhombisa lapha ukuthi ukwelashwa komdlavuza kuyenzeka. Esikucelayo kumele azi ogulayo ukuthi aselaphi umkhuhlane ozovele uthi wohlo, kumele kuliwe nedimoni elizokufuna ukudla kwalo ngezindlela zonke. Okunye okubalulekile ukuthi izinsuku ezintathu zokuqala sisuke sisashintsha indlela umzimba wakho osebenza ngawo. Umzimba kumele unyuse okuthile egazini kube phezulu. Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi ogulayo uzongena ebhandeni lokungadli ikakhulu zonke izidlo ezinoshukela ukuze sikwazi ukufinyelela ezingeni elithile egazini. Ukuqhubeka uya phambili, kumele azi ogulayo ukuthi kumele azincishe ukudla, phambili ushukela nokusashukela,Ukudla okugazingiwe (processed), olamthuthu nenyama yasezitolo ephuma ezilwaneni ezibiyelwe, ezingazidleli ngokuthanda. Kubalulekile kogulayo azi ukuthi uma ekhetha ukwelashwa ngendlela lena esiyihambisa phambili, ingxenye yokwelashwa izoncika ezintweni azidlayo. Ngeshwa akekho ozohlala eyilokhu emgadile, uyena ozozigada uma efuna ukuphila.Akukho okungikhathaza njengokubona abantu bezibona bengenayo enye impendulo ngaphandle kwale ndlela yokushiswa nekhimo, okanye imijovo abayithathayo belapha umdlavuza. Ukuba bengiyibona bengiyobeka phambili ukwelashwa ngendlela yokuncisha umdlavuza izibiliboco zawo. Enye inselelo esinayo okumele siyivume, siyisizwe ukuthi uma into siyitshelwa ngumuntu webala siyakholelwa kuyo ngisho isisisa emgodini, ngoba udokotela owasho owebala okanye owalesiya sizwe, noma sengikuchazela mina omnyama ofana nawe, hhayi angifiki khona. Lokhu siyakubona empilweni jikelele, ibala lisathatha indima enkulu ezinqumeni ezibalulekile ngathi. Le nto kumele ishintshe ngoba iyasidukisa kakhulu, hhayi kancane. Umdlavuza uyelapheka, sidinga amasonto okungenani amathathu ukuwubamba siwuklinye siwubuyisele emuva, sidinga ingaphakathi elisebenzayo kungaze kuthi phihli konke. Yingakho kubalulekile ukukhawuleza uze kithi, sidinga wena njengesiguli ukuzithiba ezidlweni lezi ezithandwa ngabantu abaningi futhi uzimisele ukuhlukana noshukela nayo yonke into edliwayo enoshukela, ukuvikela impilo yakho, ikusasa lezingane nomndeni wakho.Mpilonde!UMSEBENZI wokuba ngudokotela wezilwane uza nengcindezi eningi ehambisana nokusebenza kanzima okungafani nhlobo nomnikazi othanda isilwane ozizwa enelisekile ngokunakekela leso silwane.Lokhu kushiwo nguDkt Tarry Dent, owudokotela wezilwane enhlanganweni ebhekelele impilo yezilwane, iZoetis South Africa. UDkt Dent ubesho lokhu njengoba ngoMgqibelo, kuzobe kuwusuku lokunakekelwa kwezilwane emhlabeni, iWorld Veterinary Day.Uqhube wathi odokotela bezilwane banethuba eliyingqayizivele lokwenza umehluko obonakalayo empilweni yezilwane nabangane bazo abangabantu ngokwelapha izifo, ukuvimbela izifo, nokufundisa abanikazi ngokunakekelwa kwezilwane ngendlela efanele.“Kuwumsebenzi onomvuzo, ohlonishwayo futhi sibheke ngabomvu ukuwugubha unyaka nonyaka nabalingani bethu. Ngiyazi ukuthi ukuba ngudokotela ngumsebenzi oyiphupho ezinganeni eziningi zakuleli kanjalo nakwabadala. “Abawuthandayo lo msebenzi kumele bazi ukuthi unengcindezi engaholela ekutheni ugcine unesifo sengqondo uma ungalutholanga usizo, okuyinto esibhekene nayo kakhulu. Uma ungumuntu othanda izilwane, udokotela wakho wezilwane uneqhaza elibalulekile empilweni yakho neyezingane zakho ezinoboya. Masizinikeze konke ukwesekwa esingakwenza,” kusho uDkt Dent.Uthe izinto ezidala ingcindezi, ngukusebenza amahora amade nomsebenzi onzima, ukuhlangana nezilwane ezigulakakhulu okumele zixilongwe kutholakale ukuthi zinaziphi izifo. Lokhu kuhambisana nabanikazi bezilwane abafika bekhathazekile, benethemba lokuthi izilwane zabo zizokwelapheka.“Kuba nzima kakhulu uma udokotela kudingeka ukuthi enze isincomo sokuthi isilwane sithenwe. Kwesinye isikhathi ukuthenwa kwesilwane kungaholela ekutheni sife. Lo mphumela wenza udokotela wezilwane abe nokuzisola ngesinqumo asithathile. Uyakhathazeka okugcina kumfakele ingcindezi.“Lokhu kukhathazeka kuvame ukuphazamisa ukusebenza kwengqondo kadokotela. Kusemqoka ukuthi bahlale bephilile ngokwengqondo ukuzebabhekane nezidingo zemihla. Ngaphezu kwalokho, sikhuthaza abanikazi bezilwane ukuthi basekele odokotela bezilwane zabo,”usho kanje.Uqhube wathi enye indlela abanikazi bezilwane abangeseka ngayo odokotela ngukuthi babe nokuxhumana okuyikho.“Abanikazi bezilwane bangakwazi ukukhuluma ngezinto ezibakhathazayo, abakulindele, nokuthi banamalini abayihlelele ukuthi isetshenziselwe ukwelapha izilwane zabo.“Uma benza njalo, kuba lula ukuthi udokotela athi eqala ukwelapha isilwane asebenzise izinsiza umnikazi wesilwane azokwazi ukuzikhokhela, kunciphe namathuba okuthi bagcine sebexabana ngoba bebengavulelananga izifuba ngesikhathi kuqala umsebenzi wokwelashwa kwesilwane," kusho yena.UDkt Dent weluleka ngokubaluleka kokuthi abanikazi bezilwane ezifuywayo bahloniphe isikhathi nobuchwepheshe bodokotela babo bezilwane.“Ukufika ngesikhathi ukuze uthole isikhathi esimisiwe, ukufika nomlando wezokwelashwa wesilwane, nokunamathela ezinhlelweni zokwelashwa onikezwe zona, kubonisa inhlonipho kudokotela wezilwane," kusho uDkt Dent.UKWANDA kwesifo somdlavuza sekuholele ekutheni kube nezindlela eziningi zokuwelapha ezikhona.Indlela ejwayelekile ngeyokuthi kubulawe wonke ama-cell emzimbeni ngethemba lokuthi kuzofa lawa anomdlavuza lawa amanye abuye avuke, i-chemotherapy nokuthi umuntu afakwe emshinini kushiswe umdlavuza, i-radiation.Enye indlela engadumile kakhulu kubantu abamnyama, yindlela engasebenzisi amakhemikhali ebizwa nge-metabolic therapy.UDkt Bongani Nxumalo wesibhedlela, eYangakithi Medicals, esiseMtubatutuba,  ungomunye wodokotela abayisebenzisayo le ndlela echazwa ngokuthi ukuncisha umdlavuza ukudla okudlayo egazini bese uyafa.Uthe le ndlela ingcono kakhulu ngoba ayinazo izifo ezidalayo esigulini, kubhekwana ngqo negciwane.Uthe umdlavuza udla ushukela obizwa nge-glucose uma ususemzibeni ne-glutamine."Odokotela abelapha ngale ndlela baqala ngokuthi bancishe umzimba i-glucose ukuze igciwane lilambe. Igciwane lomdlavuza liwuthanda kakhulu ushukela, uma isiguli singasakudli ukudla okuthi uma sekugayekile emzimbeni kuphendule ushukela, liyashintsha lidle i-glutamine. Uma umzimba ungasenayo iglucose sivala ukusebenza kweglutamine. Igciwane lomdlavuza noma ngabe yiliphi liyezwana namafutha aba sonqenqemeni lwesibindi kusuke kumele sihlakaze lawo mafutha ukuze lingabe lisaqhubeka liziphindaphinda,"  kusho yena.Uthe ushukela uyinkinga enkulu emzimbeni womuntu izifo eziningi zidaleka ngenxa yokuthi abantu badla ukudla okunoshukela noma ukudla okuphenduka kube ushukela uma sekugayekile esiswini. "Ukudla okuyi-starch uma sekugayekile kuphenduka ushukela egazini, abantu bakithi badla i-starch esiningi, badla uphuthu, izambane, amahewu,  konke lokhu kuphenduka ushukela kanti usazobuye adle ushukela, uswidi noshokoledi nabo abawushukela. “Uma ungacabanga ukuthi zingakanani izinto eziwushukela ozidlayo ngosuku ungabona ukuthi izifo eziningi zingagwemeka uma abantu bengehlisa ukudla okunoshukela nokuphenduka kube wushukela emzimbeni baqinise kakhulu ezitshalweni eziluhlaza," kusho yena.UNkk Dudu Shandu waKwaHlabisa, owumhlengikazi osethathe umhlalaphansi, ongesinye seziguli ezelashwa nguDkt Nxumalo, nge-metabolic therapy, uthe ubeneqhuzu elisebeleni wacela ukuhlolwa wathola ukuthi unodlavuza webele osesigabeni sesibili."Ngiqale uhlelo lokwelashwa ngisebenzisa i-chemotheraphy ngoba nami njengoba kade ngiwumhlengikazi iyona engiyaziyo. Bengingekho ntekenteke ngaphambi kokuqala ukuhlelo lokwelashwa. Ngiye esibhedlela ngoba ngesaba ukuthi uma ungingasheshi ukuwulapha umdlavuza uzosabalala kodwa nginele ngaqala ukwelashwa ngaba nezinkinga eziningi. “Ukudla kwangangeni, ngehla isisindo, ngaphalaza  ngazizwa ngiphelelwa amandla, ngagcina ngingasakwazi nokuhamba ekubeni kade ngiluqale lolu hlelo ngiziphilela," kusho uNkk Shandu.Uthe wezwa ngohlelo lokwelashwa nge-metabolic therapy, waqala ukwenza lona, lwamsiza kakhulu waqala ukubona umehluko ezinsukwini ezintathu."Ngiziphonse kulolu hlelo ngoba ngibona ukuthi ngisenkingeni kanti luzongisiza. Njengamanje ngidla ukudla okufana namadumbe nezinye izitshalo, ushukela ngiyawugwema," kusho uNkk Shandu.UMnuz Lucky Gumbi waseJozini onomdlavuza wobende nesibindi, owelashwa ngalolu hlelo lokwelashwa, uthe akazange abe nenhlanhla yokulaliswa esibhedlela yize ebenesigaxa ebesisesiswini."Okwami bekunzima kakhulu ngoba bengingakafiki esigabeni sokuthi kuhlonzwe ukuthi isigaxa esisesiswini siwumdlavuza, bekusahlolwa.  Kwaqale kwathiwa kusolwa ukuthi iphaphu lami linamagciwane (lung infection). Ngakholwa ngoba ngake ngahlaselwa yiTB phambilini.“Kwazanywa ukwelashwa sona kodwa kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya. Bekuthi uma usuku enginikwe lona esibhedlela ngilubona lukude ngiye kodokotela abazimele. Ukhona udokotela owathi uma sengisesibhedlela ngicele bangihlolele umdlavuza noma i-TB yamathumbu. Ngaba neshwa lokuqondana nabasebenzi abangazange bakushaye mkhuba lokho,"  kuchaza uGumbi.Uthe ubuhlungu ayebuzwa babungabekezeleki wabe esekhetha ukuthi aqale uhlelo lwe-metabolic therapy."Ngibone umehluko omkhulu. Isigaxa sampontshwa udoti ngoba bese sisikhulu. Ngilubona lusebenza ngoba isigaxa simane sancibilika nami angikholwanga," kusho yena. IMAKETHE yabadayisa izincwadi zodokotela eziwumgunyathi yenziwa ngabantu abakhohlakele abazithengayo.Lokhu kushiwo wusihlalo wenhlangano yodokotela, iSouth African Medical Association (Sama), uDkt Mvuyisi Mzukwa.UMzukwa usho kanjena nje kunezigameko eziningi ezibikwe wumkhandlu wabasebenzi bezempilo, iHealth Practioners Council South Africa,   zokuboshwa kwabantu abadayisa izincwadi zodokotela eziwumgunyathi.Ngeledlule kuboshwe umuntu enkabeni yedolobha eThekwini ekhiqiza izincwadi zomgunyathi e-internet cafe, esebenzisa imininingwane kadokotela waKwaMashu. Incwadi ngayinye ubeyidayisa ngo-R150."Siphila ezweni labantu abathanda ukwenza inkohlakalo. Asikho isiguli esingaya kudokotela waso sifike sithi ngizothenga incwadi. Incwadi isiguli siyithola ngoba udokotela ethe uma esihlola, wabona ukuthi ngeke sikwazi ukusebenza. Lokhu kuvula ithuba kulaba abafuna ukuzenzela imali esheshayo nabafuna ukulova emsebenzini. Abathega izincwadi bayazi ukuthi abazithenge kubo kababona odokotela kodwa bayaqhubeka bakwenze ngoba nabo bafuna ukwenza ubugebengu. Abanye banikeza iziguli  izinsuku ezingazifanele izifo abazibhale kulezo zincwadi. Okubi kakhulu wukuthi lo mkhuba wokudayiswa kwezincwadi uthinta nomnotho ngoba umsebenzi okumele ngabe uyasebenza unikezwa inqwaba yezinsuku, ebe edingeka emsebenzini," kusho uMzukwa.Uthe abaqashi kumele baziqaphele izincwadi, uma engayiboni kahle unelungelo lokufona abuze ukuthi udokotela uke wasibona yini lesi siguli yize engeke akwazi ukubuza kabanzi ngesifo esisiphethe, noma aziyele mathupha kwadokotela ayobona ukuthi yindawo enjani."Uma kunodokotela osetshenziswa ngabasebenzi abaningi, kumele athumele abazoya kobheka ukuthi lo dokotela unjani ngoba kungenzeka ukuthi wudokotela mbumbulu. Kwayona incwadi kumele ayibhekisise ngoba abanye basebenzisa incwadi endala bese bacisha imininingwane emidala, bafake abakuthandayo. Kimina bathatha incwadi endala engangiyibhalele lesi siguli, bashintsha izinsuku. Babhala ukuthi isiguli kumele singasebenzi izinsuku ezingu-18 sibe siphethwe umkhuhlane. Umqashi wafona efuna ukuthola ukuthi ngimbonile yini umsebenzi wakhe ngosuku olubhaliwe, ngalandula  kwaba ukubanjwa kwakhe," kusho udokotela.Uthe lo mkhuba kawenziwa ngezincwadi zodokotela abazimele kuphela kodwa uyenziwa nangezitembu nezincwadi zasezikhungweni zikahulumeni.BALINGANISELWA ku-6.5 million abantu abadinga usizo lwezempilo oluqondene nokuphazamiseka kwengqondo ezweni.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe kulaba bantu kukhona abadinga usizo olujwayelekile lokunakekelwa nabadinga ukunyangwa okusezingeni eliphezulu, okubalawa nokulaliswa ezibhedlela. Uthe imibhede ehlelelwe ukuthi kulale kuyo iziguli ezinezifo zokuphazamiseka kwengqondo ingu-19 000 eNingizimu Afrika. Lapha kubalwa imibhede esezikhungweni zempilo zikahulumeni nezizimele.UPhaahla ubesho lokhu ngesikhathi ephendula umbuzo obuzwe nguNkk Michéle Clarke weDA ePhalamende mayelana nokuthi mingaki imibhede ehlelelwe ukulala iziguli ezinezifo zokuphazamiseka kwengqondo kuleli nokuthi iziguli zona zingaki, ongoti bezempilo abakhona abakwazi ukuzelapha bona bangaki?Ungqongqoshe uthe kulesi sibalo kulinganiselwa ekutheni abangu-1.2 million abasha abaneminyaka engu-15 kuya phezulu, abadinga ukunakekela okusezingeni eliphezulu kodwa imibhede ekhona ezikhungweni zempilo ingu-19 752."Ezikhungweni zempilo zikahulumeni ingu-14 060 imibhede ehlelelwe ukulalisa iziguli ezinezifo ezithinta ukuphazamiseka kwengqondo, ezikhungweni ezizimele ingu-5 692 imibhede ehlelelwe iziguli ezinalezi zifo," kusho yena.Lokhu kusho ukuthi ongoti abelapha lezi zifo bayashoda kanjalo nemibhede ekhona imbalwa kuneziguli ezinalesi sifo.Umbiko obhalwe phansi obufundwa wungqongqoshe uveze ukuthi izifundazwe eziyisishiyagalolunye sesizivalile izikhala ezingu-451 zodokotela abangabeluleki bezengqondo nomphemulo, izikhala ezingakagcwaliswa zingu-187.Uqhube wathi zintathu izifundazwe eziqashe odokotela abangongoti abaningi kulesi sibalo.I-Western Cape yiyona ehamba phambili ngokuqasha amapsychologist njengoba iqashe angu-99, ilandelwe yiNorth West eqashe angu-41 neKwaZulu-Natal enangu-35, ezinye izifundazwe zihlanganisiwe ziqashe angu-17.ILimpopo inamapsychologist ayisithupha kuphela, iFree State inamane, iMpumalanga inamathathu, i-Eastern Cape neNorthern Cape banamabili isifundazwe ngasinye.Uqhube wathi amapsychologist ashodayo angu-187 kumele agcwalise izikhala ezifundazweni eziyisishiyagalombili, iWestern Cape kudingeka igcwalise isikhala esisodwa kuphela.E-Eastern Cape, Limpopo naseMpumalanga kunezinga eliphezulu lokushoda kodokotela abangongoti zonke lezi zifunda izinga lokushoda liphakathi kuka-80% no-83.33%.E-Northern Cape izinga lokushoda kongoti lingu-66.67%, eFree State lingu-50%, KwaZulu-Natal lingu-28.57%, eNorth West lingu-12.77%, eWestern Cape lingu-1%.EWestern Cape ungoti oyedwa welapha iziguli ezingu-71 856.Uthe izibalo zaseGauteng azikho ngoba alukho ulwazi lwakhona olukhombisa ukuthi ungoti ngamunye ubhekene neziguli ezingaki.UNkk Clark uthe iDA isazothumela eminye imibuzo ePhalemende ukuze uMnyango wezeMpilo uzochazela ikomiti lezempilo ngamasu nezinhlelo onazo zokulungisa isimo."Kuyamangaza ukuthi usizo luncane ngesikhathi izwe libheneke nenkinga abantu abaningi benezinkinga zokuphazamiseka komqondo nengcindezi ngenxa yesimo somnotho, ukuphela kwemisebenzi nezinye izinkinga zansuku zonke.“Akukho lapho bezosizakala khona ngoba izikhungo zempilo azinabo ongoti kabenele,” kusho uNkk Clark. UMBUZOMAGUMEDE ngiyindoda  esikhulile eseminyakeni eko-50. Ngiphila nemizwa yobulili obubili (bisexual). Ngike ngashada nenye indoda phambilini kodwa yashona. Sengicabanga ukuthatha intombi nje engangami, engizoyitshela iqiniso ngiqala nje ukukhuluma nayo ngoba angisiye umuntu ophila nezimfihlo.Inkinga dadewethu wukuthi kunzima kimi ukushela izintombi ngoba ngijwayele kakhulu ukushela izinsizwa.Izintombi zike zingishele, ngivele ngibe namahloni. Ngibaleke ngazo zombili izinyawo. Ngisacela uke ungibonise ukuthi kumele ngenze njani uma ngishela intombi? Ngiyabonga.IMPENDULOMINA bengithi kungcono usale usuqhubeka nawo amadoda ngoba vele neminyaka isihambile. Angazi kungani ufuna ukuqala phansi uthathe umuntu wesifazane ozophinde umtshele ukuthi wena uthanda amadoda, nabafazi. Okokushela kulula kakhulu. Shela ngale ndlela oshela ngayo amadoda. Ngitshele nje, ngubani umuntu wesifazane obheke eminyakeni ewu-50, ozovuma, aphinde amukele ukuthi umnakwabo uyindoda? Angikwahluleli kodwa icabangisise kahle into ofuna ukuyiqala. Ngikufisela inhlanhla.DKT BONGANI NXUMALOKWAKHE kwafika isiguli sesifazane esasineminyaka eyevile ku-33, esasiqala ukuza kwesinye sezikhungo zethu, sikhala ngokukhathala okwakuvithiza umzimba, amalungu omzimba, izicubu nomqondo kucobeke. Ukuba kwakuya ngaye ungathi wayengaba yinto ehlala izilalele nje, kungavumi lutho. Ukusukuma wayephoqwa ukuthi umsebenzi wakhe wayewuthanda, futhi kumele enze imisebenzi yasekhaya njengomama wekhaya. Wayexabana nomyeni wakhe ngento engenamsebenzi, futhi wazithola engasakwazi ukuma aqoqe umqondo engxoxweni, amagama abekwazi ukuwaphimisela engasaphumi kalula, angiphathi uma esengxoxweni esampikiswano; wayezithola esevele asheshe anikezele into ayengayijwayele.Wayeshaywa wuvalo ayengalujwayele umzimba wakhe wawuqhaqhazela uma ebeka unyawo, nalapho ethi uyabamba into ngesandla, yiso leso uyaqhaqhazela, ajuluke kakhulu azwele ukushisa nomzimba ushise.Ibhalansi emzimbeni yayingesakho kahle esehamba ekhutshwa wubala nasemzimbeni nje wayezibona encipha. Engxoxweni esaba nayo sathola ukuthi ukugula kwakunesikhathi esevile onyakeni kumshuka, enenkinga yokuqwasha ebusuku ehlala kuze kube zintatha ekuseni kungalaleki. Ubelokhu ecabanga ukuthi unengcindezi yomqondo, ebuka nokukhandleka emsebenzini nasekhaya njengembangela yokushintsha kwesimo sempilo. Abangani ayenabo baya belokhu bencipha ngenxa yokuthi bese enenhliziyo encane. Ekuhambeni kwesikhathi uthi wazithola engasenandaba nocansi, engasafiki kuvuthondaba, inhliziyo yabe isincane, izinto eziningi ebezibalulekile engasenandaba nazo. Wayenengane eyodwa ayithola engakashadi nayo isindala, lapha emshadweni kudala bezama beguduza imimango yokuthola umntwana, lutho kungenzeki. Odokotela ayehamba kubo babelokhu bemi ngokuthi unokhwantalala futhi unesifo sokwethuka okuthiwa yiPanic Disorder, nemishanguzo yomqondo wayeseyiqalile kodwa engawuboni umehluko. Uma ebuyela kodokotela bakhe babelokhu beshintshana ngaye bemthatha igazi kodwa imiphumela yayilokhu ingaphumi nalutho okanye kuthiwa ilahlekile. Yimpilo le abese eyiphila saze  sahlangana naye.Lesi sifo esigxile kuso namhlanje asithathi ohlangothini oluthile kwezobulili, noma nje izinombolo zigebela kwabesimame ikakhulu futhi  nezincwadi ezinkulu ziyakuvuma lokhu. Kunomunye umfo ongumuntu wesilisa, oneminyaka eyevile ku-50 owayelokhu ekhala ngovalo, ukungalali ebusuku, naye wayencipha umzimba ukhathala. Yena kwakuzwakala sengathi ingalo yakhe iyaqanda sakuvithizeka phakathi engalweni. Uthi kwakungebuhlungu kodwa kwakulokhu kunokuvithizeka kwengalo okwakuzwakala ngaphakathi le kude kuhambisana nomuzwa osabu’tiya’. Uchaza uthi le nto yayifika ngaphambi kokulala, awulali uma ikuphethe uze ulale lapho iphela khona. Kwesinye isikhathi  kuyenzeka kube nento enyuka iyothi ngci esifubeni kungaphefumuleki, kokunye kuze kushe nezwi. Ekuphandeni sathola ukuthi bese enenhliziyo encane, esenomkhuba wokubeka unkosikazi nezingane isandla, kungasekho ukuthula ekhaya. Induku yavele yaziwela yangavuma ukuvuka, yawela phakathi, yagcina izinciphela nangokosayizi. Ukusuza kwathi ngila, into ebingenzeki. Konke lokhu kwengeza ingcindezi yomqondo, odokotela belokhu bemyalela ukuthi makabonane nosonhlalakahle nodokotela wengqondo.Lezi zigameko zombili zibangwa ukuvuvukala, nokuphunduleka ukusebenza kwendlala iThyroid. Le ndlala ilapha ngasegilweni emqaleni, ihlukaniswe kabili. Umsebenzi wayo ojwayelekile ukuba ngunondweba womzimba, lokhu kuchaza ukuthi okwenzeka emzimbeni kugqugquzelwa yile ndlala, uma ingasasebenzi  izinto ziyonakala. Imbangela yokuphunduleka ukusebenza kubangwa amasosha omzimba avele asuke ahlasele le ndlala, ayidlikidlikize igcine seyenza ukuthanda kwayo emzimbeni. Emuva kokuthi lezi ziguli  sihlangane nazo, kwangicacela ukuthi imbangela yalokhu kugula yile ndlala iThyroid. Okuhle ukuthi lezi ziguli zabuyela ezimeni zazo zaphila, usisi wagcina emtholile nomtwana.  Ubaba wayeka nesibhaxu ekhaya, induku yabuyela ekusebenzeni kwayo; kwaba mnandi emndenini.Engicela sikubone lapha ukuthi zonke izifo zinomsuka wazo, umsebenzi wami njengomthunywa wezempilo ukuthi uma isiguli siphambi kwami angenze konke okusemandleni ukuthi ngiyithole imbangela yokugula kwaso. Kimi njengomuntu okuzofunwa usizo kuyena akungabi lula ukuthi leli gazi nalokhuya akuniki mpendulo, imbangela yokugula kwakho asiyazi, ngakhoke hamba uye kwabezenhlalakahle mhlawumbe kunento abazokusiza ngayo okanye hamba uye kudokotela oweluleka ngokomqondo kungenzeka kunesimo ongasinakile esenza ugule ngale ndlela. Yebo kungaba yiqiniso lokho kodwa sonke siphila nengcindezi ethile emqondweni, angithi? Omunye uzothi, phela dokotela abantu abamukeli, izinto azizweli ngokufana emzimbeni womuntu. Nalokho ngiyakuvuma, kodwa uma ubuka lezi ziguli ezingenhla ukuba asithathanga isinyathelo sokucinga, sisuse izidindi ukuze sithole umthombo wokugula asazi ukuthi  isimo sabo ngabe sinjani namhlanje, mhlawumbe namanje nengane ngabe akaze ayithole usisi, isibhaxu ngabe siyaqhubeka ekhaya, induku yenza ukuthanda kwayo kowesilisa.Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi wena onenkinga yokuthola abantwana, wena oke wakhulelwa kodwa kwavele kwama nse, wangasazi isizathu, bheka ukuthi iziphi ezinye izimpawu ezisemzimbeni ngaphambi kokuthi ulahle ithemba, okanye uthi kwangena isilwane mhlawumbe imimoya yavala isibeletho. Hamba uye kudokotela  noma kumuphi umsizi wakho wezempilo ozokuhlolisisa afune imbangela. Nathi thina bafowethu nodadewethu ezikhungweni zokusebenza ngezempilo, ake sifunisise imbangela yokugula kwabantu bethu. Kubuhlungu kumuntu ogulayo okuthi isifo simhlukumeza, thina silokhu sithi ukugula akubonakali, yena engamile ethatha igazi, kushintshane odokotela ngento efanayo kulokhu kuthathwa igazi. Ekugcineni anqobeke umuntu. Bese kuba khona lokhu kokuvele sithi imbangela yi-acid noma isifo samathambo njalo nje. Akekho okuphikisayo uma ngempela kunjalo kodwa ngithi asingakhohlwa ukuzibeka esayidini lesiguli okanye labasondelene nogulayo izikhathi eziningi.Mpilonde!Baningi abantu bakithi abavumela izibiliboco zokudla zingcweke, zihlukumeze usinyaka, bazithole sebephalaza, kugcwalelane ucabango kuhambisana nezinhlungu, bagcine sebephelelwa ngamandla ngenxa yento eyodwa emele ngabe iyabasiza; okungukudla.Usinyaka yingxenye yomzimba ebalulekile ngenxa yemisebenzi eyahlukene nebalulekile eyenzeka ngezikhathi nasezimeni ezingafani. Usinyaka ndini utholakala esiyingini somzimba eduze kwesibindi uze uyokapakela ngasobendeni kwesobunxele. Imisebenzi ebalulekile kasinyaka:Ngithe angichaze kanje ngenxa yokwanda kwabantu abahlushwa ukuphalaza okungazwani nokudla kuvele kubuye ngokushesha. Uma uthi uyakufaka, ukudla kunuke kukude, sibe buhlungu isisu, kube nento ethi ngci ocabangweni, kungaphefumuleki. Uma ukhishwa yisisu kuphuma indle enuka kakhulu, ayaphela amandla, wehle nasemzimbeni ngokushesha. Uma uzwa kanje emzimbeni, bhasobha nakanjani kusuke sekugadlile ukudla, kwaphihliphihliza usinyaka, uyokhala uzithulise!Abantu bakithi bayaphuza ukufika, kokunye kusuke kuwukujikeleza ngapha nangapha, kulokhu kuthiwa banezilonda emathunjini (ama-ulcers) noma kuthiwe bane-esidi eningi njalo njalo. Uyaye uthole isiguli sesilashwa izilonda undendende wento kodwa kungabibikho umehluko. Ngiyafisa ukugcizelela ukubaluleka kokubelesela udokotela wakho ukuthi makafune imbangela (ngisho umsusa) wokugula kwakho, akunikeze incazelo ezokwenelisa. Yekani ukwesaba, sibuzeni ukuthi isifo sibangelwa yini?Usinyaka uzungezwe yinyongo nesibindi kwesokudla, ubende esinxeleni, iningi lamathumbu azungeze agcwala ngezansana nawo. Engosini edlule, sagcizelela ingozi elethwa ukudla lokhu esathi kuphehliwe (processed) njengopholoni, ama-Rashiyeni azo zonke izinhlobo. Sekukhona nalawa okuthiwa ngo-Yababa, ama-burger, inyama ebomvu eyosiwe, isitambu esizipheka imizuzu embalwa manje. Yini singazibuzi ukuthi yini esifakiwe eyenza sisheshe sivuthwe kangaka? Iziguli eziningi ezifika nezimpawu engizibale ngenhla uthola ekuhloleni ukuthi usinyaka yiwona olimele kakhulu. Abagulayo bafika beshisa emzimbeni, bephalaza, bekhala ngezinhlungu ocabangweni kuhlanganisa namahlombe, kwabanye luze luvuvukale, amandla emzimbeni engekho, ogulayo evevezela, omunye sekunzima ukuzihambela. Uma ubheka emuva ufuna imbangela uyathola ukuthi ukudla esikudlayo yikho okubelesela usinyaka uhuzuleke uze ugcine usuvuvukele usukhiqiza amakhemikhali aququda ingaphakathi lamathumbu, ugcine sewukhishwa yisisu kuphume indle engamanzi esho phezulu ngephunga elinuka kabi.Ngifisa ukucacisa ukuthi ezinye izimbangela zokulimala kukasinyaka yilezi;Ngaphezu kwalokho, eminyakeni esesiphila kuyo, kunokudla okuphehliwe okuza kuyizinhlobonhlobo, namakhemikhali amaningi akuphehlayo. Lokhu kusenza sisondele ekutheni ukudla yikhona okushaya usinyaka udume lwengozi olukhipha umongozini oza nenqwaba yezinkinga. Ngingamvumela futhi othi ukudla kwesinye isikhathi kuhlanganyela usinyaka nezinye izimbangela, kodwa yikona okungubhongoza ozihola phambili.Ngiyaphinda ngiyagcizelela ukuthi ukudla kuyingozi okuningi kwakho, kudala izifo ezibulala imindeni nesizwe. Namhlanje sikhulume ngengozi eyenziwa ukudla engxenyeni eyodwa ewusinyaka, ungazicabangela nawe ukuthi ingakanani ingozi eyenziwa wukudla emzimbeni uwonke? Asikwazi ukusina endaweni eyodwa sibe ingozi siyibona. ISilo samaBandla onke esisanda kukhothama, komunye umhlangano sathi, “Kuwubuwula obuphindiwe ukungena esizibeni sigcwele izingwenya, wena uzitshele ukuthi ngeke zikwenze lutho …”Mpilonde!ESIKHATHINI sanamhlanje akusekho lula ukukhetha iselula ngenxa yezinga lobuchwepheshe obuqukethwe amaselula amaningi abizwa ngama-smart phone, kusukela kwashibhile kuya kwabizayo. Eminyakeni edlule kuqaphelekile ukuthi sandile isibalo sabantu abasebenzisa ama-smart phone eNingizimu Afrika kanti lokhu sekuholele ekutheni kunyuke isibalo sezinkampani ezikhiqiza amaselula ezisezingeni eliphezulu kuleli. NgoMashi ka-2020, ngesikhathi kuqala ukuvalwa kwezwe njengendlela yokunqanda ukusabalala kwe-Covid-19 kuleli, inkampani yaseChina, iTecno, yamemezela ukuthi amaselula ayo asezodayiswa eNingizimu Afrika.Ngokocwaningo, ukuthengwa kwama-smart phone eNingizimu Afrika, Nigeria nase-Egypt, kunyuswe yizinga lamaselula abiza amanani aphansi kodwa aqukethe cishe yonke into oyifunayo kwiselula.Ngenyanga edlule ngithole ithuba eliyingqayisivele lokuvivinya enye yamaselula akhiqizwe yiTecno Mobile, iSPARK 5, ephume ngoSepthemba nonyaka.Into yokuqala engichazile ngale selula yibhokisi layo. Ngiyazi abantu abaningi abakunaki lokhu, kodwa indlela iselula ethulwa ngayo ebhokisini layo ibalulekile. Ifika ngebhokisi elikhulu, elingeke likufakele amahloni uma kungathiwa le selula uyithenga njengesipho sohlekisana naye, ingane yakho, noma uzithengela wena nje. Ngifake isithombe ngezansi ukuze uzibonele ukuthi bekumele ngiphawule ngebhokisi layo (packaging).Ngaphakathi kuleli bhokisi akuphumi iselula kuphela, ihambisana nama-HiPods H2 earphones, okungama-earphones asebenza nge-bluetooth.  Anomsindo ogcwele ama-HiPods H2 kanti okuhle ngawo ukuthi uyakwazi ukuwasebenzisa uma kungena ucingo futhi uma uwumuntu othanda ukuzivocavoca uyakwazi ukukwenza lokho engaphumi ngoba ayabambelela ezindlebeni. Ama-earphones aphuma nebhokisi lawo elisebenza njenge power-bank yoku-charger.Into evame ukubhekwa abantu abaningi uma bethenga iselula namhlanje yizinga lekhamera. ISPARK 5 igxile kakhulu ekuqhikizeni izithombe namavideo amahle njengoba iqukethe amakhamera amahlanu. Inamakhamera amane ngemuva, neyodwa yama- ‘selfie’ engaphambili.Kwamane angemuva iqukethe ehamba phambili ewu-13MP, ewu-2MP yokushutha okuseduzane, iMacro lens ewu-2MP kanye ne-AI (Artificial Intelligence) Camera. I-AI Camera ifakelwe ukuqinisekisa ukuthi kuphuma izithombe eziveza imibala yosuke ukushutha njengoba injalo. Ukuvivinya lokhu ngithathe izithombe ezimbalwa ukubheka izinga lale khamera.Ngaphandle kwekhamera, iSPARK 5 iqukethe i-battery ehlala isikhathi eside ingacishi. Iphethe amandla awu-5000mAh, okusho ukuthi ingahlala u-16 hours ukhuluma ocingweni ingacishi, noma uchithe u-14 hours ubuka ama-video ingacishi.Lokhu kuhambisana nosayizi wayo omuhle wokugcina amafayela eselula owu-32GB.ISPARK 5 sisebenza ngobuchwepheshe be-Android, okuwubuchwepheshe okujwayelekile kubantu abasebenzisa ama-smart phone okubalwa kuwo iSamsung neHauwei. Le selula iqukethe eyayo injini ngaphezu kwalokho iHelio A22 chipset yeMediaTek.Sekuhlangane uthola iselula esheshayo uma uyisebenzisa, kumnandi nokuthinta i-screen sayo ngoba silandela kalula okwenzayo futhi sinama-graphics agqame kahle. Bakwenzela umsebenzi ube lula ngama-App abakufakela wona, ikakhulukazi awakwa-google, kodwa uyakwazi ukuwasusa uma ungawathandi uzifakele awakho.Le selula uyakwazi ukuyivula (unlock) ngomunwe nangobuso (facial recognition).ISPARK 5 ungayithola ngoR2999 kulezi zitolo: Chatz Connect, Vodacom 4U, Cellucity, GAME, Hi store, Foschini, Totalsports naseTechX.UKUZIGCINGCA ngezicoficofi ngokweqile ngesikhathi samaholidi kungaba nomthelela ongemuhle kwabanesifo sikashukela.Ongoti bezempilo bathi kubalulekile ukuthi abantu baqaphele uma bedla oncamce, nokunye ukudla okunoshukela uma benesifo sikashukela ngisho kuyisikhathi samaholidi. Bathi ukugudluka kancane endleleni ojwayele ukuphila ngayo kungakudalela inkinga.Baqhuba bathi ngesikhathi samaholide abantu abajwayele ukuphuza iziphuzo ezinoshukela uma beqeda ukudla, bengenze ngoncamce ngoba bezijabulisa.Ungoti wezokudla uNkk Michelle Govender, wesikhungo esisiza abantu akuthi balandele uhlelo lokudla ngendlela enempilo i-Eetwell, uthe abanye  abantu basuke bengaqondile ukuchezuka endleleni abajwayele ukuyiphila. Wathi kwenzeka ngesikhathi bethi bajabulisa izivakashi ngoba akubukeki ukuthi unikeze izivakashi ukudla wena ungakudli kanti sebeyamosha."Kubalulekile ukuthi siqaphele ngalesi sikhathi ngoba ukudla okunoshukela uma sekugayekile kuphenduka ushukela, okusuke kufanele omunye wawo ukhishwe wumzimba kodwa uma i-insulin ingasasebenzi kahle kuba yinkinga,“ kuchaza uNkk Govender.Ubesho lokhu namhlanje njengoba kuwusuku olusetshenziselwa ukuqwashisa nokufundisa ngobungozi besifo sikashukela emhlabeni, iWorld Diabetes Day.UNkk Govender uqhube wathi akhona amasu angasiza iziguli ezinalesi sifo njengokuthi ziqede ukudla zihambahambe noma kungaba yisendlini  imizuzu eyishumi. Uthe lokhu kuyasiza ekutheni kugayeke ukudla.Ukudla imifino nezaqatha ngaphambi kokuthi udle ukudla ohlele ukukudla, uthe kungaholela ekwehliseni ukukhiqizeka kwe-insulin emzimbeni wakho. Insulin yi-hormone ebhekele ukulawula ushukela egazini.“Ukuxuba amaprotheni nokudla okunothe nge-carbohydrate kunganciphisa ukumuncwa kwama-carb futhi kuvimbele ukukhuphuka kwezinga likashukela egazini,” kuchaza ungoti wezokudla.Isifo sikashukela singesesibili esibulala abantu abaningi eNingizimu Afrika. Bangu-12% abantu abadala abanalesi sifo kuleli.Ucwaningo lweSA Demographic Health Survey yango-2016, luveza ukuthi  ukuthi u-67%  wabesilisa nabesifazane baqale babe nezinkomba zokuthi bazongenwa yisifo sikashukela kepha kungaziwa ngenxa yokuthi abazihloleli lesi sifo baya ezikhungweni zezempilo ngoba sebegula.Ngokocwaningo isifo sikashukela esingalashwanga noma esingalawulwa ngendlela efanele, singaholela ekutheni umuntu anqunywe izitho zomzimba, ukwehluleka kokusebenza kwezinso ngendlela efanele nokungaboni emehlweni.Luqhuba luthi iningi labantu abangayilandeli indlela yohlelo lokulawula ushukela egazini labo baba nomfutho wegazi ophakeme futhi bagcine sebeshawa yisifo sohlangothi ngenxa yokopha ebuchosheni.“Ukukhuluphala kuhlobene nesifo sikashukela kanti siyakhula isibalo sabantu abakhuluphele ngokweqile kuleli, bangu-11% abesilisa abakhuluphele ngokweqile,  bangu 41% abesifazane abasesimeni esifanayo. Kulindeleke ukuthi ngo-2030 senyukele ku-50% isibalo sabesifazane abakhuluphele ngokweqile,” ngokombiko wocwaningo.Luqhuba luthi imbangela enkulu yokukhuluphala ngokweqile, nesifo sikashukela ukudla ngokweqile ushukela. Ngokusho kocwaningo ushukela owuketshezi waziwa njengoyingozi kakhulu futhi awunalo izinga lokudla okunempilo. Yingakho abezempilo kuleli bencoma ukuthi kube nentela engu-20%  ezokhokhwa ngabakhiqizi beziphuzo ezinoshukela okubalwa namajusi ango-100%. SEKUPHELE izinsuku ezinhlanu izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli ziba ngaphezulu kuka-5 000 ngosuku.Lokhu kwenyuka kwezibalo zeCovid-19 kutolikwa ngokuthi sesisemome isiqubu sesithathu sokuhlasela kweCovid-19 kuleli. Kwezinye izifundazwe lesi siqubu sesingenile.Izibalo zakamuva zikhomba ukuthi bangu-5 074  abahaqwe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 okuholele ekutheni izibalo zabahaqwe yileli gciwane zibe ngu-1 696 564.Ababulewe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 bangu-56 osekuholele ekutheni babe ngu-56 974 ababulelwe yileli gciwane selokhu langena kuleli.Kulaba bantu abangu-56 abashonile, abayisithupha ngabaseFree State, abayisikhombisa abaseGauteng, abangu-15 abaseNorthern Cape, oyedwa owaKwaZulu-Natal, abayisithupha abaseWestern Cape. UMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli esitatimendeni uthe u-93% wabebenaleli gciwane sebeluleme okusho ukuthi abantu abangu-1 578 033 sebeluleme.UDkt David Nabarro wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni i-World Health Organization (WHO), ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba ethi okwamanje ukuqeda iCovid-19 akuyona into engenzeka.Uthe igciwane lizoqhubeka nokuziphindaphinda okuzoholela ekutheni imigomo ekhona ingabe isasebenza ngendlela ebilindelekile. Into okumele yenzeke ukuthi abantu bafunde ukuphila nalo igciwane."Ukuphila neCovid-19 yinto okumele sizifundise yona ngoba kuyabonakala ukuthi leli gciwane lisazoba khona isikhathi eside," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi into okumele abantu bayiqaphele kakhulu ukuthi ukuthelelana kwaleli gciwane kulawuleke, kungabi phezulu kakhulu.UNGQONGQOSHE wezeMpilo kuzwelonke, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe ukugunyazwa komgomo kamalaleveva iMosquirix kuzosiza i-Afrika yonke.UDkt Phaahla, owusihlalo wekomiti le-Afrika esenzansi elibhekelele ukuqedwa kwesifo umalaleveva i-South African Development Community's Malaria Elimination Eight Initiative (E8), uthe umgomo ungowokuqala ophasiswe yiWorld Health Organisation (WHO) futhi uzokwenza umehluko omkhulu ezwenikazi i-Afrika.Uthe sekuphele iminyaka eyevile kweyishumi kucutshungulwa ngomgomo kamalaleveva. Wathi uyajabula ukuthi ngemuva kwesikhathi esingaka iWHO ithathe isinqumo sokuthi iphasise ukuthi lo mgomo ukuthi ukhiqizwe bese usatshalaliswa nase-Afrika.UPhaahla uthe iMosquirix izosetshenziswa kanye nezinye izinsiza ezikhona zokunqanda ukusabalala kukamalaleveva emazweni ase-Afrika kuwo okubalwa i-Angola neMozambique.“Lo mgomo uyingqayizivele ezosiza ekulweni nalesi sifo esibulala abantu abangu-1 million ngonyaka kuwo okubalwa nezingane ezingu-260 000 ezineminyaka engaphansi kwemihlanu,"  kusho uDkt Phaahla.Uqhube wathi nakuba umalaleveva ungekho mandla eNingizimu Afrika kodwa nakhona abasengcupheni bazogoma." Ukunqandwa kukamalaleveva emazweni ahamba phambili ngokuba nayo kuzoba wusizo nakuleli njengoba umalaleveva eNingizimu Afrika ujwayele ukuphatha abantu abasuke bephuma kula mazwe. Sizokwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi umgomo utholakala emazweni odingeka kuwo ukuze kuvikelwe ukufa kwabantu abadala nezingane ezibulawa yilesi sifo ,"  kusho yena.Uqhube wathi ukugunyazwa kofmgomo olwa nezifo ezibulala abantu ezingena ngokuthi balunywe yizinambuzane kuyinto enkulu kakhulu."Izifo ezidluliselwa izinambuzane kubantu kunzima kakhulu ukuzelapha uma ziqhathaniswa namanye agciwane akhona. Sekuphele iminyaka eminingi ososayensi bezama ukuthola izindlela zokulwa nala magciwane, yingakho ngithi umgomo ubaluleke kakhulu ukhombisa ukuthi siya phambili,"  kusho yena.UKUYA ezinsukwini kwabesifazane kuphazamisekile ngokuhlaselwa wuvalo nokhwantalala ngenxa yokukhahlamezwa yiCovid-19 emhlabeni jikelele. Lokhu kuvezwe wucwaningo  elwathulwe engqungqutheleni iSociety for Endocrinology Annual Conference, ebibanjelwe Edinburgh, e-United Kingdom (UK), ngeledlule.Lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi uvalo, ukwesaba nokungalali ngendlela kuholele ekutheni kuphazamiseke ukuya esikhathini ngendlela ejwayelekile kwabanye abantu besifazane.Lolu cwaningo luveze ukuthi le miphumela yamanje kayenele, kusadingeka ukuthi kuphinde kwenziwe olunye ucwaningo oluzoveza ukuthi ngabe lezi zinkinga zizoba namthelela muni ngokuhamba kwesikhathi?Lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi ukungalali kwenza ukuthi ama-hormones angasebenzi kahle, umuntu wesifazane angayi ngendlela ezinsukwini zakhe okugcina sekuholele ekutheni abe nesisu esikhulu. Lokhu akugcini lapho, kuphazamisa nomgudu wenzalo kube nzima ukuthi umuntu wesifazane athole abantwana.UDkt Michelle Maher ongomunye wabacwaningi ebebenza ucwaningo ngabantu besifazane abangu-1 300 oluqalwe ngo-Ephreli, uthe bebebheka ukuthi abantu besifazane banengcindezi engakanani? Bebheka ukwesaba, ukuthi balala amahora akahle yini? Bebebheka nokuthi baya kanjani ezinsukwini zabo?Uthe laba besifazane ukuya ezinsukwini zabo okungaqondile, ukungayi nhlobo ezinsukwini, ukopha kakhulu noma ukuba nobuhlungu besinye uma bezoya ezinsukwini zabo. Uqhube wathi u-56% wabantu besifazane ebebeyingxenye yalolu cwaningo bathe izinsuku zabo zishintshile selokhu kufike iCovid-19. Uveze ukuthi  u-64% uthi izihlungu oba nazo ngaphambi kokuya ezinsukwini zabo zidlulele ngalesi sikhathi kanti u-54% uthe wehlelwe ugqozi lokuya lokuya ocansini. UDkt Maher uthe laba bantu besifazane abebekhathazeke kakhulu, benovalo ngenxa yeCovid-19, bonke basesigabeni sokuthi bathole izingane. Abebevele benenkinga yokhwantalala ngaphambi kokuthi kufike lesi sifo, uthe izinkinga zabo ziphindaphindeke kabili.UDkt Maher uthe: "Esikutholile ukuthi kudingeka ukuthi kube nokwelashwa okuqondile okuhlanganisa izifo ezithinta ingqondo nokuphazamiseka kokuya esekhathini."Ngokubona kwakhe, uthe lolu cwaningo luzosiza ekutheni kube nokuqonda ukuthi umgudu wenzalo usebenza kanjani? Luphinde lusize nasekutheni uma kwenziwa nokuqonda."Lolu cwaningo lwenziwe ngesikhathi kuqalwa uhlelo lokugoma, kungenzeka ukuthi imiphumela elandelayo ingabe isafana ngenxa yokuthi abantu abaningi bazobe sebegomile, uvalo selwehlile.“Uqhube wathi ithimba labacwaningi lisafuna ukuqhubeka licwaninge ezinye izinyanga eziyisithupha, libone ukuthi kuzokwenzekani kulaba besifazane ngaleso sikhathi.Okunye athe bazokubheka, ukwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi (BP), ukukhuluphala noma ukuncipha, ukulangazelela ucansi nokuvuthwa kwamaqanda abesifazane abayingxenye yalolu cwaningo. “Abantu besifazane siyabakhuthaza ukuthi basheshe babonane nodokotela uma bebona kuphazamiseka ukuya ezinsukwini kwabo; kungaba ukweqiwa yinyanga, ubuhlungu obungajwayelekile, ukopha kakhulu, ukwehlelwa wumfutho wokuya ocansini nokuzizwa bekhathazekile, bephelelwa ubuthongo nokunye,” kusho uDkt Maher.–   Asian News Time (IOL) ONGOTI bezempilo sebethole ukuthi igciwane eselizishintshile le-HIV laba namandla, abalibiza nge-VB variant, liyagobeka ngemishanguzo yokuthithibalisa iHIV ekhona.Abacwaningi abathole igciwane elisha le-HIV bashicilele umqulu wezempilo i-Science Journal, beshiyelana ngolwazi abalutholile olukhomba ukuthi eNetherlands kuneminyaka likhona kodwa akuzange kubonakale ngoba imishanguzo ekhona njengamanje iyakwazi ukulinqoba.Uma liqhathaniswa neHIV ebilokhu ikhona, lona liyashesha ukusabalala egazini okungenza ukuthi onalo asheshe abe nengculazi uma engayidli imishanguzo.UDkt Chris Wymant waseNyuvesi i-Oxford ongomuye wabacwaningi, uthe abantu abangethuki ngoba ngesikhathi benza ucwaningo babonile ukuthi nakuba leli gciwane lishesha liziphindaphinde egazini, uma umuntu eseqale imishanguzo yokulithithibalisa, amasosha akhe omzimba athola amandla ngendlela efanayo nawomuntu oneHIV ebivele ikhona."Akumele kube nokukhathazeka ngalo. Ngokuthola kwethu ngocwaningo,  igciwane laqala ukuba khona eNetherlands ngama-80’s nama-90’s. Ucwaningo luveza ukuthi izinhlelo zaseNetherlands zokuthi basheshe bahlolwe abanalo, bese bedla imishanguzo, zisizile ekutheni igciwane lingawatholi amandla okuthi lisabalale kakhulu," kusho uDkt Wymant.UDkt Christopher Fraser naye obeyingxenye yabacwaningi, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi kulandelwe imigomo ebekwe yiNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), yokuhlolwa nokwelashwa kwabantu abane-HIV.Labo sosayensi bathi ucwaningo luveza ukuthi into ecatshangwayo ethi igciwane uma lilokhu lizishintshashintsha liphelelwa ngamandla, ayilona iqiniso ngaso sonke isikhathi njengoba kuqhathaniswa nokwenzeka kwiCorona.Igciwane elisha liqale ukutholakala kubantu kumasampula angu-17 abayingxenye yocwaningo oluqhubekayo olwaziwa ngeBEEHIVE, olubheka ukuthi ngabe i-HIV selokhu yaba khona, izintshintsha kanjani? Ocwaningweni bekuthathwa amasampula egazi kubantu okutholakale ukuthi banesandulela-ngculazi e-Europe nase-Uganda. Amasampula egazi okutholakale ukuthi ane-viral load ephezulu (okuyizinga le-HIV), abecutshungulwe kabanzi, kubhekwa ukuthi kwenziwa yini? Ngesikhathi kuqhutshekwa kucutshungulwa, kusetshenziswe amasampula  abantu baseNetherlands, Switzerland naseBelguim. Abacwaningi babe sebecubungulisisa kahle amasampula abebenawo ocwaningweni, bathola ukuthi empeleni ngawaseNetherlands ebemaningi abe nezinga eliphezulu. Kube sekuvela ukuthi izinga eliphezulu lenziwa wukuthi besekuyigciwane elisha. Abacwaningi bathe uma becwaninga ulwazi bebheka indlela i-HIV ebiyenza ngayo emizimbeni yabo, bathola ukuthi igciwane, cishe laba khona ngama-80’s nama-90’s. Ulwazi lukhombise ukuthi ngo-2010, kube noshintsho ngendlela eliziphatha ngayo, laqala ukwehlelwa ngamandla.  KULEZI zinsuku uzwa abantu bekhala ngokuthi le yinyanga yokudla iklabishi ngenxa yokuthi imali yokuthenga inyama ayikho.Namhlanje sizobheka ukuthi iklabishi ngabe linamiphi imisoco.Iklabishi linothe ngo-vitamin K, vitamin C nemisoco esiza ukwehlisa umzimba. Amaqabunga alo aluhlaza anezakhamzimba ezisiza ukulwa nezifo, ama-antioxidants.Ongoti bezokudla bathi iklabishi uma liqhathaniswa neminye imifino alibizi, okwenza babe baningi abantu abakwazi ukulithenga. Ngaphezu kwalokho, linama-calories amancane, okusho ukuthi alinazo izinto ezenza ukuthi umuntu akhuluphale. Abantu abanezinhlelo zokwehlisa umzimba bajwayele ukulifaka  ezidlweni zabo ngenxa yalokho.Umpheki, uNkk Nokuthula Dlamini uthe iklabishi ungalidla ngezindlela eziningi. Ungalipheka ulenze isishebo, ungalenza isaladi, ungalidla lingaphekiwe, ungalenza ama-roll, abanye benza nejusi ngalo.Amino AcidsIklabishi linemisoco eyaziwa ngama-amino acid akhiqiza ama-antioxidant,  asiza ekutheni umzimba usebenze kahle kungakheki uketshezi oludala ukuthi abantu baguge ngokushesha - ama-free radicals. Ama-amino acid ayasiza nasekutheni imizwa ehambisa umyalezo ebuchosheni isebenze kahle, aphinde asize ekugayekeni kokudla.Ama-PolyphenolUmqingo wezempilo i-American Journal of Clinical Nutrition, uveza ukuthi iklabishi linothe ngama-polyphenols asiza ngokuthi: ungavuvukali (okungaba ukuvuvukala kolimi okuhambisana nokudideka okudalwa ukuba buthakathaka kwamasosha omzimba); avikela ukuthi ugule kalula uma udle ukudla okuthile okungahambisani nawe (allergy); asiza ekutheni ukudla kugayeke; asiza nasekutheni inhliziyo isebenze kahle; anciphisa amathuba okuthi uhlaselwe wumdlavuza, okungaba umdlavuza wesikhumba, umdlavuza wendlala yesinye, i-prostate cancer, umdlavuza wamanyikwe, i-pancreatic cancer, umdlavuza wombilo i-oesophageal cancer nokunye.NgokweMedical News Today, indlela yokwehlisa isisindo - iCabbage Soup Diet - eyaqala ukusetshenziswa ngabantu ngama-1950s, iyasebenza kodwa uma usuyiyekile umzimba ubuyela kulokho obuyikho futhi.IZINHLOBO ZEKLABISHIIKLABISHI ELILUHLAZAIklabishi linothe ngo-vitamin K, vitamin C nemisoco esiza ukwehlisa umzimba,  amaqabunga alo aluhlaza anezakhamzimba ezisiza ukulwa nezifo, ama-antioxidant.Iklabishi elibomvu (purple) linemisoco efanayo nale etholakala kweliluhlaza bese lengeza ngama-anthocyanin asiza ekuvikeleni ukuvuvukala.SAVOY CABBAGELinemisoco efanayo netholakala kuleli elijwayelekile kodwa lona liqinile uma  uliqhathanisa nelijwayelekile eliluhlaza.BRUSSELS SPROUTIklabishi elingamabholana amancane kunaleli elijwayelekile linothe ngo-vitamin K, C, antioxidant. Kuyenzeka libe nezinsiza ezivikela ukuthi uhlaselwe wumdlavuza.KALENayo ingena ngaphansi komndeni wemifino eyiklabishi, inothe ngo-vitamin C, K. Inothe kakhulu nangama-antioxidants nezinsiza ezinciphisa amathuba okuvuvukala.Cishe wonke umuntu uyakuthanda ukuphila, ngisho ngabe usugula kanjani, ngaphandle kwezimo ezimbalwa, abaningi abantu bathanda ukuphila baze bakhokhobe. Ukuhamba emhlabeni kwabantu abaningi kubuhlungu kodwa sazi kahle ukuthi uma usukuhlaziya kuyaye kutholakale ukuthi bekuyinto ebingavikeleka. Nami ngiyavuma ukuthi ekuhlaziyeni engike ngabandanyeka kukho alikho nelilodwa ilanga lapho esathola khona ukuthi abaningi abashonile bekungenxa yesimo ebesingeke sivikeleke, lapha ngihlanganisa abancane nabadala.Kunalokhu kucabanga okuthi abantu asebebadala vele kufanele bagule bashone ngoba basuke sebegugile.Ngihlale njalo ngilwa nale micabango ngoba iyingozi futhi iyawulahla umkhondo.Imicabango efuze lena ngokwami isiholele ekushoneni kwabantu ikakhulu asebekhulile abaningi, omama nobaba, ogogo nomkhulu okumele ngabe bayaphila namhlanje.Imbangela yalokhu kushona kangaka ilelephi, zikuphi iziphethu zale nsambatheka? Uzothi omunye kuyoncika ekutheni ubuzwa kubani ngoba kuningi okuthinta ukwelapha umuntu.Ake sibukisane nakhu okusanda kwenzeka: kugule umama osemdala obelokhu eya kodokotela, emtholampilo nasesibhedlela ehlushwa ushukela, ukukhathala komzimba, ubuhlungu bezicubu namajoyinti ikakhulu enqulwini, emanyongeni, amadolo nomfasankomo wakhona. Umhlume wawudla amagalane kuye, equmbelana, esuza, ukukhathala emzimbeni kubuzwa kuye, izicubu zezitho, izinyawo kungahambeki, nendle yayisiqalile ukuziphumela ingalawuleki. Ngenxa yokuthi wayehlale ekhala ngokungabi mnandi ocabangweni, nasesifubeni kushisa, kunenkezela inhliziyo kuthi makaphalaze, odokotela bakhe babelokhu bethi unezilonda lezi esithanda ukuzibiza ngama ‘ulcer’ lapha ngasocabangweni, esewaphuze amaphilisi okwelapha lezi zilonda kwaze kwashikisha ufudu.Babodwa abesebethi une esidi egcwele umzimba nesifo samathambo. Ubeseke wahlinzwa emgogodleni, enyongeni nasedolweni. Emva kwalokhu kuhlinzwa aziphelanga izinhlungu. Wayelokhu ekhale njalo ngezinhlungu ezingapheli ezibamba zinkonkoshela amanyonga nomgogodla, idolo lakhe okwakuthiwe kuphele ungwengwezi oluvikela ukugudlana kwamathambo, ababethe emuva kokumfakela lona idolo, lizobuyela esimeni lisebenze kahle, kuphele iminjunju yokugwaza satshumetshu, ukuvuvukala babethe odokotela kuyoba yinto yayizolo, kuphi la? Odokotela ababemhlinzile base belapha kude, sebemkhomba kodokotela laba abelulayo umzimba, bethi uyolulamela khona. Umama lona uthi wayezibuza ukuthi uzokwelulwa amajoyinti nezicubu kanjani phela ngoba kwangesisona nje isimo sokungathi angaqinisela, izinhlungu zazingabekezeleki ephuma ekhala njalo kulokhu kwelulwa. Phela base bemnikeze inqola emuva kokuhluleka ukugwedla ngezinduku.Abantu bakithi abagula bahlukumezeke ngale ndlela, behliswe isithunzi bagcwele yonke indawo, sibabona mihla namalanga futhi aziyekile izinombolo zabo ukwenyuka.Ngicela ukuyibeka kanjena le nto: kunesithombe esidwebekayo esithi abantu bakithi bazibona sebengene ogebeni lokuhlinzwa bengachazelekanga kahle ukuthi kuzokwenziwani, isizathu yini, beyingekho yini enye indlela yokukwelapha lokhu kugula ngaphandle kokuhlinzwa. Incazelo abayaye bayilokothe uma ubabuza iyaye igudle njalo ekutheni udokotela wathi uma ngingahlinzwa ngizohamba ngenqola nezinhlungu ngeke ziphele. Uyabona-ke noma ngabe ubani uma ungathi kuxoxwa kube kulobiziswa isimo senqola nezinhlungu ezingeke ziphele, ezigulini kuvele kugqame ukuhlinzwa njengesisombululo; ezinye izindlela zokwelashwa zingavakashelwanga. UDokotela uNxumalo akalwisani nokuhlinzwa. Ngithanda abantu bakithi banikezwe ulwazi olwanele ngesifo nangohlelo lokwelashwa kuhlanganisa nezinye izinhlelo zokwelapha lesi sifo, bangazitholi sengathi sebeyasatshiswa. Nathi ndlu yakithi asifunde ukungathathi okushiwo ngudokotela njengomnqamulajuqu. Asifunde ukuyobuza komunye umsebenzi wezempilo ngenikuxoxe nodokotela, asihambe siyoshunqisa impepho sibuze emsamo wakini ngokushiwo ngudokotela. Uma kukuvumela, hamba uyophonsa amathambo. Asingaveli nje sivume yonke into.Lo mama ushone ukudla kungasahlali, esephalaza kakhulu, ubekuzwa ngephunga sekumnukela kukude okuya ngasethunjini, ushukela usujomba uye phezulu ungafuni ukwehla ngisho usufakwe imijovo ethenjiwe ukuwehlisa. Bekuthi njalo ume wehlile kube nzima ukuwunyusa, ngisho sekufakwe imijovo emikhulu, waphuziswa umbhubhudlo kube nzima satshe.Kuningi okungaba izimbangela zokusheshe asishiye emhlabeni lo mama, kodwa engifisa sikubukisise:isifo sikashukela sakhe. Umama ubelokhu elanda amaphilisi, kungekho ukumeseka ngokucoyisisa ukusebenza kwawo amaphilisi emzimbeniLezi zifo ezaziphethe lo mama ziyelapheka, ogulayo aphile saka. Baningi kakhulu abantu esibelapha mihla namalanga bephethwe ngokufanayo nokungaphezu kwalokhu. Asizincenge sisondele kubasebenzi bempilo abazokwazi ukukwelapha, hhayi laba abangenasikhathi nathi, abafuna imali kuphela okanye laba abadlala ngabantu bakithi bezihluphekela bekhangisa bebadayisela izinhlanganisela ezibatshazwa ukwelapha yonke into ngesikhathi esisodwa.Engifisa ukukucacisa ukuthi masihambele kude ekwelashweni lapho kumimilitwa khona imithi, ukwelashwa okungalwi nomsusa kuphela kulwisanwa nezimpawu. Ngaleyo ndlela sisuke sisondeza ilanga lokuhamba emhlabeni eduze. Umsebenzi wami nawe mfowethu nodawethu, mama, baba, gogo, mkhulu, sonke nje ndlu yakithi ukulwa nesiphethu sokugula; leyo ndlela yokwelapha iyokwelula izinsuku emhlabeni siphile. Asalile nokuhamba emhlabeni, umphefumulo okaJehova kuphela, engiphume inqina ngilwa nakho ukwelashwa okusondeza abantu bakithi ekufeni.Mpilonde!!UMENGAMELI wakuleli uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa uthe inkampani ekhiqiza umgomo weCovid-19 iJohnson & Johnson (J&J) ithembise ukuthi izoyiletha ngokushesha eminye imigomo kuleli.Isikhungo esibhekelele ukuphepha kwemithi e-United States, iFood and Drug Association (FDA), imemezele ngoLwesihlanu ukuthi uphenyo lwayo luveza ukuthi imigomo engu-16 million, ekhiqizwe esikhungweni esikhiqiza imigomo yakwaJ&J eBaltimore,  yonakele ngoba inezinsalela ze-AstraZeneca.I-AstraZeneca kwatholakala ukuthi ayikulungele ukugoma abantu bakuleli ngenxa yegciwane eselizishintshile. Ingu-2 million imigomo ekuleli ethintekayo kule, okuthiwa inezinsalela ze-AstraZeneca.  Leyo migomo umengameli uthe izolahlwa.URamaphosa,  obekhuluma  emhlanganweni iG7 obuse-United Kingdom, uthe  i-Aspen ithe isiqalile ukulungisa imigomo okumele ithunyelwe kuleli kuleli sonto.Uhlelo lokusatshalaliswa kwemigomo kuleli luhamba kancane ngenxa yokuthi imigomo ifika kancane kodwa uRamaphosa uthe kuzolunga ngoba useke wakhuluma nanomengameli wase-US uMnuz Joe Biden ukuthi izwe lakhe linikele ngemigomo ezogoma abantu base-Afrika.“Ngesikhathi sikhuluma noBiden ngikucacisile ukuthi imigomo ezonikelwa yi-US kumele kube ngezosiza e-Afrika neNingizimu,”  kusho yena.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo  obambile uNkk Mmamoloko Kubayi-Ngubane, uthe ukulahlwa kwale migomo kuzoluphazamisa kakhulu uhlelo lokusatshalaliswa kwemigomo kuleli.UDkt David Manyae, ungoti wezokuxhumana kwamazwe emhlabeni eNyuvesi yaseJohannesburg, uthe sekuyisikhathi sokuthi amazwe athathe isinqumo sokuthi kuxegiswe imithetho kudedelwe amazwe azikhiqizele imigomo yamazwe awo.“Njengamanje azidingeki izimpi nokuklolodelana ngokuthi yiliphi izwe elingcono phakathi kwamazwe aseNtshonalanga neChina. Into edingekayo ukuthi kusindiswe abantu bonke kungakhathalekile ukuthi bahlala emazweni acebile noma cha,"  kusho yena.USolwazi Mosa Moshabela weNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal, uthe ukonakala kwemigomo okuthiwa kwenzekile emigomeni yakwa J&J kusho ukuthi inezinsalela zeminye imigomo, akukhona ukuthi yakhiwe ngezithako ezonakele.“I-FDA ikwaze ukuthola ubufakazi kwi-batch eyodwa ukuthi inezinsalela ze-AstraZeneca eminye kuyasoleka ukuthi nayo intintekile,"  kusho yena. UKUFUNDA izincwadi noma amaphepha kuhlale kuchazwa njengento eyenza ukuthi ingqondo yengane ikhule kodwa ungoti ocwaninga ngezingane uSolwazi Diana Leyva,  uthi ukunikeza ingane imisebenzi ethile yasendlini kuyayisiza kakhulu ukuze ikwazi ukucabanga ngokushesha nokuthi ikwazi ukuhlanganisa imibala nokuthi izinto zihambisana kanjani ngesikhathi yenza le misebenzi.Lolu cwaningo lushicilelwe kwiThe Conservation lwenziwe nemindeni engu-248 engamaLathini (Latino) ehlala e-United States.Laba bazali bebechaza ukuthi benza kanjani ukuthi izingane zabo zisheshe zibe nezinga eliphezulu lokucabanga besebenzisa imisebenzi yasekhaya ngoba bekubonakala ukuthi izingane zabo uma sezisesikoleni zenza kangcono ekuxoxeni izindatshana nokukwazi ukubhala nokubala.Laba bazali batshele abacwaningi ngemfihlo yabo, abacwaningi base behlukanisa abazali izigaba ezimbili kwaba khona abazali abalulandelayo uhlelo lokunikeza izingane imisebenzi yasekhaya nabangazinikezi ngemuva kwezinyanga ezinhlanu kwabe sekubonakala ukuthi ngempela ukhona umehluko kulezi zingane ezinikezwa imisebenzi yesekhaya.Lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi imisebenzi esiza ingane ukuthi icabange kungaba ukuthi ilungiselela isidlo somndeni ngokubeka izitsha zokudla etafuleni, ukubhala igilosa ezothengwa , ukuzikhethela ukuthi izogqokani nokunye kuyayisiza ingane ngokuthi icabange, iphinde ikwazi ukuhlanganisa imibala nokubala.1.UKUBHALA IGILOSALolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi ingane ngesikhathi ibhala igilosa ifunda izinombolo,  ukubhala, uma isencane kakhulu ize ikhuthazeke nokuthi idwebe lokho okumele kuyothenga uma kungukuthi ayikakakwazi ukubhala.Ucwaningo luveza ukuthi abanye abazali okwenziwe ngabo ucwaningo bebeziyeka izingane zizame ukubhala nokufunda igilosa okwenze ukuthi zisheshe zikwazi ukubhala." Uma umzali esebuyile ezitolo ingane kuye kudingeke ukuthi ibheke ukuthi zonke izinto ebizibhalile zithengwe zonke yini. Lokhu kuyisiza kakhulu ingane ukuthi ikwazi ukuzama ukufunda  nokubona ukuthi igama lichazani ngoba isuke iphambi kwayo,"  kusho usolwazi Leyva.2.UKUPHEKA NOKULUNGISA ITAFULAUkuqoqa izithako nokuhlela ukuthi etafuleni kuzohlala abantu abangaki uSolwazi Leyva, uthe kunikeza ingane ithuba elihle lokuthi ifunde izibalo ngoba iyabala ukuthi amapuleti, izipuni nezinye izinto okudingeka ukuthi zibekwe etafuleni  ngabe ziyalingana yini nabantu  abazodla." Imibuzo engasiza ekutheni ingane ikwazi ukubala ukuthi uyibuze ukuthi ngabe kudingeka amapuleti amangaki, noma uyithume ukuthi ikukalele izithako zokupheka noma zokubhaka. Lokhu kuzoyenza ukuthi ibale," kusho uSolwazi Leyva.3. UKUXOXA NGESIKHATHI SOKUDLAKweminye imindeni ukukhuluma etafuleni akuvumelekile kodwa lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi uma kusetshenziswa lesi sikhathi ukuze ingane ixoxe ngokuthi usuku lwayo lube njani? Kusiza ngokuthi ikwazi ukubhala indatshana uma isisesikoleni, ingayixovi ngoba isiyazi ukuthi kumele indaba ilandelane kanjani."Abazali kumele ingane bayisize ngokuthi bayibuze imibuzo engezukwenza ukuthi iphendule ngo-yebo noma cha. Okunye  okungasiza ekutheni ingane ixoxe kahle ukuthi ikhuthazwe ukuthi ikhulume ngento eyithandayo khona izovuleleka ixoxe kahle," kuchaza uSolwazi Leyva.4. ULIMI OLUSETSHENZISWA EKHAYAUcwaningo luveza ukuthi kubalulekile ukuthi ingane uma isekhaya isebenzise ulimi olulula kuyo akukhathalekile ukuthi esikoleni kusetshenziswa luphi." Okubalulekile ukuthi ingane uma isekhaya ikwazi ukuxoxa kahle indaba. Lokhu kuzoyisiza ekutheni uma isisesikoleni ikwazi ukuhlanganisa kahle isebenzisa ulimi elisebenzisa uma isisekoleni." La masu angasebenza kuphela uma umndeni ujwayele ukupheka, udle ndawonye noma ungabantu abayithengayo igilosa. Kungasiza nabazali abamatasa ukuthi bangazifaki izingane ezinhlelweni ezibizayo zokufunda basebenzise izinto ezikhona emakhaya" kusho uSolwazi Leyva.IMISHANGUZO yeHIV ewumjovo izosiza ekutheni iziguli zikwazi ukuzikhethela indlela ehambisana nazo yokwelapha noma yokuzivikela  kuleli gciwane.UDkt Siyabonga Nzimande wezinhlangano zomphakathi ezilwela ukuthi kutholakale amakhambi okwelapha lesi sifo eThekwini, iHIV Civil Society,  usho kanje njengoba iViiV  Healthcare okuyinkampani  yase-UK, enelungelo lokukhiqiza imishanguzo yeHIV ewumjovo  kulindeleke ukuthi iqale ukukhiqiza  imishanguzo engabizi kakhulu,   ama-generic abiza u-R540 kuya kuR570, umjovo ngamunye,  ngosizo lwe-US President's Emergency Plan for AIDS Relief (PEPFAR) ekuqaleni konyaka ozayo. ICAB-LA iwumjovo oyizinhlobo ezimbili wokuzivikela kwiHIV, osebenza njengamaphilisi i-Pre-Exposure Prophylaxis (PrEP) nothithibalisa leli gciwane  osebenza njengama ARV aphuzwayo,  yomibili ijovwa kanye emuva kwezinyanga ezimbili, okusho ukuthi isiguli sizojova kasithupha ngonyaka.UNzimande uthe umjovo ungasiza ezinkingeni zokucwaswa okuholela ekutheni abantu abanaleli gciwane bagcine sebeyiyeka imishanguzo yabo,  kodwa okwamanje basanxenxa uhulumeni ukuthi kube nguyena othenga le mishanguzo athengele iziguli njengoba kwenzeka ngamaphilisi akhona njengamanje." Ziningi izindlela ezintsha ezisithokozisayo ezisohlelweni okulindeleke  ukuthi ziqale ukusebenza ngonyaka ozayo, njengendukwana eshuthekwa esikhumbeni bese ilokhu idedela umuthi, i-implant nepheshi elikwenza kokubili ukuvika ukukhulelwa kanye neHIV. Siyakholwa ukuthi lezi zinto ezintsha zizokwenza umehluko ekwelashweni kwaleli gciwane kuleli kakhulukazi kubantu abasha. Okunye esikwenzayo ukukhuluma nezinkampani ezikhiqiza la makhambi ukuthi ziwadayise ngemali engambi eqolo ukuze uhulumeni akwazi ukuwathenga,"  kusho yena.IViiV Health iyona kuphela enelungelo lokukhiqiza le mishanguzo  ewumjovo kuze kube u-2031. UDkt Lauren Jankelwitz weSouth African Clinical Society, uthe abantu bakuleli bayawuthanda umuthi owumjovo.“Uma ubheka indlela umjovo wokuhlela umndeni osetshenziswa ngayo ngabesifazane uma uqhathaniswa namaphilisi enza okufanayo, uyabona ukuthi abantu bakuleli bayakuthanda ukujova ngoba ujova kanye ngemuva kwesikhathi esithile awulokhu ukhathazeka ngokuthatha amaphilisi. Into okumele siyibheke ukuthi lowo mjovo usezingeni eliyilo yini,” kusho yena.UDkt Yogan Pillay weHealth Acess Initiative SA, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo ethi, nakuba imijovo yeHIV kubukeka sengathi ingathandwa, inkinga ekhona ukuthi ibhajethi yoMnyango wezeMpilo yehlisiwe, okusho ukuthi umnyango ungakwazi ukuyithenga uma ithengwa ngemali efana nokuthengwa ngayo amaphilisi.“ Uma kungenjalo kusho ukuthi kuzomele kuthathwe isinqumo sokuthi kunezinto ezizomiswa ngesikhathi kuthengwa le mijovo,”  kusho uPillay.IMISHANGUZO eyelapha ukhwantalala, ingcindezi yomphefumulo ingaholela ekutheni abayisebenzisayo bangalulangazeli ucansi noma kushintshe indlela abebelulangazelela ngayo.UMnuz Abdurahmaan Kenny, osophikweni olubhekele izifo ezithinta ingqondo ePharma Dynamics, uthe bajwayele ukunikeza iziguli imishanguzo ngenhloso yokuthi kwelapheke izifo ezithinta ingqondo kodwa kwesinye isikhathi baye bathole ukuthi iziguli ezisebenzisa leyo mishanguzo kunokuthi zelapheke zigcina sezinezimpawu zokuthi zinengcindezi ephindaphindekile,  ngenxa yokuthi imishanguzo yenza ukuthi zibe nezinto ezizenza zibe namahloni futhi zihlambalazeke.Uthe imithi eyelapha ukhwantalala nengcindezi yomphefumulo ama-antidepressents abajwayele ukuyinika iziguli basuke befisa ukuthi angashintshi impilo yazo yocansi,  kodwa kuyenzeka bathole ukuthi isiguli sesibonakala sinengcindezi enkulu ngoba le mishanguzo isiholele ekutheni zibe nezinkinga zocansi ezidalwe imishanguzo, i- emergent sexual dysfunction  kuye ngokuthi isiguli sisebenzisa yiphi inhlobo yemishanguzo.Uthe ezinye  iziguli ezisebenzisa imishanguzo eyelapha ingcindezi yomphefumulo nokhwantalala ziye zibike ukuthi zizizwa zingasalulangazeleli ucansi,  okuye kuholele ekutheni zingabe zisathanda ukuqhubeka nokusebenzisa imishanguzo yazo.Ezinye uthe zibikile ukuthi azisafinyeleli kuvuthondaba, uthe lokhu kwenziwa ukuthi imishanguzo kuyenzeka iphazamise ukugijima kwegazi ezinzweni okuholela ekutheni amadoda angafiki kuvuthondaba uma bezithokozisa.Abesifazane nabo baye babike ukuthi abafiki kuvuthondaba kwesinye isikhathi bathi isitho sabo sangasese asinalo uketshenzi olwenele olwenza ukuthi kushelele kahle, abanye bathi uma bekitazwa ngophathina babo abasabuzwa lobo bumnandi.UKenny ubesho lokhu njengoba u-Okthoba kuyinyanga yokuqwashisa ngezifo ezithinta ingqondo.Uthe akuzona zonke iziguli eziba nokuba nokuphazamiseka okuthinta impilo yazo yocansi."Indlela umzimba ophazamiseka ngayo uma usebenzisa imishanguzo eyelapha izifo ezithinta ingqondo iyehluka esigulini ngasinye kodwa imishanguzo eyaziwa nge-serotonin reuptake inhibitors (SSRIs) ingaholela ekutheni iziguli zibe nokuphazamiseka okuthe xaxa uma ziqhathaniswa nemishanguzo eyaziwa ne-norepinephrine dopamine reuptake inhibitors (NDRIs).“Ukuphazamiseka kwempilo yocansi kungaqeda amandla njengoba kuthinta kakhulu isimo somuntu sisonke. Izinga lempilo, ubudlelwane  bakhe  kanye nenhlalakahle. Ukusondelana ngokocansi kuyingxenye ebalulekile othandweni. Uma oyedwa noma bobabili abalingani  behlangabezana nenkinga ethinta ucansi lokho kungathikameza ubudlelwane babo, kube nokukhathazeka, indumalo nokucasuka kwabathandanayo. Kungenzeka futhi kuholele ekucindezelekeni kwengqondo, okuhlanganisa ukukhathazeka, ukwehla kokuzethemba. Ukungasebenzi kwemizwa  kwenza ukuthi izinkinga ezithinta ucansi zidlange," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi uma uhlangabezana nenkinga ethinta ucansi ngesikhathi usebenzisa imishanguzo eyelapha ukhwantalala nengcindezi yomphefumulo kubalulekile ukuthi ukhulume nodokotela wakho.“Udokotela angakusiza ngokuthi ashintshe  indlela akwelapha ngayo. Ngezinye izikhathi, angancoma amasu noma imithi eyengeziwe, eyelapha inkinga yocansi esidalwe imishanguzo oyisebenzisayo. Kubalulekile ukukhuluma nomlingani wakho ukuze aqonde okwenzekayo,"  kusho uKenny.UMnuz Ahmed El Hofy wenkampani ekhiqiza imithi iJohnson &Johnson, uthe kuningi okuphazamisekayo endleleni umuntu abejwayele ukuphila ngayo uma ehlaselwe ingcindezi nokhwantalala, okungaba ukwehluleka ukwenza  umsebenzi wakhe  ngendlela  kanye nokuba ntekenteke  kwamasosha omzimba. UKUSETSHENZISWA kwemithi eyelapha ukuvuvukala kwamehlo eyaziwa ngama-steroid, kungaholela ekutheni kulimale imbumbulu yehlo eyenza ukuthi umuntu abone kahle, agcine esehlaselwe yinhlanganisela yezifo ezingelapheki, okuthiwa yi-glaucoma.Ama-steroid avamise ukusetshenziswa ngodokotela ngemuva kokuthi isiguli kade sihlinzwe esweni kulasha ukuvuvukala kodwa uma esetshenzisa njalo angadala izinkinga.UDkt Chinedu Njezi owungoti wokwelashwa kwezifo eziholela ekutheni umuntu abone luvivi ezigcina zenze ukutho umuntu angaboni nhlobo uma zingalashiwe,  uthe abantu kumele baqaphele uma besebenzisa imithi engamaconsi efakwa emehlweni ngoba uma leyo mithi ingama-steroid, bangazithola besenkingeni ngokuhamba kwesikhathi. Uthe nakuba ucwaningo lwesayensi lungakavezi ngokusobala ukuthi i-glaucoma idalwa yini kodwa kuyavela ukuthi ukusebenzisa ama-steroid njalo, kudala ukuthi isimo sibe sibi kakhulu kanti umonakalo osewenzekile awube usalungiseka.Usho lokhu nje, yingoba le nyanga esikuyo isetshenziselwa ukuqwashisa nokufundisa nge-glaucoma kuleli.Lezi zifo singezinye ezihamba phambili eziholele ekutheni abantu bangaboni emhlabeni. I-glaucoma uma ingelashwanga ibulala imithambo emincane esehlweni okuyiyona eyenza umuntu ukuba abone kahle.UDkt Njezi uthe umonakalo odalwa yi-glaucoma ehlweni awube usalungiseka.Ucwaningo olwenziwe eNigeria ngo-2015, lukhomba ukuthi ukungafundiseki kwabantu nge-glaucoma, kuholele ekutheni kube nenqwaba yabantu abaneminyaka engu-40 kuyaphezulu, abanalezi zifo.ENingizumu Afrika bangu-4.5% kuya ku5.3% abantu abaneminyaka ewu-40 kuya phezulu abahlaselwa yi-glaucoma.KUNOKULANGAZELA ukwazi ukuthi insangu yelapha ziphi izifo njengoba iningi belazi ukuthi lesi sihlahla sidume ngokuthi siyabhenywa futhi  bekungavumelekile ukutshalwa kwaso kuleli. UDkt Carmen James  osebebenzela eHillcrest ongomunye wodokotela abanemvume yokunikeza iziguli zabo imithi ethakwe ngensangu etshalelwe izidingo zezempilo, iCannabis, obengomunye wodokotela abebechaza ukuthi insangu yelapha kanjani embukisweni wemikhiqizo eyenziwe ngensangu , iCannabis Expo,  uthe isifo esihamba phambili ekwelashweni kusetshenziswa insangu, izinhlungu ngokuhlukana kwazo, nokhwantalala."Izinhlungu thina bodokotela siye sizihlukanise ukuze sinikeze isiguli umuthi ozosiziza ukuze selapheke. Udokotela ogunyaziwe uyakwazi ukunikeza iziguli imithi ethakwe ngensangu kodwa kumele aqale ethole ukuthi izinhlungu eziphethe isiguli ngezinjani. Ngabe ubuhlungu okungathi buyagwaza, ubuhlungu obudalwe ukuthi uthinte into ethile elimazayo njengokusha, ubuhlungu obungaselapheki okungubuhlungu obukuvusa noma usebuthongweni," kusho uDkt James.Uthe ubuhlungu abuyona into encane ngoba buthikameza impilo yomzimba wonke uma bungelashwa." Umqingo olawula indlela odokotela abelapha ngayo  izinhlungu ngokwehlukana kwazo, iPain Journal ka-2020 iyona esilawulayo ukuthi imuphi umuthi okumele uwunike isiguli ngokukala ubuhlungu esibuzwayo. Ezinganeni udokotela ubheka ubuso bengane ngoba ayikwazi ukuchaza.  Iningi laleyo imithi inamakhemikhali kanti imithi eyenziwe ngensangu ayinawo amakhemikhali,"  kusho yena.Uthe yena njengodokotela ogunyanziwe ukwelapha ngensangu usebenzisa imithi efuthwayo (sprays),  amaphilisi, uketshenzi oluthelwa  emanzini, uwoyela, amaphilisi ashuthekwa ngemuva nokunye uma elapha iziguli zakhe kuye ngokuthi ubuhlungu obuphethe leso siguli budinga luphi uhlobo lomuthi."Imithi eyenziwe ngansangu ithumela umyalezo ozokwenza ukuthi ubuhlungu behle kwizinzwa eziwumsuka wobuhlungu. Le ndlela ibizwa nge-Endocannabinoid System. Isetshenziselwa ukwelapha izinhlungu, ukuqinisa amasosha omzimba ukuze akwazi ukuzilwela nezifo nezinye izifo,"  kusho uDkt James.UNkk Anna Mulder  obechaza ngamakhowe ayinsangu, uthe ukusetshenziswa kwamakhowe ayinsangu ama-psilocybin mushroom kwelapha izifo ezifana nengcindezi yomphefumulo, ukhwantalala, abanenkinga yokuphuza ngokweqile, abafuna ukuyeka ukubhema."Amakhowe bawadla enjengoba enjalo noma agaywe enziwe impuphu, ashintshwe enziwe uwoyela ofuthwayo nokunye. La makhowe njengoba ewumuthi akumele uwadle noma uwasebenzise noma ikanjani ngoba ayadaka uma weqise isikali. Ngaphezu kwalokho njengeminye imithi kungenzeka angakuphathi kahle ube nenhliziyo encane, ube nenkwashu, ukwethuka nokunye. Ngithi nokunye nje ngoba enza izinto ezingafani kumuntu nomuntu okumele ukwenze uma ufuna ukwelashwa ngawo ukuwadla okokuqala. Leyo ndlela ozizwe ngayo uqala ukuwadla, iyona ndlela azokuphatha ngayo uma sewelashwa .  Okunye iziguli okumele zikwazi ukuthi kumele ube nobufakazi bokuthi usebenzisa wona ngoba uma uhlolwa kuyavela ngakho kumele ube nobufakazi bukadokotela bokuthi uyelashwa,"  kusho uNkk Mulder.DKT BONGANI NXUMALOUSHUKELA emzimbeni ungumbulalazwe angikhulumi ngalona esiwudlayo etiyeni, ekudleni okunhlobonhlobo, eziphuzweni, ushukela osezidlweni lezi esizithandayo nalowo esiwuthola otshwaleni nakwezinye izinto. Selokhu ngabona ngikhula kunale ndlela yokukala lo shukela egazini isikhathi esiningi okuyaye ucofwe emunweni bese ithonsi legazi lisetshenziswa ukukala ushukela osegazini. Iyona ndlela esafundiswa yona kwezempilo kuthiwe asiyisebenzise sibheke ukunyuka kwawo egazini, la manani enza sithathe  izinqumo zokuqala abantu bakithi emishanguzweni kashukela. Le ndlela yokubheka inkinga kashukela egazini yiyona engumbulalazwe uqobo.(Ngicela ukufaka isiqondiso esithi lapha ngikhuluma ngesifo sikashukela lesi okuthiwa uhlobo iType II Diabetes, hhayi iType I. I Type I Diabetes yilena eqhamuka nje isifuna ujovwe zibekwa nje njengoba kwenzeka kulabo abancane)Empeleni ayikusizi ngalutho uma izinombolo zikhomba amanani amahle kuwe, mangithi nje ziyakuhlomekisa kakhulu ukube kuya ngami ngabe siyayeka ukusebenzisa le ndlela.Ngiyacabanga ukuthi baningi asebezibuza beziphendula bethi uthini udokotela namhlanje? Ngiyaphinda, angiphuphi emini, ngithi le ndlela esibheka ngayo ubuningi bukashukela egazini ngokucofa sifake ithonsi emshinini yiyona ebhebhethekisa izifo eziningi kuhlanganisa nezikashukela, ukube bengisemandleni ngabe ngithi ayiyekwe.Ngikhuluma ngokubhebhethekisa izifo zohlangothi, umfutho ophezulu wegazi, ukungaboni emehlweni, ukufa kwezinso, ukushaywa yinhliziyo, amafutha awushevu ahlala egazini, izifo zokudungeka komqondo, amakhanda angapheli, umhlume, izifo zokuwa nomdlavuza uqobo.Emizimbeni yethu sonke kunendlala elawula ushukela nokusebenza komzimba uwonke nje, le ndlala enkulukazi kuthiwa yi- insulin. Wonke umuntu kumele abe nenani lale ndlala elisezingeni elamukelekile, uma leli zinga lingalawuleki umzimba ungaba buthaka kabi ezingxenyeni eziningi zawo. Isibonelo le ndlala uma inyukile umzimba uvele ukhiqize amafutha esibindini, adlule lapho abe kusinyaka, esiswini nasezicutshini. Ngaphandle nje kwalokho muningi umonakalo oba khona ngenxa yokwenyuka kwale ndlala egazini.Ucwaningo  olwenziwayo noselwenziwa lucacisa bha ukuthi kuthatha iminyakana elishumi nangaphezudlwana le ndlala yenyukile ngaphambi kokuthi ushukela uzibonakalise egazini. Esinye sezizathu ezibhubhisayo ukuthi ngesikhathi kwenyuka egazini le ndlala esiyibiza nge-insulin vele kusuke emithanjeni yegazi sekunobuthi obuyingozi obugcina sebudale isifo sohlangothi, ukuhlaselwa kwenhliziyo nezinye izinkinga eziningi. Umbuzo uthi yini eyenza nesiphoqa ukuthi silinde iminyaka kodwa sesiqalile isifo sikashukela ukwenza esidume ngakho ngaphakathi emzimbeni? Impendulo yalo mbuzo ithi ushukela lona esiwukalayo usuke ungakabonakali okanye ungakanyuki ngokwanele egazini ukuze le ndlela esiwuhlola ngayo ikwazi ukuwubamba?Olandelayo umbuzo uthi kuyasisiza yini ukulinda iminyaka ube ushukela usukhombisile ukungalawuleki ngaphakathi emizimbeni yethu? Impendulo: yiyo le nto ebhubhisa isizwe ngesifo sikashukela ngoba silinda isikhathi eside ube ushukela ungayekile ukusibulala ngaphakathi.Omunye angabuza athi: kungasisiza kangakanani isizwe ukusheshe sisukumele isifo sikashukela ngalesi sikhathi sisaqala?• Ukushesha sibanjwe sisavela isifo sikashukela kungaholela ekushesheni ukuqala ukusilawula isifo singakalawuli wena.• Ekulawuleni isifo sikashukela njengoba singumbulalazwe ungakwaziukungayisebenzisi imishanguzo lena ejwayelekile kuphela kodwa ulawule ukudla okudlayo.• Awucabange sesikwazi ukungayisebenzisi le mishanguzo kashukela, sesikwazi ukuzivikela siphinde siwushaye ngesithende uma kungukuthi bese uqalile.• Isizwe semikhaba siyophela sibe yinto yayizolo ngoba ukushintsha indlela yokudla kuyoletha izinguquko ezinkulu emzimbeni.• Izinga lezifo zohlangothi liyokwehla, ukuhlaselwa yinhliziyo kuyokwehla, kuphele ngamakhanda angaqondakali imvelaphi yawo, kunciphe isibalo sabantu bakithi abagcina benqanyulwe imilenze, izifo zomfutho ophezulu wegazi ziyokwehla, kuyokwehla nesibalo sabantu abayoba nenkinga yamafutha i-cholestorol egazini, kuningi nje engingakubala.• Awucabange nje sesikwazi ukwehlisa isibalo sabantu abanenkinga yezinso neyamehlo, ogogo nomkhulu sebengakhulumi ngongwengwezi okufanele lwengulwe?Konke lokhu nokuningi kungenzeka  uma nje singasintsha indlela yokubheka ushukela egazini sisebenzise ukuthatha igazi emuva kokudla siyobheka i-insulin siyeke ukucofa sithathe ithonsi legazi ngoba sibheka ushukela egazini ngenhloso yokuhlonza lesi sifo esibulala izwe. Le ndlela ayisisebenzeli kumele siyishintshe.Iqiniso lithi ngesikhathi ushukela usubonakala egazini usuke usuneminyaka eyishumi nangaphezulu unalesi sifo sikashukela, ngaphakathi usuqalile ushukela ukulimaza imithambo, izinso, amehlo nezinye  izindawo eziningi.Njengoba ngichazile yi Type II Diabetes esikhuluma ngayo, hhayi iType I.Mpilonhle Mpilonde!!Wonke umuntu engikhuluma naye unengebhe ngesifo esibulala sithikameze ukusebenza komqondo. Ukuba nomqondo ongasasebenzi kahle kubuhlungu kakhulu kubantu osuke usuhlezi nabo ngoba kumele kube yibo abakusekelayo kukho konke okwenzayo nongasakwazi ukukwenza ngendlela eyiyo. Lesi sifo esijwayele ukubizwa ngokuthi ukudideka emqondweni uma sisaqala sigcina sekuyi-Dementia. Kuleli zinga lokugcina sijwayele ukuzwa kuthiwa usibanibani une-Alzheimers, olunye uhlobo yi-Lewy Body Dementia. Phela i-Lewy Body Dementia yilena ebulale uClive Barker obedume ebholeni lezinyawo. Lesi sifo sihlasela singakhethi bulili kodwa sithanda ukuwela kakhulu kwabesimame, izincithabuchopho kokunye ziyaye zikulumbanise lokhu nokwehla kwe-estrogen ngesikhathi kuqala ukuphela kwesikhathi sokuya ezinsukwini zinyanga zonke kowesimame. Isizathu salokhu sithi ngaphambi kokuphela kwesikhathi kowesimame i- estrogen isuke isebenza ukuvimbela i- acid okuthiwa yi-uric acid lena ephehla isifo sobhozo, idolo nezihlakala okuthiwa i-gout ukuthi ingahlaseli owesifazane kodwa inele ingehla emazingeni kuleyo minyaka ivele inyuke ngamandla i uric acid bese ziqala izinhlungu ukubaququda. Okunye okubalulekile okwenziwa yile acid ukuphehla ushukela lona okuthiwa yi-fructose, lo shukela yiwona ngqo odala ukuthikamezeka komqondo. Ikakhulu lesi sifo sidlanga eminyakeni esuka ku-60 kuya phezulu, kokunye  singaqala ngaphansana kwalokho. Empeleni ucwaningo lwakamuva lukubeka kucace ukuthi siyakwazi ukuzibonakalisa naseminyakeni engaphansana kuka-40, futhi lolu cwaningo luyasho ukuthi uma singaqinisa ekusisiphuleni lapha ekuqaleni lesi sifo eminyakeni engengakanani ngabe sekuyisifo esingasaziwa.Ngikhuluma ngani uma sikhuluma ngomqondo osuthikamezekile? Mhlawumbe okuzosiza kangcono ukubuza umbuzo othi siqala kanjani lesi sifo esibuhlungu kangaka?Esesimphethe:Imbangela enkulu yalesi sifo ushukela, ushukela, ushukela. Ushukela osesiyingini, kulandele ukudla okunesitashi esiningi njengalokhu:Okunye okuyimbangela usawotii ikakhulu esiwuthola okudleni okuphehliwe(ultra processed foods). Lo sawoti uyakwazi ukungena ngaphakathi ebuchosheni ngobuningi ufike uphoqe ukushintsha okusashukela i-glucose ibe i-fructose, le fructose iyona esithi ingujikelele kulokhu kugula ngomqondo.Abanye bazibuza ukuthi kwenzekani kulesi sifo?
