Ngicela ukuchaza kafishane ngithi:Ushevu owushukela esiwuthola emajusini, eziphuzweni ezihlohlozayo, ko-ice cream ungena ngaphakathi ufike ebuchosheni wenze: Izakhi zobuchopho zamandla zingasebenzi, bese umzimba uphelelwa ngamandla.Kubalulekile sikhumbuzane ukuthi lesi simo siyelapheka siphele nya.Kudingeka ogulayo simlalise esibhedlela selaphe amafutha esibindini, i-uric acid esebuchosheni, sishintshe ukudla sikhiphe konke okunoshukela ukuze sinciphise i-fructose okuyiyona esuke isidlangile isishintshe konke ngaphakathi ebuchosheni.Kubalulekile ukuchaza ukuthi abantu abaphathwa yiCovid-19 basengozini enkudlwana yokungenwa yilesi sifo ngenxa yamakhemikhali adalekayo nenkungu eyaba sebuchosheni ngesikhathi unalesi sifo.Ngiyaphinda ngithi umqondo osuthikamezekile uyelapheka, kodwa kuhle ukuzivikela kulesi sifo usheshe welashwe ngoba siyabulala.Mpilonde!!EQINISWENI asikho isigaba sokukhula komuntu lapho esiyaye sithi khona usibanibani hhayi usengahamba emhlabeni, noma-ke nje iningi livamise ukuthi akwethusi kakhulu ukuhamba komuntu osekhulile ngokweminyaka.Kuyakhathaza ukubona abantu beshona bebancane, kuphinde kudide kakhulu uma kungabantu abazikhathazayo ngokugcina imizimba yabo ilolongekile. Abantu abazivocavocayo bayashona ngapha nangapha besebancane ngenxa yesifo senhliziyo.Ezikhathini eziningi ivele ijike ibe ngumqwayiba, emuva kwalokho isizoshaya umklamo omusha ongumgxobanyamo, agcine eshonile lowo ohlabekile. Ziningi iziqubu lapho uzwe kuthiwe lowo mfanyana sewashona, kokunye athathwe yikho ukufa esenkundleni edlala noma ezilolonga, qimu phansi, akhihlize amagwebu, akweqe amehlo, hhawu sekumenele.Abasakhumbulayo bazokhumbula ngomunye unyaka esinye isilomo somdlali webhola salapha e-Afrka siwa enkundleni, siqimuzeka phansi. Kunesifo senhliziyo esingumnqamulajuqu esihlasela ikakhulu abasebancane.Yize ngokobulili lesi sifo senhliziyo sihlasela ngokungakhethi kodwa izembe ligawula litshekele ngapha kwabesilisa kakhulu. Inhliziyo yakheke ngezicubu ezilekanyene, esinye phezu kwesinye zaze zaba ntathu.Kulesi sifo isicubu esilele isibili, sivele sigile igoda lokushintsha njengoba sengike ngakhuluma ngenhla, ngathi isicubu sishintshasibe ngamafutha omileyo abe ngumqwayiba. Lolu shintsho lwenza kushitshe ukushaya kwenhliziyo, ivele inhlanhlathe ihambe lena lapho ingadalelwe ukuhamba khona. Umzimba uvele ukhathale ube yinto ethi lala, ungakwazi ukwenza obujwayele ukukwenza.Omunye mhlawumbe angabuza ukuthi yini imbangela yokuthi uma ingxenye yenhliziyo isiwumqwayiba yenza ohlabekile ashone ngokushesha?Asikhumbule ukuthi omunye wemisebenzi yenhliziyo wukufingqana ikhiphe igazi elingaya emaphashini, okanye liye emzimbeni. Uma isicubu sayo sesingumqwayiba kusho ukungqangqazela, igcine isihluleka wukufingqana ikhiphe igazi noma ilamukele njengokusebenza kwayo.Esikugcizelela namhlanje wukuthi inhliziyo enjena ibanga ukwehluleka ukuthi ikhiphe igazi ngenxa yokulahla kwayo umkhondo igcine isiphumile esipolweni. Igazi okumele likhishwe okanye lamukelwe lizoncipha kakhulu,bese eyawa ashone lowo ohlabekile.Lokhu kungenzeka, ikakhulu umaephakamisa izwi ethetha, ecasukile, ehamba okanye uma esemdlalweni. Baningi abantu abasebancane asebehambe emhlabeni ngokuzuma okukhulu, okushiya abasondele nabo bekhungathekile, bezibuza ukuthi kwenzekeni, yini esiyonile, esemncane kangaka pho?Angisengi esezixegisile umangithi abaningi bagcina bebhenele ekuhambeni beyofuna umhlolo, okulandela lapho wukuxabana okujulile emndenini. Kubuhlungu ukunukwa ungazi lutho, umndeni ukuphendukele uzithole usuwedwa kade kunemfudumalo, kumnandi nihlezi nisingethene.Ngiyafisa ukusika elijikayo ngezimpawu zalesi simo nanxa zingakacaciswa kahle kodwa masizilindele lezi ezilandelayo: Inhliziyo eshaya ngendlela engajwayelekile kade uyazi ishaya kahle usuzoyizwa ithi ‘gidigidi’ ushaywe wuvalo, kuphele amandla isiyezi esingajwayelekile, kuthi ebuncaneni usephelelwa wumuzwa wocansi, akusafikeki kuvuthondaba ungowesifazane. Lokhu kuhambisane nokusuza okungamandla ebuncaneni nokukhohlwa. Kowesilisa omncane induku isheshe ichithe ocansini, iwe iphakathi, ingaqini, inciphe,ube “nguqhwasha” umncane - uveleukwazi ukugcina emzuliswaneniowodwa nje kuphela.Kubalulekile ukuqaphelisisa ukuthi izimpawu ezinye zisazovela ngenxa yocwaningo olunhlobonhlobo oluqhubekayo. Ngiguqa ngawo womabili, ngithi uma unalezi izimpawu, ikakhulu uma umncane sondela kudokotela ozokwazi ukukusiza, ungalindi emathonsi abanzi. Yimpilo yakho!Mpilonde!!!UKUBA nezempilo ezehlukene kabili kuholele ekutheni iNingizimu Afrika ibe semuva uma kukleliswa amazwe enza kahle kwezempilo.IWorld Population Review, Best Health Care Sytem 2023, ebibheka ezempilo emazweni omhlaba muva nje, ibeke iNingizimu Afrika kunombolo 87 okuyenza ikuthi ibe ngemuva kwamazwe okwaziwayo ukuthi adonsa kanzima kwezempilo afana neBotswana, iVietnam, Sri Lanka, iMongolia nePhilippines.Ngesikhathi kuhlaziywa ezempilo emazweni omhlaba, bekungabhekwa kakhulu ukushoda kwabasebenzi, izinsiza okuyizinto ezijwayele ukushoda kuleli kodwa kuthiwe into eyenza ukuthi ibekwe kule nombolo ebekwe kuyo ukuthi inemikhakha emibili yempilo, ozimele nokahulumeni okwenza ukuthi ukunakekelwa kwabantu kwezempilo kungalingani. Abampofu balashwa ezikhungweni zezempilo zikahulumeni, abahola kangcono balashwa ezikhungweni zezempilo ezizimele.Uhlelo lokunakekelwa kwezempilo lukahulumeni lwaseNingizimu Afrika luwumgogodla, lusiza cishe u-80% wezakhamuzi zalo ezicishe zibe ngu-60 million. U-80% wodokotela bakuleli basebenza ohlelweni oluzimele, okushiya uhlelo lukahulumeni lushoda kakhulu ngezinsizakusebenza futhi lusilele emuva.Izinhlelo zokunakekelwa kwezempilo emhlabeni wonke zibonakale zisebenza kahle kwamanye amazwe emizameni yawo yokuqeda ukwehlukana kwezinhlelo zokwelapha. UMnyango wezeMpilo wakuleli  uhlose ukulinganisa iziguli ngohlelo lwayo oluhlongozwayo lweNational Health Insurance (NHI).Isikhulu esiphezulu se-Innovative Pharmaceutical Association South Africa (IPASA), uMnuz Bada Pharasi, sithe esinye sezibonelo zalolu hlelo wuhlelo lwaseRwanda, i-Universal Health Coverage (UHC), olusetshenziswa wu-90% wabantu baseRwanda.“IRwanda yenyuse inombolo yezikhungo zezempilo zikahulumeni zisuka ku-1 036 ngo-2013 zafinyelela ku1 457 ngo-2020, okuholele ekutheni iningi lomphakathi likwazi ukufinyelela ezikhungweni zezempilo ebese ziseduze nomphakathi, kwehla nesikhathi esihlalwa yiziguli ezikhungweni uma ziyokwelashwa,” kusho uPharasi.Uthe okunye okwenziwe yileli lizwe ukuthi ngesikhathi lishintsha isimo sezempilo, litshale imali yokuthi kwakhiwe izikhungo zezempilo ezindaweni zasemakhaya lapho bezingekho khona. Kwehliswa nemali ekhokhwayo ukuze bonke abantu bakwazi ukuthola ukwelashwa. UPharasi uthe ukuze kuzuzwe inhloso yeNHI, uMnyango wezeMpilo uzodinga ukubukela kwiRwanda.Ucwaningo luphakamisa ukuthi ukulungiselela izibhedlela iNHI eNingizimu Afrika, kuzomele kube nemali ebekelwe ukuthenga izinsiza zobuchwepheshe, kwandiswe isibalo sabasebenzi, kuthuthukiswe ingqalasizinda nokutholakala kwemithi, abasebenzi bezempilo banikezwe ukuqeqeshwa okwanele, hhayi emikhakheni ethile kuphela.UCWANINGO olwenziwe uhlaka lwezempilo olubheka ukuthi ikhona yini imithi yokwelapha nemigomo ezikhungweni zezempilo zakuleli i-Stop Stockouts Project (SSP) luveza ukuthi ziyashoda izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni.Lolu cwaningo lwenziwe lwakhiwe yinhlangano yodokotela, i-Doctors Without Boarders, i-Rural Doctors Association of SA, i-Rural Health Advocacy Project, i-Section 27 ne-Treatment Action  ngokubambisana ne-Ritshize okuyinhlangano eyakhiwe yizinhlangano ezibhekelele i-HIV ne-TB  ezehlukene. Luveze ukuthi ngo-Ephreli 2022 kuya kuJuni 2023, abanye abantu besifazane ababeye ezikhungweni zezempilo KwaZulu-Natal, e-Eastern Cape  naseNorth West, babuyele emakhaya belambatha bengazitholanga izinsiza abazifunayo.Lolu cwaningo olusanda kukhishwa yi-Ritshize lubizwa ngokuthi Ukusatshalaliswa kwezinsiza zokuhlela umndeni- ukuphela kwesitoko nezizathu zako.  Lukhishwe ngoLwesihlanu okuhambisana nokuphela kwenyanga yabantu besifazane ebiphela ngempelasonto. Ocwaningweni kuveza izinselelo ezibhekana nabantu besifazane uma beyofuna izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni ukuze bazivikele ekutheni bakhulelwe bengahlelile. Ngokwalolu cwaningo bonke abesifazane abebeyingxenye yocwaningo bekuke kwenzeke bangazitholi izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni ebebezidinga emitholampilo abebeye kuyo ngesikhathi.“Esikutholile wukuthi uhlelo lokuthengwa kwempahla kuzwelonke aluhlelekile, luholela ekutheni kube nokushoda kwezinsiza zokuhlela umndeni nokuphela kwesitokwe. Ezingeni lezifundazwe izimbangela zokuphela kwesitokwe zibandakanya ukucishiswa kwesabelomali nokungalawulwa ngendlela kwesitoko," kubhalwe kanjeni. UNkk Tendai Mafuma ongumcwaningi kwi-Section 27, uthe imiphumela yalo idala ukukhathazeka. “Kuyakhathaza ukuthi uye emtholampilo ubuye ungakutholanga obukudinga. Okunye okusikhathazayo ukuthi abanye bebeze baphoqeleke ukuthi bazithenge izinsiza abebezidinga esikhundleni sokuzithola mahhala esikhungweni sikahulumeni,” kuchaza uNkk Mafuma. Kubuye kwavele ukuthi abasebenzi bezempilo bayazama ukuthi iziguli zingabuyeli emakhaya zilambatha ngokuthi bazinike ezinye izinsiza ezisuke zikhona esitokweni noma kungezona iziguli ezizisebenzisayo noma zizidlulisele ezikhungweni ezinesitokwe.Okunye okuvezwe ilolu cwaningo ukuthi kuyenzeka usizo lokuhushula isisu nalo lungatholakali ngesikhathi.Ucwaningo olushicilelwe nyakenye ebelubheka ukutholakala kwezinsiza zokuhlela umndeni phakathi kuka-Ephreli 2021 kuya kuJuni 2022, luveze ukuthi izinsiza ezivame ukushoda kuba amaphilisi aphuzwayo nemijovo. Nakulo nyaka kuvele ukuthi izona lezi zinsiza abebeyingxenye yocwaningo ababike ukuthi bekubuyekwenzeke bangazitholi ezikhungweni abavame ukuya kuzo. UMASIPALA weTheku unxusa abantu abahlala kuleli dolobha ukuthi uma kwenzeka belunywa yizinja baphuthume emitholampilo ukuze bathole ukwelashwa.Okhulumela lo masipala, uMnuz Msawakhe Mayisela, uthe kule nyanga kubikwe izigameko ezimbili zabantu abalunywe yizinja ezinamarabi kuleli dolobha. Ziyisikhombisa izigameko esezibikiwe kusukela ngoJanuwari."Siyabanxusa abanikazi bezinja ezingagonyiwe ukuthi bagome izinja ukuze kuvikelwe ukusabalala kwalesi sifo," kusho yena.UMayisela uthe izindawo okuke kwabikwa kuzo izigameko zamarabi kule ndawo ise-Adams, Nsimbini, Mbumbulu, Ngonyameni, Clare Estate, KwaDabeka, eSt Wendolins naseNanda.Usho kanjena uMasipala weTheku nje, isikhungo esibhekelele izifo ezithathelanayo, iNational Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD), sithe zingu-17 izigameko zamarabi adluliselwe yizilwane kubantu   ezibikiwe kuleli kusukela kuqale unyaka.Lesi sikhungo sithi lesi sibalo esiphezulu kunazo zonke esezike zabikwa kusukela ngo-2016.Lesi sifo sitholakala ezilwaneni zasekhaya ezifana namakati nezinja, kubantu sidluliseleka ngokuthi umuntu alunywe yinja noma ikati elinaso. Ongoti bezempilo bathi ubungozi buba ngcono uma umuntu esheshe waya emtholampilo ngemuva kokulunywa yinja.Lesi sikhungo sithe e-Eastern Cape, eNelson Mandela Bay naseBuffalo City zingaphezulu kuka-400 izigameko zamarabi ezilwaneni ezibikwe kulezi zifunda kulo nyaka.Akekho ongaphikisana nokuthi isifo sikashukela singumbulalazwe uqobo lapha kwelakithi eNingizimuu Afrika. Ngokwezibalo isifo sikashukela silele isibili ohlwini lwezifo zokuqala eziyishumi ezibulalayo kwelakithi, bese siba ngesesishiyagalolunye ezibalweni zezifo ezibulalayo emhlabeni wonke jikelele. Lapha kwelakithi isifo iTB sihamba phambili kwezibulalayo, bese kuthi emhlabeni wonke jikelele kubhongoza phambili ukuhlaselwa yisifo senhliziyo. Uma ucubungula lokhu nje kukodwa, kuyacaca ukuthi isifo sikashukela siwumthwalo osemahlombe ethu njengesizwe, size siyothwalisa kanzima uhulumeni ophethe izwe.Ushukela emzimbeni ulawulwa yingxenye okuthiwa ngusinyaka. Usinyaka sike sakhuluma ngawo engosini edlule nakuba ingosi yayingaqondene ngqo noshukela, esasikhuluma ngakho kwakungubuhlungu nokungabi mnandi kwesisu. Usinyaka wakheke waba nezinyandana eziyiminyango yokukwazi ukuzwa uma ushukela usumningi egazini bese ushukela ungeniswa ngaphakathi kuwo usinyaka uyolawulwa ngosiko lwakhona. Inkinga idaleka uma usinyaka lona esehluleka ukuzwa ukunyuka kukashukela egazini okusho ukuthi usinyaka ungasakwazi ukungenisa ushukela ngaphakathi kuwo uyolawulwa. Indlela yokulawulwa ngaphakathi kusinyaka ihlanganisa imigudu ngemigudu yama-protein anhlobonhlobo. La ma-protein kwesinye isikhathi kuyenzeka azwele kuze kweqe angabe esafuna ukwenza lutho oluya phambili.Ushukela uma usugabadela emzimbeni udala:Ukungaboni uphunduleke emehlweniIsifo sohlangothi i-strokeIsifo sokuhlaselwa yinhliziyoUkuvuvukala kwenhliziyo igcwale amanzi, kulimale kuphunduleke izinsoUbuhlungu bezinyawo obunhlobonhlobo, zishise, zihlatshwe izinaliti, zivuvukale, zebuze, zibe nezilonda ezingapheli abanye baze banqunywe amalungu ezinyawo nemilenzeUmhlume, okuhambisana nenduku eyimvithi, engavuki ewela phakathi, isheshe ichithe ingafuni nje ukuphinde ivuke. Abanye baqumbelana, bangayi kozikhulula, basuze into engapheli, iqolo libe buhlungu ingathi linemboboUkufa kwezinso ugcine usufakwe ohlelweni lokuhlanza izinso ngemishiniUmphako engiwuphethe namhlanje ukhuluma ngokuthi isifo sikashukela sesisimbi sinjena; siyelapheka siphele uphumule emaphilisini nasemijoveni kulabo asebejova. Kuneziguli esizelaphile zaphuma emishanguzweni kashukela, zaphila impilo ngaphandle kwamaphilisi nemijovo.Ezigulini esesizelaphile impumelelo yabasindile iqala kwabayisikhombisa kwabayishumi esithi siyakwazi ukubelapha siphele lesi sifo. Okusho ukuthi uma sineziguli eziyishumi, abayisikhombisa babo bayasinda, bese kusala le ngxenyana yeziguli ezintathu, engithi basaphazanyiswa yila ma-protein asevele atshodayo angabe esafuna ukunyakaza ashintshe aphinde angenise ushukela kusinyaka ukuze amazinga awo aphinde alawuleke ngendlela yakhona.Esikwenzayo sithatha umuntu ophila ngokudla amaphilisi kashukela ukuwulawula, thina simfaka ohlelweni lwezinsuku ezinhlanu zokukhipha udoti ngaphakathi ngale yondlela sifaka usinyaka emlalazini, siwulolela ukuthi uphinde usebenze ukwazi ukulawula ushukela ngendlela ejwayelekile.Empeleni kade saqala senza lo msebenzi kodwa sathi asime ukukhuluma ngawo kuze kube izinombolo zabantu asebesindile ziyazikhulumela zona. Sikulelo zinga namhlanje!Ake sibuyele kulabo abasafisa ukuqhubeka nokudla amaphilisi abo baphinde bajove. Ekusebenzeni kwami njengodokotela ngithole ukuthi abantu abaningi ababulawa yilesi sifo, bahamba emhlabeni lapho amazinga kashukela engasalawuleki avele anyuke abe phezulu kakhulu angafuni ukwehla, okanye avele ehle abe phansi kakhulu angafuni ukwenyuka. Abanye bagcina sebengene kwi ‘khoma’ uma sebeguduza kulezo zimo. Kukhona nesimo esibucayi lapho ogulayo avele amaswayi aphunduleke egazini, igazi lishintshe libe muncu, ogulayo aphefumule kanzima into emuncu, aphelelwe amandla; isimo sibe sibi kakhulu. Kuzo zonke lezi zimo ngifisa ukugcizelela ukubaluleka kokugcina amaswayi ebhalansile egazini. Ngiphinde ngigcizelele ukubaluleka kokudla izidlo eziyikho, sibalekele nemikhuba esisondeza kushukela ongalawuleki. Zingane zakwethu kafishane ngichaza ukuthi:Masiyeke ukudla izinto kwenye ingosi esathi ‘zilungiselelwe’ (processed) ngoba ziyasibulala, zidala ushukela, imidlavuza, nezinye izifo. Lapha sathi: amabhega, pholoni, viyena, inyama ebomvu eyosiwe, pizza, amarashiyeni nokunye.Okungenani wena osudla amaphilisi nemijovo kashukela, thola i-drip kanye ngenyanga kudokotela wakho okanye ekiliniki. Le drip izokusiza ekubhalanseni itswayi egazini. Lokhu ukwenza ngaphezu kokuphuza amanzi lokhu okuhlale kucelwa njalo.Ngicela ukugcizelela bafowethu nodadewethu ukuthi asiyeke, sigcine namhlanje uma besikwenza ukudla sekuleyithi. Ngisho ukuthi ebusuku umuntu useyadla, phela ngalesi sikhathi umzimba usuke usulele, nosinyaka lowo esephumule. Uma wena usudla ngalesi sikhathi zibuze ukuthi loshukela owufaka egazini uzolawula ngubani ngoba phela sekulelwe layikhaya? Okuzolandela ukungenwa yisifo sikashukela, kade uziphilela nje. Asiyeke ukudla ebusuku, uma kuzokuphoqa ukuthi udle sekuhlwile: phela yenza uhlelo lokuthi udle ngesikhathi esifanele ngoba uzongenwa izifo ezingumbulalazwe.Ekugcineni sithi isifo sikashukela siyelapheka, uphume uphele emaphilisini nasemijoveni!Mpilonde!ININGIZIMU Afrika isemazweni angu-30 ahamba phambili ngokuba nabantu abaningi abahaqwe isifo sofuba iTB yize lesi sifo selapheka.Ziningi izinhlelo zokulwa nokusabalala kwalesi sifo esibulala abantu ababalelwa ku-54 000 kuleli ngonyaka ngokombiko okhishwe iGlobal TB report nyakenye, okukhathaza ongoti nezincithabuchopho ezisemkhakheni wezempilo.Njalo ngonyaka labo ngoti, abezempilo izinhlangano ezisiza emikhankasweni yokulwa nalesi sifo  nososayensi bakuleli baba nengqungquthela lapho bedingida khona ngalesi sifo.Kudingidwa ngezindlela ezintsha zokwelapha lesi sifo ezihambisana nemigomo ebekwe inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), izinselelo eziholela ekutheni lesi sifo silokhu sisabalala nokunye.Kulo nyaka le ngqungquthela yesishiyagalombili, i8th SA TB Conference, izoba seThekwini. Izoqala namhlanje iphele ngoLwesihlanu. Umongo walo nyaka uthi “sisheshisa inqubekela phambili yokuqeda i-TB  phecelezi Accelerating progress to end TB" .Usihlalo wengqungquthela uSolwazi  Sizulu Moyo, uthe kule ngqungquthela bahlose ukuthi bakhombise ukuzinikela okuletha ithemba elisha ekuqedeni izifo ezifana neTB neHIV nezinye izifo ezingathathelani  ezihambisana nalesi sifo." Le ngqungquthela yenzeka ngesikhathi esiyingqophamlando eNingizimu Afrika, njengoba u-2024 kuwunyaka lapho iNingizimu Afrika igubha iminyaka engu-30 yentando yabantu. Okuphawulekayo ukuthi ingqungquthela izokwenzeka ngesikhathi  sokushintsha kwemithetho nemigomo elawula ezempilo kuleli  njengoba iNingizimu Afrika isezinhlelweni zokuqala umshwalensi wezempilo obhekele bonke abantu, ukuze kuphuculwe indlela yokwelashwa kwabantu. Inhloso ukuthuthukisa ezempilo nokususa imigoqo ebikhona phambilini. Kithina kuvula  ithuba elihle lokuthi sibhekane nalesi sifo ngokuthi sivule inkundla yokuthi sibonisane ngalesi sifo,"  kusho uSolwazi Moyo.“UMSEBENZI owenzayo akungabi yiwona ocacisa ukuthi usizo lwezempilo uzoluthola kuphi, kumele zonke iziguli zithole usizo lwezempilo olulinganayo.”Lokhu kushiwo nguDkt Joe Kutzin wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ngesikhathi kugujwa usuku i-International Universal Health Coverage Day, izolo. Umhlangano wokubheka izinhlelo zokuzama ukuqeda igebe elikhona phakathi kwabampofu nabacebile kwezempilo ububanjelwe kuleli.UDkt Kutzin uthe emazweni amaningi uma umpofu awukwazi ukuthola ezempilo ezisezingeni ngoba kunezinhlelo eziningi ezihlelelwe abanemali, abampofu bagcina bengalutholanga usizo.Uthe kudingeka ukuthi kutshalwe imali ohlelweni olulungele bonke abantu ukuze kusizakale wonke umuntu.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe kuleli njengakwamanye amazwe kunezinhlelo ezimbili zezempilo, olukahulumeni noluzimele, lapho kusizakala khona abanemali."Sivumele ukuthi ezempilo zizimele okwenza ukuthi izinsiza ezikhona ezingenele singakwazi ukuzisebenzisa sonke. Kuleli uma ufuna ukubonwa ngudokotela owungoti wesifo esithile, kumele uze uye esibhedlela noma kudokotela ozimele. Lo mkhakha wabazimele kunzima satshe ukuwulawula, uthola ukuthi isiguli simane sazihambela saya kungoti ngaphandle kokudluliselwa ngudokotela ojwayelekile ngoba kuzokhokha i-medical aid. “Nayo i-medical aid ayibuzi mibuzo ngokuthi kungani lesi siguli singayanga kofuna usizo kudokotela ojwayelekile kuqala. “Yona le medical aid ngemuva kwezinyangana uzwa kuthiwa isiphelile, isiguli sekumele siye kuhulumeni. Le nto yenza ukuthi sibone ukuthi kufanele ezempilo zihlanganiswe ukuze kungabi khona abantu abazosala ngaphandle okuhambisana nesibophezelo samazwe ahlangene, iSustainable Development Goals (SDG) ka-2030," kusho uPhaahla.Uthe iNingizimu Afrika isiqalile ukulungisa leli phutha ngokuthi kube nomshuwalense wezempilo, iNational Health Insurance (NHI), esahlongozwa."Ukuqalwa kwalolu hlelo kuphazamisekile ngenxa yokuthi kuthe kusakhishwe umthethosivinyo ngawo ukuthi abantu abaphawule, kwahlasela ubhubhane lweCovid-19 kodwa kubuye kwabuyelwa ekusetshenzweni kwalo mthethosivivinyo kubhekwa izinto zomthetho. Okuyinkinga ukuthi yize lolu hlelo lungakaqali ukusebenza, sekunezinkampani esezifake umnyango enkantolo. “Lokho kwenziwa ukuthi izinkampani ezingabanikazi bezibhedlela ezizimele zicebile, ngeke zivume ukuhlwithwa iqatha emlonyeni kalula, zizozama konke okusemandleni ukuze zizuze," kusho uPhaahla.Uthe uhlelo lwezempilo olubhekelele bonke abantu akusho ukuthi lufuna ukuthi abantu bagcwale ezikhungweni zezempilo kodwa lufuna abantu baphile okusho ukuthi kumele kube nohlelo lokulawulwa kwezifo, iPrimary Health Care olusebenza kahle.UDkt Kenny Jacobs, usihlalo wekomiti lezempilo ePhalamende lakuleli, uthe sekuphele iminyaka emithathu umthethosivivinyo weNHI uphazamiseka kanti lolu hlelo lwezempilo luzosiza ekutheni bonke abantu bakwazi ukuthola ezempilo ezisezingeni elifanele kungabhekwa ukuthi bampofu noma bacebile.UZOKWEHLA umthwalo kubantu baseNingizimu Afrika abadinga ukuhlolwa iCovid-19 njengoba iCompetition Commision imemezele ukuthi amaCovid-PCR Test asezobiza uR500 esuka kuR850.Okwamanje izinkampani ezisayine isivumelwano neCompetition Commission yiLancet ne-Ampath.UKhomishana weCompetition Commission, uMnuz Tembinkosi Bonakele ucele wonke ama-laboratory ahlola abantu iCovid-19 ukuba angakhokhisi abantu imali engaphezu kukaR500.“Siqale uphenyo emuva kokuthola izikhalo kubantu akade bekhala ngokuthi bakhokhiswa imali enkulu ema-laboratory ukuhlola iCovid-19. Siye sakwazi ukwenza isivumelwano ne-Ampath neLancet sokuthi ngeke besakhokhisa abantu uR850 kodwa bazobakhokhisa uR500 kusukela namhlanje (ngeSonto 12/12/2021),” kusho uBonakele.Uthe enye inkampani akade beyiphenya iPathcare ayivumanga ukuba yingxenye yesivumelwano sokwehlisa imali eyikhokhisa abantu ngokubahlola iCovid-19.Le nkampani uBonakele uthe bazoxoxisana nayo baze bathathe izinyathelo zomthetho uma kuphoqa.Ucele nama-laboratory amancane angeyona ingxenye yesivumelwano sabo ukuba angakhokhisi abantu imali engaphezu kukaR500.Uveze ukuthi ekuqaleni ukuhlola iCovid-19 bekubiza uR1 400 kodwa emuva kokungenelela kukahulumeni nabo beyiCompetition Commission kwehla kwaba wuR850. Emuva kwalokho baye baphenya ngoba bebona ukuthi uR850 mkhulu bafinyelela kulesi sivumelwano sikaR500.Uthe isimo bazosiqapha ngeso lokhozi ukuthi ngeke bakwazi yini ukucela lezi zinkampani ukuba ziyehlise imali ngoba bazobheka ukuthi kwenzekani njalo emuva kwezinyanga ezintathu.Uphethe ngokuthi kubalulekile ukuthi abantu bangakhokhiswa imali emba eqolo ngoba ukuhlola iCovid-19 ngenye yezindlela zokulwa nokubhebhetheka kwalesi sifo.Uveze ukuthi ukunyuka kwezibalo zabangenwa yiCovid-19 kusho ukuthi baningi abazodinga ukuhlolwa ngakho imali akufanele imbe eqolo.Amalungu omphakathi akhokhiswa imali engaphezu kukaR500 ukuhlola iCovid-19 angathumela izikhalo kwiCompetition Commission ngokuvakashela u-www.compcom.co.za.UMNYANGO wezeMpilo kuleli uyakuphika ukuthi kukhona ukushoda kwenzinsiza zokuhlela umndeni ezikhungweni zezempilo zikahulumeni yize kunocwaningo olukhomba lokhu.Ucwaningo lusanda kukhishwa yiThe Stop Stockout okuwuhlelo olwenziwa yinhlangano yodokotela, iRural Doctors Association of South Africa (RDASA).UDkt Indira Govender, weRDASA, uthe ulwazi olukhomba ukuthi izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni ziyashoda luqoqwe ezikoleni zamabanga aphansi ezingu-400 zakuleli."Sithole ukuthi kushoda umjovo wokuvikela ukukhulelwa, iDepo. Lo mjovo unikezwa abesifazane njalo ngemuva kwezinyanga ezintathu. Abasebenzi bezempilo bebephoqeleka ukuthi banikeze abesifazane okunye kokuhlela umndeni okukhona. Ukwenza kanjalo kuphuca umuntu wesifazane ilungelo lokuzikhethela ukuthi umndeni ufuna ukuwuhlela ngani. Ukushintshisa umuntu wesifazane uthi akasebenzise lokho okukhona akuyona indlela ekahle ngoba nalokho okukhona kuzogcina kungasaneli," kusho yena.Uthe ngokuthola kwabo, kwaphela inkontileka yenkampani ebinikeza umnyango le mijovo ngo-2017, kwaqala lapho ukuba nokuphazamiseka kodwa umnyango, esitatimendeni osithumele, uthe awunalo ulwazi lokuthi kunokushoda kwezinsiza zokuhlela umndeni.UNksz Claire Waterhouse, wenhlangano yodokotela iDoctors Without Boarders, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba ethi ukukhuthazwa kwabesifazane ukuthi basebenzise ezinye izindlela zokuhlela umndeni, ezifana namakhondomu, kubeka abesifazane engcupheni yokuthi bakhulelwe ngoba abesifazane kumele babonisane namadoda kuqala ngodaba lokusetshenziswa kwekhondomu."Siyazi ukuthi eNingizimu Afrika kunezinga eliphezulu lodlame olubhekiswe kwabesifazane, ukubonisana ngodaba lwekhondomu kungenzeka kungabi lula," kusho uNksz Waterhouse.Le nhlangano beyenza ucwaningo ibheka ukushoda kwemithi eyehlukene kuleli okubalwa kuyo izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni, imishanguzo yesifo sofuba nezinsiza zokuhlola izifo ezifundazweni i-Eastern Cape, Free State, Gauteng, KwaZuluNatal, Limpopo, Mpumalanga naseNorth West.Kulolu cwaningo olwenziwe izinyanga ezintathu kukhulunywe neziguli ezingu-15 750.Kuvele ukuthi kunemithi eshodayo ezikhungweni zezempilo zikahulumeni kuyo okuhlanganisa nazo izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni.Kulolu cwaningo u-40% weziguli okukhulunywe nazo uveze ukuthi kushoda izinsiza zokuhlela umndeni, u-19% wathi awuyitholanga imithi noma azihlolwanga ngendlela obekumele zihlolwe ngayo, u-17% wathi awuyitholanga imigomo, u-16% waveza ukuthi awuyitholanga imishanguzo yengculazi noma uthole engaphelele ngesikhathi uyoyilanda ezikhungweni zezempilo.NJENGOBA isigoqwa inyanga yabantu besifazane, ongoti bezempilo bakhuthaza ukuthi abesifazane baqaphele bahlolwe izifo ezijwayele ukubahlasela.Umdlavuza webele ungumdlavuza ohamba phambili ohlasela abantu besifazane. Ongoti bezempilo bakhuthaza abantu besifazane abaneminyaka ewu-18 kuya phezulu ukuthi baqale ukuzihlola bona emakhaya ukuthi abanazo yini izigaxa abangazijwayele emabeleni abo.Abesifazane abeneminyaka engu-40 kumele baye kohlolwa ukuthi abanaso yini isimila emabeleni okwaziwa nge-mammogram njalo ngemuva kweminyaka emibili.Ingozi enkulu ngomdlavuza webele ukuthi uyadlondlobala uma iminyaka yowesifazane ikhula kodwa abanye abantu besifazane kuyenzeka bawuthole besebancane kunalokho.Ufuzo nalo luneqhaza ekubekeni engozini abesifazane abazalwa emindenini enomlando wabantu besifazane abanomdlavuza.Umdlavuza womlomo wesibelethoOngoti bathi kubalulekile ukuthi abesifazane bahlolwe ukuthi alukho yini ushintsho emlonyeni wesibeletho kusenesikhathi bathi lokho kuyasiza nasekutheni belapheke ngokushesha. I-pap smear esetshenziselwa ukuhlola ushintsho emlonyeni wesibeletho, iphinde ihlole ukuthi owesifazane akanayo yini i-human papillomavirus (HPV) okuyigciwane elidala izinhlobo eziningi zomdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho. Njengamanje usukhona umgomo ovikela amantombazane ukuthi angalitholi ligciwane le -HPV.HIVUcwaningo lukhombisa ukuthi abesifazane batheleleka kakhulu ngegciwane leHIV njenxa yokwakheka kwemizimba yabo, basengcupheni enkulu yokuthola leli gciwane.  Ongoti bathi ubungozi buqhutshwa ukuthi kusenokungalingani uma kubhekwa abesilisa nabesifazane. Abesifazane basahluleka ukuzithathela izinqumo mayelana nokuthi bafuna ukuthi kusetshenziswe izinsiza zokuzivikela uma kuyiwa ocansini. Bancoma ukuthi abantu besifazane bahlolwe i-HIV minyaka yonke.Ukudleka kwamathamboAbesifazane uma bekhula, amathambo abo ayadleka  futhi abe buthakathaka, okungadala ukuthi kube lula ukuthi akhumuzeke. Ngakho-ke ukuhlolwa kokuqina kwamathambo (i-DEXA scan) kuyanconywa kwabesifazane abaneminyaka engu-65 noma ngaphezulu.Umdlavuza wesikhumbaUmdlavuza wesikhumba udalwa ukukhula okungavamile kwamagqamuzana esikhumba (cells), ngokuvamile esikhumbeni esijwayele ukushiswa yilanga noma kungathiwa lokho akwenzeki njalo.  Abesifazane abanenqwaba yeziqu zoboya esikhunjeni noma izinguquko ezibonakalayo kumele bahlolwe ukuthi abanawo yini umdlavuza wesikhumba.Ukukhuluphala ngokweqile“Ngokocwaningo lwakamuva, cishe u-70% wabesifazane baseNingizimu Afrika ukhuluphele ngokweqile .Ongoti bancoma ukuthi abesifazane basebenzise i-Body Mass Indicator (BMI) ukuze bazihlole ukuthi isisindo somzimba wabo siyahambisana yini nobude babo.Ukukhuluphala ngokweqile kunomthelela ezifeni ezifana nesifo sikashukela, ukwehla nokwenyuka komfutho wegazi, ukuminyana kwemithambo ehambisa igazi enhliziyweni  ngakho abesifazane kumele uma bazi ukuthi bakhuluphele ngokweqile bahlolwe njalo ukuthi abanazo yini izifo ezihambisana nokukhuluphala ngokweqile.Bulelwa PayiINHLANGANO yezikole ezizimele zakuleli, i-Independent Schools Association in Southern Africa (Isasa), ifuna ukuthi uhlelo lokugonywa kwabafundi bamantombazane begomela isifo socansi esiphenduka sibe umdlavuza wesibeletho ngemuva kweminyaka ethile, iHuman papillomavirus (HPV), lusatshalaliswe nasezikoleni ezizimele.Njengamanje uhlelo lokugonywa kwabafundi bamantombazane aneminyaka ewu-9 kuya phezulu egonywelwa igciwane (HPV) kuleli lwenziwa uMnyango wezeMfundo eyisiSekelo ngokubambisana noMnyango wezeMpilo ezikoleni zikahulumeni kuphela futhi lumahhala.Umqondisi wale nhlangano, uMnuz Lebogang Montjane, uthe bafuna ukuthi uhlelo olufanayo lwenziwe ezikoleni ezizimele ngoba bayabona ukuthi luwusizo."Lo mgomo ezikoleni ezizimele ngeke ube mahhala, ungakhokhelwa  ukheshi ngabazali noma kukhokhe izikhwama zezempilo, ama-medical aid. Ezikoleni ezizimele eziningi kukhokhwa imali encane ngakho-ke azinazo izinsiza eziningi yingakho sithathe isinqumo sokuthi sikhulume nomnyango mayelana nokuthi kunganjani izinhlelo zezempilo ezikhona ezikoleni zikahulumeni zifakwe nasezikoleni ezizimele ezifisayo ukuba nazo lezi zinhlelo," kusho yena.Uhlelo lokugomela iHPV lwaqala ezikoleni zakuleli ngo-2014, kugonywa amantombazane aneminyaka ayisishiyagalolunye.Kuba imijovo emibili, owesibili ujovwa ngemuva kwezinyanga eziyisithupha umfundi egome ngowokuqala.Lolu hlelo beluhamba kahle luze lwaphazamiseka ngo-2021 ngenxa yokuthi ezinye izikole bezivaliwe ngenxa yeCovid-19, kwebezivuliwe  abafundi bebelova.USolwazi Lynette Denny, oyinhloko yophiko lwezifo zabesifazane eNyuvesi yaseCape Town, uthe ngalesi sikhathi seCovid kube khona ukuwungabaza umgomo ngoba kube nezinto eziningi ebezishiwo ngemigomo. “Umgomo weHPV uphephile, selokhu kwaqala ukugonywa ngawo azikho izinkinga ezibikiwe. Ucwaningo olwenziwe kamuva nje lukhombisa ukuthi ukugomela iHPV kwehlisa amathuba okuthi amagciwane ocansi angene kubantu abasha aphenduke abe umdlavuza wesibeletho okwenzeka uma leso sifo socansi singelashwanga. Umgomo wenza ukuthi leli gciwane lingahlali okuyinto ebiyenzeka eholela ekutheni ngemuva kweminyaka elinganiselwa kwengu-12 umuntu omusha abe nomdlavuza wesibeletho," kusho uSolwazi Denny.USolwazi Denny uthe phambilini imijovo yeHPV kwakuthiwe ayibe mithathu, owesithathu kwakungowokunikeza amandla, i-booster, kodwa kwabuye kwabonakala ukuthi isidingo salokho asikho ngoba imijovo emibili iyamvikela owesifazane impilo yakhe yonke. IGCIWANE iCovid-19 iDeltacron lakamuva eselikhona kunovalo lokuthi lizosabalala kakhulu kunamanye amagciwane. Ongoti bezempilo bathi lakheke ngokuthi kube nomuntu obephethwe yigciwane iDelta ne-Omicron ngesikhathi esisodwa.Leli gciwane elitholakale ngasekupheleni kukaJanuwari selikhona eFrance, United States nakwamanye amazwe kodwa alikakafiki kuleli.UDkt Maria Van Kerkhove wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), uthe uhlelo olusetshenziswayo lokubheka ukuthi leli gciwane lisabalala kangakanani emhlabeni lukhomba ukuthi okwamanje alikasabalali kakhulu kodwa kuseva ukuthi bangaqiniseka ukuthi ngeke lisabalale kakhulu."Leli gciwane liselisha akukuningi ososayensi abakwaziyo ngalo kodwa bayazi ukuthi lakheke ngokuthi kuhlangane amagciwane amabili kumuntu oyedwa. Yinto eyenzekayo nakwamanye amagciwane. Sisakubheka ukuthi lizoziphatha kanjani," kusho uDkt Van Kerkhove.Ongoti bezempilo bathi nakuba besacwaninga ngaleli gciwane kodwa zikhona izimpawu ezihamba phambili, abantu abangabona ngazo ukuthi bahaqwe yilona.Kuzo kubalwa ukukhathala, ukuba namafinyila, ukunkenketha kwekhanda, umphimbo obuhlungu, ukuthimula, ukugodola, imfiva, ukukhwehlela okunganqamuki, ukuhoshozela kwezwi uma ukhuluma, ubuhlungu besifuba, ubuhlungu bomzimba noma ukungalizwa iphunga nesiyezi.KULINDELEKE ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika iqale uhlelo lokujova amantombazane amancane ngomjovo owavikela ekutheni athole igciwane lengculazi ekuqaleni konyaka ozayo.Lolu uhlelo okuzobe kungolokuhlola ukuthi lungasebenza yini kuleli, kunethemba lokuthi lungasiza ekutheni luvikele abantu abangu-52 000 ekutheni batheleleke ngaleli gciwane eminyakeni engu-20 ezayo. Njengamanje bangu-8 million abantu abaneHIV kuleli.Lolu hlelo luyingxenye yokunikezwa kwabantu imishanguzo yokuzivikela, iPre-Exposure Prophylaxis (PrEP) enikezwa abantu abangenalo igciwane ukuze bavikeleke kwiHIV.I-PrEP engamaphilisi iyasetshenziswa kuleli, yaqala ukutholakala ngo2016. Uhlelo olusha ngolokuzwa amanzi ngobhoko kanti luwumjovo, kulindeleke ukuthi luqale ngonyaka ozayo. Luxhaswe ngemali yi-Unitaid, eyingxenye yeGlobal Health Initiative.I-Unitaid ithe ilindele ukuthi isikhungo esilawula ukusebenza kwemithi kuleli, iSouth African Health Products Regulatory Authority (SAPHRA), siwugunyaze ngonyaka ozayo lo mjovo okujovwa ngawo njalo ngemuva kwezinyanga ezimbili. Amaphilisi ePrEP akhona njengamanje aphuzwa zonke izinsuku.Uphiko lwezempilo eNyuvesi iWits, iReproductive Health neHIV Institute (Wits RHI) noMnyango wezeMpilo babambisene kulolu hlelo. Kuhlelwa ukuthi kulo bajove abesifazane abasebancane abangenalo igciwane.Ukusetshenziswa kwePrEP kwezinye izifundazwe kuphansi njengaKwaZulu-Natal. I-PrEP uma abayisebenzisayo beyilandela yonke imiyalelo yokusetshenziswa kwayo ibavikela engcupheni yokuhaqwa yiHIV.Imiphumela yokuhlola ukusebenza kwalo mjovo eyenziwe kuleli iveza ukuthi uvikela ukutheleleka kwabantu ngeHIV ngo-80%. Yize kunjalo, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO) ikholwa wukuthi baningi abazowusebenzisa ngenxa yokuthi kujovwa kanye ngemuva kwezinyanga ezimbili kanti amaphilisi aphuzwa zonke izinsuku.Lo mjovo waphasiswa isikhungo esigunyaza ukusababalaliswa kwemithi yokwelapha, e-United States of America (USA), i-United States Food and Drug Administration ngoDisemba 2021.I-ViiV Healthcare ekhiqiza lo mjovo yafaka isicelo kwiSAHPRA ngoAgasti 2021.Lo mjovo njengoba kwenziwa uhlelo lokuhlola ukuthi ungasebenzi yini kuleli, uzotholakala ezikhungweni zezempilo ezikhethiwe nezingomahamba nendlwana, nasemakhemisi.Umqondisi wenhlangano eyenza ucwaningo ngezempilo, uDkt Francois Venter, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba eqinisekisa ukuthi isitolo iClicks izobe ibambisene noMnyango wezeMpilo kulolu hlelo. Wathi umjovo uzobe uhambisana neringi ekhipha umshanguzo ovikela iHIV efakwa esithweni sowesifazane sangasese, i-vaginal ring efakwa kanye ngenyanga bese ilokhu ikhipha umshanguzo ovikelayo inyanga yonke.Ucwaningo lokuhlolwa kweringi olwenziwa phambilini, lwaveza ukuthi ivikela abesifazane ekutheni besuleleke ngaleli gciwane ngo-50%.UMnyango wezeMpilo neWits RHI kulindeleke ukuthi baqale uhlelo oluhlola ukufakwa kwabesifazane iringi ukuthi lungasebenza yini kuleli kuyo le nyanga.Okunye okuvelayo wukuthi e-USA, kubiza uR391 000 ukunikezwa kwesiguli esisodwa lo mjovo ngonyaka. Abacwaningi bathi kuleli kungadingeka ukuthi ubize uR1 800 ngonyaka ukuze iNingizimu Afrika ikwazi ukuwuthenga.IZIGULI ezingakudli ukudla okunempilo zijwayele ukuba nezifo eziyimixhantela ezidalwa imithi eziyisebenzisayo.Lokhu kushiwo uDkt Siyathemba Nxele imenenja ye-Aids Healthcare Foundation (AFH, KwaZulu-Natal,  ngesikhathi kwethulwa ngokusemthethweni ingadi yeziguli esemtholampilo eSiphingo okuzosizakala kuyo iziguli ezilanda imishanguzo yokulawula izifo zazo kulo mtholampilo.UDkt Nxele uthe isivande sitshalwe kulo mtholampilo ngokubambisana  kophiko lwale nhlangano olubhekele ukutshalwa kokudla i-AHF Food  For Health noMasipala weTheku ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuthi iziguli ezidla imishanguzo yokulawula izifo zithola imifino nezitshalo ezifanele ikakhulukazi iziguli ezineHIV.Le ngadi itshalwa ngamalungu omphakathi ayiziguli zakuwo lo mtholampilo nangezona athanda ukutshala. Ingxenye yomkhiqizo okhiqiziwe uphiwa iziguli, enye ingxenye idayiswe.“Lolu hlelo lokutshala olubizwa nge-vertical garden luyindlela esiza kakhulu ezindaweni ezisemadolobheni lapho indawo yokutshala incane. Ngokusebenzisa le ndlela okuhambisana nokusebenzisa izinto ebese zilahliwe senze ngazo umquba sishaya izinyoni ezimbili ngetshe elilodwa okungukubhekana nesimo sezulu esishintshashintshayo nokukhiqiza endaweni encane,"  kusho uNxele.UNksz Pamella Ndlovu, ongomunye wabalima kule ngadi ohlala eSiphingo Hills, uthe ubekuthanda ukulima ingakho usukumele phezulu uma kuthiwa abasondele abafuna ukujoyina uhlelo lokutshala emtholampilo."Esikufundile lapha ngokutshala kuzosisiza impilo yethu yonke. Besikwazi ukutshala kodwa le ndlela esetshenziswa lapha besingayazi sesifunde okuningi njengoba siyingxenye yalolu hlelo. Njengamanje umnotho uphansi, wonke umuntu udinga ukuthi kube nokuthile akwenzayo ukuze engeze emalini ayitholayo, phezu kwalokho kwathina sithola ukudla okuphuma emhlabathini okunomsoco," kuchaza uSr Ncamisile Mgobhozi oyimenenja yomtholampilo iSiphingo okutshalwe kuwo ingadi, uthe lo mtholampilo usetshenziswa ngabantu abaningi okusho ukuthi ubhekana neziguli ezinezifo eziningi ezikhathaza abantu kusukela esifweni senhliziyo, ukukhuluphala ngokweqile, iHIV nezinye." Ingadi iyasiza kakhulu uma unengcindezi nakithina bahlengikazi iyasiza uma ufika engadini uzwa sengathi uzalwe kabusha. Okunye okuhlukile kule ngadi ukuthi kutshalwe emapayipini, ezinye izitshalo azinamathele, emhlabathini konke lokhu uma ukubona uzizwa nawe sengathi usuzelwe kabusha kwehle ingcindezi,"  kusho uSr Mgobhozi.IZOVULWA usihlalo woMkhandlu weNgculazi  iSouth African National Aids Council (SANAC) ingqungquthela okuzobe kudingidwa kuyo izinto ezithina lesi sifo eqala namhlanje.Iphini likaMengameli elingusihlalo weSANAC, uMnuz Paul Mashatile, lizovula ingqunguthela ezobe iseNkosi Albert Luthuli International Convention Centre, eThekwini , eqala namhlanje iphele ngoLwesihlanu.Indikimba yengqungquthela ithi “Akube khona okwenzayo, xhumana nabanye ukuze uqede lolu bhubhane, "Act, Connect and End the Epidemic”Kule ngqungquthela kuzobe kuhlangene abathintekayo embhidlangweni wokulwa neHIV kubo okuhlanganisa  osoSayensi, abacwaningi, izishoshovu ezilwela abanaleli gciwane, abasiza ekutheni kuqalwe izinhlelo zokwelapha nokugwema igciwane, abasunguli bemithetho nenqubomgomo elandelwayo ukuze kwelashwe noma kugwenywe leli gciwane kusizwe nabaphila nalo.Bazobe bebuyekeza  nenqubekelaphambili esiyenziwe mayelana nokulawulwa kwe-HIV/AIDS ne-TB kulesi sikhathi esinezifo eziningi eziwubhubhane ezikhona emhlabeni nezinye izinto eziphazamisa ukwelashwa kwezifo.Isitatimende esithunyelwe ihhovisi likamengameli sithe I-SANAC, ibambe iqhaza eliphambili  ekusungulweni kwamasu amasha okubhekana neHIV/AIDS, National Strategic Plan (NSP)ka-2023-2028 ye-HIV, TB, kanye nezifo ezithathelana ngokocansi."ISANAC ivula ithuba lokuthi bonke abathintekayo bakhulume ngokusebenzisana kwezinhlaka ezahlukene okuhlanganisa uhulumeni, umphakathi nezinkampani ezizimele,” kusho ihhovisi likaMengameli esitatimendeni.UMashatile uzokwethula inkulumo yosuku esigcawini sokuvula ingqungquthela okuzokhuluma kuso uNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal, uNkk Nomusa Dube Ncube nezinye izikhulu zikahulumeni.UDkt  Nelson Igaba  weRight to Care ezobe ikhuthaza ukuthi abesilisa basoke nokuthi bahlale bezihlola ukuthi abanazo yini izifo kuyo le ngqungquthela, uthe : “Abesilisa bancamela ukubonwa odokotela  besilisa ngenxa yezizathu eziningi, abesilisa abazizwa bekhululekile ukuthi baye kodokotela noma ezikhungweni zezempilo, ngakho bayephuza ukufuna usizo lwezempilo, bajwayele ukuya esikhungweni sezempilo sebegula. Ukudembesela ungayi kozihlola kunemiphumela emibi kakhulu yezempilo” Uthe  imizamo yokubhekana nezinto eziyizithiyo ezenza ukuthi amadoda angajwayeli ukuya emitholampilo iyenziwa  kodwa ekugcineni umthwalo wokuthi avakashele ezikhungweni zezempilo usemahlombe awo, ukuze ahlolwe izifo.Uqhube wathi iRight to Care isebenzisana nezinye izinhlangano ukuthuthukisa nokwandisa izinsiza zokunakekelwa kwabesilisa. Wathi okunye abakwenzayo ukuya ngqo  emphakathini bakhulume namadoda.“ Ukuhlolwa i-HIV njalo kubalulekile. Izimpawu zokuqala ezifana nomkhuhlane uma ungabhekwa umsuka wazo isiguli singagcina sine-AIDS. Ucansi olungavikelekile, ikakhulukazi nabalingani abaningi, kwandisa ingozi yokusabalalisa i-HIV. Izindlela zokuvimbela ezisebenzayo ukusebenzisa  amakhondomu, ukusokwa kwabesilisa iMedical Male Circumcision (MMC) , kanye nokusebenzisa okuzokuvikela ekutheni ungalitholi igciwane uma uye ocansini nonalo, i-pre-exposure prophylaxis (PrEP).Uqhube wathi ukusoka kunciphisa amathuba okutheleleka ngeHIV ngo-60% .“ Kulindeleke ukuthi ngo-2030, uhlelo lwaseNingizimu Afrika lokusokwa kwabesilisa  lube selugweme ukutheleleka okusha nge-HIV  kubantu abangu-500 000,”  kusho u-Igaba.NJENGOBA sekungene ihlobo baningi abantu abazofuna ukwehla emzimbeni abanye baqale bashintshe indlela abadla ngayo nokudla abakudlayo.Abanye badla imikhiqizo ebathembisa ukuthi emva kwesikhathi esithile bazoncipha emzimbeni okubuye kubizwe nge “spot reduction”Abanye bake bazibuze ukuthi kungenzeka yini ukuthi unciphe endaweni ethize kuphela? UNksz Zinhle Masango obizwa nge-fitness Junkie oyi-nutritionist, athlete yase Under Armour utshele iphepha eliwuzakwethu i-IOL News ukuthi ngeke ukwazi ukunciphisa amafutha endaweni ethile kuphela.“Amafutha agcwele umzimba wonke. Uma uzivocavoca  usuke ushisa amafutha nama-calories umzimba wonke. Awukwazi ukuthi wenze ama squats bese uthi uzoncipha amathanga,” kuchaza uNksz Masango.Uthe ukuncipha emzimbeni kuhamba nendlela yokudla ebhalansile ezoba nama-vitamin nama-carbohydrates ngoba zonke lezi zinto umzimba uyazidinga, ukuzivocavoca, ukuphumula, ukulala ngokwanele nokuphuza amanzi amaningi.UMnuz Sibongiseni Ndwandwe oyi-fitness trainer utshele i-IOL News ukuthi uma ufuna ukuncipha emzimbeni kumele unyakaze.“Kumele kube khona okwenzayo noma ukudlala nezingane, ukuhamba, noma ukwenza ingadi. Kulabo abasebenza behleli noma abangakwazi ukunyakaza kumele baqinise kakhulu ekudleni abakudlayo bangadli ukudla okunama-calories amaningi,” kuchaza uNdwandwe.UNdwandwe uthe: “Abantu abangajwayeli ukuyeka ukudla ama-carbohydrates uma befuna ukwehla emzimbeni ngoba iwona anika umzimba umdlandla. Ukudla okunamafutha ungakudla kodwa hhayi njalo.”Uphinde waxwayisa ngokuthi abantu uma bengena kwizinhlobonhlobo zama-diet kunokudla okuthile abangakudli okusuke kunomsoco odingwa umzimba, ungakuziba lokhu kudla ngaleso sikhathi kodwa kungabi ukuthi usuyakuyeka nje ngoba ingozi iqala lapho.Uthe ukufuna ukubukeka kahle akumele kukufakele ingcindezi. “Abantu bazifakela ingcindezi kakhulu nokungenza ukuthi bafune izinto ezingeke zenzeke emizimbeni yabo, nezinto ezingagcina zibalimaza. Engingakusho ukuthi umuntu kumele abheke ukudla akudlayo, bese eyazivocavoca usuku nosuku,” kusho uNdwandwe. KUQHAKANJISWA ukuthi uthuthukiswe umkhakha wabahlengikazi kuleli ngenxa yokubhekana nezinselelo eziningi emsebenzini abawenzayo. Namhlanje kugujwa usuku lwamanesi, olugujwa umhlaba wonke ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi Nurses: A voice to lead. UDkt Champion Nyoni, ongumcwaningi ophinde afundise esikoleni sabahlengikazi esiseNyuvesi yaseFree State, uthe kuningi abahlengikazi ababhekane nakho ngo-2020. “Kuningi futhi okusazokwenzeka ngomuso. I-Covid-19 iphonsele umkhakha wezempilo izinselelo ezihlukene, abahlengikazi ababhekana kuqala nalezi zinselelo. Abahlengikazi bathintekile ngokomqondo, izinga labo lokubekezela nokwenze bakwazi ukusebenzisana kangcono,” usho kanje. “Esikhathini esizayo, idinga ukuthuthukiswa indima yabahlengikazi, ukukhula komsebenzi wobuhlengikazi kubalulekile. Abahlengikazi bazokwazi ukuqhubeka nomsebenzi wabo uma bezithuthukisa emsebenzini, ekubambisaneni bebodwa kanye nokusebenzisana nabanye abasebenzi bezempilo,” usho kanje. Uthe ikusasa lonesi liqhakazile ngoba kule minyaka ewu-60 eyedlule lo mkhakha utshengisa ukukhula. Kwamanye amazwe ububukeka njengomkhakha odelelekile kodwa manje ubumqoka bawo sebuyabonakala.Uqhube wathi amanesi kumele abheke ekutheni afune izinsiza ezizokwenza umsebenzi wawo ube lula.Abantu bakuleli balujabulele lolu suku ezinkundleni zokuxhumana: We shall execute our duties nomatter how hard it is #NursesDay2021 pic.twitter.com/JRBHB2xfCWSELUQALILE uhlelo lokubheka bonke abake bathintana nabanezinhlobo ezineCorona -19 ezitholakala e-India nase-UK kuleli.USolwazi Koleka Mlisana, ongusihlalo wekomiti eleluleka ongqongqoshe abasemkhandlwini obhekele iCovid-19 kuleli, iMinisterial Advisory Committee (Mac), uthe lolu hlelo luqalwe ngemuva kokuthi kuvele imiphumela eqinisekisa ukuthi kunabantu abane bakuleli abatheleleke ngeB.1.167 yase-India, nabangu-11 abaneB1.1.7 etholakala e-UK.USolwazi Mlisana uthe nakuba lungakabi khona ulwazi oluphelele abangakwazi ukulusebenzisa ukuze bakwazi ukuqhathanisa kahle la magciwane kodwa abakwaziyo wukuthi elase-India lithelelana ngokushesha, ekubeni nakuleli kune-501Y.V2 nayo etheleleka ngokushesha."Ukuzishintsha kwaleli gciwane kuzohlale kwenzeka. Okumele sikuqaphele singabantu wukuthi silandela imigomo ebekiwe yokuqhelelana, sifake izifonyo sigeze nezandla.  Leyo yimigomo esiza kunoma yiluphi uhlobo lwegciwane olufikile," kusho uSolwazi Mlisana .Uthe uhulumeni kumele enze isiqiniseko sokuthi abaphuma kwamanye amazwe bayahlolwa ngaphambi kokuthi bangene kuleli."Ukuhlolwa engikhuluma ngakho kangisho ukubheka izinga lokushisa. Ngisho ukuhlolwa okusezingeni elingaphezulu kwalokho, okuvezayo ukuthi kalikho yini leli gciwane kumuntu," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi abakwaziyo njengamanje bengososayensi wukuthi igciwane lakamuva elitholakale kuleli, uma like lakungena likunikeza ukuvikeleka okungatheni liphinde likungene nokuthi ungabe usangenwa ngamanye amagciwane atholakale kwamanye amazwe."Emzimbeni wakha ngamasosha akuvikelayo, yize kunjalo kusamele uqhubeke ufake isifonyo. Okunye okungasisiza wukuthi uhlelo lokugoma luphuthume ngoba siyazi ukuthi yonke imigomo ekhona iyavikela ekutheni umuntu uma engenwe yileli gciwane angali kakhulu aze adinge ukuya ezibhedlela,"  kusho yena.USolwazi Shabir Madhi, waseWits University, ongungoti wezifo ezidalwa ngamagciwane, uthe ukusabalala kwaleli gciwane e-India kakudalwanga wukuthi wukuthi lisabalala ngokwedlulele kodwa kudalwe wukuhlangana kwabantu abaningi ndawonye, okuholele ekutheni babe baningi abantu abahaqekayo ngesikhathi esisodwa."Nakithina lokho kungezeka uma sizoqhubeka nokulungiselela ukhetho. Uma kulungiselelwa ukhetho kusho ukuthi kuzoba nokuhlangana kwabantu abaningi. Asikwazi ukuvumela isimo esinjengaleso senzeke kuleli. Uma sikuvumele lokho, ekugcineni kuzoba nenkinga," kusho uMadhi.Uthe okwaziwayo ngegciwane eselizishintshile elitholakala e-India wukuthi lisabalala ngokushesha okungalinganiselwa ku-60% ekubeni  elase-UK lisabalala ngo-40%.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, unxuse umphakathi ukuthi ugweme ukuya ezindaweni ezinabantu abaningi ukuze unqande ukusabalala kwaleli  gciwane.Mbali Khanyile UGQUGQUZELE omama ngokubaluleka kokuncelisa izingane zabo ubisi lwebele uNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, uNkk Nomagugu Simelane-Zulu ngesikhathi kwethulwa izibalo zabantwana abazalwe ngosuku lokuqala ku2021.Ungqongqoshe ohalalisele  yonke imindeni yezingane ezizalwe ngalolu suku, uthe umnyango uyakholelwa  kakhulu  ekutheni uzihluphe ngesimo sempilo yezingane. Uthe  kusemqoka ukuthi wonke umzali ancelise ingane yakhe ubisi lwebele  ngoba lubalulekile emzimbeni wayo.“ Siyazi ukuthi akusiyo into ehlale ilula ukuncelisa ingane ubisi lwebele kodwa sithi abazame omama njengoba ludlala indima enkulu ekwakheni izakhamzimba enganeni. Lolu hlobo lokuncelisa alugcini nje kuphela ngokwakha izakhamzimba kodwa luphinde luqinise ubudlelwano obuhle phakathi kwengane nonina wayo,” kusho uNgqongqoshe.Eqhuba uthe kumele omama balihloniphe ishadi elibafundisa ngokukhuliswa nokunakekelwa kwezingane ukuze zihlale ziyimiqemane ngaso  sonk iikhathi.Zingu-140 sezizonke izingane ezizalwe  ngosuku lokuqala ku-2021 ngokwembiko yomnyango wezempilo esifundazweni. Zingu-77 izingane zabafana  ezizalwe ngalolu suku. Angu-63 amantombazane esewonke.UNksz Slindile Mkhize (35) waseNhlungwane, KwaSiqobelo otete amawele esibhedlela, iNkonjeni eMahlabathini, ubonge abasebenzi balesi sibhedlela ngokumlekelela ekuteteni izingane zakhe ngale kokuhlangabezana nenkinga.“ Ngibonga indlela abangeseke ngayo  onompilo baseNkonjeni ngesikhathi bengitetisa. Bekunzima kodwa ngikwazile ukunqoba ngenxa yendlela  abebengisingethe ngayo,” kubonga uNksz Mkhize, umama wamawele.KUGQUGQUZELWE abantu abanovalo lokugoma ukuthi bangesabi, ngenkathi kugonyelwa iCovid-19 ePeople’s Park, eMoses Mabhida, eThekwini, izolo.Kulolu hlelo, oluqale ngoMsombuluko, bekugcwele abantu asebekhulile abaqhamuka ezindaweni ezahlukene zakuleli dolobha.USomlomo weTheku, uNkk Weziwe Thusi, uthe umkhandlu uhlele ukugoma abantu abadala abangu-330 000.Phakathi kwezinye izindawo ezinhlanu athe kuqhutshwa kuzo lolu hlelo, ubale iPinetown Civic Centre, KwaMashu Indoor Sport Centre, Amanzimtoti Civic Centre nezibhedlela, iClairwood nePrince Mshiyeni eseMlaza,Uthe izindawo okugonyelwa kuzo zizokwanda uma kunyuka isibalo sabantu ababhalisela ukugoma.“Sihlele ukuthi sigome abantu abadala abangu-67% ngaphansi kwalo mkhandlu. Siyabanxenxa bonke abantu abadala ukuthi bagome njengoba benezifo ezingamahlala khona ezibeka impilo yabo engcupheni. Sicela nabaholi bomphakathi babe nesandla ekusilekeleleni ekutheni sigqugquzele abantu abadala ngobumqoka bokuba yingxenye yalolu hlelo,” kubeka uNkk Thusi.UDkt Nandipha Phahla (53) waseMhlanga, ongumsebenzi wezempilo, obengomunye wabantu abebeyogonywa izolo, uthe kumele abantu bazi ukuthi akukho zinkinga abazohlangabezana nazo uma begoma.“Ngibhalisele ukugoma esigabeni sokuqala ngoFebhruwari kodwa ngabe senginquma ukudedela ozakwethu abasebenza ngabantu ngoba mina ngiwumsebenzi ozinze kakhulu ehhovisi. Kulesi sigaba sesibili, ngisukumele phezulu njengoba ngingomunye wabantu abazogoma namhlanje (izolo). Kubalulekile ukuthi sigome sonke uma sisazimisele ngokuphila,” kubeka uDkt Phahla.UMnuz Falake Mkhwanazi (62) waseNkandla kodwa ozinze eThekwini ngokomsebenzi, uthe ubone kumqoka ukugoma njengoba emdala ngokweminyaka.“Ngingumuntu ozilandela kakhulu izindaba futhi bengilokhu ngibona imibiko engemihle yabantu abebethathwa yileli gciwane. Yingakho ngingahudulanga izinyawo ngenkathi kumenyezelwa ngohlelo lokugoma,” kubeka uMkhwanazi.UNkk Nana Cele (64) waseMbilo uthe ubone kukuhle asheshe azivikela kwiCovid-19 kunokuthi alashwe sesimkhahlamezile emzimbeni.“Njengamanje sibheke kwisivuvu sesithathu ngakho-ke kubalulekile ukuthi abantu bangalindeli ukuthi balashwe ngoba sebegula,” kuphetha uNkk Cele.INHLANGANO yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation igubha usuku iWorld Mental Health Day  njalo ngonyaka ngomhla ka 10 Okthoba.Inhloso enkulu yokugubha lolu suku, ukuqwashisa ngokusebenza kwengqondo nokuveza izingqinamnba ezikhona. Yize izinselelo zabaphila nezifo zengqondo zingasafani nakudala kodwa  kunokucwaswa okudala mayelana nezifo zengqondo nokwelashwa.Abantu basanqikaza ukuyofuna usizo noma ukukhuluma ngalesi sifo emindenini yabo nakulabo abasondelene nabo ngoba besaba ukucwaswa nokugxekwa.Okubalulekile ukuthi kufanele sifune usizo lwezempilo uma kukhona lapho silimele khona ukuze sithole usizo. Lokhu kubalulekile ukuze sihlale siphilile emzimbeni nasengqondweni.Iphini likamengameli weSouth African Depression and Anxiety Group (SADAG), uMnuz Zamo Mbhele, lithe usizo lukhona.“I-World Mental Health  Day ibanikeza ithuba bonke abakule ndima yokwelashwa kwezifo zengqondo ibanika ithuba lokuxoxa ngemisebenzi yabo nokuthi iyini edinga ukwenziwa isiqinisekiso sokuthi wonke umuntu odinga usizo lokwelashwa uyaluthola.Isiqubulo salo nyaka seWorld Federation For Mental Health sithi #BeKi8ndToYourMind, ngenxa yokuthi ukusebenza kwengqondo kuthathwa njengento ebalulekile emhlabeni.Inhlangano iMental Health Foundation isisebenze ngokuzikhandla iminyaka engu-70  ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ingqondo nomzimba kunakekelwa ngokwezinga elifanayo.Iqiniso ukuthi wonke umuntu unengcindezi emndenini, emsebenzini, nasemphakathini, kanti ukuze sigweme  izifo zengqondo kumele sizinakekele.IWorld Health Day inikeza ithuba lokuthi kukhulunwye esidlangaleni ngezifo zengqondo, kuqhanyukwe namacebo okuthi yini edinga ukwenziwa ukuzinakekela nokuthi kubaluleke kangakanani ukuyofuna usizo.MBALI KHANYILEINHLANGANO iSouth African National Blood Services ikhala ngeCovid-19 eholele ekutheni kwehle isibalo sabantu abanikela ngegazi kuleli.Lokhu kuvezwe nguMnuz Mohamad Goolam wale nhlangano emcimbini iWellness Day, ebihlelwe wumasipala weTheku ngenhloso yokuqwashisa abantu ngokuzinakekela eMoses Mabhida, eThekwini.UGoolam uthe igazi eselitholwa yile nhlangano kubantu abanikela ngalo, sekuba yigazi elishesha liphele njengoba belihambisa ezibhedlela."Ngokujwayelekile siqoqa igazi elingu-500 units kodwa kulezi zinsuku sithola elingu-100 units kuphela. Lesi sibalo esesisithola siphela ngosuku olulodwa njengoba ngokujwayelekile igazi esiliqoqayo lisilonda izinsuku ezinhlanu. Kuwumqansa kulo nyaka njengoba lesi sikhathi esesikuso samaholidi silidinga igazi eliningi ngenxa yesibalo sezingozi eziningi eziholela ekutheni kudingeke igazi elizolekelela abasuke bophe kakhulu ngesikhathi belimala," kubeka yena.Uthe umcimbi iWellness Day usemicimbi asebethembele kuyo ukuqoqa igazi njengoba kumqoka ukuthi bayihambele ngoba babhekene nengwadla.UMnuz Vusi Mazibuko weMoses Mabhida Stadium, uthe inhloso yomcimbi ukukhuthaza abantu ngokuzinakekela njengoba iCovid-19 ishintshe izinhlelo eziningi kubantu." Yize kuneCovid-19 sivumelekile ukuthi sizivocavoce futhi siqikelele ukuthi sidla ukudla okunempilo ukuze silwe naleli gciwane. Njengoba abantu abaningi bebenezinkinga zemali kulo nyaka ngenxa yesimo esizithole sikuso, sonke sibone kufanele ukuthi umcimbi ube nabamabhange ngenhloso yokweluleka ngezikweletu ezingenaso isidingo. Okumele kube mqoka kubantu wukuthi asigcini nje kuphela ngokuba yinkundla yezemidlalo njengoba siphinde sikhombise ukuzikhathaza ngesimo sempilo yabo ngemicimbi efana nale," kusho uMazibuko.Kulo mcimbi obekuphinde kube nemibukiso yemikhiqizo eyahlukene yokunakekela imizimba bekuphinde kuhlowe igazi, amehlo, isifo sashukela nezinye izifo.IMeya yeTheku uMnuz Kaunda, ithe leli dolobha linezinhlelo zokuthi kushaye u-2030, seliyindawo okuphileka kamnandi kuyo eyaziwa njengedolobha elinakekela impilo yabantu.Uthe lezi zinhlelo zidinga ukuthi wonke umuntu abambe iqhaza ekutheni ziphumelele.AMATHE abuyele kwasifuba kumiswa ucwaningo obeluhlola umgomo wokuvikela iHIV, obelwenziwa e-Afrika kuthiwa mancane amathuba okuthi imiphumela yalo ikhombise ukuthi umgomo uyasebenza. Kulolu chungechunge locwaningo oluvivinya imigomo eminingi yeHIV emhlabeni, iHIV Vaccine Trial Network, bekuhlolwa inhlanganisela yemithi emibili eyenzelwe ukuvikela iHIV nohlobo olusha lwe-pre-exposure prophylaxis (PreP). Lolu cwaningo belusesigabeni sesibili, luholwa yi-Afrika, lwesekwa yi-Europe futhi lunezinhlaka ezimbili. Ukuvivinywa kwe-PreP kusaqhubeka. Ososayensi ababenza lolu cwaningo bathi bese kuwumzamo wokugcina wokuhlola nokuvivinya umgomo kusetshenziswa imithi ezoqinisa  amasosha omzimba angakhethi. Kuzodingeka ukuthi baqale kabusha.UDkt Larry Corey, owungoti owenza ucwaningo ngezifo ezidalwa amagciwane, ohola lolu cwaningo, ephawula ngokumiswa kwalo uthe akukho okubethusile ngoba ucwaningo olubili, nalo obeluvivinya imithi eqinisa amasosha omzimba, lwamiswa ngoba kubonakala ukuthi imiphumela yalo ayithokozisi."Imiphumela yalolu cwaningo izosisiza ekutheni sazi ukuthi ngokulandelayo kumele senzeni ukuze sakhe umgomo esicabanga ukuthi ungasebenza," kusho yena.Uthe imizamo engaphumeleli yokuthi kube nomgomo weHIV ifaka ingcindezi ezigulini nakososayensi, ikakhulukazi ngoba umgomo ovikela iCovid-19 wenziwa ngokuphuthuma."Nakuba ekhona amanye amathuluzi okuvimbela iHIV, umgomo iyona ndlela ehlangabezana nezinjongo zokuqeda iHIV emhlabeni wonke  ukuze kuvikeleke ukuthi kwenyuke isibalo sabasaqhubeka nokutheleleka ngaleli gciwane. Njengamanje sisekude kakhulu ukufinyelela emgomeni esizibekele wona wokuqeda igciwane lengculazi ngo-2030. Ukuba khona komgomo kungasisiza," kuchaza uSolwazi Corey.Isitatimende esithunyelwe wumqondisi we-International Aids Society (IAS), uNkk uBirgit Poniatowski, sithe: "Ngeke silahlekelwe ithemba lokuthi umhlaba ube nomgomo osebenzayo wokugomela iHIV ozotholwa yibo bonke abawudingayo noma ngabe bakuphi."I-USA ikhiphe imiphumela yomunye umgomo onemiphumela  ekhomba ukuvikeleka kwiCovid-19 ngo-94.5% ngoMsombuluko .Kwenzeka lokhu ngemuva kwesonto kuvele imiphumela yokuhlolwa komunye umgomo kulo leli lizwe ekhombisa ukuvikeleka kwiCovid-19 ngo-90%.Umgomo wakamuva ubuhlolwa yiModerna Inc,  ucwaningo lwawo olwenziwe kubantu lukhomba ukuvikeleka ngo-94.5%.Ngeledlule iPfizer neBioNtech ikhiphe imiphumela yowayo umgomo obukhomba ukuvikeleka okungu-90%.Imiphumela yale migomo yomibili kusengeyesikhashana. Amavolontiya ayingxenye yocwaningo lweModerna  angu-30 000.Isitatimende esikhishwe iModerna sithe ucwaningo olwenziwa kubantu lusesigabeni sesithathu kanti imiphumela yesikhashana ikhomba ukuthi kukhona ukuvikela okwenziwa yilo mgomo ohlolwayo.Yomibili imigomo ohlolwe iModerna nohlolwe iPfizer isebenzisa ubuchwepheshe obufanayo obaziwa nge-mRNA.Okwamanje imigomo ayikabhaliswa esikhungweni esilawula ukukhiqizwa kwemithi kuleliya lizwe ngoba ubuchwepheshe obusetshenziswe kuyo busha abaziwa. Imigomo ehlolwayo idinga ukuhlala efrijini kodwa iPfizer idinga  isiqandisi esibanda kakhulu esingekho ezibhedlela eziningi, bekunemibuzo yokuthi uma kungathiwa iyaphasiswa  izogcinwa kuphi futhi uma ihanjiswa ezibhedlela izofakwa kuphi ukuze ingonakali kanti iModerna ingakwazi ukuhlala nasefrijini lasekhaya elijwayelekile.UDkt Jabulani Ncayiyana waseNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal uthe ulwazi oluningi oluthinta  le miphumela alukadalulwa ngakho akukuningi kakhulu okwaziwayo ngale migomo kodwa imiphumela yayo inikeza ithemba.“Imininingwane yokuthi ngabe isebenza kanjani, ngabe ivikela ukuthi umuntu angangenwa yiCovid-19 noma iyamelapha asikabinayo.  Le migomo njengoba  ikhiqizwa e-USA uma ingaphumelela kungathatha isikhathi ukuthi ifike e-Afrika. Uma isifika ngicabanga ukuthi kuyoba nohlelo lokuthi ngobani okumele bagonywe kuqala okungaba abantu abanezifo ezingamahlalakhona, abadala nabasebenzi bezempilo ngoba umgomo ngeke uthi ufika ube sewenele ukugoma bonke abantu,” kusho yena. UKUTHANDA ukubukeka kahle, bafaneleke uma begqokile kwenza ukuthi abanye abantu besifazane basebenzise i-sellotape ukunamathisela amabele ngoba bekholwa ukuthi u-bra awuyilungele impahla abasuke bezoyigqoka ngaleso sikhathi. Lokhu kwenza amabele ame ngendlela abayifisayo.Lo mkhuba, owenziwa kakhulu kulezi zinsuku, waziwa nge-breast taping. Kusetshenziswa izinto ezehlukene ukunamathisela amabele ame ngendlela ezohambelana nengubo umuntu asuke efuna ukuyigqoka.UNksz Mamsie Mkhwanazi we-Afrolicious uthe abantu besifazane abaningi bayazifela ngokugqoka izimpahla ezithungwe ngendwangu eyaziwa ngokuthi i-Illusion fabric (lace)."Le ndwangu yenza ukuthi ubone konke okusemzimbeni womuntu, ayigqokeki no-bra. Osaziwayo bona baye bahlinzwe amabele ukuze ame ngendlela futhi kubukeke kahle. Abantu abangenayo imali yokuyohlinzwa nabo bayathanda ukubukeka kahle, base beqala indlela yokuthi basebenzise izinto zokunamathisela amabele ahambisane naleyo ngubo. Abanye bakwenza ngoba kwenziwa ngabantu abadumile. Thina njengabasiki bengqephu senza lokho okufunwa yikhasimende. Njengamanje abantu bayazifela ngokugqoka izinto eziveza imizimba. Akuwona amabele kuphela anamatheliswa ngezinto ezithile, nezisu kwenziwa okufanayo kuzo. Abanemali bayazihlinza, abangenayo imali  bathenga imikhiqizo eyehlukene ukuze zincishiswe," kusho uNksz Mkhwanazi.I-breast taping yenzelwa ukuphakamisa amabele ukuze kwenzeke i-cleavage noma alale athi mba esifubeni, kungabonakali ukuthi akhona noma abukeke emancane futhi ame. Abanye bakwenzela ubuhle, abanye bakwenza uma bezobe bedansa noma benza izinto ezizobenza banyakazise umzimba, bengafuni ukuthi amabele abaphazamise.Abenza i-breast taping bathi kuyenzeka abesifazane abazishintshile baba ngabesilisa (transgenders) nabo bakwenze lokhu.Ngokujwayelekile kusetshenziswa i-sellotape ejwayelekile, i-medical tape ne-sports strapping tape.Ongoti bezempilo bathi ukumpintsha amabele ngo-bra ngoba ufuna ukubukeka kahle uma ugqokile kuyingozi, ingasaphathwa eyokuthi amabele ananyatheliswe nge-sellotape engadalelwanga ukunamathela esikhumbeni.Bathi lokhu kungalimaza isikhumba ngaphandle, kudale ukuthi amabele nengxenye yomzimba enanyatheliswe nge-sellotape ivuvukale noma noma ibe nezigaxa.Ucwaningo olwenziwe yisishoshovu sezempilo, uDkt Sydney Ross Singer,  alushicilelele encwadini yakhe, iDress to kill: the link between breast cancer and bras, luveza ukuthi ukugqoka u-bra isikhathi eside kungaba nomthelela wokuthi abesifazane babe nomdlavuza webele.Le ncwadi ike yafundwa engqungqutheleni, iWorld Congress on Breast Cancer ngo-2018, iveza ukuthi nakuba o-bra benzelwe ukuthi benze ibele lime ngendlela kodwa banobungozi.Omunye wodokotela, ocele ukungadalulwa ngoba ethi okwamanje alukho ucwaningo oluke lwenziwa mayelana nalo mkhuba, uthe: " Indlela yokuphila kuyenzeka ibe nomthelela ezifeni yingakho phambilini kwawona umdlavuza ubungemningi kubantu abathile ngoba indlela ebebephila ngayo beyehlukile. Ukushintsha kwempilo kuholele ekutheni bande abantu abahlaselwa umdlavuza neminyaka obahlasela bekuyo nayo ishintshe. Isikhathi esikuso manje sesiqhamuka nendlela entsha yokuzenza ubukeke kahle ngokunamathisela amabele, nakho lokhu kuzoqhamuka nezinye izinkinga zempilo," kusho yena.LUSELUDE ukhalo mayelana nokutholakala kwekhambi lokwelapha iHIV noma umgomo ovikela leli gciwane kodwa inganqotshwa ngokusebenzisa imishanguzo eyicindezelayo egazini.Abezempilo bathi nakuba ikhona inqubekela phambili ekwelashweni kwaleli gciwane kusetshenziwa imishanguzo eyilicindezelayo kodwa kusenzima ukusho ukuthi ikhambi lokwelashwa lingatholakala nini ngoba okwamanje ososayensi abakaqhamuki nalo.Umqondisi wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus, uthe inselelo enkulu ukuthi iningi labantu abazi ukuthi banayo yini iHIV kumbe kabanalo, wathi lokhu kwenza ukuthi umgomo wokuthi kuqedwe iHIV ngo-2030, kubukeke sengathi ngeke ufezeke."Bangu-30 million abantu abadla imishanguzo yeHIV emhlabeni, bangu- 9.2 million abangakakwazi ukuthola imishanguzo yokuyicindezela ngenxa yezinselelo ezikhona emazweni abo. Njalo ngosuku kushona abantu abangu-1 700 bebulawa izifo ezisondelene neHIV, abangu -3 500 bangenwa ileli gciwane nsukuzonke. Inqwaba ayisazi isimo sayo seHIV. “Sisalelwe iminyaka eyisikhombisa nje kuphela kushaye u-2030, obekelwe ukuthi siqede ngawo leli gciwane. Kumele sibambisane kakhulu ukuze sifeze amasu aziwa nge-95-95-95 okuyiwo asiphendlela indlela eya ekunqobeni iHIV," kusho uDkt Ghebreyesus.Uqhube wathi luningi ucwaningo olwenziwayo ukuze kutholakale ikhambi lokwelapha ingculazi kodwa okwamanje akukho okuthembisayo okuvelayo. Umqondisi osabambile ophikweni olubhekelele ukwelashwa kweHIV/AIDS nezifo zocansi ezithathelanayo eMnyangweni wezeMpilo kuleli, uMnuz Petros Khoza,  uthe kuyakhathaza ukuthi kunesibalo esingaziwa sabantu abangazazi ukuthi banayo noma kabanayo iHIV. Yize ukhona umehluko ekwelashweni kwaleli gciwane kusetshenziswa amaphilisi okulicindezela lingabonakali egazini, ukusetshenziswa kwamakhondomu, ukusoka  namaphilisi avikela ukuthi uthole leli gciwane uma kwenzeka uya ocansini nomuntu onalo, iPre-exposure prophylaxis, iPrep kodwa iseyinde indlela.INingizimu Afrika izibekele ukuthi ngo-2025, u-95% wabantu bakuleli babe sebezihlolile besazi isimo sabo seHIV, u-95% wabantu okutholalakale ukuthi banaleli gciwane uqale imishanguzo yokulicindezela, u-95%  wasebedla imishanguzo igciwane egazini labo libe selicindezelekile.UDkt Julie Turner weRight To Care, uthe iHIV inganqontshwa ngo-2030, uma umgomo we-95-95-95 ungafezeka."Ngesikhathi kukhulunywa nge-90-90-90 kwakubukeka kuyinto engeke yenzeke. Kodwa ucwaningo lwango-2022 lweHuman Science Research luyasitshela ukuthi u-90% wabantu bakuleli usuyasazi isimo sabo seHIV, u-91% wabasaziyo isimo sabo seHIV, sebedla imishanguzo, u-94% wabadla imishanguzo iHIV egazini labo isicindezelekile. Uma singafinyelela ku-95-95-95 ngo-2025, singayinqoba iHIV ngo-2030. “Akukhathalekile ukuthi asikabi nalo ikhambi lokwelapha leli gciwane. Asilidingi kangako ikhambi uma abantu abaneHIV bonke bedla imishanguzo, igciwane egazini labo licindezelekile. Akekho umuntu omusha ongamthelela, ngaleyo ndlela ayikho ingane engazalwa ineHIV. Ngikusho lokhu ngoba ososayensi bethu sekunesikhathi becwaninga ngekhambi kodwa akukho okuqhamukayo. Uma singabambelela kulokhu esinakho, singanqoba. Kungekudala kuzoba nemijovo ejovwa ngemuva kwezinyanga ezimbili noma eziyisithupha nezinye izinsiza," kusho uDkt Turner.UKUXOXISANA nengane ngezocansi kuseyisihloko esinzima kubazali abaningi. Ngokusho kongoti, yize kulumela kunjalo kepha kusemqoka ukuthi abazali bafundise izingane zabo ngokuya ocansini. Ungoti kwezobudlelwano nezocansi uDkt Nomcebo Mthembu, uthi ayasinda futhi ayalumela amagama ezitho zangasese ngokwehlukana kobulili nezinto ezingocansi kepha kusemqoka ukweluleka izingane.Uqhuba athi uma ingane isithombile, umzali usuke esengaqala ukuyicathulisa noma engeke ayitshele konke ngesikhathi esisodwa kodwa kuyisigaba esifanele sokuqala izingxoxo ngezocansi.UDkt Mthembu weluleka abazali ngokuthi bangaqala ukwendlalela inkulumo ngezinto ezibalulekile futhi batshele izingane ukuthi ukukhuluma ngalesi sihloko kusiza zona, ukuze zingangeni ogibeni.  “Kuyenzeka izingane zifakelane zodwa ingcindezi. Enye igcine seyiya ocansini ukujabulisa abangani bayo ngoba ifakelwe ingcindezi. Ukukhulelwa kwezingane eziningi kuqala nangaso lesi sigaba ngoba zisuke zifundisana zodwa ngasese," kuchaza uDkt Mthembu.Ukuyihebeza ingane uma ikuhloma imibuzo akusona isisombululo ngoba ikhula ngokubona into, bese ifisa ukwazi ukuthi kwenziwelani, kunalokho ungoti uthi umzali kumele akujabulele ukubuzwa yingane kuqala. Ukukhuluma ngobuhle bothando nokuba sebudlelwaneni obungajahile ukuya ocansini nakho uthi kungaba wusizo kwenze umehluko enganeni yakho ingadidiseki kalula. UDkt Mthembu uthe ukuthi ingane inemibuzo akusho ukuthi kukhona esikwenza nesikwazi kodwa isuke ifuna ukuqonda kahle ngocansi." Ungagcini nje ngokuyiyala ukuthi ingajahi ukuya ocansini kodwa ibekele nezizathu ezozizwa. Uma ubona ukuthi kukhona ongakwazi ukufinyelela khona kahle, sebenzisa izithombe nemininingwane ebhalwe phansi ukwenza umsebenzi ube lula. Fundisa ingane ngezifo zocansi uyikhombise ukuthi umuntu ongalalelanga nozibandakanya nokuya ocansini nomuntu angamazi, uphetha enjani esithweni sangasese," kweluleka uDkt Mthembu.Ephetha ungoti uthe izihloko akumele ziphendulwe bgokobulili kumele yonke ingane ekhona ekhaya okungaba umfana noma intombazane, ifundiswe ngendlela efanayo.Nakhu okunye okubalulekile:-Ungalezi iphutha lokuqagela ukuthi ingane yakho sekukhona ekwaziyo ngokuya ocansini ngoba uzoshiya izinto ezibalulekile ukhulume ngezinto ezingeke ziyakhe.-Qinisekisa ukuthi awuyiniki ulwazi oluningi ngesikhathi esisodwa futhi awuthi zisuka ube uyimfunza konke engakaqondi nokuthi kungani nikhuluma ngesihloko sezocansi.-Ungagxili kwezocansi kuphela ngoba ubudlelwane bezothando nemizwa yokungaphatheki kahle ngezinye zezinto eziholela izingane zigcine sezizibandakanya nocansi. Zicabange ukuthi yilapho zizothola khona intokozo.-Ungambadazi futhi unganyusi umoya uma ingane ikwazisa ukuthi seyize yaqala ukuzibandakanya nezocansi. Thola ukuthi ngabe yisiphi isizathu esiholele lapho nokuthi seyihambe ibanga elingakanani.-Sebenzisa izinkundla zokuxhumana ngoba kunamakhasi asabalalisa ulwazi futhi nezingane zikhonze amaselula kulezi zinsuku, kusuke kuzoba lula. Ithelevishini nomsakazo nakho kuqukethe izinhlelo zokukhuliswa kwezingane ngezindlela ezahlukene-Khuluma izinto ngeqiniso nengane futhi ulalele uma ikhuluma kungabi ngezimfuno zakho konke enikuxoxayo. Vumela inkulumo yenu kube ingxoxo mpikiswano ngoba kulesi sigaba ingane isuke izobuza nangezinto ezithinta wena mzali nokuthi kwenzeka kanjani kuwe. ZILINGANISELWA ku-33 million Iizingane okufanele zigonywe phakathi kuka-2023 no-2025 ukuze pkufezeke isibophezelo samazwe omhlaba esithi ngo-2030, kumele kunqandwe ukufa kwezingane ezibulawa yizifo ezigwemekayo ngokugoma. Njengoba kuyisonto lokuqwashisa ngokubaluleka kokugoma, iWorld Immunisation Week, eqale ngoMsombuluko ephela ngeSonto, inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithe uhlelo lokuthi kuvikelwe izifo ezibulalala izingane ezigwemekayo ngokuthi zigome, luphazamisekile ngesikhathi kuhlasele iCovid-19.Le nhlangano ithe ngesikhathi kuhlasele iCovid-19, uhlelolokugonywa kwezingane lubambezelekile okuholele ekutheni senyuke ngo-16% isibalo sezingane ezeqiwe yimigomo nezingakaze zigome nhlobo.UDkt Matshidiso Moeti umqondisiwe WHO e-Afrika, uthe lolu bhubhane luyibuyisele emuva kakhulu imizamo ye-Afrika yokugoma futhi lubeka engcupheni izigidi zezingane engozini yokuhlaselwa izifo ezivikeleka ngokugoma, ezinye zazo eziholela ekufeni."Amazwe alwa kakhuluekuphumeni ethunzini leCovid-19, ngeke sikwazi ukulahlekelwa futhingokuthi kuqubuke izifo ezidalwa wukuthi izingane kazigomile. Kumele kwenziwe yonke imizamo yokuqinisekisa ukuthi yonke ingane iyayithola imigomo ebalulekile,” kusho uDkt Moeti.UDkt Joseph Cabore ongumqondisi wokuphathwa kwezinhlelo ehhovisi leWHO elise-Afrika, uthe isibalo sezingane ezingakaze zithole umthamo owodwa womgomo, sikhule sisukaku-7.7 million ngo-2020 saya ku-12 million ngo-2022. Kulo nyaka (2023), amazwe angu-31 ase-Afrika abhekane nokuqubuka kwezifo ezivikeleka ngokugoma. Muva nje, iWHO yethule umkhankaso ozosiza amazwe ukuthi agome izingane ezisilele emuva ngesikhathi seCovid-19. Lo mkhankaso ubizwa ngeBig Catch Up Campaign.UDkt Cabore uthe ngawo iWHO izoletha izinsiza ezengeziwe emazweni okudingeka ukuthi kugonywe izingane eziningi kuwo. Uqhube wathi emazweniawu-10 aseqhulwini asehloliwe, kubalwa iMalawi, Mozambique, Tanzania, Zambia neZimbabwe, lapho bekugonywelwa isifo sovendle nyakenye."Kusukela ngo-2019, umgomo kamalaleveva wokuqala emhlabeni ubutholakala ezingxenyeni zaseGhana, Kenya naseMalawi njengoba bekusenziwa uhlelo lokuzwa amanzi ngobhoko, kubhekwa ukuthi ngabe lolu hlelo luyasebenza yini? Eminyakeni emine luqhubeka, izingane ezingaphezu kuka-1.4 million ziwutholile umgomo kuwo wonke amazwe amathathu," kusho uCabore.Uthe esinye isimo esiphuthumayo sezempilo ezwenikazi i-Afrika kube ngukuqubuka kovendle lwasendle ngo-2020. Kwaphinde kwaba ngukuvela kwegciwane elidala isifo sohudo nokuphalaza iRotavirus kodwa lezi zifo zinqontshiwe.“Uvendle (Wild Poliovirus) lunqotshiwe, savikela izingane ezingu-33 million ngokuzigomela uvendle ngonyaka odlule. Ukugomela iRotavirus kwehlise ukufa kwabantu ngenxa yohudo lwaleli gciwane ngo49.1%.“Ngemuva kwalokho, bonke ohulumeni base-Afrika bafake umgomo weHPV, ovikela amantombazane kumdlavuza wesibeletho," kusho uCabore.Ngeledlule, umqondisi weWHO, uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus, uvakashele kuleli nethimba lososayensi abavela kwamanye amazwe ngenhloso yokuzocobelena ngolwazi lokwenziwa kwemigomo eyenziwa ngobuchwepheshe i-mRNA.IKHOMISHINI yokuLingana ngokoBulili, isishayela ihlombe isinyathelo soMnyango wezeMpilo sokuthi uphenye ngezinsolo zokuthi kunabesifazane abakhishwa izibeletho ngempoqo ezikhungweni zezempilo, KwaZulu-Natal naseGauteng ngoba benegciwane lengculazi.NgoFebhuwari ikhomishini yethula umbiko ngabesifazane abakhishwa izibeletho ezikhungweni zikahulumeni zezempilo KwaZulu-Natal naseGauteng ngenxa yokuthi babenesandulela ngculazi. Yayithole isikhalo ngo-2015.  Kulo mbiko ikhomishini yathi abesifazane baphucwa ilungelo lokuzikhethela ukuthi bayathanda yini ukuba nezinye izingane noma cha.Ngeledlule uNgqongqoshe woMnyango wezeMpilo uDkt Zweli Mkhize uvele ngaphambi kwekomiti lasePhalamende lezempilo, abesifazane, intsha nabaphila nokukhubazeka ngalolu daba, ezochaza ukuthi  umnyango wakhe usuhambe kangakanani  ngophenyo njengoba ikhomishini yayenze izincomo zokuthi uphenye.UDkt Mkhize ngemuva kokuphuma kombiko wamemezela ukuthi usesungule ithimba elizophenya ngezinsolo eliholwa ungoti wezifo ezithinta umgudu wenzalo kwabesifazane, uSolwazi Motshedisi Sebitloane waseNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal.UDkt Mkhize uthe uphenyo seluqalile kodwa luphazamisekile ngenxa yokuthi kuhlasele iCovid-19  lusaqalwa.UMqondisi jikelele woMnyango wezeMpilo  uDkt Sandile Buthelezi, uthe kwabesifazane abangu-18 abafaka izikhalo  bathole abayisishiyagalolunye. Ithimba kulindeleke ukuthi lithole amafayela abesifazane, libheke imibiko yabo yezempilo, libheke  ukuthi bawasayina yini amafomu okuthi bafuna ukuvala inzalo, uma bawasayina kubhekwe ukuthi zazikhona yini izizathu zezempilo ezazenza ukuthi kube nesidingo sokuvalwa inzalo, lithole abasebenzi bezempilo abathintekayo.UNkk Tamara  Mathebula usihlalo weKhomishini  yokuLingana ngokoBulili uthe: “Kuyasijabulisa ukuthi kukhona okwenziwayo  siyethemba ukuthi ngeke kusaba khona ukubambezeleka kophenyo nokuthi uphenyo luzoholela ekutheni kwenziwe ubulungiswa ngalolu daba.”Uthe bazobheke ukuthi uphenyo luqhubeka kanjani.“Abesifazane abathintekayo sicela babambisane nethimba eliphenyayo. Kumele bathinte amahhovisi ethu akhona kuzo zonke izifundazwe  uma befuna ukufaka izikhalo,”  kusho yena.Owesifazane waseMlaza othi wakhishwa isibeletho kwesinye sezibhedlela abelethela kuso, uthe ulinde ukuthi bajeze abasebenzi bezempilo abamphuca ilungelo lokuzikhethela. Uthe abahlengikazi abebedinwe ukuthi ukhulelwe ebe enesandulela ngculazi  uthe bamsayinisa ifomu ayezitshela ukuthi eyokuthi uzohlinzwa ngoba isibeletho sakhe sinenkinga.“Ngezwa ngemuva kweminyaka ngabeletha ukuthi isibeletho anginaso ngoba nganginezinhlungu engangicabanga ukuthi ezesibeletho . Ngemuva kokuhlolwa ngatshelwa ukuthi sakhishwa.  Ngaphucwa ilungelo lami lokuzikhethela, Ngizizwa  ngingaphelele. Uyise wezingane zami angikaze ngimtshele ukuthi isibeletho sakhishwa,”  kusho yena.MBALI KHANYILENJENGOBA sekusele usuku olulodwa kuqale ukubhalwa kwezivivinyo zika-matric, ziningi izindlela ezisetshenziswa abafundi ukuze babe nomdlandla abanye bafunde kuze kuse.Ukuze bangalali abanye basebenzisa iziphuzo ezinikana amandla ngenhloso yokuthi umqondo ungakhathali uma betadisha.Inkinga ngalo mkhuba wukuthi uyajovana futhi awubi nomthelela omuhle ngokusho ngongoti bezempilo.UMnuz Ndabe Myeza ongungoti oweluleka ngokwezengqondo, uthe kumele abafundi bakugweme ukudukela emikhiqizweni okuthiwa ikhuthaza umqondo noma ikunika umdlandla ngoba igcina ibagulisa abanye.“Iziphuzo ezikhuthazayo zivamise ukwenza inhliziyo ishaye ngamandla, okuholela ekutheni ugcine usuzizwa untekenteke ngokuhamba kwesikhathi. Abafundi kumele bahambele kude nazo.”Uthe kumele bazinike isikhathi esanele uma befundela izivivinyo ukuze bangagcini sebezithola bengaphansi kwengcindezi, sebezama ukubamba yonke into okumele bavive ngayo.Amathiphu abangawase-benzisa abafundi abalungiselela izivinyo:- Gwema ukufunda ngokweqile ukuze ungazitholi usukhohlwa wokufundile uma usubhala. Umqondo uyaphunyuzwa futhi awukwazi ukubamba yonke into ngesikhathi esisodwa.- Bheka indlela yokufunda ekusebenzelayo nehambisana nawe. Gwema ukwenza imikhuba oyibona yenziwa ngabanye abafundi ngenhloso yokuvivela izivivinyo ngoba yikho okungagcina kuholela ekutheni ungaphumeleli.- Zihlelele kusenesikhathi ukuze ungazitholi usutatazela ngomzuzu wokugcina.- Qikelela ukuthi ukuphethe konke ozokudinga uma usubhala izivivinyo ngaphambi kokusuka ekhaya.- Gwema ukufika ekuseni kakhulu esikoleni uma uzobhala ukuze ungazitholi usutatazeliswa ngabanye abafundi ababuzana ukuthi ufunde wagcina kuphi. Kugweme nokugeja isikhathi sokuqala kwesivivinyo ukuze ungabhali usutatazeliswa yisikhathi.- Zama ngakho konke ukuhambisana nesikhathi uma ubhala ukuze ungazitholi usunenkinga yokungaliqedi iphepha. Ufunde imibuzo ngokuyiqonda. Lokhu kuzophinde kukusize ekutheni ube nesikhathi esanele sokubhekisisa izimpendulo zakho ngaphambi kokuthi uphume ekilasini obubhala kulo. Qala ngokuphendula imibuzo oyiqonda kangcono.UMFUNDI ka-matric waseChief Luthayi High eMpumalanga, uZithulele Tshagala, ematasa nezifundo zakhe njengoba kusasa eqala ukubhala izivivinyo Isithombe: BONGANI MBATHABAZOKWAZINDISWA abahlengi abazofakwa emagunjini elapha izifo zabantu besilisa KwaZulu-Natal.Lokhu kushiwo wuNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, uNksz Nomagugu Simelane eluleka amadoda ngokuthi kumele ajwayele ukuya ezikhungweni zempilo, ohlelweni lwakhe olusakazwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana njalo ngoLwesihlanu.UNksz Simelane uthe njengoba kuyinyanga yamadoda banezigcawu lapho bekhuluma khona namadoda, bewagqugquzela ukuthi angabekezeli uma egula aye emitholampilo."Amadoda, kakhulukazi asekhulile asitshele ukuthi ngabe ayaya emitholampilo manje kunzima ukuthi avuleleke akhulume nabahlengikazi besifazane, okujwayele ukuthi kube ngabesifazane ababaziyo. Bathi kunzima ukuthi ufike emtholampilo utshele umama noma intombazane yakwamakhelwane ngezinkinga zakho ezithinta ubuntu bakho. Lokhu sikubone ukuthi kubalulekile. “Singumnyango kumele sibandise abahlengi emagunjini elapha izifo zamadoda, khona amadoda engeke abe nenkinga yokuvuleleka. Lokho kuzosisiza nangokuthi uma amadoda asheshe afike emtholampilo nezifo zawo zisheshe zibonakale, zelashwe ukufa kungakakahambi kakhulu egazini kunokuthi afike esegula kakhulu. Kwesinye isikhathi nathi singeke sisakwazi ukuwasiza ngoba isifo sisuke sesihambe kakhulu," kusho uNksz Simelane.Uthe abahlengi bazokwandiswa okungenani ezikhungweni ezingu-80 esifundazwenni.“Uma sihlaziya ulwazi esinalo, sibonile ukuthi yingakho kwesinye isikhathi noma indoda isizidelile yaya esikhungweni sezempilo inezimpawu ezibonayo, okungenzeka ukuthi ngezokuthi inenkinga yomdlavuza wendlala yabesili, uma isifikile esibhedlela ingasho ukuthi iphethwe yini. Kunalokho ithi iphethwe yikhanda noma isho esinye isifo," kusho uNksz Simelane.Uthe okunye okuvelayo wukuthi amadoda ajwayele ukuya emtholampilo kunenkolelo yokuthi antekenteke noma athambile."Akulona iqiniso ukuthi indoda eya emtholampilo ithambile, kumele uma ungazizwa kahle uye esikhungweni sezempilo. Okunye okuyingozi okwenziwa ngamadoda wukuthi athembela ekutheni imiphumela yokuhlolwa kwamakhosikazi awo noma izintombi zawo, uma ithi aphile kahle, kusho ukuthi nawo ayaphila."Kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu aziyele yena emtholampilo ahlolwe ukuze azi isimo sakhe sempilo."UKUGONYWA kwamaphoyisa kuzosiza ukutheni enze umsebenzi wawo wokuvikela isizwe ngendlela nawo evikelekile.Lokhu kushiwo uNgqongqoshe wamaphoyisa uMnuz Bheki Cele, izolo ngesikhathi kuqala uhlelo lokugonywa kwamaphoyisa egonyelwa iCovid-19, eSoweto .Uthe kuyajabulisa ukuthi uhlelo lokugoma luyaqalwa yize  lufike sebelahlelekwe inqwaba yamaphoyisa abulawe yilolu bhubhane."Amaphoyisa angu-672 ashonile selokhu kuqale lolu bhubhane kuleli nyakenye, alinganiselwa ku32 000 ahaqwe yilolu bhubhane.
