Ukugula kwamaphoyisa kuholele ekutheni kuphazamiseke umsebenzi wawo wokuvikela isizwe,"  kusho uCele.Izolo uthe kulindeleke ukuthi kugonywe amaphoyisa angu-600."Ukuba kuya ngokwami ngabe amaphoyisa angu-180 000 azogonywa ngokushesha , ukuze sazi ukuthi amaphoyisa avikelekile , siyethemba ukuthi uhlelo oluqaliwe luzoshesha,"  kusho yena.UCele usho kanjena nje izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane kuleli zisalokhu zikhuphuka.Ongoti bezempilo bathi kulindeleke ukuthi ziqale ukwehla ngemuva kwesonto noma amabili ezayo.Izibalo zakamuva ezikhishwe ngesonto zikhomba ukuthi bangu-16 585 abantu abasha abahaqwe yileli gciwane  okuholele ekutheni isibalo sabahaqwe yileli gciwane senyukele ku -2 062 896Abashone emahoreni angu-24 bangu-333 okuholele ekutheni isibalo sababulewe yizifo ezihlobene naleli gciwane senyukele ku-61 840.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli osabambile, uNkk Mmamloko Kubayi- Ngubane, uthe bajabule kakhulu ngokuthi lolu hlelo luqale. “ Sinethemba lokuthi amaphoyisa ngeke asiphoxe azokwenza njengothisha abalulandela kahle uhlelo lokugoma,”  kusho yena.Umkhuzi wamaphoyisa kuleli uGeneral Khehla Sitole, uthe ukuqalwa kwalolu hlelo kuyingxenye yohlelo lwamaphoyisa  lokuphepha, iPolice Saftey Strategy  lokuthi amaphoyisa kumele aphephe wona kuqala ukuze nawo akwazi ukuvikela umphakathi.“ Amaphoyisa abambe iqhaza elikhulu ekulweni nobugebengu obuthinta imigomo kuleli, amaphoyisa yiwo abopha izigilamkhuba ezisabalalisa imigomo engombombayi kuleli ngakho kumele nawo avikeleke ukuze ahlale ekhona enqanda lezi zigameko,”  kusho yena. IYATHEMBISA imiphumela yakamuva ngocwaningo olubheka ukuthi ngabe umhlonyane uyayelapha yini iCovid-19 Lolu cwaningo lwenziwa emazweni amaningi kusukela   iMadagascar yaveza ukuthi isebenzisa umhlonyane omila kuleliya  lizwe owaziwa nge-artemisia annua  njengekhambi lokuzivikela nokwelapha lesi sifo. Abantu bakuleli lizwe babethi baphuza itiye lawo. Ngemuva kwalokhu kwaba nemibuzo eminingi eyayingaphenduleki ngalokhu, abanye bebuza ukuthi yini eyelaphayo ngabe amaqabunga, isiqu noma izimpande. Abanye befuna ukwazi ukuthi uwuphuza uma usugula noma owokuzivikela, abanye bebuza ukuthi ngabe umhlonyane wakuleli i-artemisia Afra nawo uyelapha yini. Lokhu kuholele ekutheni amazwe amaningi enze ucwaningo kubhekwe ukuthi ngabe ungasiza yini umhlonyane.Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO)   isanda kumemezela ukuthi  umshanguzo owelapha i-malaria owenziwe ngomhlonyane, i-artesunate ungeminye yemishanguzo emithathu ehlolwayo ukuthi iyayelapha yini iCovid-19 enikeze ithemba esigabeni sokuqala socwaningo , okuzokwenziwa ngayo isigaba sesibili socwaningo.I-artesunate isetshenziselwa ukwelapha i-malaria futhi sekuphele iminyaka eminiingi isetshenziswa. Yona neminye imishanguzo emibili inike ithemba ngesikhathi ihlolwa e-laboratory.Imiphumela yesigaba sokuqala salolu cwaningo iveze ukuthi  i-artesunate iyakwehlisa ukuvuvukala, kukholakala ukuthi ingasiza ekuvikeleni  ukonakala kwamaphaphu okwenzeka ezigulini eziphethwe yiCovid-19.Umqondisi weWHO uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus, uthe ukuthola ikhambi lokwelapha iCovid-19 kuseyisidingo esikhulu.Umhlonyane wakuleli owaziwa nge-artemisa afra  ungelinye lamakhambi esintu elisetshenziselwa ukwelapha umkhuhlane. Abelaphi bendabuko bathi uthakwa namanye amakhambi kwenziwe isiphungo.IWHO imemezela lokhu nje baningi ososayensi abenza ucwaningo ngomhlonyane emazweni ehlukene. NgoMeyi abacwaningi beNyuvesi iColumbia neyaseNew York bamemezele ukuthi imiphumela yocwaningo lwabo obelwenziwa e-laboratory inikeze ithemba lokuthi umhlonyane uyalelapha leli gciwane .Olunye ucwaningo olushicilelwe emqingweni wezempilo, iJournal  Ethnopharmacology ,eshicilelwe ngoFebhuwari luveze ukuthi leli khambi alikuvikeli ekutheni uthole igciwane kodwa livikela ukuthi leli gciwane liziphindaphinde uma selingene emzimbeni.Amanye amazwe enza ucwaningo ngomhlonyane yiDenmark neGermany. Wonke amazwe enza ucwaningo, ucwaningo lwawo lusasesigabeni sokuqala .Umhlonyane uhlukene kaningi izinhlobo ezidumile, i-artemisia  annua,  artemisia Afra, i-wormwood , i-silver mound neminye. Abacwaningi bazama ukuthola ukuthi kulezi zinhlobo iyiphi esiza ukwelapha iCovid-19.LUZOGXILA ezindaweni zasemakhaya ucwaningo oluzobe lubheka ukuzishintsha kwegciwane lesandulela ngculazi, ngemuva kokuhlasela kweCovid-19 ezweni.Lokhu kushiwo nguSolwazi Frank Tanser waseStellenbosch University, ongusosayensi ozobe ehola ucwaningo oluzobe lwenziwa yile nyuvesi ngokubambisana neNyuvesi yaKwaZulu Natal, i-Africa Health Research Institute (AHRI), i-University of Lincoln, i-University of Heidelberg, i-University of Washington, iNew York University ne- University of Cincinnati.Uthe ulwazi oluzosetshenziswa woluke lwenziwa yi-AHRI ngaleli gciwane ezindaweni zasemakhaya enyakatho yeKwaZulu-Natal.Lolu cwaningo lusanda kunikwa imali enguR40 million esikhungweni i-US National Institutes of Health (NIH).UTanser uthe lolu olwaziwa ngeThe Changing Face of HIV in the era of Covid-19,  luzosiza ekutheni luveze isithombe esiyiso ngaleli gciwane ngoba libakhahlameza kakhulu abantu abahluphekayo."Imizamo yokwehlisa ukutheleleka kwabantu ngaleli gciwane  nokwelashwa kwalo eyenziwayo ayikafinyeleli esigabeni okumele ukuthi iba kuso, ukuze linqandeke. Njengamanje sibhekene nokuthi amantombazane amancane yiwona atheleleka kakhulu ngaleli gciwane. Esikubonayo manje sekuyashintsha, sesiyanda nesibalo sabesifazane asebevuthiwe abatheleleka ngaleli gciwane," kusho yena.Uthe iNingizimu Afrika inesibalo esiphezulu sabantu abahaqwe yiHIV kunawo wonke amazwe emhlabeni, ngakho ucwaningo olunjengalolu lubalulekile."Esikwaziyo wukuthi imishanguzo yokuthithibalisa iHIV isiza ekutheni bangabi baningi abantu abashonayo bebulawa yilesi sifo. Uma beqhubeka banda abantu abahaqekayo kuzogcina kufika esigabeni lapho izwe lingasakwazi ukuthengela bonke abahaqekile imishanguzo," kusho yena.Uthe ucwaningo oluzothatha iminyaka emihlanu, luzobe lubheka ukuthi ukuhlasela kweCovid-19 kuleli kwenze ukuthi leli gciwane liziphathe kanjani kukho okuhlanganisa nokusabalala kwalo nendlela eliziphatha ngayo egazini nokunye.Uthe imiphumela yalo izosetshenziselwa ukuqhamuka namasu amasha okwelapha nokuvikela igciwane, okubalwa ukukhuthazwa kwabantu ukuthi basebenzise imishanguzo yokuzivikela kulo, iPre-exposure prophylaxis (Prep).IPhini leSekela-Shansela neNhloko yekolishi lesayensi ethinta ezempilo e-UKZN, uSolwazi Busisiwe Ncama, lithe: "Ngithanda ukuhalalisela ithimba labacwaningi nenhloko yabo ngokuthola uxhaso lweNIH. Lo msebenzi ubaluleke kakhulu ekusizeni izwe ukuthi liqonde ukuziphathe kweHIV ngemuva kweCOVID-19, ukuze kulungiselwe isikhathi esizayo ezifweni ezithathelanayo."PHILI MJOLIINHLANGANO yodokotela iSouth African Medical Association (SAMA), inxusa uhulumeni ukuthi aqinise imithetho yokuhamba kwabantu ukuze kunqandwe ukusabala kweCovid-19, ukuze isigaba sesithathu singeke sisheshe sihlasele.UDkt Mvuyisi Mzukwa, oyiphini likasihlalo wenhlangano, uthi kumanje kunegciwane lakuleli eselizishintshile, nelitholakale e-India nelinye elitholakale e-United States (US).Uthi bafisa ukuthi uhulumeni avale ukuhamba kwabantu phakathi kuka-10 ebusuku kuya-5 ekuseni, kuvalwe nemingcele yakuleli kuphinde kuqinisekiswe ukuthi ababaningi abantu abaya ezikhungweni zokugomela iCovid-19."Njengamanje uhlelo lokugomela iCovid-19 seluqalile kodwa ukulawulwa kokuhamba kwabantu kusadingeka ngoba umjovo okugonywa ngawo uthatha isikhathi ngaphambi kokuthi wakhe amasosha omzimba azobhekane negciwane uma kwenzeka lingena umuntu,“ kusho uDkt Mzukwa.Uthe kuthatha amasonto amathathu kuya kwamane ukuthi umzimba wakhe amasosha azobhekana negciwane. “ Kusazothatha isikhathi ukuthi sibone umehluko wokuthi abantu sebegomile. Okunye okumele umphakathi ukwazi ukuthi umgomo awuvikeli ukuthi igciwane lingene kodwa uvikela ukuthi umuntu agule kakhulu aze adinge ukuya esibhedlela," kuchaza udokotela.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli uDkt Zweli Mkhize, phambilini ephawula ngalokhu wathi ukuqiniswa kwemithetho ukuze kunqandwe ukusabalala kweCovid-19,  ngeke kugwemeke.Phakathi kwemithetho engase iqiniswe, ukulawulwa kokudayiswa kotshwala, ukwehliswa kwesibalo sabantu abavumelekile ukuthi bahlangane, kulawulwe isikhathi sokuhamba kwabantu ebusuku.Imibiko yabezindaba iveze ukuthi umkhandlu wongqongqoshe ababhekele iCorona kuleli, iNational Coronavirus Command Council (NCCC) ube nomhlangano ngoLwesibili,  lapho ubudingida ngezindlela ezingalandelwa njengoba kubonakala zikhula izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19. Lokhu kusho ukuthi isivunguvungu sesithathu sokuhlasela kwegciwane sesifikile. PHILI MJOLILUYAQHUBEKA  uhlelo lokugomela iCovid-19 kusetshenziswa umgomo wakwaJohnson&Johnson obumisiwe kuleli.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, uthe ukugonywa kwabasebenzi bezempilo okwenziwa ngaphansi kohlelo locwaningo, iSisonke Protocol, luzoqhubeka ezikhungweni ezingu-95 zokugoma ezikuleli.Uthe isikhungo esigunyaza ukusetshenziswa kwemithi kuleli, iSouth African Health Products Authority (Sahpra)  senza isiphakamiso ePhalamende sokuthi ukugoma kuqhubeke kodwa kuqashwe.Uthe njengamanje imigomo ekhona, okuzogonywa ngayo ngaphansi kwalolu hlelo, ingu-500 000.Lo mgomo wamiswa kusagonywe abasebenzi abangaphansi kuka-300 000 kwabangu-1.2 million."Ukugoma esigabeni sokuqala kulindeleke ukuthi kuphele ngoMeyi 16. Sizimisele  ukugoma abasebenzi abasele ngobuningi babo, yize kuke kwaba khona ukuphazamiseka. Sinxusa abasebenzi bezempilo nabelaphi bendabuko abangakabhaliseli ukugoma ukuthi babhalise kwi-website yoMnyango wezeMpilo," kusho uDkt Mkhize.Ukugoma ngalo ngomo kwamiswa kuleli ngemuva kokuthi kutholakale abesifazane abayisithupha e-United States benesifo esingajwayekile, sokuba namahlule egazini okusolwa umgomo, okubizwa ngeVaccine Induced Thrombotic Thrombocytopenia (VITT). Manje sebeyisishiyagalombili abesifazane abajove ngawo base beba neVITT."Ngesikhathi kumiswa ukugoma ngalo mgomo kwakusanikezwa ososayensi ithuba lokuthi bacwaninge bese bekhipha isinqumo sokuthi lo mgomo ungasetshenziswa kanjani. Ucwaningo luveze ukuthi amathuba okuthi umuntu abe nalesi sifo ngoyedwa kwabayisigidi. Abesifazane okungenzeka bangenwe yilesi sifo ngabaneminyaka ephakathi kuka-18 kuya ku-48. Nakhona kuthiwa amathuba okuthi igazi libe namahlule mancane. Ososayensi emhlabeni benze isiphakamiso sokuthi kuqhutshekwe nokugoma ngalo mgomo,"  kusho  uDkt Mkhize.Uthe kuleli uphiko olwenza ucwaningo ngemithi, iSouth African Medical Research Council  (SAMRC), wuMnyango wezeMpilo neSahpra nezinye izikhungo zezempilo bazobe bewuqaphile umgomo ."Bonke ababhalisele ukugoma ngalo mgomo bazonikezwa ifomu eshoyo ukuthi yibuphi ubungozi balo mgomo. Bazoyisayina ngaphambi kokuthi bagome,"  kusho uMkhize.YIZE umgomo weCoronavirus usufikile kuleli, ezinye izikole ezizimele sezivuliwe kanti ezikahulumeni zizovulwa maduzane, abanye abazali basazoba netwetwe njengoba izingane zabo zibuyela ezikoleni ngoba besaba ukuthi zingase zithelelane ngaleli gciwane.Uvalo  lwabazali abanezingane ezifunda amabanga aphansi ludalwa wukuthi zikhonze ukudlala ndawonye uma kuyikhefu noma uma sekuphume isikole. UDkt Bongani Nxumalo, uthe kumele abazali bakhumbule ukuthi isivunguvungu seCovid-19 sibhubhisa wonke umuntu ongazinakekeli nongayihloniphi imigomo ebekiwe. Uthe ukuqikelela kwabazali ngaso sonke isikhathi kuzosiza kakhulu ekutheni bagweme ukuthi  izingane zabo zizithole sezithelelana ngegciwane.“Isivunguvungu sesibili asibhubhisi abadala kuphela kodwa nabancane siyabahlasela. Lo mkhuhlane awufani neminye. Izimpawu zeCovid-19 sesike sazibona  ebantwaneni abaneminyaka emibili kanjalo nabaneminyaka engaphezulu. Leli gciwane linamathela emlonyeni, emakhaleni, emankankeni, emaphashini nakwezinye izitho zomzimba bese liyagadla kumuntu osuke ezwa izinhlungu kula malungu omzimba. Ingane ibanjwa yisisu esibuhlungu noma izwele ukushisa ngendlela exakile noma iphelelwe ngamandla.” Uthe kubalulekile ukuthi abazali baqhubeke nokufundisa izingane zabo ngokubaluleka kokuthi zisebenzise izifonyo nokokuhlanza i zandla ngaso sonke isikhathi. Uthe ukufundisa izingane ngobumqoka bokuzinakekela kuzolekelela kakhulu ekutheni zihlezi ziqwashile futhi zifundisekile ngobungozi begciwane. Ephetha uthe kumele abazali baqinisekise ngaso sonke isikhathi ukuthi izingane ziyayilandela imigomo ebekiwe  ukuze ibonakale imiphumela yokulwa nalolu bhubhane. UBUDEDENGU bokuya ocansini olungaphephile lungakushiya unesifo socansi esingelapheki.Lona ngumlayezo kaNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, uNksz Nomagugu Simelane, othe esikhathini samanje akusewona umsebenzi wowesilisa ukuthi aphathe amakhondomu ukuze owesifazane azivikele kodwa bobabili abathandanayo kumele babe namakhondomu."Kulesi sifundazwe izibalo zabantu abangenwa yizifo zocansi ziyakhuphuka okusho ukuthi ivangeli lokuthi abantu abajabule bazibheke kumele silishumayele kakhulu kunakuqala," kusho ungqongqoshe.Usho kanjena nje ngokwekhalenda lezempilo, isonto eledlule bekungelokuqwashisa nokufundisa ngezifo zocansi ezithathelanayo, iSTI/Condom Week.Izifo zocansi ezivamile kuleli, iHIV/ Aids ehaqa abantu abaningi. I-HIV idala ingculaza, futhi iphazamisa amasosha omzimba ekutheni akwazi ukulwa nezifo.Uthe ukunqotshwa kweHIV kuleli kulele ekutheni abantu bahlolwe lesi sifo basazi isimo sabo.Inhlangano yengculazi emhlabeni, i-UNIAIDS izibekele umgomo wokuthi ngo-2030 babe ngu-95% abantu abahlolwe lesi sifo, u95% wabahlolile uqale imishanguzo yokuthithibalisa igciwane, u95% wasebedla imishanguzo igciwane emizimbeni yabo libe sesigabeni sokuthi alisakwazi ukuziphindaphinda, i95-95-95 strategy,  eNingizimu Afika uMnyango wezeMpilo njengamanje uthe  bangu-94% abasahlolwe leli gciwane, u78% wabo usuqale  imishanguzo yokulithithibalisa, u89% wabadla imishanguzo igciwane emizimbeni yabo alisakwazi ukuziphindaphinda.IHuman papillomavirus (HPV), isifo socansi esivamile , abantu abaningi abane-HPV abanazo izimpawu kodwa bayakwazi ukuthelela abanye ngaso. Izimpawu zaso zibonakala ngokuhamba kwesikhathi okuvame ukuthi kube izinsumpa esithweni sangasese noma esikhumbeni ezizungezile.Alikho ikhambi lokwelapha leli gciwane,  izinsumpa kuyenzeka ziziphelele zingelashwanga. Uma kwenzeka umuntu elashwa lesi sifo kususwa izinsumpa. Njengemanje sekunomgomo  ovika izinhlobo ze-HPV kuzo okukhona nohlobo oluvamile oludala izinsumpa esithweni sangasese noludala umdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho kwabesifazane. Lo mgomo unikezwa amantombazane aneminyaka ewu-10 kuya ku-12.iGenital herpesIsifo esithathelana ngocansi esivame ukubonakala ngokuthi onaso ezwe kubuhlungu  esithweni sangasese abe nezilonda kodwa siyelapheka.IGonorrhoeaIsifo esithathelana ngokocansi, esidala ubuhlungu nokuphuma koketshezi esithweni sangasese,  uma singelashwanga sidala izinkinga zenzalo.iSyphilisIsifo socansi osithola ngokuya ocansini nonaso, uqala ngokuba nesilonda esithweni sangasese  esingebuhlungu, kwabaningi siyaziphelela bese kumila amaqhutshana nawo ayaziphelela kungabe kusabakhona phawu kuze kube isifo sesihambe kakhulu egazini sesihlasela imizwa yamehlo, inhliziyo nobuchopho.1953: UFICWA wukufa uJoseph Stalin, eseMoscow, kanti nguyena obesengumholi weSoviet Union kusukela ngo-1924.1960: UMCULI waseMelika, u-Elvis Presley, ubuyela ekhaya emuva kokuqeqeshwa iminyaka emibili embuthweni wamasosha.1966: KUPHAHLAZEKA ibhanoyi i-A BOAC British Boeing 707 eMount Fuji, eJapan, maqede kufe abagibeli abangu-124.1956:  INKANTOLO enkulu yase-US igunyaza umthetho olwa nokubandlululwa kwabafundi ngokwebala ezikoleni, emakolishi nasemanyuvesi.1963:  UDLULA emhlabeni umculi uPatsy Cline, obalwa nabanye abadumile e-United States of America (USA).1985: IZIPHATHIMANDLA zaseMexico, zithola umzimba ka-Enrique “Kike” Salaazar, obedume ngokuba ngungqondongqondo wezidakamizwa.1986: KUBA nomcimbi omkhulu wezindondo zamafilimu iBritish Film and Television (Baftas). Ifilimu enedumela elikhulu, iThe Killing Fields ihlonishwa ngendondo.1994: KUBOSHWA umculi waseMelika, odumile uGrace Slick, ubekwa icala lokukhomba iphoyisa ngesibhamu.1997:  IZITHUNYWA zaseNorth Korea naseSouth Korea, zihlangana okokuqala ngqa eNew York, ngemuva kweminyaka ewu-25 ziyobhunga ngoxolo.2003: KUFA abantu abangu-17 bakwa-Israel, ngemuva kokuqhuma kwebhomu eHaifa.2012: ABAQAPHI abangu-27 base-Iraq, babulawa ngesihluku ngamadoda angaziwa, afika azenza amaphoyisa. 2013: UMENGAMELI waseVenezuela, uMnuz Hugo Chavez, udlula emhlabeni eneminyaka ewu-58, yobudala.UKWENYUSELWA kwezwe ezigabeni zokuvalwa kwezwe eziphezulu yinto engeke igwemeke.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba ethi maningi amathuba okuthi lokhu kwenzeke njengoba zilokhu zikhula izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane kuleli.Ngeledlule izibalo zabahaqwe yileli gciwane zike zaba ngu-3000 ngosuku. Uqhube wathi umkhandlu wongqongqoshe ababhekelele iCorona kuleli, iNational Command Council (NCC) eholwa uNgqongqoshe wezekuBusa ngokuBambisana, uDkt Nkosazana Dlamini-Zuma, nezinhlaka ezithintekayo bazoba nomhlangano babonisane ngesinyathelo okumele sithathwe ukuze kunqandwe ukusabalala kweCovid-19."Uma izibalo zikhuphuka izigaba zokuvalwa kwezwe zizokwenyuswa, uma zehla kuzoxegiswa," kusho uDkt Mkhize.Seziqalile neziphakamiso zokuthi uhulumeni ubheke ukuthi ngeke yini kumiswe ukudayiswa kotshwala nogwayi ngoba kunenkolelo yokuthi kunomthelela ekutheni abantu bathelelane ngaleli gciwane.Imboni yabadayisa utshwala kuleli, iSouth African Liquor Brandowners Association (Salba), ne-Vinpro ithe  uma uhulumeni engathatha isinqumo sokumisa ukudayisa utshwala futhi uzobe ebeka engcupheni  imisebenzi engu-200 yabasebenza kule mboni.UMnuz Sibani Mngadi, weSalba,  uthe uhulumeni akakaze aziveze izizathu ezibambekayo zokuthi kungani evala ukuthi utshwala budayiswe, ababuthengayo babuphuzele emakhaya  ngezimpelasonto.Ngeledlule ikhabhinethi lelule isikhathi sokuthi leli lizwe lithathwe njengeliyinhlekelele okuzophela ngoJune 15.UNdunankulu waseGauteng, uMnuz David Makhura, ngeledlule umemezele ukuthi sesingenile isivunguvungu sesithathu kulesi sifundazwe.I-National Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD) ngeledlule imemezele ukuthi iFree State ingesinye sezifundazwe isivunguvungu sesithathu esesifikile kuyo nakuba izinombolo zabahaqwa yileli zingakafinyeleli esibalweni esibekiwe esisho lokhu kodwa ukwenyuka kakhulu kwezibalo zakhona sekukhomba khona.Izibalo zakamuva zabahaqwe yiCovid-19 kuleli, ezikhishwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli ngoMgqibelo, zikhomba ukuthi bangu-2750 abantu abahaqwe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 okuholele ukuthi isibalo sabahaqwe yileli gciwane senyukele ku-1 611 143. Ababulelwe yizifo ezisondelele nalesi sifo ngesikhathi esifanayo bangu-59 okuholele ekutheni isibalo sabahaqwe yileli gciwane senyukele ku-55 183, kubo abangu-20 bashone eGauteng, abangu-18 abaseNorthern Cape , abayisishiyagalombili abaKwaZulu-Natal, abayisithupha abaseWestern Cape,  abahlanu abaseFree State, eMpumalanga kushone ababili.UmbuzoNgibingelele MaGumede nabalandeli. Ngiyintokazi eneminyaka engu-23. Ngithandana nobhuti oneminyaka engu-28. Sesiside isikhathi sindawonye iminyaka eyisishiyagalolunye. Inkinga imi kanje, ngikhulelwe nginezinyanga ezine. Ngike ngakhulelwa ngaphambili kabili. Izisu ziphuma, wathi asiye kumuntu silungise le nkinga. Saya-ke kumuntu njengoba sengikhulelwe futh izinto zikhombisa ukuhamba kahle. Inkinga yakhe ubesebenza ehola njalo ngolwesihlanu, engabuyi endlini. Ubebuya ekusen njalo uma eholile, alove nasemsebenzini uma imali isekhona. Kwenzeka-ke waphelelwa wumsebenzi ubhuti, njengamanje akasasebenzi ngezimpelasonto. Njalo uyaduka, abuye ezodla edakwe emanzi. Aphinde ahambe ngoze ngimbone ngoMsombuluko. Manje angazi noma uyajola noma ingoba uphethwe umzwangedwa wokuphelelwa umsebenzi. Kwenzekile emsebenzini bamfakela imali, wathatha enye wayo-laybuyer  izinto zengane, wabuya wanginika i-slip. Ngizamile ukukhuluma naye ngendaba yokungabuyi endlini ngezimpelasonto, wathi uyaxolisa, naye akazi ungenwe yini. Ngicela ningisize ningibonise.ImpenduloSawubona sisi, ngiyayizwa inkinga yakho kodwa bekumele umnqande esasebenza umyeni wakho, umkhuze ngokulova nokudakwa ngoba lokho bekusho ukubeka engcupheni umsebenzi wakhe njengoba esevele waxoshwa nje. Ngokubona kwami umyeni wakho ubhekene nengcindezi ehambisana nomzwangedwa kanye nokhwantalala. Okubuhlungu ukuthi nawe ukhulelwe futhi udinga ukwesekwa ngakho ke nawe kuzoba nzima ngeke ukwazi ukweseka omunye umuntu kodwa futhi ngeke ngithi mlahle ndawo ngoba isoka lakho futhi ubaba wezingane zakho, kodwa nje eqinisweni indoda yakho ihlulekile ukuzicabangela. Okwamanje sisi gxila ekutheni ukhulelwe, yikhona ungeke uzithole nawe usuphethwe umzwangedwa.OWAZALWA engumuntu wesilisa, uNomalizwi "MC" Mhlongo, kodwa wazishintsha waba ngowesifazane, uthi akukho nkomo yowesifazane engamelana neyakhe ocansini nowesilisa. UNomalizwi (31) wasesigcemeni sakwaF, eMlaza, ofundisa e-Old Mill High eMpangeni, uthi wazalwa enguMlungisi ngaphambi kokuguqula ubulili bakhe emuva kokunukubezwa mihla namalanga yisihlobo sakhe eseneminyaka eyisishiyagalombili."Ayikho (inanazi) eyofika kule yokuzenzela, ulozolo."Ebuzwa ukuthi wazi ngani ukuthi unolozolo lwenanazi, uNomalizwi uthe watshelwa yindoda yakhe."Umlingani wami ngiyazi ukuthi kungenzeka ukuthi wayeseke wayizwa eyomuntu wesifazane ngokudalwa. Eyami ngeyokuzenzela, okusho ukuthi kunomehluko." Uthe emuva kokuzitika ngocansi ngosuku lokuqala nesithandwa sakhe, wasibuza ukuthi sizwe kunjani? Uthe asiwuvalanga umlomo ngobumnandi esibuzwile.Ebuzwa uNomalizwi ukuthi kwabanjani ngosuku lokuqala ayangalo ocansini, uthe kwafana nokwenzeka kuwo wonke umuntu wesifazane. "Kodwa mina bekumele ngilinde ukuze ngiphole ekuhlinzweni." Exinwa ngemibuzo ngempilo yakhe yangasese, uNomalizwi uthe ucela ukungagxili kuyo ngoba eyangasese. Le ntokazi seyidume kakhulu ezinkundleni zokuxhumana kangangoba ize yaqokwa emunxeni weBest Traditional Social Media Influencer kumaSouth African Traditional Music Achievement (Satma) Awards aseMbombela Stadium, eMpumalanga, ngo-Okthoba 1.UNomalizwi ukubonge kakhulu ukuqokwa kulo mqhudelwano ngoba kusho ukuthi igama lakhe selisematheni ezinkundleni zokuxhumana."Kusho ukuthi sewuyabonakala nomsebenzi engiwenzayo wokubuyisa ukuzwana kubantu, kungakhathaleki ukuthi bangobani, baphumaphi futhi bawuluphi uhlaka nokuthi baphila mpiloni."UNomalizwi uthe ukuqokwa kukodwa kumenza afane nomuntu osenqobile."Okokuwina sekuyoba ibhansela uma kwenzeka, kodwa abantu bazongazi futhi nginesiqiniseko bazothanda ukusebenza nami. Kubalandeli bami engibabiza ngomndeni kwiFacebook, ngiyabonga ukungiphakamisa ningangazi nokungamukela ezimpilweni zenu," kusho uNomalizwi oqhathwe nomlingisi weDurban Gen, uNelisiwe Sibiya, imbongi uBrighton Shandu, Yenkosinabadala Makhoba, Zamambo Mkhize, Audrey Sikhosana, Bafana Mkhize, Thato Angel, Thando Mahlangu, Faith Mgobhozi noTinyiko Khoza.Uthe uhlale ephunga izesheli ezimfuna njengomphefumulo nezimthanda njengemali. UNomalizwi, obuye aphathe izinhlelo zemicimbi, ubeqokwe kumaSebenza Woman Awards emunxeni ofanayo.*Ukuvotela uNomalizwi naqhathwe nabo, ungena kulewebsite: www.satmaawards.co.zaUmbuzo:Ngingumuntu wesilisa oneminyaka engu-30. Kunosisi engithandana naye othe kancane ukukhula kimi ngeminyaka. Ngiyamthanda  ngenhliziyo yami yonke. Inkinga ukuthi sigcina ngokukhuluma ezinkundleni zokuxhumana kuphela. Uma ngimshayela ucingo akayibambi iselula futhi akangishayeli ucingo. Akanaso isikhathi sami kodwa uma esho uthi uyangithanda. Manje mina sengiqala ukukhathazeka. Ingiphatha kabi le nto ngoba ngizama ngakho konke okusemandleni ami ukuthi eze kimi, ngisho ngabe imali anginayo kahle. Akhulume kabi ubona ukuthi uyenyanya. Ngiyamthanda futhi nemali ngiyamfakela uma nginayo, ngisho engazoza kimi. Manje iyangihlukumeza le nto yokungabonani kwethu futhi angifuni ukulahlekelwa nguye.Impendulo:Yebo, ngiyezwa impela uyamthanda kodwa into engikhathazayo ukuthi umthanda kanjani umuntu eningakaze nibonane naye kodwa omazela ezinkundleni zokuxhumana? Wazi kanjani noma umuntu okhona ngempela yini loyo? Isibindi nje sokufakela imali umuntu ongamazi nangamehlo, usithathaphi ngempela? Yini indaba, azikho yini izintombi ngakini noma usindwa yimali? Lo muntu ukucacisela ngokusobala ukuthi akakufuni futhi akazimisele ngokuza nokubonana nawe. Into nje ayifunayo ukuzidlela imali yakho, elokhu ekukhohlisa ngokuthi uyakuthanda.Vuka emaqandeni, ushele umuntu ozokuthanda! akwazi nokuza kuwe uma umdinga.Alukho uthando lweqiniso ongaluthola ezinkundleni zokuxhumana bhuti wami, ngaphandle-ke uma ufuna ukuzichithela isikhathi ngempilo yakho. ABANTU abanesifo sokushintsha kwebala lesikhumba abazalwe nalo libe ngelimhlophe, i-vitiligo kumele balamukele ngoba alikho ikhambi lokuselapha.UDkt Fundile Nyathi weProactive Health Solutions, uthe iningi labantu abahlaselwa yilesi sifo bayehluleka ukusemukela, bagcine bephethwe wukhwantalala nengcindezi yomphefumulo kanti lesi sifo asiyona ingozi futhi ayikho indawo eba buhlungu uma sikuphethe.Uthe lesi sifo sidalwa ukuthi amasosha omzimba akuma-cells akha ibala lesikhumba, i-pigmentation, avukelane wodwa alwe noma wukulimala kwesikhumba.Uthe lokhu kuvukelana kudala ukuthi isikhumba sibe namabala amhlophe engxenyeni ethize okungaba yizingxenye zomzimba ezinendawo evulekile okuvame ukuthi kube umlomo, amakhala noma amehlo."Lesi sifo asifani ne-Albinism lapho umuntu uzalwa seyenzekile futhi yona yenzeka emzimbeni wonke. I-vitiligo ngokujwayelekile ivamise ukuvela kubantu abaneminyaka engaphansi kuka-30. Kwabanye iyavela kodwa ingasabalali kakhulu kodwa uma onayo eke waba nengcindezi yomphefumulo noma wukhwantalala iyasabalala kakhulu," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi abukho ubuhlungu abantu abaphila nalesi sifo abanabo ngaphandle kokushintsha kwebala libe mhlophe. Uma kodwa ihlasele emehlweni, amehlo abo ayezwela elangeni kudingeke ukuthi bafake izibuko. Kudingeka futhi basebenzise ukhilimu ovikela ukuthi isikhumba singalinyazwa yilanga ngoba leyo ngxenye emhlophe iyalimala uma ishiswe yilanga."Abantu abaningi abanalesi sifo bavamise ukuphathwa yingcindezi yomphefumulo nokhwantalala ngoba bengemukeli isimo sabo kuze kube sengathi kukhona ubuhlungu abanabo kanti cha, sona uqobo isifo asibuhlungu," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi ibala elimhlophe uma selenzekile awukho umuthi wokulibuyisela emuva noma into engenziwa wudokotela ukushintsha leso simo. “Kwabanye kuyenzeka isikhumba sizibuyele sona ebaleni laso elidala kodwa odokotela bayazama ukunqanda ukuthi i-vitiligo isabalale emzimbeni," kusho yena."Odokotela okwamanje abazi ukuthi kungani ezinye iziguli ibala lazo libuye libuyele. Ososayensi emhlabeni basenza ucwaningo esinethemba lokuthi luzosinikeza izimpendulo," kusho uNyathi.Okunye okuvelayo ngalesi sifo ukuthi kuyenzeka abazalanayo badluliselane sona ngofuzo."Lesi sifo akusona isifo esivamile. Bambalwa kakhulu abantu abanaso ngakho ngeke kwenzeke ukuthi babe baningi abasithole ngofuzo. Izwe elinabantu abaningi abanalesi sifo yi-India kodwa lokho akwenziwa ukuthi bawuhlanga oluthile. Kwenziwa ukuthi isikhumba sabo sinsundu ngakho siyashesha ukubonakala uma beqhathaniswa nabantu abanebala elimhlophe," kusho yena. NJALO emizuzwini emibili abesifazane abangu-250 000, ikakhulu abasebancane, batheleleka ngeHIV e-Afrika.Inhlangano yezempilo iBroadreach Development, yethule ucwaningo olushaqisayo ngesimo sokutheleleka kwamantombazane ngaleli gciwane.Ucwaningo lushicilelwe emqingweni wezindaba ezithinta leli gciwane emhlabeni jikelele, i-United Nations Programme on HIV/AIDS (UNAIDS). Kuhlaluka ukuthi amantombazane amancane ajwayele ukubandakanyeka ebungozini kuba yilawo aya ocansini esemancane, ukungawasebenzisi amakhondomu nokuya ocansini nabantu abaningi.UDkt Veni Naidoo wocwaningo uthe ngokuvamile abantu abasha bazigaxa engozini bedudana ngoba befuna kubonakale ukuthi nabo bayakwazi ukwenza izinto ezenziwa ngabanye ontanga yabo.Ucwaningo olwenziwe yile nhlangano ngo-2021 luveza ukuthi abantu abasha abatheleleka ngeHIV bangu80% wesibalo sabatheleleka ngegciwane njalo ngonyaka."Abantu besifazane kunamathuba amaningi okuthi bathole iHIV kontanga yabo besilisa ngenxa yokuthi bajwayele ukuthola ingcindezi ehambisana namasiko nenkolo eholela ekutheni bazithole sebeya ocansini nabantu besilisa bengahlelile," kusho uDkt Naidoo.UDkt Naidoo uthe abesifazane basabhekana nengcindezi ephindaphindiwe uma beqhathaniswa nabesilisa uma kumele bazikhethele ukuthi baya nobani ocansini."Kweminye imiphakathi akwamukelekile ukuthi umuntu wesifazane azikhethele, ukhethelwa umndeni, yena akakwazi ukusiphikisa leso sinqumo esesithathiwe sokuthi uyaganiswa. Okunye okudala ingcindezi ukuthi abantu besifazane abakwazi ukuphumela obala batshele abazwana nabo ukuthi bafuna ukuthi kusetshenziswe ikhondomu. Kuvame ukuthi owesilisa abe mdala, owesifazane emncane futhi ondliwa nguye owesilisa. Manje kuba nzima ukuthi owesifazane asho ukuthi ufuna kwenzekeni. Zonke lezi zizathu ziholela ekutheni amantombazane abe sengozini ephindaphindiwe yokuthola leli gciwane kunontanga yabo besilisa nakwabadala.Uthe ucwaningo abebelwenza luveza ukuthi zikhona izinhlelo zikahulumeni ezihlelelwe ukuthi zisize abantu abasha kubo okubalwa namantombazane. “Ezinye zalezi zinhlelo, uhlelo lwamaphilisi anikezwa abantu abangenalo igciwane ukuze abavikele bangalitholi igciwane iPre-exposure Prophylaxis, iPrEP, uhlelo lokuhlelwa komndeni, uhlelo lokwelulekwa kwabantu ngokuthola abantwana, ukwelashwa kwezifo zocansi, ukwelulekwa ngempilo jikelele ukuze abantu bathathe izinqumo benolwazi kodwa ngesikhathi seCovid-19 sinyukile isibalo samantombazane amancane akhulelwe," kusho yena.Uthe okunye, amantombazane okumele akuqaphele wulwazi olubhalwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, ngoba abanye uthe bavamise ukuyeka imishanguzo yabo ngoba befunde izinto ezibhalwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.Uthe ngesikhathi benza ucwaningo bathole ukuthi abantu abasha abaningi abasazi isimo sabo seHIV, yize kunjalo abakholwa ukuthi basengcupheni yokuthola leli gciwane noma ukulidlulisela kwabanye ngakho abasiboni isidingo sokusebenzisa izindlela zokuzivikela. “Ukuzihlola ukuthi awunalo yini leli gciwane kungenye yezindlela zokuzinakekela esizikhuthazayo ukuthi abantu abasha bazijwayele," kusho yena.UDkt Andrew Kambugu wesikhungo esicubungula ngezifo ezithelelanayo e-Uganda, i-Ugandan Institute for Infectious Diseases, uthe ucwaningo abalwenzile luveza ukuthi abesifazane abasebencane base-Afrika baneHIV kodwa kabanalo ulwazi lokuthi banayo."Ukuze kuzanywe indlela engenza ukuthi abantu besilisa baye emitholampilo, sesiqale ukwenza imitholampilo yesikhashana ebekwa eduze kwalapho kuhlala khona abantu ngoba imitholampilo ekhona amadoda athi awaphathwa kahle kuyo," kusho uKambugu.Njengoba zivulwa ngoLwesithathu izikole, abafundi balangazelele ukubuyela esikoleni. Ongoti bezempilo bathi kubalulekile ukuthi abazali ngaphambi kokuthi bahambise izingane esikoleni babheke izinto ezithile zempilo. Bathi lokhu kuqinisekisa ukuthi izingane zabo zifunda kahle, aziphazanyiswa wukugula obekungavikeleka ukube zihanjiswe emitholampilo noma kodokotela ngaphambi kokuya esikoleni.UDkt Estelle Lawrence obhekele ezempilo nokuzinakekela, eMnyangweni wezeMpilo eWestern Cape, ukhuthaza abazali ngezinto ezisemqoka okumele bazibhekisise ezinganeni ngaphambi kokuthi bazibuyisele esikoleni. Uthe into yokuqala umzali okumele ayibheke ngaphambi kokubuyisela ingane yakhe esikoleni, wukuthi iyigomile yini imigomo ehambisana neminyaka yayo. Uthe uma esekhohliwe angazikhumbuza ngokubheka ikhadi lengane, iRoad to Health. "Imigomo ibaluleke kakhulu. Ivikela ingane ekutheni iphathwe yizifo ezivikelekayo,  iphinde ivikele nezinye izingane okwenza ukuthi ukufunda kube lula. Ezinye izifo ezigonyelwayo kazigcini ngokugulisa ingane kodwa zingaholela nasekutheni ingane ikhubazeke,“ kuchaza uDkt Lawrence.Phakathi kwezifo ezigonyelwayo, ubale isimungumungwane, umkhuhlale umpenge (whooping cough), Hepatitis B, Pollio nezinye.Uthe okunye okubaluleke kakhulu uma ingane inesifo esithile esifana nesifuba somoya,  umzali kumele aye esikoleni ayobheka ukuthi yini engenza ukuthi lesi sifo sivuke ingane isesikoleni."Kubalulekile ukuthi uxoxe nothisha uma ingane yakho inesifuba somoya, noma ezinye izifo, uphinde ukhulume nodokotela wayo ingane. Mhlawumbe ikhona imithi noma izaba angazenza ukuze kuvikelwe ukuthi ingane ivukwe yisifo sayo isesikoleni, okudalwa yizinto ezisetshenziswayo esikoleni noma imvelo," kusho yena.UNkk Sibongile Xaba wenhlangano ebhekele izingane, iSiyakhana Child Organisation, uthe ngesikhathi ezinye izingane zijabulela ukuvulwa kwezikole ezinye zisuke zinokwesaba nengcindezi."Kubalukekile ukuthi umzali akhulume nengane ngokuthi ijabulile yini. Uzozwa lapho ukuthi iphendula ithini. Kwezinye kusuke kungukwesaba ngoba ingazi ukuthi ilindeleni ebangeni ezolifunda kodwa ezinye zisuke sezike zaxhashazwa ngezinye, zesaba ukuthi nakulo nyaka kuzoqhubeka lokho. Isisindo sento eyenza ingane ingakhululeki noma ibe novalo asifani. Kuyenzeka kube yinto elula umzali angayikhuluma nengane, ayinike izeluleko kodwa okunye kusuke sekuyinto edinga abeluleki abakufundele ukukhuluma nezingane, ikakhulukazi lezi zingane ezisuke sezifunda amabanga aphezulu," kusho  uNkk Xaba.UNksz Hlengiwe Dweku, obhekele ukuzilolonga kwabafundi kwezinye izikole eThekwini, osebenza ngokuzimela, uthe enye into esuke ijahwe ngabafundi wukubuyela emgqigqweni wezemidlalo."Ngenyanga yokuqala kumele ubhekisise uma ulolonga abafundi ngoba abanye basuke bekhuluphele, abanye uma bezilolonga baba nobuhlungu obuthile. Kumele niqale ngezindlela ezingawugqilazi umzimba, ukuze abafundi bangene kahle egiyeni,"   kusho uNksz Dweku.UDkt Lawrence uthe ngoNovemba kuya kuMashi kuvamile ukuthi izingane zibe nesifo sokukhishwa yisisu, abazali nabanakekela izingane kumele bakuqaphele lokho.Okunye athe kubaluleke wukuthi uma ingane iyofunda kwesinye isifundazwe wukuthi umzali aqaphele ngoba kungezeka ihlaselwe yizifo ezingajwayele ukuyiphatha, ngenxa yokuthi indawo ayiyijwayele.NGAPHEZU kokuthi kunemikhankaso eminingi eyenziwa ngongoti bezempilo yokukhuthaza omama ukuthi bancelise ibele, izibalo zikhomba ukuthi bancane omama abenza njalo eNingizimu Afrika.Ngokwemigomo yenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, World Health Organization (WHO), mayelana nempilo kamama nezingane ezisanda kuzalwa, izingane kufanele zinceliswe ubisi lwebele ezinyangeni eziyisithupha zokuqala. Ngemuva kwalokho omama bayakhuthazwa ukuthi bancelise ibele njalo, uma ingane isiqale ukunikezwa ukudla okuqinile kancane, kancane kusukela ezinyangeni eziyisithupha.Abezempilo bathi inzuzo yokuncelisa ukuthi impilo kamama nengane iyathuthuka kunciphe nezindleko zokuthenga ubisi. Phezu kwalokho, ingane encela ibele ayivamile ukugula, ngaleyo ndlela kuncipha nezindleko zokwelashwa.Njengoba ngoLwesine kuqala isonto lokukhuthaza ukuthi omama bancelise ibele iWorld Breastfeeding Week, ongoti bezempilo bathi kunezizathu eziningi ezenza omama bangaqali ukuncelisa ibele noma bayeke ngaphambi kwesikhathi. Kwesinye isikhathi kusuke kuyizizathu zokwelapha ezingenakuvinjelwa, kodwa ngokuvamile omama babhekana nezithiyo abangakwazi ukuzinqoba bebodwa. Okhulumela i-Association for Dietetics in South Africa (ADSA), uNkk Tsholofelo Mohloane, ongungoti wokudla nokuncelisa uthe: "Ngenza umsebenzi omningi ezibhedlela zikahulumeni, ngihlangana nomama abanezinkinga eziholela ekutheni ubisi lwebele lungatholakali. Kungaba izingono ezibuhlungu, ubisi olugcwele kakhulu ebeleni oluholela ekutheni lungasakwazi ukuphuma ngendlela engonweni, ibele elivuvukele libe buhlungu. Ulwazi olungenele ngezinzuzo zokuncelisa ibele, okuholela ekutheni omama bakhethe okunye esikhundleni sobisi lwebele nakho kunomthelela. Kukhona nokuntuleka kokwesekwa kokuncelisa ibele emakhaya, emindenini nasemiphakathini,"Abezempilo bathi omama abasebenzayo kumele bazihlele uma bezoqhubeka nokuncelisa ibele noma sebebuyele emsebenzini.UMnuz Murray Hewlett oyisikhulu esiphezulu e-Affinity Health, uthe omama abasebenzayo banelungelo lokuthola isikhathi sokukhama ibele kumqashi kodwa nabo kumele bazi kabanzi ngamalungelo abo.Nazi izinto athe uma ungumama oncelisa ibele osebuyele emsebenzini okumele uzazi: Funda inqubomgomo yalapho usebenza khona emayelana nokuncelisa ibele nokukhama ubisi usebenzisa umshini."Ukwazi amalungelo akho kanye nokwesekwa okutholakalayo kungenza ushintsho lube lula,"  kusho uHewlett.Uthe ukuba nesikhathi esimile sokukhama ubisi  kusiza ekutheni ingane ibe nesikhathi esingaguquki sokuncela ibele.Uqhube wathi eNingizimu Afrika, omama abancelisayo banamalungelo asemthethweni okuthi banikezwe isikhathi sokukhama ubisi besemsebenzini."Ngokomthetho wezimo eziyisisekelo zokuqashwa, iBasic Conditions of Employment Act (BCEA) isigatshana esibhekelele abasebenzi ngesikhathi sokukhulelwa nangemuva kokubeletha, abaqashi kufanele bavumele omama abancelisa ibele okungenani amakhefu amabili emizuzu engama-30 nsuku zonke ukuze bakhame ubisi. Lawa makhefu okuncelisa ibele athathwa njengesikhathi esikhokhelwayo futhi azonikezwa ngaphezu kwekhefu elivamile lomsebenzi letiye nelasemini. Abaqashi kufanele bahlinzeke ngendawo ehlanzekile, esesithe, nevikelekile ukuze omama bakhamele ubisi," kusho uHewlett.MANCANE amathuba okuthi iNingizimu Afrika ingakwazi ukufeza umgomo wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO),  wokuthi u-70% womama bancelise izingane zabo ibele kuphela zize zibe nezinyanga eziyisithupha ngo-2030.Ngo-2016 bebengu-32% omama abancelisa ibele kuphela  izingane zabo  zize zibe nezinyanga eziyisithupha.Uthe ucwaningo luveza ukuthi abakhiqizi bobisi lwethini babambe iqhaza ekuqeqeshweni nasekuthuthukisweni okuqhubekayo kobuchwepheshe bezempilo, babuye babe ngabaxhasi ezingqungqutheleni zezempilo babeke nezikhangiso ngemikhiqizo yabo."Kweminye imicimbi yomnyango bayakhuluma.  Bafinyelela komama ngeziteshi zemisakazo. Amaqhinga okuthengisa abawasebenzisayo enza ukuthi ukuncelisa ibele kubukeke njengento enzima, amanye enza omama bangazethembi ukuthi imizimba yabo ingakwazi ukukhiqiza ubisi olwenele ingane, abanye bazenyeze ukuveza amabele uma bencelisa. Amaqhinga abo okudayisa  amaningi asatshalaliswa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana okuyinto engalawulwa,"  kusho yena.IWHO igqugquzela ukuthi izingane zinceliswe ibele kuphela kusukela zizelwe bese kuthi uma sezinezinyanga eziyisithupha ziqale ukudla okunye ukudla.Ngokwe-Unicef (United Nations International Children’s Emergency Fund), izingane ezincela ibele kuphela zinamathuba aphindwe izikhathi ezingu-14 okuphila kahle zingaguli  zize zibe nezinyanga eziyisithupha kunalezo ezinceliswa ubisi lwethini.Le nhlangano ithe ukuncelisa ibele kunganikeza ukuvikeleka ezifweni eziningi zezingane ezifana nesifo sohudo, ukudla okungahambisani nomzimba (allergies), izinkinga zokuphathwa indlebe.Okuqaphelekayo ukuthi olwethini lwamukeleka kakhulu eNingizimu Afrika nakuba lokho kudala ubunzima bezezimali emakhaya ahola kancane. Okunye okukhathazayo ukuthi kudingeka izinga eliphezulu lenhlanzeko uma ukhethe ukuncelisa ingane yakho ubisi lwethini. Kudingeka amanzi ahlanzekile agelezayo, amanzi abilayo okubulala amagciwane namabhodlela aphephile.UNkk Maria van der Merwe, uMengameli wenhlangano yongoti bezokudla, i-Association for Dietetics in South Africa (ADSA), uthe:  “Silwa nefa lokumaketha okwakungenamingcele, okuhlanganisa nokuphiwa komama ubisi lwezingane ezincane, olunye lunikezwe abasebenzi bezempilo ukuthi baluphe omama."Kusenemfundiso-ze abantu abaningi abayikholwayo yokuthi ukuncelisa ngebhodlela elithile kuyafana nokuncelisa ibele. Ayikho into enjalo ibele lingcono kakhulu. Esikudingayo ukuthi sifundise umphakathi kabanzi ngezimfundiso-ze," kusho uNkk van der  Merwe.KUKHONA ukudla okunomsoco ofanayo ongakudla esikhundleni seqanda.Lokhu kushiwo ungoti wokudla uNkk Richelle Cavanagh onesikhungo esiluleka ngokudla ngendlela, esiseThekwini. Uthe njengoba amaqanda emba eqolo ngenxa yokuthi ayashoda ngoba kuhlasele umkhuhlane wezinkukhu kuleli, i-Avian Flu eholele ekutheni kubulawe izinkukhu eziningi kuleli kufanele abantu bafunde ukudla okunye ukudla okunomsoco ofanayo."Iqanda linemisoco efana ne-protein, amino acid esiza ekusebenzeni kwamamasela, i-Omega-3 fatty acid, i-calcium, potassium ne-choline esiza ekusebenzeni kahle kobuchopho kodwa leyo misoco ungayithola ngokuthi udle ubhontshisi, inyama yenkukhu, inyama yenkomo ebomvu , i-yoghurt, ushizi, i-peanut butter noma inhlanzi,"  kusho uNkk Cavanagh.UNksz Zinhle Mbambo, wenkampani ebhaka ibuye ifundise nokubhaka, iGel-Delish Bakery, uthe amakhekhe amaningi adinga amaqanda ngakho kubathwalisa kanzima ababhaki ukushoda kwawo."Akhona ama-recipe amakhekhe angawadingi amaqanda kodwa iningi lababhaki lisebenzisa amaqanda uma libhaka okwenza ukuthi sizithole sinengcindezi. Ukushintsha ama-recipe manje kungaholela ekutheni silahlekelwe amakhasimende a-ode azi ukuthi azothola amakhekhe angawajwayele,"  kusho uNksz Mbambo.UChef  Pam Khumalo, uthe amaqanda asebenza kakhulu uma ungumpheki ikakhulukazi uma ubhaka. "Amaqanda siwasebenzisa uma sibhaka,  asiza ekutheni inhlama ikhukhumale kahle, uma sithosa ukuze sigweme  ukuthi amafutha namanzi kungangeni ngaphakathi esidlweni. Sibuye siwasebenzisele ukuthi sinamathelise izithako ekudleni kwethu,"  kuchaza umpheki uKhumalo.Uthe yize iqanda liyisithako sokuqala esithandwa ngabapheki nababhaki kodwa zikhona izinto ongazisebenzisa esikhundleni salo ekhishini.Uthe ungasebenzisa i-apple sauce engenawo ushukela esikhundleni seqanda uma ubhaka ezinye izinhlobo zamakhekhe, ama-muffins nama-brownies.Uthe kwamanye ama-recipe  afana nama-pancakes, ama-muffins nesinkwa, ungasebenzisa ubhanana esikhundleni seqanda.Uthe ungasebenzisa i-yoghurt e-plain ukuze ikhekhe lakho lihlale lintofontofo esikhundleni seqanda.Uthe iqanda libuye lisetshenziselwe ukugcotshwa ku-pie namakhekhe ukuze acwebezele wathi esikhundleni seqanda ungasebenzisa i-silken tofu.Uqhube wathi i-baking soda no-vinegar nako kungasetshenziswa esikhundleni seqanda kwamanye ama-recipe amakhekhe."Kwezinye izitolo ezinkulu akhona ama-recipe athengwayo angafakwa iqanda,"   kusho uNkk Khumalo.UNksz Mbambo, uthe  uma usufuna ukushintshela endleleni yokubhaka ngaphandle kweqanda kudingeka ukuthi uqale uhlole ukuthi ikhekhe lizophuma kahle lifane nse nobujwayele ukulibhaka, okusho ukuthi uzolahlekelwa.Khonamanjalo ikhomishini ebhekele ukuncintisana kwabadayisa izimpahla kuleli, iCompetition Commission, isishayele ihlombe isenzo sezinye izitolo esezikalela amakhasimende inani lamaqanda angalithenga ezitolo. UMnuz Siyabulela Makunga okhulumela le khomishini, uthe ukukalwa kwamaqanda ikhasimende elivumeleke ukuwathenga kuzokwenza ukuthi umkhiqizo okhona wanele bonke abantu, ungathengwa ngabantu kakhulu ngoba benovalo lokuthi ungase uphele nokuyinto eyake yenzeka ngesikhathi kuhlasele iCovid-19.Uthe kodwa lokhu kuzoshaya kuzwele kubathengi ngoba kumele kunyuswe intengo yaamaqanda ngokushesha. NJENGOBA isiqalile isizini yomkhuhlane ongoti bezempilo bakhuthaza ukuthi abantu bawugomele, babonane nodokotela uma kunesidingo.Okunye okunconywa wongoti ukuthi abantu bangasebenzisa izinto ezikhona emakhaya eziqinisa amasosha omzimba okwenza ukuthi abahaqekile basheshe balulame.GingerEsinye sitshalo semvelo esiqinisa amasosha omzimba akwazi ukulwa nomkhuhlane. Okunye okwenziwa i-ginger ukwehlisa ukuvuvukala nokudambisa ubuhlungu bomphimbo kanye nokukhwehlela okuhambisana nomkhuhlane.Vitamin CU-Vitamin C ungesinye isithako semvelo esibalulekile ekuqiniseni amasosha omzimba. Ucwaningo luthole ukuthi ukuthatha u-1 gram kuya kwamabili ka-vitamini C ngosuku kunganciphisa isikhathi somkhuhlane ngo-8% ebantwini abadala kanye no-14% ezinganeni.Izithelo ezino-vitamin C ezisawolintshi, i-kiwi  nama-strawberriers zinothe ngo-vitamin C ongasiza ekutheni uqinise amasosha omzimba.GarlicU-garlic uwumuthi wemvelo ongasiza ekuqiniseni amasosha omzimba futhi ulwa nezifo.Ngokocwaningo olwenziwe i-Journal of Nutrition, ukudla okunalesi sithako kunganciphisa ingozi yokuthola umkhuhlane okungaze kufinyelele ku-63%.Lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi ukuthatha ama-milligram angu-180 e-allicin, okuyisithako esisebenzayo sika-garlic ngosuku kungasiza ukuvimbela nokwelapha umkhuhlane.ZincI-Zinc iyi-minerali ebalulekile yamasosha omzimba anempilo. Ngokusho kokubuyekeziwe okushicilelwe kwiCochrane of Database of Sytematic Reviews, ukuthatha izithako ze-zinc kunganciphisa ubude nobunzima bomkhuhlane.Ukubuyekeza kwathola ukuthi ukuthatha izithasiselo ze-zinc kungakapheli amahora angu-24 kuqale izimpawu zomkhuhlane kunganciphisa isikhathi sokugula kuze kufike ezinsukwini ezimbili.Amanzi anosawotiUkuhahaza (gargle)  ngamanzi anosawoti kungasiza ekuvimbeleni izifo ezithikameza ukuphefumula. Kungase futhi kwehlise ubungako bezimpawu zamakhaza, ukunciphisa ubuhlungu bomphimbo obuhlungu nokuminyana kwamakhala.Ukuhahaza ngamanzi anosawoti kungakhulula amafinyila, aqukethe amagciwane.umkhuhlane, nezinye izimo zokuphefumula, ukudambisa izinhlungu, ukwehlisa ukuvuvukala.Amafutha aziwa ngama-essential oils Amanye alamafuthai-eucalyptusi-peppermint (i-menthol)Impephoi-thymei-tea treeOSOSAYENSI bakuleli bathi ukuhola ucwaningo oluzobe luhlola amakhambi ahlukene ukuthi angakwazi yini ukuba wumgomo wokuvikela iHIV,  kuyithuba lokuthi baveze ikhono labo.USolwazi Glenda Gray ongumengameli womkhandlu ocwaninga ngezempilo kuleli, iSouth African Medical Research (SAMRC), uthe eminyakeni engu-20  eyedlule, luningi ucwaningo oseluke lwenziwa kuzanywa ukuthola umgomo weHIV kodwa bekungakaze kwenzeke ukuthi luholwe wososayensi base-Afrika,  beluholwa wososayensi base-Europe noma base-America, abase-Afrika bebesuke belekelela.Usho kanjena nje uSolwazi Gray inhlangao yezengculazi emhlabeni, ikhiphe imali engu-R867 million yokuthi ahole ucwaningo oluzobe  luhlanganise izingcithabuchopho kwezempilo zase-Afrika, ezizobe zesekelwe ngezomhlaba wonke, kuhlolwa amakhambi ehlukene khona e-Afrika. Uthe ngale mali kuzohlolwa amakhambi okunenkolelo yokuthi angaba umgomo uma kubheka ukuhlolwa kwawo ema-labolatory, azobe esehlolwa ezilwaneni nakubantu. “Ngiyazi ukuthi enqwabeni yocwaningo oseluke lwenziwa eminyakeni eminingi eyedlule imiphumela isiphoxile  kodwa njengoba ngisho nje belugxile emazweni aphesheya. Manje sekuyithuba lethu singabacwaningi nososayensi base-Afrika, lokuthi sikhule ekucwaningeni. Ulwazi esiluthole emiphumeleni yaphambilini luzosisiza ekutheni sithole indlela engcono yokuthi sibhekana ngqo nengxenye yama-cells okumele siyiqinise, ukuze igciwane lengculazi lingangeni. Imiphumela yaphambilini isikhombisile ukuthi amakhambi aseke ahlolwa, abe nakho ukuvikela okuthize,  yize ebengakwazi ukuvikela ingxenye yama-cells okuyiyona ehlaselwa yiHIV ngokuphelele ngoba ama-cells anezingxenye eziningi. Manje sesiyazi ukuthi ukuze siwine, kuzomele umgomo uqondane nengxenye esiyibiza ngeV1V2, kwi-cell,” kusho uSolwazi Gray.Uthe ukuhlowa komgomo wokuvikela iCovid-19 nakho kubasizile bengososayensi ukuthi baqhamuke nezindlela ezilula zokuhlola futhi ezisheshayo kodwa izindlela abazisebenzise ngesikhathi behlola umgomo weCovid-19 ngeke bazisebenzise zinjengoba zinjalo ngoba igciwane iHIV lihluke kakhulu. “Sinethemba lokuthi siyi-Afrika sizokwazi ukuqhamuka nomgomo ngoba leli gciwane linokwehluka kubantu abahlala emazweni ahlukene. Njengamanje sisesesigabeni sokuthi sihlanganise amathimba azocwaninga. Okungijabulisa kakhulu wukuthi ethimbeni lososayensi abaphambili abayingxenye yalolu cwaningo, baningi abantu besifazane, okusho ukuthi nabo abesifazane bayakhula emkhakheni wokucwaninga,”  kusho uSolwazi Gray.USOLWAZI Abdool Salim Karim ungoti wezifo ezithathelanayo, uthe akubethusanga ukuqhamuka kwegciwane leCovid-19 eselizishintshile i-Omicron, okumenyezelwe ngeledlule ukuthi selikhona ngoba bebevele bazi ukuthi isiwombe sesine singafika negciwane elikhona iDelta noma kube nelinye elisha."Ebesingakwazi ukuthi uma sesifika lesi siwombe sizobanjani kodwa besilandela izinkomba ezenziwa ngososayensi eziye zisize umnyango ukuze ukwazi ukuzilungisela. “Uhulumeni yingakho utshale imali esikhungweni sobuchwepheshe esihlale sicubungula ukuziphatha kwaleli gciwane. Lesi sikhungo sihlale siqaphile sibheka ukuthi leli gciwane lizishintsha kanjani kuqhathaniswa nesikhathi esedlule," kusho yena.USolwazi Karim ubekhuluma esithangamini sabezindaba ebesihlelwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli, izolo.Uqhube wathi nakuba kusekuningi okungakaziwa ngaleli gciwane njengokuthi ngabe liziphatha kanjani kubantu abasha? Ngabe uhlelo olukhona lokwelapha abanalo kumele lushintshwe yini, nokuthi imigomo ekhona yona iyakwazi yini ukulithena amandla?"Uma sibheka ukuziphatha kwamanye amagciwane phambilini, sibona ukuthi asikabi khona isidingo sokushintsha imithi esilapha ngayo abahaqwe yileli gciwane. “Ngokubona kwethu, imithi esetshenziswayo manje isazoqhubeka isebenze nakulona ngoba siyazi ukuthi noma lingazishintsha, kunzima ukuthi lishintshe amasosha (T-Cells). Sesiyazi ukuthi kumele senzeni, akusafani nasekuqaleni lapho leli gciwane belilisha, singalazi," kusho uSolwazi Karim.Uqhube wathi ngokubona kwakhe, kungenzeka babe baningi abantu abahaqekayo okuzokwenza ukuthi izibhedlela zibe nengcindezi."Esingakusho okwamanje ukuthi abantu abangagomile abagweme ukuhlanganyela nabanye emicimbini engaphakathi," kusho yena.UDkt Michelle Groome wesikhungo esibhekelele izifo ezithelelanayo kuleli, iNational Institute for Commnunicable Diseases (NICD), uthe abakuqaphelayo ukuthi izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane ziyakhula eGauteng, eMpumalanga naseNorth West kodwa iGauteng ihamba phambili."Esikuqaphelayo ukuthi eGuateng abantu abahaqwa yileli gciwane abalaliswa ezibhedlela benyuke kusukela kwabangu-18 ngosuku baya kwabangu-48 esikhathini esingangesonto," kusho yena.UDkt Anban Pillay owudokotela eGauteng uthe okwamanje abantu abaningi abafika kubo basuke benezimpawu zomkhuhlane okujwayele ukuthi kube ukukhwehlela nokujuluka ebusuku."Okwamanje kuba abagomile nabangagomile, abagomile abajwayele ukugula kakhulu," kuchaza uDkt Pillay.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe abantu abangethuki okwamanje.KUNGENZEKA ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika isingena esiwombeni sesihlanu sokuhlasela kweCovid-19 kodwa asikabikhona isidingo sokuthi abantu babe novalo yize izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane ngosuku zinyuka ngamandla.Lokhu kushiwo uSolwazi Mosa Moshabela weNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal, ngesikhathi ephawula ngokuthi ngabe sesingenile yini isiwombe sesihlanu sokuhlasela kwaleli gciwane njengoba sibona izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane zinyuka ngamandla.Uthe okwamanje izibalo  ziyanyuka kodwa abantu abangaqali bethuke ngoba abantu abaningi abakadingi ukulaliswa ezibhedlela uma behaqwe ygciwane elifuqwa iBA.4 neBA.5 okungamagciwane azalwe i-Omicron."Okumele sihlale sikulindele ukuthi kungenzeka kube nabantu abazogula isikhathi eside ngenxa yoCovid-19 nakuba bengeke balaliswe ezibhedlela kodwa uma bengabantu abasebenzayo kuzoba nesikhathi sokuthi bangasebenzi ngoba begula," kusho uSolwazi Moshabela.Izinga lokutheleleka kwabantu ngaleli gciwane selenyukele ku-25% izibalo zakamuva ezikhishwe isikhungo esibhekele izifo ezithathelanayo kuleli, iNational Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD) ziveza ukuthi bangu-5,486  abantu abasha abahaqwe yigciwane okuholele ekutheni isibalo sabahaqwe yilona selokhu lafika lisinyukele ku-3 841 388, bayisikhombisa okubikwe ukuthi libabulele ngesikhathi esifanayo osekuholele ekutheni babe ngu-100,523 abantu eselibabulele. UMoshabela uthe kusemandleni omphakathi ukuthi uzivikele ngokuthi ugome ukuze ungaguli kakhulu uma unegciwane.Usolwazi Francois Venter waseWits University,  uthe ngokubona kwakhe sesingenile isiwombe sesihlanu sokuhlasela kweCovid-19. Uthe lokho ukusho ngoba izibalo eziphezulu zabantu abahaqwe yigciwane zagcina ukuba khona ngoDisemba ukubuya kwazo kusho ukuthi sekungene esinye isiwombe."Okwamanje singasho ukuthi isiwombe sesihlanu sizobe sifuqwa iBA.4 neBA.5,"  kusho yena.USolwazi Tulio de Oliviera, wesikhungo esicwaninga  ngokuzishintsha kwe-Covid-19 iKZN Research Innovation and Sequencing Platform,  uthe ukwenyuka kwezibalo kwakamuva kukhombisa ukuthi isiwombe sokuhlasela esisha kungenzeka sifuqwe igciwane eliphume kwelinye njengoba kwenzeka manje izibalo zenyuswa iBA.4 neBA.5 okungamagciwane azalwa i-Omicron. Uthe okwamanje indlela yokugwema ukusabalala kweCovid-19 kuseyikho ukugoma.“Abantu abaningi bacabanga ukuthi ukungenwa yileli gciwane kwenza uvikeleke ekutheni ngesikhathi esizayo likungene kanti ukuvikeleka okuthola ngoba uke wahaqeka phambilini ngemuva kwezinyanga ezintathu kuyehla, okukubeka ethubeni lokuthi uphinde uhaqeke futhi,”  kusho uSolwazi  Oliviera. Uphiko olubheka izifo eziqubuka ezweni, iNational Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD) luthi amaphaphu phansi kubantu bakuleli emuva kokuqubuka kohlobo olusha lwe-coronavirus.Uhlobo olusha lubizwa nge-JN.1 kanti kuthiwa ludla lubi e-United States nase-Europe.UDkt Sibongile Walaza we-NICD uthe iSARS-CoV-2 (Covid-19) isekhona kuleli futhi balindele ukuthi ziqhubeke nokuba khona izinhlobo ezintsha.“Okwamanje imininingwane esinayo ayivezi ukuthi kufanele sithuke nge-JN.1. Besingakatholi imibiko eveza ukuthi abantu bangeniswa kakhulu ezibhedlela noma bayashona ngenxa yalolu hlobo olusha. Abantu bakuleli basavikelekile ngoba asiboni ukuthi basengcupheni kulolu hlobo olusha,” kusho uDkt Walaza.Uthe abadala nalabo abanamasosha omzimba angasebenzi kahle kufanele baphuthume bayogoma ngomjovo wokuzivikela (booster).Ubalule ukuthi izimpawu zeJN.1 zizofana nezomkhuhlane ongekho nzima.Ucele abantu ukuthi baqhubeke nenhlanzeko, abale ukuyo ukugeza izandla, ukuzivala uma bethimula noma bekhwehlela nokuhlalela kude kubantu uma ugula.Uthe izimpawu ze-coronavirus entsha zizohluka kumuntu nomuntu ngenxa yesimo sakhe sempilo nokuthi amasosha akhe omzimba anjani.Uthe okwamanje iJN.1 igcwele kakhulu eGauteng naseWestern Cape.NJENGOBA kuyisikhathi samaholidi baningi abathenga izicoficofi ezinoshukela abazithokozisa ngazo. Kepha, ongoti bezempilo baxwayisa ngokuthi ukudla okunoshukela omningi, kungadala izinkinga kwezempilo.Inhlangano egqugquzela ezempilo iHealthy Living Alliance (HEALA), ithi ukukhangiswa kakhulu kwezinto ezinoshukela futhi ezibiza imali encane, kwenza abanye bacabange ukuthi into enoshukela kumele ibe yingxenye yokudla uma bezijabulisa.UMnuz Nzama Mbalati weHEALA, uthe kujwayelekile ukuthi abantu benze izidlo ezinoshukela nemikhiqizo egayiwe uma benemicimbi noma behlangene ndawonye. Wathi lokhu kudla kuvamisile ukudala izinkinga kwezempilo ngokuhamba kwesikhathi futhi abanye bagcina bengasakwazi ukukugwema ukuzidla."Ngeshwa lokhu kudla kutholakala kalula futhi akubizi kakhulu kodwa umonakalo okuwenzayo emzimbeni mkhulu. Abantu abajwayele ukudla into enoshukela omningi negayiwe bavame ukuba nezifo ezinjengesikashukela, esenhliziyo, ukukhuluphala ngokweqile ikakhulu kubantu abantulayo,” kuchaza uMbalati.Uqhube wathi abakhiqizi bezinto ezigayiwe bayazazi izikhathi ezibasebenzelayo zokudayisa kanti esinye ngesamaholidi kaDisemba."Le mikhiqizo inemakethe ethile esuke yenzelwe yona okujwayele ukuthi kube ngabantu abasha. Lokhu kwenzelwa ukuthi bayijwayele bese begcina behluleka ukungayithengi ngaleyo ndlela umkhiqizo uhlale unabathengi. Amaswidi namabhisikidi anoshukela kwenza ukuthi kube nzima ukungawadli," kuchaza uMbalati.Uthe okunye okuyinkinga ngemikhiqizo enoshukela ukuthi eminye ibhalwe ukuthi inamafutha amancane nama-protein amaningi."Okunye okubhalwe kule mikhiqizo kuyadukisa ngoba umthetho awuqinile ekutheni kubhekwe ukuthi abakubhalile kuyikho yini. Ungathathwa yinto ebhalwe ngaphandle kepha kungenzeka ukuthi okubhalwe kuyo akulona iqiniso. “Into okumele uyibheke uma ufuna ukwazi ukuthi umkhiqizo unaziphi izakhamzimba nemisoco (nutrition), qaphela izakhamzimba hhayi okubhalwe ngamagama amakhulu ngoba kungenzeka ukuthi ngenye yezindlela ezisetshenzisiwe zokuheha amakhasimende," kweluleka uMbalati.Uqhube wathi uma ufuna ukuba nesiqiniseko sokuthi udla ukudla okunoshukela ophansi, yidla okunezithelo. Wathi iziphuzo ezihlwahlwazayo ngezinye zezinto okumele abantu bazame ukuzigwema.IKOMITI lezempilo ePhalamende lithi umthetho sivivinywa iTobacco Products and Electronic Delivery Systems Control Bill awenzelwe ukuvimbela abantu ukuthi babheme kodwa wenzelwe ukubavikela  kulawulwe nokukhangiswa kukagwayi.UNkk Thenjiwe Kibi  owusihlalo wekomiti osabambile, uthe lo mthethosivivinywa,  olawula ukusetshenziswa kukagwayi wenzelwa ukuthi uhambisane nomthetho iFramework Convention and repeal the Tobacco Control Act of 1993 (Act No. 83 of 1993) oshaywe inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni ukuze kuvikelwe abantu engozini kagwayi.Uguquko oluhlongozwayo kulo mthethosivivinywa, ukuthi kube nezindawo zomphakathi ezisendlini kanye nezindawo ezithile ezingaphandle ezizoqokwa okuzokwaziwa ukuthi akubhenyelwa kuzo ngokuphelele (100% smoke free)-Ukungavunyelwa kokudayiswa kukagwayi ngemishini ewubuchwepheshe besimanje, ukuthi iphakethe likagwayi lingabhalwa lutho olungukukhangisa ngaphandle, libe nezixwayiso zezempilo nezithombe ezikhombisa umonakalo odalwa ugwayi emzimbeni wakho-Ukunqatshelwa kwabadayisa ugwayi ukuthi bawubeke obala lapho uzobonwa khona (display)-Ukulawulwa  kwezinye izindlela zokubhema kusetshenziswa amathuluzi asebenzisa ugesi lapho ababhemayo behogela i-nicotine noma besebenzisa la mathuluzi kodwa abakubhemayo kungenayo i- inicotine.Usho kanjena nje uNkk Kibi  inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), isanda kumemezela  ukuthi kwehlile ukubhenywa kukagwayi ngabantu abadala emhlabeni. Ithe ngasekupheleni konyaka odlule ucwaningo elwenzile luveze ukuthi umuntu omdala oyedwa kwabahlanu ubhema ugwayi okuyisibalo esehlelile uma siqhathaniswa nesango-2000,  lapho umuntu oyedwa kwabathathu wayebhema ugwayi.UDkt  Ruediger Krech, owumqondisi wophiko olubhekele ukugqugquzelwa kokulandela izinto eziyimpilo kwiWHO, uthe ucwaningo lwakamuva lukhombisa ukuthi amazwe angu-150 akwazile ukunciphisa ukubhenywa kukagcwayi emazweni awo ngempumelelo.UDkt Ruediger uthe nakuba ukhona umehluko obonakalayo emhlabeni wonke kodwa abakhiqizi bakagwayi basaqhubeka nokushaya indiva imigomo yezempilo ehambisana nogwayi." Uma umkhakha wezempilo usucabanga ukuthi uwinile, abakhiqizi bakagwayi baqhamuka namanye amaqhinga okukhohlisa abezempilo,  babe beqhubeka bedayisa imikhiqizo yabo enezithako ezibulalayo. Nakuba izibalo zehla kancane ngokuhamba kweminyaka, okusinika ithemba lokuthi umhlaba uzofinyelela esibalweni ozibeleke sona sokuthi wehlise ukubhenywa kukagwayi ngo-25% ngo-2025, ngoba wehlulekile ukwehlisa ukubhenywa kukagwayi ngo-30%  ngo-2010. Amazwe angu-56 kuphela emhlabeni wonke okubukeka ezofinyelela kulo mgomo, okuyisibalo esehle ngamazwe  amane kusukela embikweni  wokugcina obuwenziwe ngo-2021," kusho uDkt Ruediger.Uqhube wathi nakuba kunokwehla okubonakala kubantu abadala, ucwaningo luveza ukuthi  isibalo sentsha eneminyaka engu-13 kuya ku15 ababhema ugwayi nemikhiqizo ene-nicotine siyenyuka emazweni amaningi." Ukuze kuvikelwe izizukulwane  ezizayo nokuqinisekisa ukuthi ukubhenywa kukagwayi kuyaqhubeka kuncipha, i-WHO izomemezela ukuthi kube nooSuku Lomhlaba lokungawubhemi ugwayi nonyaka ukuze kuvikelwe izingane," kusho uDkt  Ruediger.UCWANINGO ludalula ukuthi sinciphile isibalo sabantu abahaqwe yisandulela ngculazi kuleli. Udalulwe izolo umbiko wocwaningo iSouth African National HIV Prevalence, Incidence, and Behaviour survey VI (SABSSM VI), olwenziwe yisikhungo esenza ucwaningo olwehlukene, iHuman Science Research Council (HSRC).Imiphumela yocwaningo isuselwe olwazini olutholakale phakathi kukaJanuwari 2022, no-Ephreli nonyaka, kanti ephelele ilindeleke ukuthi idalulwe ngonyaka ozayo.Ngolwesithupha lolu cwaningo lweSABSSM VI, olwenziwe kuleli kanti belubheka indlela abantu abaziphatha ngayo nokuthi inamthelelela muni ekusabalaleni kweHIV, ukwelashwa kwayo, nokunqandwa kwayo. USolwazi Khangelani Zuma, wesikhungo iHSRC, obethula imiphumela yocwaningo izolo, uthe isibalo sabahaqwe yigciwane uma siqhathaniswa nocwaningo lwango-2017, sehlele  ku-12.7% (7.8 million) sisuka ku-14.0% (7.9 million)."Lokhu kudalwa yizizathu eziningi okungaba ukuthi ukwehla kwesibalo sabahaqwa yigciwane, ukwehla kwesibalo sezingane ezizalwa zinaleli gciwane, ukushona kwabanegciwane bebulawa yilo, ukushona kwabanaleli gciwane ngenxa yokuthi sebebadala bengabulawa yilona kepha ngezinye izifo ezihambisana nokuthi sebebedala," kuchaza uSolwazi Zuma.Uqhube wathi ucwaningo luka-2022 lukhombisa ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika, inenqubekela phambili enkulu mayelana namasu okulwa negciwane,  aziwa nge-95-95-95.Inhloso yohlelo wukuthi ngo-2025, u-95% wabantu abaneHIV babe sebezazi ngesimo sabo seHIV, u-95% wabasaziyo isimo sabo, bathole ukwelashwa ngemishanguzo yokudambisa igciwane ama-ARV,  u-95% wabadla imishanguzo yokwelapha kumele emzimbeni yabo libe selicindezelekile igciwane futhi lingasabonakali.Umbiko wocwaningo uveza ukuthi abantu abaneminyaka engu-15 kuyangaphezulu abaphila neHIV eNingizimu Afrika ngo-2022, u-90% wabo  ubususazi isimo sabo seHIV, u-91% wabasaziyo isimo sabo seHIV bese bedla imishanguzo, u-94% wabadla imishanguzo kutholakala ukuthi isicindezelekile iHIV egazini labo."Lokhu kuwukuthuthuka uma kuqhathaniswa nokwatholwa ucwaningo luka-2017, lapho i-UNAIDS yayihlose ukuthola u90-90-90 kodwa iNingizimu Afrika, yafinyelela ku-85% -71% -87%. Ushintsho olukhulu ludalwe ukushintshwa kwemigomo ngo-2016, yathi umuntu otholakale ukuthi uneHIV akaqale imishanguzo kungakhathalekile ukuthi iCD4 Count yakhe ingakanani kanti phambilini abanegciwane bebeqala ukudla imishanguzo uma iCD4 Count yabo ingu-500," kuchaza uZuma.Ngokwalolu cwaningo abesifazane abathe ukukhula bayidla kangcono imishanguzo uma beqhathaniswa namadoda, njengoba u-83 % wabesifazane usunegciwane elicindezelekile kanti wu-79% wamadoda adla imishanguzo anegciwane elicindezelekile kuwo.  Liphansi izinga kwabesifazane abasebancane (15-24)  ngoba u70% wabadla imishanguzo,  unegciwane elicindezelekile emizimbeni yabo.Okunye okuvezwe wucwaningo ukuthi uhhafu wabesilisa abaneminyaka ewu-15 kuya ku-24 basokile, ngo-2017 kwakungu-43% wabanale minyaka ababesokile.Okunye wukuthi izifundazwe  okuyiKwaZulu-Natal, yiMpumalanga, neFree State, zisahamba phambili ngokuba nabantu abaningi abanegciwane futhi kwehlile ukusetshenziswa kwamakhondomu.UDkt Thembi Xulu, womkhandlu obhekele ezengculazi kuleli, uthe kuyajabulisa ukuthi ikhona inqubekela phambi kodwa lokho akusho ukuthi impi isinqotshiwe."Kuyakhathaza ukuthi abantu abasha abadla imishanguzo, kalicindezekile kubona igciwane, amakhondomu nawo abawasebenzisi kakhulu,“ kukhononda uDkt Xulu. Inhloko yoMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Sandile Buthelezi, ithe bayawemukela umbiko futhi basazowufunda kahle bese bephendula ngokuthi balungise imigomo ethile elawula ukwelashwa kwegciwane kuleli.ISIFO sabantu besifazane esixina isibeletho nokuya esikhathini kwabo i-endometriosis, siyimbangela yezinkinga zenzalo kwabangu-50% kuleli.Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithi u-10% wabantu besifazane ophathwa yilesi sifo uze udinge ukuthi welashwe.ENingizimu Afrika lesi sifo singezinye zezifo ezinganakiwe kangako ngenxa yokuthi izinsiza zokusihlonza nokuselapha ziyabiza, nokuthi  kuleli lo mkhakha awukathuthuki kahle.UDkt Abri de Bruin owungoti walesi sifo eGenesis Reproductive Center neMediclinic eseKloof, uthe imikhankaso yokuqwashisa ngokusabalala kwe-endometriosis ibalulekile, ukuze abesifazane bajwayele ukuzihlola ukuthi umgudu wenzalo usesimweni esiyiso ukuze kunqandeke lesi sifo esibonakala sanda kule minyaka.I-Endometriosis yisimo lapho ama-cells akha ulwelwesi lwesibeletho ekhula ngaphandle kwesibeletho. Izimpawu ze-endometriosis ziyahlukahlukana kodwa ngokuvamile ziholela ekutheni kube buhlungu uma owesifazane esezinsukwini zakhe ubuhlungu bamanyonga obungapheli nobuhlungu uma beya ocansini.“I-Endometriosis idlange kakhulu manje kunaseminyakeni engu-20 edlule futhi iya ngokuya idlanga kwabesifazane abasebasha. Ochwepheshe bathi lokhu kwenyuka kwezibalo zabesifazane abahlaselwa yiyo zidalwa ukuthi iningi labesifazane liba nokhwantalala nengcindezi namahomoni atholakala ekudleni esikudlayo," kusho uDkt de Bruin.UDkt Kamlanathan Subrayen, owungoti walesi sifo esibhedlela iLenmed Ethekwini Hospital and Heart Centre, eThekwini, uthe: "Akekho umuntu esingeke simphathe lesi sifo ngoba kuthiwa usemncane noma imuphi umuntu wesifazane singamhlasela," kusho uDkt Subrayen.Uthe okubalulekile ukuhlolwa nokwelashwa kusenesikhathi, wathi izimpawu zalesi sifo zingaqala ukubonakala ngesikhathi owesifazane eqala ukuya esikhathini."Kwesinye isikhathi kuye kudingeke ukuthi sikhishwe isibeletho yize nakho kungayilaphi i-endometriosis kodwa kwenza ukuthi umuntu wesifazane angayi ezinsukwini zakhe okunciphisa ubuhlungu. Kunciphe nesidingo sokuhlinzwa kuphindelelwa," kuphetha uSubrayen.BABALELWA ku-4 million abantu abadala bakuleli abanesifo sikashukela kuleli ngokwezibalo ezintsha ezikhishwe yi-International Diabetes Federation (IDF) ngeSonto ngengoba kuwusuku lokuqwashisa ngesifo sikashukela emhlabeni, iWorld Diabetes Day.Ngokwalesi sibalo kusho ukuthi kubantu abadala abayisishiyagalolunye oyedwa unesifo sikashukela.Okushayisa ngovalo ngalezi zibalo ukuthi kuthiwa uhhafu walabo bantu awazi ukuthi uphila nalesi sifo. Lezi zibalo ziphinde ziveze ukuthi kubantu abathathu bakuleli oyedwa kunamathuba amaningi okuthi angenwe u-type2 ngoba iiglucose egazini lakhe ayikho esimeni okumele ngabe ikuso okubabeka engcupheni yalesi sifo.Ngokwezibalo ze-IDF bangu-537 million abantu abadala abaphila nalesi sifo emhlabeni wonke, okusho ukuthi isibalo sabanalesi sifo senyuke ngo-16% (74)  uma siqhathaniswa nezibalo zayo ezikhiphe ngo-2019.Lezi zibalo zakamuva zikhomba ukuthi iNingizumu Afrika ihamba phambili uma iqhathaniswa namanye amazwe ase- e-Afrika ngokwanda kwalesi sifo njengoba lezi zibalo zikhomba ukuthi izinga lokwanda kwalesi sifo kuleli  lingu- 11.3% .Lesi sifo silawulwa ngomjovo owaziwa nge-insulin kanti kulo nyaka kuphela iminyaka engu-100 wasungulwa lo mjovo.Akhona namaphilisi aphuzwa abantu abanaso.Ngokwalolu cwaningo izizathu ezenza ukuthi senyuke isibalo sabahlaselwa isifo sikashukela kuleli, ukufudukela emadolobheni kwabantu abaningi, ukungazivocavoci noma ukwenza imisebenzi enyakazisa umzimba kubantu okuholela ekutheni bakhuluphale ngokweqile okubabeka engcupheni yokungenwa yilesi sifo.UDkt Patrick Ngassa Piotie obekhuluma ngesikhathi kunengqungquthela yeSouth African Diabetes Summit yokuqala, ebihlelwe iNyuvesi yasePretoria, ngempelasonto uthe isifo sikashukela singesinye sezifo ezingamahlalakhona esibeka abantu engcupheni yokuthi bashone uma behlaselwa yiCovid-19.“Sithathe inqumo sokuthi kube khona esikwenzayo ngale nkinga esiyibona ikhula kuleli. INingizimu Afrika ayikulungele ukubhekana nenselelo yesinye isifo esingalawuleki njengoba kwenzekile ngesikhathi kufika iCovid-19 kuleli, kusho uDkt Piotie.Inhlangano yezeMpilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation(WHO) ithi ukwanda kwalesi sifo kudalwa ukufudukela emadolobheni kwabantu abaningi okuholela ekutheni bashintshe ukudla abebekudla besahlala emakhaya. NgokweWHO uma abantu sebefudukele emadolobheni badla ukudla okubakhuluphalisayo bese beba sengcupheni yokungenwa yizifo kuzo okubalwa nesifo sikashukela.Ungoti ohlonza aphinde elaphe izifo ezidalwa ukungasebenzi kahle kwama-hormones kuzo okubalwa nesifo sikashukela i- endocrinologist, uDkt  Zane Stevens, uthe abantu abaningi bayavilapha ukuzivocavoca noma ukwenza imisebenzi eyenza ukuthi banyakazise umzimba, ngaphezu kwalokho baphuza iziphuzo ezihlohlozayo nokudla okunama-carbohydrates okwenza ukuthi impilo yabo ingabi yinhle.Uthe bancoma ukuthi abantu badle ukudla okunamafutha amancane, okusanhlamvu, izithelo nemifino. Uma befaka amafutha ekudleni bafake amafutha angeke abadalele izifo njenge-olive oil, amakinati  bagweme ukudla okugayiwe okwaziwa nge-processed food.UPoiter uthe kule ngqungquthela bakhethe ukuthi kube khona abantu abanalesi sifo ukuze kube yibo abakhulumayo ngokuthi bazinakekela kanjani uma sebenalesi sifo wathi banethemba lokuthi lokho kuzobasiza ekutheni bacwaninge kabanzi ngaso.KUSUKELA ngonyaka ophelile ngilokhu ngiqaphela ukwenza kwezinso ezifweni ezehlukene, kuhlanganisa nobuhlungu obukubamba umzimba wonke kusukela onweleni kuya ozwaneni. Kunesimo esibuhlungu engicabanga ukuthi baningi abafowethu abakwezempilo asebeke basiqaphele. Ngikhuluma ngokuyohlola ukusebenza kwazo izinso, uzithole zingenankinga ngokwegazi kodwa kuthi uma usuphinda uhlola igazi engakapheli amasonto ayisithupha, uthole imiphumela esikukhomba ngokushesha ithi izinso kazisasebenzi mpela, wena sekumele uhluzelwe igazi ngemishini, kungenjalo igade leli labaphilayo uzolishiya. Yini le esiyenzekile kulesi sikhashana ugcine ukuhlolwa izinso ngokuthatha  igazi?  Kungabe ukuhlolwa ukusebenza komzimba ngokuthatha igazi kumele sikwethembe kangakanani, uma imiphumela inje? Akufanele yini  abezempilo babukele ukusiqala kabusha isimo?Yimibuzo lena okufanele abezempilo futhi nawe uyisiguli nizibuze yona, ifuna izimpendulo ezineqiniso ngokuphelele.Evikini elidlule isiguli esisesincane esingakafiki naseminyakeni engu-40 sibe nesimo esifuze lesi. Uhlolile izinso ngokuthathwa igazi liyoxilongwa esikhungweni esiqondene – imiphumela yaba mihle kakhulu. Kodwa kuthe sekubhekwa izinso ezinyangeni ezingafikile kwezimbili, imiphumela ibisithi azisasebenzi mpelampela izinso. Ubesevuvukele emzimbeni, esephalaza, ephelelwa ngamandla, isimo sesisibi kakhulu. Kwathi sekubhekwa isimo sokusebenza kwezinso, kwatholwa isibalo esikhombisa ukuhluza kwazo sekusesihlanwini kuphela. Yimiphumela eshaqisayo lena: ngabe kwenzekani? Isiguli sidle ushevu? Noma kuguquke imishanguzo yavele yangazwana nomzimba waso, mhlawumbe amasosha omzimba avele aphendukele umzimba aqobaqobe izinso?Izinso zinemisebenzi emibili ehamba phambili: ukubhalansa okusamaswayi egazini nasemizimbeni yethu, okugcina umzimba uhlanzekile ngokukhuculula udoti ukhishelwe ngaphandle. Ukudembesela noma ukufeyila kwezinso kuholela ekutheni umzimba uqoqelane udoti uze ube yinqwatshana. Ukunqwabelana kwalezi zinqwatshana kuholele ebuhlungwini bendawana leyo ethintekayo emzimbeni.Amaqoqwana ngamaqoqo emzimbeni agcina esedale ubuhlungu kuleyo ndawo ethintekayo. Izinga lobuhlungu lincika ekuthini likuyiphi indawo iqoqo futhi lisondelene naziphi izindawo. Isibonelo: uma iqoqo lokusadoti lizoba seduze nemizwa ethile, ubuhlungu buzokwanda bube bukhulu kuye nangokuthi ubuyini umsebenzi wesicubu nomuzwa loyo; wena usuyozwa ngokunkenketha obungakuvusa ngisho ucambalele. Lezi zinhlungu ziyakwazi ukunombela edolweni, ziliqaqele idolo emacaleni amabili, ubuhlungu bujule buye phakathi nedolo nangemuva emfasankomo, emahlombe ikakhulu lapho kuhlangana khona amathambo lawa enza ihlombe, ubuhlungu obuba sesiphangeni ezansi nasenhla naso, izinhlungu eziba sezigabeni ezahlukene zentamo. Kokunye zigcina sezenze ikhanda namehlo kube buhlungu, ubuhlungu obukubamba phakathi nengxenye engenhla yengalo buzwakale buzikile ngokushona nezicubu. Kokunye buze bufike endololwaneni, iminwe nayo ayisali kulezi zinhlungu kwabanye kuze kube nokuvuvuka okuqinile kuyo uqobo.Asikwazi ukukhohlwa yiminjunju eba semvilaphini uma izinso sezibheda. Abantu asebake bahlelwa yilobu buhlungu bayokuxoxela ukuthi kuba nzima nokuma kodwa lokhu. Ngalesi sizathu kunabantu asebehamba ngenqola yokukhubazeka ngenxa yalobu buhlungu. Baningi abantu abakhala ngobuhlungu ezithweni kuze kuyofika ngaphezu kwezinyawo. Ubuhlungu bezitho abubekezeleleki, abanye behluleka nokunyathela.Empeleni izinso zenza umzimba ikakhulu izicubu kuhlanganisa nemisipha kube nenkwantshu, amajaqamba, ubuhlungu obugwazayo nobunkenkethayo umzimba uvele ukhathale kulezo zinhlungu.Okukhulu wukuthi uma sewunezinso eseziqhuga, kumele uzelaphe ngokushesha. Abantu bakithi kulapho abafeyila khona; ekusukumeleni ukwelapha. Mangikubeke ngingakuhloniphisi ukuthi uma unquma ukungazelaphi izinso, okuzolandela wukuvuvukala, ukhathale, uphalaze, uphelelwe yigazi, umzimba ushintshe ibala ugqunqe, uhlale ukhathele; ugcine ngokuwushiya umhlaba omagade.Kuyazicacela ukuthi isifo umhlume sizobhebhetheka siye phambili uma izinso zingasasebenzi seziqhuga. Masingazibuzi ukuthi yini indaba induku yakho iwe kangaka, ingafuni ukuvuka, inciphe kunezinye, isheshe kangaka ukudedela: impendulo isekutheni umhlume okumuntu onezinso eseziqhuga isimo sokugula sidlondlobala kakhulu, kuthathe isikhathi eside ukuselapha.Masizisukumele izinso, ziyingozi, asizelaphe.MpilondeUMNYANGO wezeMpilo ucela abantu abake basondelena nabantu abanopokisi wezinkawu, i-monkeypox (mpox) ukuthi bavakashele ezikhungweni zezempilo.Lokhu kulandela ukuthi isikhungo esibhekelele izifo ezithathelanayo i-National Institute of Communicable Diseases i-NICD, iqinisekise ezinye izigameko ezimbili  zeziguli ezinalesi sifo esibhedlela, i-Addington Hospital ne-Netcare St Augutine eThekwini muva nje.Ngokwesitatimende soMnyango wezeMpilo izigameko ezimbili zakamuva zihlobene nesigameko sokuqala e-Addington phambilini.Umnyango uthi kubalulekile ukuthi abantu beze ezikhungweni zezempilo ukuze kunqandwe ukusabalala kwalesi sifo KwaZulu-Natal.Isibalo sabantu asebeqinisekisiwe ukuthi banaso sesifinyelele kwabane, abathathu KwaZulu-Natal noyedwa eGauteng.Zonke iziguli ngabesilisa baseNingizimu Afrika abeminyaka eko-30.Umnyango uthe igciwane lidluliselana ngokusondelelana, ukuthintana ocansini, ukuhlangana koketshezi lomzimba, okungaba amaconsi oketshezi aphuma uma uphefumula kanye nokusebenzisa izinto ezike zasetshenziswa onalesi sifo zokulala namathawula.Ngokuvamile umnyango, uthe kuthatha izinsuku eziyisithupha kuya kwezingu-13 ukuthi i-monkeypox ibonakale."Abezempilo bathembele ekuhlolweni nasekubambisaneni neziguli ukuze kutholakale abake bathintana neziguli osekuqinisekiwe ukuthi zinazo. Uma singabathola ngokushesha abake bathintana nalezi ziguli kuzokwenza ukuthi isifo singaqhubeki nokusabalala," kusho isitatimende.Siqhuba sithi umnyango ngokubambisana nabo bonke ababambe iqhaza basiqaphile isifo futhi bayaxhumana nomphakathi.Ngokwesitatimende, ukucwaswa kwabanalesi sifo kungaholela ekutheni abazisolayo ukuthi banaso bangasukumi ngokushesha ngoba besaba ukucwaswa.Izimpawu ezijwayelekile ze-monkeypox kubalwa ukuqubuka, okungase kuhlale amasonto amabili kuya kwamane, umkhuhlane, ikhanda elibuhlungu, ubuhlungu bemisipha, ubuhlungu beqolo, ukuphelelwa ngamandla nokuvuvukala kwezindlala.“Amaqhuqhuva abukeka njengamabhamuza noma izilonda asebusweni, ezintendeni zezandla, esifubeni, ezinyaweni, esithweni sangasese angase achaze ukuthi unalesi sifo,"  kusho umnyango esitatimendeni.ZIYAQONGA izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli njengoba kuvele ukuthi ngosuku bangu-4 236 abangenwe yileli gciwane. Uma kuqhathaniswa nangoLwesihlanu babe ngu-3 332, abatholakale benegciwane ngosuku olulodwa. Lokhu kukhomba ukuthi izibalo ziyenyuka zinsuku zonke kuleli zabatheleleka ngegciwane.Ngokusho kukaNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli uDkt Zweli Mkhize,  bangu-1 635 465 abakuleli abatholakale benegciwane. Abashonile ngenxa yegciwane ngoMgqibelo kutholakale ukuthi bangu-53, eGauteng babengu-27, Free State 17, babehlanu KwaZulu-Natal, kanti bathathu eWestern Cape 3, bese eba yedwa e-Eastern Cape. Abekho okubikwe ukuthi bashonile eLimpopo, Mpumalanga, North West nase- Northern Cape. Lokhu kusho ukuthi abantu asebeshonile kuleli bangu-55 802. Abasindile bangu:1  539 395, okusho ukuthi bami ku:94.2%. Abantu asebehloliwe selokhu kwabheduka igciwane bangu: 11 354 930. Khonamanjalo ucwaningo olwenziwe i-African Covid-19 Critical Care Outcomes Study (Acccos), luveza ukuthi emazweni angu-10 ase-Afrika, okubalwa nelakuleli siphezulu isibalo sabafayo ngenxa yaleli gciwane. Lolu cwaningo olwenziwe kubantu abadala abangu-3 140, phakathi kukaMeyi noDisemba nyakenye, luveza ukuthi siphezulu isibalo sabafayo uma sebengeniswe emagunjini abagula kakhulu ngenxa yegciwane. Luthole ukuthi uhhafu weziguli zishona ngaphandle kokunikekwa i-oxygen. Ucwaningo luthole nokuthi labo abanoshukela mancane kakhulu amathuba okusinda. UCWANINGO lwakamuva luveza ukuthi ukushintsha kwesimo sezulu kuhambisana nokunyuka kwezinkinga zezifo zengqondo, kwazise abantu bachitha isikhathi esiningi bezivalele.UNkk Sandy Lewis, ofundisa ngezifo zengqondo eNetcare, uveze ukuthi abacwaningi bathi uma kushintsha inkathi yonyaka nezingqondo ziyashintsha indlela ezisebenza ngayo.“Ebusika ilanga liphuma amahora ambalwa, bese labo abanezifo zengqondo bezithola bengahlalisekile (kahle) uma ilanga selishonile. Njalo uma kushintsha inkathi yonyaka abanezifo zengqondo bashintsha indlela ababhekana ngayo nempilo,” kusho uNkk Lewis.Uthe kubalulekile ukuthi abantu bangakuthathi kancane ukungazizwa kahle uma kushintsha inkathi yonyaka ngoba kwesinye isikhathi kungasho ukuthi badinga usizo lodokotela.Uveze ukuthi kubalulekile ukuthi abanezifo zengqondo bazinakekele kakhulu uma kushintsha inkathi yonyaka, bangazitsheli nje ukuthi bakhathazwe wukungena kobusika ngoba ingqondo yabo isuke ibatshela ukuthi mabashintshe okuthile.Ubalule ukuthi abanezifo zengqondo bakhathala kalula uma sekufanele bashintshe indlela abaphila ngayo ngenxa yokuthi kusebusika.Wenze isibonelo sokuthi ebusika abantu abasitholi isikhathi esanele sokuzivocavoca ngenxa yokuthi kuyashesha ukuhlwa.Lokhu kuba yinkinga kumuntu ojwayele ukuzivocavoca ukuze angacabangi kakhulu ngezinto ezithile noma ozivocavoca ukuze ingqondo yakhe ihlale iphapheme.Kwabanye ukuhlwa kusho ukuthi kufanele basheshe babuyele emakhaya bayohlala bodwa njengoba abangani noma labo abasebenza nabo basuke sebebuyele emakhaya.Ugqugquzele abantu ukuthi bazazi izimo zabo sengqondo futhi bakhulume uma bezizwa bephatheke kabi ngaso sonke isikhathi.Lokhu uthe kuzobasiza ukuthi bafune usizo olufanele kungakahambi isikhathi.Labo abasabayo ukukhuluma nabangani noma abasaba ukuhlulelwa ngabaseduze kwabo bangashayela iSouth African Depression and Anxiety Group (Sadag) ku-0800 205 026. Iyatholakala nakwiWhatsapp ethi 087 163 20 30.OWESIFAZANE osemncane usebusiswe ngezingane eziyisishagalolunye ngesikhathi. UNksz Halima Cisse (25) waseMali ubelethe lezi zingane eziyisishagalolunye esibhedlela saseMorocco nokubikwa ukuthi zonke ziwumqemane. Ubelethela eMorocco kulandela ukuthi umnyango wezeMpilo waseMali ngoMashi umenzele izinhlelo ezisezingeni eliphezulu njengoba bekuvele kulindeleke athole izingane eziningi.Odokotela kubikwa ukuthi bebeqagula ukuthi uzothola izingane eziyisikhombisa kanti kunezinye ezimbili ebebengaziboni nokwenze zaba yisishagalolunye. Okhulumela umnyango wezeMpilo eMorocco uRachid Koudhari yize bebengenalwazi lokuthi zizoba ziningi kangaka kodwa bayakuqinisekisa ukuthi ziphile saka lezi zingane okungama ntombazane amahlanu nezinsizwa ezine. Bakuvezile nokuthi akazange akwazi ukuzibelethela nokwenze wateta ngomthungo. INHLANGANO yakuleli engenzi nzuzo  iCheck Know Prevent (CKP) isungule ibhodisi onemininingwane efundisa abesifazane ngokuthi bazihlola kanjani umdlavuza webele.Lolu hlobo lukabhodisi olunendwangu ethambile ngaphakathi  lulungele ukugqokwa abesifazane abaphuma ukuyohlinzwa futhi nabazivocavocayo bangawugqoka ngoba wakhiwe wakwazi ukubamba kahle inyama ngaphansi kwamakhwapha kodwa ungashiyi omaka nezibazi ezimbi emzimbeni. UNkk Jenny De Oliveira, umsunguli wale nhlangano, uthe lolu hlobo lukabhodisi lunombhalo ngaphakathi okhumbuza abesifazane ukuthi kubaluleke kangakanani ukuthi ugqoke ubhodisi okulingana kahle ongakumpintshi nokuthi uzihlole njalo ukuthi awunazo yini izimpawu zomdlavuza webele obulala abesifazane abaningi emhlabeni."
