Ulwazi olukhona luveza ukuthi abantu abaningi okuye kutholakale ukuthi banomdlavuza bafika ezikhungweni zezempilo umdlavuza ususabalele, ngibone ukuthi uma umyalezo wokuthi uzihlola kanjani ungabhalwa kubhodisi okuyinto abesifazane abaningi abayigqokayo sizokwazi nathi ukuphonsa esivivaneni sokulwa nalesi sifo,"  kusho yena.Umqingo okubhalwa kuwo ukuthi bangakanani abahlaselwa ilesi sifo iNational Cancer Registry yakuleli ka-2017 uveza ukuthi kubantu besifazane abangu-26 oyedwa usengcupheni yokuhlaselwa umdlavuza webele.Olunye ulwazi olukhona ngalesi sifo ukuthi u70% weziguli ezinomdlavuza webele wasizwa ukuhlale uzithinta ibele ukuze uthole ukuthi kunokuthile okungajwayelekile ebeleni, uma sekuhlolwa kwatholakala ukuthi unomdlavuza webele.Ngokwalo mqingo uma kutholwe ukuthi unalo mdlavuza   usasesigabeni 0  amathuba okuthi welapheke angu-100%.Le nhlangano  ithe ngenxa yalolu lwazi olutholakala kwiNational Cancer Registry  ibone kukuhle ukuthi yenze ubhodisi obhalwe ukuthi uzihlola kanjani nokuthi uya esikhungweni sezempilo uma uthe uyathinta wezwani ebeleni.Ithi ikwenza lokhu ukuze kugwenywe ukushona kwabantu besifazane obekungamele bashone ngenxa yokuthi bafike ezikhungweni zezempilo umdlavuza ususabalele kakhulu egazini.“Sithole ukuthi kukhona abantu besifazane abangenalo ulwazi lokuthi bangazihlola kanjani ukuthi abanawo yini umdlavuza. Sabe sesibona ukuthi kule nyanga okungeyokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza webele, asenze ubhodisi ozofundisa ngezinto ezibalulekile,  ukuthi kumele ugqoke ubhodisi okulinganayo nokuthi uzihlola kanjani ngokuzithinta wena ibele ekhaya,"  kusho i-website yale nhlangano.Labo bhodisi badayiswa nge-internet kwi-website yale nhlangano, umunye ubiza uR399.Le nhlangano ithe kobhodisi abahlanu abathengwe kule nyanga, imali yowodwa izonikela ngayo ngokuthi ithenge owodwa ozonikezwa umfundi ofunda uGrade-11 noma uGrade-12 owudingayo.UKUPHUZA ngokweqile nokuya ocansini olungavikelekile, yizinto ezihamba phambili kweziyingozi ezingakubeka engcupheni yokuthola izifo kuleli.Lokhu kuvezwe muva nje, wucwaningo olwenziwe yisikhungo, iSouth African Medical Research Council (SAMRC). Lolu cwaningo luveza ukuthi izifo eziningi ezihlasela abantu ziyamaniswa nosikompilo abazikhethele lona.USolwazi Debbie Bradshaw wophiko olucwaninga ngezifo kulesi sikhungo, uthe ucwaningo lwakamuva luveza ukuthi esikhathini esiningi, uma kubhekwa imbangela yokufa komuntu ngaphambi kwesikhathi, bathole izinto ezidala lokho."Izinto ezifana nodlame lwasekhaya noma olwenzeka emphakathini, ukuya ocansini olungavikelekile, umfutho wegazi ophezulu, yizinto ezihamba phambili ezibulala abantu kuleli, esikholwa ukuthi zingavikeleka," kusho uSolwazi Bradshaw.Uqhube wathi kulolu cwaningo, ezinye zezinto ezitholakale kulo ziyefana nezitholakale ngo-2012, okuyizinto okumele ukuthi ziqashelwe ukuze kwehle izifo ezibulala abantu singekho isidingo.“Sikholwa wukuthi kusukela ngo-2020, ukuya ocansini olungaphephile sekwehlile. Ukusetshenziswa kwamakhondomu kwenyukile kodwa ukusabalala kwesifo akukehli. Uma singakwazi ukugwema ukuya ocansini olungaphephile singabona kwehla isibalo sabahaqwa yiHIV nezifo zocansi ezithathelanayo. Ukuphuzwa kotshwala kuyasetshenziswa njengendlela yokuthola ucansi olungaphephile," kusho uSolwazi Bradshaw.UGWAYI oxutshwe nokusamanzi okuthiwa usiza abafuna ukuyeka ukubhema obizwa nge-eletronic cigarette (e-cigaratte ) kawusizi ekutheni uyeke ugwayi ojwayelekile kanti futhi uyabiza.I-electronic cigarette kuthiwa iyindlela esetshenziswa ngabakhiqizi ukuze bahehe intsha ukuze ingene ithi shi ekuyisebenziseni. Ngakho kumele kube nendlela yokulawula ukusetshenziswa kwayo ngokuthi umthetho sivivinyo, iControl of Tobacco and Electronic Delivery System Bill ka-2018, wenziwe ube ngumthetho olawula ukusetshenziswa kwayo.USolwazi Olalekan Ayo wophiko lwesayensi ethinta ezempilo eNyuvesi iSefako Makgatho, uthe ucwaningo olwenziwe iHealth 24 ngo-2018  olubheka iminxa eminingi nge-e-cigarette, lukhomba ukuthi abantu abasebenzisa lolu hlobo lukagwayi olubhenywa ngokumunca isisi sikagwayi esiphuma sesinephunga lejusi, abayeki ukubhema. Uma kwenzekile bayeka kuba isikhashana kodwa babuye babuyele ekubhemeni ugwayi ojwayelekile."Esikutholile ngesikhathi senza ucwaningo ukuthi ngesikhathi lufika lolu hlobo lukagwayi, abakhiqizi bathi luwumuthi osiza ekutheni abafuna ukuyeka ugwayi bayeke kalula kodwa lokho akulona iqiniso ngoba lokho akwenzeki kwasebeke bawusebenzisa. Abantu abaningi abake bawusebenzisa uma kwenzekile bayeka ugwayi babuye babuyele kuwo futhi ngemuva kwesikhashana bewuyekile. Abanye kuvela ukuthi bakusebenzisa kokubili ngesikhathi esisodwa, uma besendaweni engakuvumeli ukuthi babheme ugwayi ojwayelekile babhema i-e cigarette. Uma besendaweni abakwaziyo ukubhema ugwayi ojwayelekile babheme wona," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi ucwaningo luveza ukuthi abantu ababuye babuyele ekubhemeni ugwayi bangu-60%.U-17% ukusebenzisa kanye kanye."Kubukeka sengathi abakhiqizi balo gwayi bahlose ukuheha abantu abasha ukuze bangene kuwo ngoba wona awulawulwa, ayikho intela abayikhokhayo. Zingu-240 izitolo ezidayisa ama-e cigarette kuleli. U-40% wazo uqhele ngamakhilomitha angu-10 ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme, u-65% wazo uqhele ezikhungweni ngamakhilomitha angu-20,"  kusho yena.USolwazi Israel Agaku ongumcwaningi oke abhale imiqingo yezempilo ngalolu hlobo lukagwayi, uthe abakhiqizi be-e cigarette baye bathi ushibhile uma uqhathaniswa nogwayi ojwayelekile."Ucwaningo olwenziwe ngo-2018, luveza ukuthi umuntu obhema zonke izinsuku ongabhemi ngokweqinile ubhema amabhokisi kagwayi angu-219 ngonyaka. Ngaleso sikhathi ibhokisi likagwayi elilodwa belibiza uR30.94c, okusho ukuthi ngonyaka usebenzisa uR4 387 kanti i-e cigarette isebenzisa izinto eziningi. Kuzo kuhlanganisa amalahle (batteries) ashintshwayo,  ijusi engu-100 ml kuya ku-200 ml ngesonto, nokunye okwenza ukuthi kuphume okusantuthu nakho okushintshwayo, konke lokho kwenza ithuluzi elilodwa elibhenywayo," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi umuntu obhemayo njengamanje usebenzisa uR6 933  ngonyaka kanti osebenzisa i-e cigarette usebenzisa uR8 781 kuya kuR19 781.UNkk Zanele Mthembu weSmoking Free Org,  uthe ulwazi abaluthole kososayensi luzobasiza ekutheni balwele ukuthi lo gwayi ulawulwe ngoba njengamanje kunabathi bawusebenzisa noma ikanjani ngoba bezitshela ukuthi uyelapha futhi ushibhile. INHLANGANO engenzi nzuzo, ebhekelele ukucwaninga ngamakhambi ezifo ezahlukene, iNational Association for Continence (NAFC), isiveze ukuthi ukhwantalala ngenye yezinto eholela ekutheni abantu bazichamele uma belele.I-NAFC iveze ukuthi inkinga yokuzichamela uma ulele phecelezi, i-bedwetting, ayihluphi izingane kuphela njengoba bekhona nasebekhulile abalala bavuke sebezishobingele ekuseni ngenxa yezinkinga ezahlukene.Enye yezinkinga ezidala lokho wukhwantalala, wukugqilazeka komqondo, wukuphathwa yizifo ezifana nesohlangothi, ukuvuvukala kwe-prostate gland, yinkinga yokuqwasha ebusuku nenkinga yokucindezeleka, ungakwazi ukuphefumula kahle uma ulele. I-NAFC ithi nakuba ziningi izizathu ezidala le nkinga, kodwa cishe u-2% wabantu abanenkinga yokuzichamela belele idalwa yizizathu zezempilo, ezingalapheka uma bezisukumela ngokushesha.“Kwezinye izingane ukuchama zilele kuyingxenye yokukhula, kepha ukuqhubeka noma sezikhulile kungaba yizimpawu salesi sifo esidinga ukufakelwa izibuko ngokushesha,” kusho iNAFC ocwaningweni lwayo.Ngokusho kweNAFC, ubungozi balesi sifo wukuthi sinomkhuba wokuqhubekela esizukulwaneni esizayo kulabo abakhule sibaphethe.Ithi ngokocwaningo elwenzile, izingane zabafana yizona ezisengcupheni yokuqhubeka nokuzichamela ngisho sezindala.Ukugwema ukuzithola usukule nkinga, ikhuthaza abantu ukuqaphela indlela abaphila ngayo, bagweme ukuphuza amanzi sekusele amahora ambalwa balale.“Okunye okusizayo wukuthi konke okuphuzwayo umuntu akuphuze aze adele phakathi nosuku engakadli isidlo sakusihlwa, ukwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi ipayipi lomchamo alunamthamo omningi ngesikhathi sokulala.“Abazame nokugwema ukuphuza utshwala neziphuzo ezine-caffeine; itiye nekhofi, ngezikhathi zasebusuku. Nakho ukuqala ngokuchama ngaphambi kokulala kusiza kakhulu ukugwema ukuzichamela usulele,” kucebisa iNAFC.I-NAFC inxuse abadala nabancane ukukhuthalela ukuhlola emtholampilo ukugwema ukuhlaselwa yizifo ezifana nalesi, nokuthi uma kwenzeka uqalwa yile nkinga usumdala, uphuthume kudokotela ukuze uthole usizo kusenesikhathi.AMADODA angaphila isikhathi eside uma engaqonda ukuthi ukuhlola izifo anazo kusemqoka futhi kuyawasiza. Kumele akufanise nalokho akwenza emotweni ukuze aqinisekise ukuthi ayinazo izinkinga.Lokhu kushiwo ngungoti oweluleka ngokomqondo, uDkt Aaron Mkhondo, eluleka amadoda ngokuthi azijwayeze ukuzihlola. Wathi lenyanga ephezulu ngokwekhalenda lezempilo kuleli, ngeyokubhekelela ezempilo emadodeni, iMen's Health Month.Ucwaningo olwenziwe kuleli luveza ukuthi mancane amathuba okuthi amadoda aye ezikhungweni zezempilo uma ezizwa sengathi kukhona angakuzwa kahle. Kuthiwa ayalinda aze agule kakhulu, ngaleso sikhathi izifo zisuke sezingene zagxila egazini.UDkt Mkhondo, ubeke kanje: "Sidinga ukuthi amadoda siwafundise ukuthi ukuzihlola kubaluleke njengokushintsha amathayi ezimoto, ukuhambisa imoto kwi-service noma ukupenda ekhaya. Amadoda kufanele aqonde ukuthi angaya kudokotela noma yinini, ngenhloso yokuyozihlola ukuthi aphila kahle, ukuzihlolela izifo zengqondo noma ukuyoxoxa nodokotela ngakuzwayo okungaba yingcindezi.”Uthe kumele kuqale ngokuthi abafana bazi ukuthi ayikho indaba yokuthi indoda ayikhali.Inhlangano yamadoda iMedshield Movement, ithe iminyaka yokuphila yamadoda yehle kakhulu eminyakeni edlule uma iqhathaniswa nango-1920.“Ngo-1920 iminyaka yokuphila yabesifazane nabesilisa beyehlukene ngonyaka owodwa, okusho ukuthi amadoda abengaphansi kwabesifazane ngonyaka owodwa. Ngo-2017 ucwaningo luveza ukuthi iminyaka yokuphila yamadoda ibisingaphansi kwephilwa ngabesifazane ngeminyaka emihlanu," kuchaza  iMedshield  Movement.Ngokolwazi lwenhlangano olutholakala kwi-internet, izifo ezihamba phambili ezibulala abesilisa kubalwa isifo senhliziyo, esomdlavuza nesikashukela.Siqhuba sithi amadoda kuyadingeka ukuthi abhekisise ukuthi adlani futhi azivocavovoce. UMnuz Murray Hewllet we-Affinity Health, uthe okunye ukudla kubangela ukuthi amadoda abe sengcupheni yokuhlaselwa yiqoqo lezifo zenhliziyo ezaziwa nge-ischaemic heart disease, okuyizo ezihamba phambili ngokubulala amadoda emhlabeni."Amadoda kumele agweme ukudla inyama ebomvu, ukudla okugayiwe okwenziwe ngayo inyama ebomvu, ukudla okuthosiwe, ukudla okugayiwe okwenziwe ngommbila, ukudla okunosawoti omningi. Kumele adle ukudla okune-omega -3 eningi," kusho uHewlett.Uthe imega -3 itholakala ngokudla inhlanzi okungaba yi-salmon, yi-mackerel, u-sardine noma yizitshalo ezinjengeFlaxseed, namakinati ama-walnut.Uthe enye into ebalulekile ukuthi ugcine ukhalo lunempilo. Uma ukhalo lwakho lungaphezulu kuka-101.6, lukhombisa ukuthi unamafutha amaningi esiswini. Ngokwe-National Heart, Lung, and Blood Institute, uma unomkhaba kusho ukuthi usengozini yokungenwa yizifo yezihlobene nokukhuluphala njengesikashukela esidalwa yindlela ophila ngayo, u-type2, isifo senhliziyo, nesifo sohlangothi.UHewlett uqhube wathi amadoda awakunaki ukuphuza amanzi enele. Uthe amanzi enele emzimbeni asiza ekutheni umzimba ukwazi ukumunca imisoco oyidingayo. Uthe okungenani umuntu kumele aphuze amalitha amathathu oketshezi ngosuku. Kubalwa itiye elenziwe ngamakhambi, amanzi nolunye uketshezi olungenalo utshwala noma i-caffeine.Uthe ukudla ngokweqile emadodeni kungenye yezinto ezidala ukukhuluphala ngoba athanda ukudla ipuleti eliqongile. NJENGOBA isiwombe sesithathu seCovid-19 sihlasele kuleli odokotela bayanxusa ukuthi iziguli ezidla imithi yokulawula izifo ezingamahlalakhona ziyidle ngendlela efanele ukuze kunciphe amathuba okuthola lesi sifo.UNkk Joy Steenkamp owusokhemisi eMedipost Pharmacy, uthe isiwombe sesithathi seCovid- 19 siqhutshwa ukusabalala kakhulu kwegciwane eselizishintshile iDelta .Iziguli ezinezifo ezingamahlalakhona uthe kumele ziqaphele ukuthi ziyidla ngendlela imithi yokuzilawula ukuze kunciphe amathuba okuthi zingenwe yileli gciwane." Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), leli gciwane ilichaza njengelisabalala kakhulu kunawo wonke akhona emhlabeni. Abantu abanezifo ezingamahlalakhona kunamathuba amaningi okuthi bathole leli gciwane ngenxa yokuthi amasosha abo omzimba asuke entekenteke, kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu onemithi ayidlayo ayidle ngendlela ukuze bangabi sengcupheni,"  kusho yena.Uthe kubalulekile ukuthi iziguli zisebenzise izinhlelo ezikhona zokuhanjiswa kwemithi emakhaya zingalokhu zidinga ukuthi ziyolanda imithi emitholampilo noma emakhemisi.Kukholakala ukuthi u-97% wabantu abahaqwe yiCovid-19 kuleli bangenwe yiDelta.“Okunye okubalulekile  ukuthi abantu asebegomile bazi ukuthi nabo isengabangena iCovid-19 futhi bakwazi ukuyidlulisela kwabanye abantu. Bona mancane amathuba okuthi leli gciwane libagulise kakhulu njengoba sebegomile. Kubalulekile  ukuthi abantu noma sebegomile bayilandele imigomo bagweme ukuhlangana nabantu uma singekho isidingo. Ukuthunyelelwa imithi yakho ekhaya kungenye yezinto ezingakusiza ukuze ungahlangani nabantu okukunciphisela amathuba okuthola leli gciwane. Uma uke wahlangana nomuntu onaleli gciwane kusabalulekile ukuthi ugonqe izinsuku eziyishumi" kusho yena.Uqhube wathi kuwumsebenzi wesiguli ukuthi silandele indlela eyiyo yokudla imithi yaso. Usokhemisi kumele asichazele isiguli ngolimi esiluqondayo ukuze kungabi khona inkinga,"  kusho yena.UNkk Rentia Myburgh naye weMedipost Pharmacy, uthe  njengamanje kungakuhle ukuthi ugweme ukuya ekhemisi ngenxa yokuthi uzohlangana nabantu, kodwa ikhemisi kubalulekile ukuthi lihlele ukuthi ufonelwe umuntu okhuluma ulimi lwesiguli ukuze sizwe kahle konke esichazelwa kona ngemithi." Uma lokho kungeke kwenzeke  isiguli kumele siye ekhemisi noma esikhungweni sezempilo lapho silanda khona imithi bese silandela imigomo yokuqhelelana ngesikhathi sichazelwa,"  kusho yena.UKUDLA okuthile kungaholela ekutheni imithi yokwelapha isifo somdlavuza ithikamezeke.UDkt Omy Naidoo owungoti wezokudla, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi isiguli esinomdlavuza seseke umzimba waso ngokudla ukudla okunempilo  namavithamini ukuze umzimba waso uthole imisoco oyidingayo."Iziguli ezinomdlavuza kuyenzeka zingakuthandi ukudla, ngakho kumele ukuthi ukudla ezikudlayo kube nesiqiniseko sokuthi kunemisoco edingekayo," kusho uDkt Naidoo.Uthe ezikhungweni zezempilo ezelapha umdlavuza akekho ungoti oweluleka lezi ziguli ngokuthi yikuphi ukudla okumele zikudle."Uma unelungu lomndeni elinalesi sifo kumele wazi ukuthi yini okumele idliwe yisiguli. Kumele ukhulume nodokotela, kube nguyena okwelulekayo. Uma ufisa ukunikeza isiguli imithi yemvelo, kumele ukhulume nodokotela kuqala ngoba kungenzeka imithi oyinika isiguli ishayisane nemithi eselashwa ngayo," kusho yena.Uqhube wathi kunokudla okumele iziguli ezinomdlavuza ezisohlelweni lokwelashwa okumele zikugweme noma zehlise kukho.Kulokhu kudla ubale utshwala. Okunye wukudla okugaywe kwacoliseka kakhulu, okunoshukela kakhulu, okuhlanganisa amakhekhe noswidi neziphuzo ezinoshukela, wokunosawoti omningi, okunamafutha amaningi ezilwane nenyama enongiwe okufana nobhekeni, amasosishi nenyama yengulube.Nakhu ukudla athe kunconywa ukuthi iziguli ezinomdlavuza zikudle:Izithelo eziningi nemifino zonke izinsuku, yinyama enganonile okungaba yinyama yenkukhu (umkhwepha) noma inhlanzi.Okusanhlamvu okungaba wubhontshisi, wuphizi ama-lentils ne-quinoa.Okunokolweni kungaba yirayisi elinsundu nepasta.Amakinati ngezinye zezinto okumele iziguli ezinalesi sifo zigxile kuwo.Ukudla okunamafutha okunempilo athe kuzilungele iziguli ezinomdlavuza wukwatapheya, i-olive oil nenhlanzi yohlobo lwe-sardine."Iziguli ezinomdlavuza isikhathi esiningi ziba nenkinga yokucanuzela kwenhliziyo, ziphalaze kwesinye isikhathi zikhishwe yisisu, ngakho kubalulekile ukuthi uma kubonakala ukuthi ngeke sikwazi ukudla isiguli, usinike okunye ukudla okuzosinika umsoco olinganayo. Ezinye iziguli kudingeka ukuthi zinikezwe ukudla okunqamula ukucanuzela kwenhliziyo nokuphalaza," kusho uDkt Naidoo.Uthe uma unenkinga yokuthi ilungu lomndeni kalikuthandi ukudla noma licanuzelelwa yinhliziyo, zama ukulinika ukudla ngezikhawu  kunokuthi lidle kathathu njengoba kujwayelekile."Uma isiguli sihluleka nokuphuza uketshezi yenza ijusi ne-yoghurt yenze isiqeda ukuze siyincele. Uma sikwazi ukudla i-yoghurt faka amakinati kuyona," kuchaza uDkt Naidoo.Uthe kubalulekile ukuthola iseluleko kudokotela sokuthi uma isiguli sehla isisindo. UKUDLA okunesikhutha kungadala izinkinga zempilo, okubalwa kuzo ukuphazamiseka kolibovuzo, umdlavuza wesibindi kubantu nasezilwaneni.Ngempelasonto isitolo esidayisa ukudla nezimpahla, iPick n Pay, sihoxise ukudayisa i-peanut butter eyizihlobo ezintathu ngoba sithe sihlola imikhiqizo, okuyinto abathi yenziwa njalo. Sithole ukuthi inohlobo lwesikhutha i-aflatoxins.Lesi sikhutha abezimpilo bathi siwushevu futhi singaholela ekutheni umuntu ashone uma edle ukudla okunezinga eliphezuli laso.Inhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), kwisizindalwazi sayo, ithi isikhutha i-aflatoxins siyingxenye yomndeni wezikhutha owaziwa ngeMycotoxins, akhela ezitshalweni."Imiphumela yokudla ukudla okunamanye ama-mycotoxins kungaba wukugula ngokushesha ngemuva kokudla lokho kudla, eminye kuba wukugula isikhathi eside okuhlanganisa ukungenwa isifo somdlavuza. Ama-mycotoxins avamise ukutholakala ekudleni angu-12," kusho iWHO. Umbiko weWHO okhuluma ngobungozi besikhutha nezinhlobo zazo okhishwe nyakenye, uveza ukuthi ama-aflatoxins ayingxenye yomndeni yezikhutha imycotoxin, enobuthi kakhulu futhi akhiqizwa yisikhutha i-Aspergillus flavus ne-Aspergillus parasiticus. Simila enhlabathini, ezitshalweni ezibolayo, otshanini nasezitshalweni ezisanhlamvu. Izitshalo ezivame ukuthinteka kuba sezitshalweni ezisanhlamvu, ummbila, amabele, ukolweni nelayisi. Ezitshalweni ezikhiqiza imbewu yamafutha itholakala kwisoya, amakinati, imbewu kabhekilanga nekakotini. Ezinongweni itholakala kupelepele ojwayelekile, upelepele omnyama, i-coriander, i-turmeric ne-ginger. Emantongomaneni asezihlahleni itholakala kwi-almond, i-walnut, ukhukhunathi nakwiBrazil nut. Lobu buthi bungatholakala nasobisini lwezilwane eziphakelwa ukudla okunalesi sikhutha.Olunye uhlobo lwesikhutha oludumile yi-Ochratoxin A,  ikhiqizwa i-Aspergillus nePenicillium, ivame ukutholakala ezitshalweni ezisanhlamvu,  okuwubhontshisi wekhofi, izithelo zomvini owomile, iwayini nejusi yamagilebhisi, nasezinongweni zotshwala. Lolu hlobo lwesikhutha lwakheka ngesikhathi  isitshalo sisagciniwe futhi saziwa ngokuthi sigulisa izilwane eziphakelwe izitshalo ezinaso.Uma kwenzekile umuntu wadla lolu hlobo lwesikhutha olungaphezulu kokwamukelekile, angalimala izinso, uma kuyingane kungehla ukusebenza kwamasosha omzimba.IPatulin  ngolunye uhlobo lwesikhutha olungena ngaphansi komndeni i-Mycotoxin ekhiqizwa yi-Aspergillus, Penicillium neByssochlamys. Ivamise ukutholakala ezithelweni ama-aphula  nasemikhiqizweni eyakhiwa ngalo i-apula. Uma isilwane zidle ukudla okunalesi sikhutha sihlaselwa isifo sezinso, ubende nesibindi konakale namasosha omzimba waso. Kubantu sidala ukucanuzela kwenhliziyo ukuphalaza, isilungulela nokunye.Fusarium fungi, wolunye uhlobo lwesikhutha esitholakala enhlabathini. Sivamise ukwakhela ezitshalweni ezikhiqiza izidlo zasekuseni. Lesi sikhutha kubantu sidala izinkinga zesikhumba, emathunjini sidala uketshezi oludala ukuthi umuntu ahanjiswe isisu. I-WHO ithi kuke kwabikwa ukuthi lolu hlobo lwesikhutha lungaholela ekutheni umuntu ahlaselwe wumdlavuza wombilo, ezilwaneni singaholela ekutheni zibe nomdlavuza wezinso nesibindi.UmbuzoNGINGOWESILISA owalimala engozini yemoto maqede washayeka ngezansi. Odokotela bazama ukungisiza kodwa kubukeka sengathi bayahluleka. Yize sekuphele iminyaka emine ngalimala kodwa namanje imizwa yami nobuntu bami akusebenzi ngendlela efanele. Sengize ngahlukana nomuntu ebengizwana naye ngenxa yokuthi bengingasakwazi ukumanelisa ngezidingo zakhe zocansi. Ngikhathazekile ngoba ngiyafisa ukuba nomuntu wesifazane kodwa ngiyabona ukuthi ngeke kusenzeka. Ngifana nento efile, ngibe ngiphila.Ngicela uma kukhona ongangisiza ngenduku yami nemizwa yami ukuze kubuyele esimweni, angisize. Ngicela ozongicebisa  ngokuthi ngingenzenjani uma kwenzeka ngithola owesifazane.ImpenduloNgiyazwelana nesimo sakho bhuti. Njengoba ubona ukuthi odokotela bahlulekile, awuke uzame nezimbiza zesintu, mhlawumbe uzosizakala. Uma kuhlula lapho-ke, kuhle uma uthola owesifazane obonayo ukuthi uzimisele ngawe umchazele ngenkinga yakho bese niba nesu lokuthi nizojabulisana kanjani. Ngizokunika izindlela ongazisebenzisa ukuze ujabulise owesifazane.*Ningathenga ithoyizi ozomdlalisa ngalo aze afike kuvuthondaba.*Ungasebenzisa ulimu umkhothe aze achame noma umdlalise ngomunwe.Konke lokhu uzokwenza ngokuvumelana naye emuva kwengxoxo yenu ejulile nokuyilapho uzomchazela khona yonke into ngoba inhloso ukwakha umuzi. Ngikufisela inhlanhla.DKT BONGANI NXUMALOSisesikhathini sonyaka lapho imindeni nabathandanayo bezoba ndawonye, abanye bazohlangana emva kwesikhathi eside bagcinana. Abazukuhlangana nje kuphela kodwa bazoba ndawonye isikhathi eside uma uqhathanisa nezinye izikhathi.Abantu besilisa ezindaweni ezehlukene baphansi phezulu bayazilolonga, bayazibhila ngezindlela ezehlukene, bazicijela ukuthi bafike babe 'yizikhokho' ekujabulisaneni ngokocansi ngalawa maholidi.Izimo ezinjena azibhekene kuphela nabafowethu abasuke bengekho emakhaya isikhathi eside kodwa  nalabo abahlale besemakhaya banenselelo efanayo.Indaba yovuthondaba wutalagu abanye abaluzwa ngendaba, asebeluzame isikhathi eside kodwa lutho!Kokunye sebaze bazitshela ukuthi mhlawumbe baloywa ngukhokhovu olwashona seluvaleke amehlo nomlomo.Sake sachaza kule ngosi ukuthi uvuthondaba lufika njengomnkenenezo, kube sengathi kunokubanda eqolo nasemgogodleni, zonke izicubu zomzimba zivele zivume ngengoma eyodwa; uzizwe usuphimisela amazwi ongeke wazi ukuthi afike kanjani ezindebeni zomlomo kokunye uze umemeze uthi, ‘alibongwe igama leNkosi, wamuhle Jehova, Ameni!’Umbuzo obalulekile uthi sifika kanjani kuvuthondaba? Yini eyenza abanye bafike kathathu emzuliswaneni owodwa ekubeni kukhona abaluzwa ngendaba akufikeki mpela mpela.Impendulo yale mibuzo ilele ekukhumbuleni ukuthi ucansi akusiyena ungena uyaphuma sengathi uxova udaka ngezinyawo.Ucansi akusikhona ukujaha omunye ngomunwe, umvalele ekhoneni umuntu wabantu, ugcine ufake amagciwane esithweni sakhe sangasese.Angikhohlwa ukugcizelela ukuthi ucansi akusikhona ukuhlasela amabele, upheke izingono ngebhodwe lendlala ngoba wezwa kuthiwa ungabowakhohlwa amabele.Ucansi ngukulungisana ngendlela efanele, kusukela engxoxweni yamehlo, ezandleni ezifukamele inkulumo, kuze kuyofika ekudlaliseni ubulili.Fikani ekwabelaneni ngobulili ngokungqongqoza kancane kancane!Lokhu akudingi halakasha lwenduku, kuphela ulwazi lokuthi uthi qo qo kuphi bese ulandelisa kuphi?Uyabona umuntu owazi ukungqongqoza ngendlela ehlelekile ngeke umkhohlwe empilweni yakho!Akuyi nhlobo ngokuthi uphethe umshiza nohalakasha lwenduku, akungeni ndawo lokhu.Uyazi nawe ukuthi uma usondela enkosini uyagaqa uhlonipha.Nakhona uma nizijabulisa awuvele ufuhleleke nje ungene kepha ungena uhlonipha, ushaye indesheni ukuze ungene kamnandi nithokoze nobabili.Ngaso sonke isikhathi kumele ukhumbule ukuthi kubalulekile ukuthi nobabili nomlingani wakho kumele nijabule, makungajabuli wena wedwa.Uma wenze njalo, uyozwa ngemikhemezelo nemisinjwana yokuzwakalisa ubumnandi ezobe ifakazela ukuthi umsebenzi ushaya khona nakuwe sekunzima ukuqinisela.Ngena kahle nje unyakazise igumbi laseNtshonalanga, Nyakatho, Ningizimu neMpumalanga ulokhu uwaphindaphinda amagumbi.Uma uzimisele ngokuthola unqambothi lovuthondaba zifundise ukulalela umlingani wakho yikhona uzokuzwa uma uthinta lapho kumnandi khona kakhulu noma uma uthinta ngendlela ewunqambothi.Uyozwa izwi elithi ‘Uyesabeka Ongabonwayo!Khumbula ungaxhamazeli, thatha isikhathi sakho, landela isigqi somlingani wakho ahamba ngaso, nithokoze nobabili.Ngalesi sikhathi uzithinta ngenduku yakho lezi zindawana, izandla zakho zona zilumbanisa imizwa esezihlathini, ekhanda, emabeleni, entanyeni, ucumbaza izindlebe, amazwi amtoti emlonyeni!Nakanjani uyozwa senikhuluma izilimi, nozwakala nobabili senithi, ‘ngiyabonga akukaze kubenje’….. qathatha senifikile kuvuthondaba!Tshela mina iliphi-ke iqhaza lohalakasha kabhomubhomu wenduku la?Mpilonde!!UKUNGAZIGEZI izandla kuholela ekusabalaleni kwamagciwane adala izifo ezihlasela izingane ezincane.U-Dkt Nellie Naranjee wophiko olufundisa ubuhlengikazi eNyuvesi iDurban University of Technology (DUT), uthe ukuqubuka kwezifo eziningi, uzagiga, isimungumungwane, ukuvuvukala komphimbo okuhambisana nokushisa iDiphtheria ezinganeni kwesinye  isikhathi kudalwa wukuthi izingane ezincane azizigezi izandla.Ngenxa yokubona lokhu lolu phiko luqale uhlelo lokuthi lufundise izingane ezisezikoleni zamabanga aphansi ngokubaluleka kokugeza izandla, oluluqale ngo-Agasti."Izingane zisengozini enkulu yezifo ezihlobene nokuntuleka  kwamanzi ahlanzekile, ukuhanjiswa kwendle nokuhlanzeka. Ukufundisa indlela efanele yenhlanzeko kuyisinyathelo esibalulekile ekwehliseni ukugula nokusabalala kwezifo eziningi. Ukugeza izandla ngendlela efanele kunganciphisa amathuba okuthola amagciwane, kunciphisa namathuba okugula," kusho uDkt Naranjee.Izitshudeni ezenza izifundo zobuhlengikazi kule nyuvesi okuyizona eziqhuba lolu hlelo, zenze izifundo zokunqanda ukusabalala kwamagciwane, i-Infection Prevention and Control Certificate ukuze zikwazi ukufundisa ngenhlanzeko abafundi basezikoleni zasemabangeni aphansi.U-Dkt Naranjee uqhube wathi amasosha omzimba ezingane asuke engakaqini ngokwenele futhi nazo izingane ziyathanda ukusebenzisa izandla zithinta izinto ezithile, zibuye zifake lezo zandla emlonyeni."Kuyenzeka ukuthi izandla ezisuke sezithinte izinto ezinamagciwane zizifake emlonyeni noma zithinte izingxenye zomzimba bese lawo magciwane engena emzimbeni. Ingane igcine iguliswa yisifo ebesingavikeleka ukube beyifundisiwe ukuthi kayigeze izandla njalo,"  kusho uDkt Naranjee.Usho kanjena nje ngeSonto bekuwusuku lokugqugquzela ukuthi abantu bageze izandla, iWorld Handwashing Day, olugujwa minyaka yonke ngo-Okthoba 15, kusukela ngo-2008.U-Nkk  Claire Bowen wenkampani ekhiqiza izinto zokugcoba  nensipho iShower to Shower, uthe ukuze ube nesiqiniseko sokuthi izandla zigezeke kahle kumele uzigeze imizuzwana engu-20." Ukuze ube nesiqiniseko sokuthi uthathe isikhathi esanele ngesikhathi ugeza izandla, ungacula ingoma yosuku lokuzalwa uyiphinde kabili. Ngesikhathi uzigeza izandla khipha udoti ezinzisheni naphakathi kweminwe,"  kugcizelela uNkk Bowen.Uqhube wathi kumele uqiniseke ukuthi ugcoba insipho ezandleni, uyihlikihle kahle ngaphambi kokuthi uyihlambulule ngamanzi."Amagciwane angacasha ezindaweni ezingalindelekile. Qinisekisa ukuthi kawugezi intende yezandla  kuphela, geza iminwe namalungu akho. Amalungu avame ukunganakwa, kanti nawo ayawathwala amagciwane. Khuhla ngaphansi kwezinzipho zakho ngebhulashi lezinzipho noma usebenzisa iminwe yakho. Nakuba amanzi abandayo nawo ewenza umsebenzi kodwa amanzi afudumele  asusa amafutha namagciwane kalula. Bese wesula izandla zakho ngethawula noma uzomise ngomshini wokomisa izandla okhipha umoya,“ kugcizela uNkk Bowen. UKWENYUKA kwezibalo zabantu abavakashela odokotela bekhiswa yisisu kukhomba ukuthi igciwane le-Covid-19 lisekhona emoyeni futhi liyakwazi ukudala inkinga yokukhishwa yisisu ezinye izimpawu zingabi khona.UDkt Morgan Mkhatshwa, oyinhloko yokusebenza kwansukuzonke kwiBonitas Medical Fund, uthe uma kwehla izibalo zabahaqwa yi-Covid-19, kukhomba ukuthi umphakathi usufundile ukulandela imigomo yokunqanda ukusabalala kwaleli gciwane, wathi kodwa ukwanda kwabantu abahlushwa yisisu kukhomba ukuthi lisekhona.Uthe okunye okubuye kufake ingcindezi yesisu ukuthi phakathi kukaNovemba noMeyi, amagciwane aholela ekutheni abantu baphathwe isisu asuke ekhona emoyeni.UDkt Mkhatshwa uthe umkhuhlane wesisu ojwayelekile  i-igastroenteritis  ubonakala ngokuhlambuluka kwesisu, amajaqamba esiswini,  ukuphalaza, ubuhlungu bekhanda, ukucanuzela kwenhliziyo nokomela amanzi.Uthe lezi zimpawu zivela kumuntu phakathi kwamahora angu-24 kuya kwangu-72 ethole igciwane.Uthe ngokujwayelekile lezi zimpawu ziyaphela ngemuva kwezinsuku ezintathu noma ezine, akujwayelekile ukuthi umuntu angazizwa kahle kuze kuphele isonto.Uthe igciwane lesisu elijwayelekile nelingene ngokudla agulisana ngendlela efanayo.Uthe ucwaningo ngeCovid-19 luveza ukuthi u-10%  wabantu abadala abahaqwe yiCovid-19  bakhishwa yisisu, baphalaze okuhambisana nenkinga yokuphefumula, nokukhwehlela kodwa kwabanye kuyenzeka sihambe sodwa."Ngeshwa akulula ukwazi ukuthi isisu esikuphethe umsuka waso uyini, ngaphandle uma uzobuye ube nezimpawu ezifana nobuhlungu besifuba kanye nokungalizwa iphunga nobumnandi. Uma ube nalezo zimpawu kuba lula ukuhlukanisa," kusho  yenaUthe uma usola ukuthi izimpawu zesizu onazo kungenzeka ukuthi zisho ukuthi une-Covid-19, kumele ufonele udokotela wakho."Udokotela usuke ezokweluleka ngokuthi uyozihlola ukuthi awunayo yini iCovid-19, uma ebona ukuthi lezi zimpawu onazo zisondelene neCovid-19. Amagciwane athinta uhudo athelelana kalula ikakhulukazi emahoreni angu-72 okuqala, kubalulekile ukuthi uzinakekele," kusho yena.Uthe ukusondelana nomuntu onawo ngokuthintana ngemilomo noma ukuthinta lapho kade ethinte khona kungaholela ekutheni nawe ulithole leli gciwane.UNGQONGQOSHE wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, uNkk Nomagugu Simelane-Zulu unxuse abantu besifazane ukuthi bakukhuthalele ukuhlola umdlavuza webele ne-pap smear.UNkk Simelane-Zulu  uthe kuyamkhathaza ukuthi izinhlelo zokuqwashisa nokukhuthaza  abantu ukuthi bazihlole umdlavuza ziyaphazamiseka ngenxa yokuhlasela kweCovid-19.“Ukuhlolwa komdlavuza webele ngebhadi kubukeka kungabalulekile njengokuvika ukusabalala kweCovid-19 esibhekene nayo. Ukuhlolwa umdlavuza webele kubalulekile kubantu besifazane nasemadodeni . Abantu besifazane kubalulekile ukuthi bahlale bezihlola ukuthi abanawo yini umdlavuza webele kanti amadoda wona kumele ahlale ebheka ukuthi izibele zawo azinalo yini ushintsho. Uma kukhona okubonakala kuwushintsho kumele babonane nabezempilo ngokushesha,"  kusho yena.Uthe ukuhlale uzibheka uma uyindoda kumele kwenziwe ngamadoda aneminyaka ewu-35 kuya phezulu ngoba yibo abasengcupheni yokuthi bahlaselwe umdlavuza webele.." Kubalulekile ukuthi sikhuthaze ukuthi abantu bahlolwe umdlavuza ngendlela elinganayo nesigqugquzela ngayo ukuthi abantu bazame ukuziphephisa kwiCovid-19,"  kusho uNkk Simelane-Zulu.Uthe KwaZulu-Natal kusenabantu abakholelwa ekutheni ngeke baphathwe umdlavuza ngoba bekholwa ukuthi umdlavuza uphatha abantu abamhlophe kuphela." Ukucabanga kanjalo kuholela ekutheni noma umuntu esegula aphuze ukuya esikhungweni sezempilo ngoba engacabangi ukuthi unomdlavuza. Agcine eye esikhungweni sezempilo sekuhambe isikhathi nokugula sekuhambe kakhulu kanti imidlavuza eminingi iyelapheka uma usheshe waqala uhlelo lokwelashwa,"  kusho uNgqongqoshe.I-website i-Pinkvilla kuleli sonto iveze ukuthi ukukhuluphala ngokweqile kwenyusa amathuba okuhlaselwa umdlavuza webele.Le website iveze ukuthi abantu abaningi bakhuluphaliswa ukuthi abaqapheli ukuthi badlani. Ithi iningi labantu linengcindezi yomsebenzi okuholela ekutheni  bagcine bedla ukudla okungenayo impilo bese beyakhuluphala, okubadalela inkinga yokuthi kube lula ukuthi bangenwe yizifo okukhona kuzo nesifo somdlavuza.Ngokwale website abantu besifazane bakhuluphala kakhulu uma sebefika esikhathini lapho bengasayi ezinsukwini zabo kodwa ithi lokho akusho ukuthi uma ukhuluphale ngaphambi kwale sikhathi ungcono." Uma ukhuluphale ngalesi sikhathi uqala ukuba sengozini ngesikhathi kubonakala ukuthi ukhuluphele ngokweqile, abakhule bevele bekhuluphele ngokweqile ubungozi bungcono kubo uma beqhathaniswa. nabesifazane abasengcupheni enkulu abanamafutha amaningi esinqeni, emathangeni nasokhalo,"  kuchaza i-website.Inhloko yoMnyango wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal , uDkt  Sandile Tshabalala, ithe kubalulekile ukuthi abantu babheke kakhulu ukudla abakudlayo kakhulukazi ukudla okunoshukela, bagweme nokubhema. UKUNGALALI ngokwanele kungaholela ekutheni iziguli ezinegciwane lesandulela ngculazi zihlaselwe izifo ezifana nesifo sikashukela esidalwa indlela umuntu aphila ngayo, ukukhuluphala ngokweqile nezifo zenhliziyo.Lokhu kushiwo uDkt Nomathemba Chandiwana ongumqondisi nososayensi esikhungweni esenza ucwaningo ngeHIV, Ezintsha Research Centre  esiseJohannesburg.Uthe ukuphumula ekhaya nokulala kubalulekile kubantu bonke ngoba uma kungenzeki kudala izinkinga zezempilo."Umuntu ophila negciwane lesandulela ngculazi, oseqale imishanguzo ngesikhathi, kufanele aphile isikhathi esifanayo njengesomuntu ongenayo i-HIV, kodwa esikwaziyo ukuthi umuntu one-HIV, ngokwesilinganiso, uphila iminyaka  engaphansi kwaleyo abengayiphila uma engenasifo ngeminyaka engu-16.“Lezi ziguli zivame ukuhlaselwa isifo sikashukela sohlobo II, izinkinga zempilo yengqondo, ukukhuluphala ngokweqile nesifo senhliziyo. Siyazi ukuthi ukungalali kahle kuhlobene nalokhu, "kusho yena.UDkt Chandiwana uthe isayensi ecubungula ukulala isewumkhakha omusha wezokwelapha. Uqhubeke ngokuthi kunocwaningo olwenziwa yilesi sikhungo, sibheka ukuthi ukungalali ngabe kuwaphazamisa kanjani amasosha omzimba kanjalo nokuthi kungani iziguli ezineHIV zigcina zinesifo sokuvuvukala noma ngabe ziphile kahle futhi nemishanguzo igazi lazo liyemukela kahle.Uthe ngenxa yokuthi kuningi okungaziwa kahle ngalo mkhakha kusadingeka ukuthi kutshalwe imali yokucwaninga, kuphinde kuqeqeshwe nabacwaningi ukuthi bakwazi ukucwaninga ngalo mkhakha."Sinemininingwane emincane yase-Afrika mayelana nokuphazamiseka kokulala nokungalali kahle," kunezelela uChandiwana.USolwazi Karine Scheuermaier we-Wits University Brain Function Research Group, okuyisikhungo esidala kunazo zonke esicwaninga ngokubaluleka kokulala isikhathi esenele kuleli.Uthe umphakathi uyaliqonda iqhaza lokuzivocavoca nokudla ukudla okunempilo kodwa awuqondi ukuthi kubaluleke ngani ukuthi ulale isikhathi esenele ukuze umzimba usebenze kahle. Uma ungalali wenza ukuthi kube lula ukuthi umzimba uthole izifo."Senza konke ngesikhathi okumele ngabe silala ngaso. Ukulala kwabanye kuthathwa njengophawu lobuvila emphakathini owazi ukuthi ukusebenza ikona okubalulekile kunokulala," kusho uSolwazi Scheuermaier.Uqhube wathi ukuhlelwa kwezindawo zobandlululo kwaphoqa abantu abamnyama ukuthi bahlale kude nezindawo zemisebenzi.Abasebenzi abaningi basavuka ekuseni kakhulu bayosebenza. Uma bephuma emsebenzini bama olayini abade belinde izinto zokugibela  bafike emakhaya sebekhathele. Emakhaya bafika banakekele izingane noma amalungu omndeni asekhulile ngaphambi kokuthi balale."Ukuhlala emijondolo eminyene kuphazamisa ukulala kahle, kunomsindo ophezulu kuhlale kukhanya.“Emikhakheni yokusebenza kunamashifu okusebenza ebusuku kubo okubalwa abasebenza ezinkundleni zezobuchwepheshe, abashayela izimoto ezikhokhelwa ngebanga ezilihambile konke lokhu kuphazamisa ukulala," kuphetha uSolwazi Scheuermaier.Ukuxubha kabili nsuku zonke akwanele ukuqinisekisa ukuthi amazinyo akho ahlala ehlanzekile, futhi ngeke kukusize ukugwema iphunga elibi elithaphuka emlonyeni wakho uma ukhuluma noma uzamula.Lokhu  kushiwo wudokotela wamaziyo ozimele uDkt Fanele Mthethwa weHlangalezwe Dental Care, yaseMzinyathi, eNanda enyakatho yeTheku.UDkt Mthethwa uthe amazinyo omuntu nomuntu azalela izilwanyana ezibizwa ngama-micro-organism ezidla izinsalela zokudla okudliwa wumuntu ezigaxela emazinyweni uma uqeda ukudla.“Kuthi noma seziphelile izinsalela zokudla, lezi zilwanyana ziqhubeke ziququde amazinyo omuntu, agcine esenezimbobo, okwenza kube lula ukungena udoti kuzona. Udoti lowo uthi ungagcwala ezimbotsheni, udale iphunga elibi elithaphuka uma umuntu esekhuluma noma ezamula.“Enye into edala iphunga elibi emlonyeni wukungagayeki kahle kokudla esiswini, okudala ukuthi uma umuntu esekhuluma, kuthaphuke iphunga elibi ngoba umoya esiwuphefumulayo usuka phansi esiswini, uye phezulu,” kusho uDkt Mthethwa.Eqhuba, uthe inkinga enkulu wukuthi abantu abakukhuthaleli ukuya kodokotela bamaziyo ukuhlanza amazinyo abo njalo emva kwezinyanga eziyisithupha, njengokuyalela kwabezempilo.“Abantu abaningi bazitshela ukuthi ukuxubha kabili ngosuku kwanele ukugcina amazinyo ehlanzekile, kanti akunjalo. Kuningi okumele umuntu akuqaphele futhi akwenze ukuhlanza amazinyo akhe, futhi agweme iphunga elibi emlonyeni,” kusho yena.Ucebise ngokuthi abantu baqale ngokudla ngaphambi kokuxubha, hhayi ukuxubha bese ugcina ngokudla.Uthe okunye okubalulekile wukusebenzisa i-tooth floss, okuyintambo yokuvungula ukudla okusalele emazinyweni ngaphambi kokuxubha.“Ngicebisa abantu ukusebenzisa izixubho ezibhalwe ukuthi soft noma eziwu-medium, hhayi eziwu-hard ngoba zona zilimaza amazinyo nezinsini. Kumqoka futhi nokuthi umuntu ashintshe isixubho asisebenzisayo njalo emva kwezinyanga ezintathu.“Abantu abathenge nama-mouth wash, imikhiqizo esiza ukukhuculula amagciwane angasuseki ngesixubho, bese bezijwayeza ukubonana nodokotela bamazinyo ukuze amazinyo abo ahlale ehlanzekile futhi kunganuki kabi uma umuntu evula umlomo,” kuphetha uMthethwa.UKUNQATSHELWA kweziguli ezingenawo amaphepha achaza ukuthi zingobani bakuphi ezikhungweni zezempilo zakuleli kuholela ekutheni izifo zisabalale.Lokhu kushiwo uDkt Tasanya Chinsamy weMédecins Sans Frontières (MSF), ebuye ibizwe ngokuthi iDoctors Without Borders ngesikhathi kunesithangami sokucobelelana ngolwazi ebesibheka ukuthi ngabe abesifazane abazithwele nezingane ezineminyaka engaphansi kweyisithupha, abahlala kuleli bayasizakala yini ezikhungweni zezempilo zakuleli mahhala njengoba kulawula uMthethosisekelo.UNkk Sibusisiwe Ndlela weSection 27 uthe imibiko abayitholile ukuthi abesifazane nezingane bangaphandle abangenawo amaphepha kuyenzeka banqatshelwe usizo ezikhungweni zikahulumeni, noma kuthiwe abakhokhe ngoba abanawo amaphepha. UDkt Chinsamy uthe: “UMthethosisekelo wakuleli uthi bonke abesifazane abahlala ezweni, abangenayo imishwalense yezempilo banelungelo lokuthola usizo lwezempilo mahhala, uma bekhulelwe nezingane abazizalayo ezineminyaka eyisithupha noma ngaphansi kumele zithole usizo lwezempilo mahhala ezikhungweni zezempilo. Akukhathalekile ukuthi banawo amaphepha noma cha. Lokhu akwenzeki kwezinye izikhungo ikakhulukazi ezibhedlela. Laba besifazane bayaya emitholampilo, badluliselwe ezibhedlela bafike babhekane nenkinga yokuthi kuthiwe abakhokhe," kusho yena.Uthe ukunqatshelwa kwabo kungabukeka sengathi kungukonga izinsiza ezibekelwe abantu bakuleli kodwa ngakolunye uhlangothi kungukusabalalisa izifo."Ake ucabange ukuthi uma kunqatshelwa isiguli usizo lwezempilo kanti sinesifo esithathelanayo esifana neHIV nesifo sofuba singasisabalalisa kubantu abaningi bakuleli," kusho yena.Uthe ezinye iziguli zize zisizakale ngokuthi zingene ezibhedlela sezifika ngamaambulensi."Lezi ziguli ziyasizakala kodwa kwesinye isikhathi azinikezwa ubufakazi bokuthi zibelethile, bese zingakwazi ukwenzela izingane zazo izitifiketi zokuzalwa. Uma ingane ezelwe idinga ukuya esikhungweni sezempilo noma esikoleni iba nenkinga ngoba akukho bufakazi bokuthi yazalelwa kuphi." UNkk Lisel Muller weCentre for Child Law, uthe uMthethosisekelo wakuleli ugunyaza bonke omama abazithwele nezingane ukuthi bathole usizo lwezempilo abaludingayo mahhala ezikhungweni zezempilo zikahulumeni."Abantu abaningi uma benqabela abangaphandle usizo basuke bekwenziswa ukuthi abanamaphepha. Inkinga ekhona ukuthi noma ngabe bakwenza ngoba becabanga kanjalo kodwa kunabantu abaningi bakuleli abangenawo amaphepha achaza ukuthi ngabakuphi ngoba abazali babo abanabo omazisi. Kuleli obaba basanda kunikezwa igunya lokuthi nabo bangakwazi ukushayela izingane zabo izitifiketi zokuzalwa kodwa uma beya emahhovisi oMnyango wezaseKhaya abavunyelwa. Inkinga eyenzekayo eyokuthi uma umama wengane engenawo umazisi akakwazi ukushayela ingane isitifiketi sokuzalwa. Izingane ezizalwe zalahlwa kwesinye isikhathi kunzima ukuthola ubuzwe bazo, ababhalise izitifiketi sekudlule isikhathi kuphela isikhathi eside zingenawo amaphepha azichazayo. Ngaleso sikhathi zisalindile azisizakali ezikhungweni zezempilo," kusho uNkk Muller.Uthe lezi zingane kuba nzima nokuthi zingene ezikoleni yize umthetho uzivumela.Uma sifisa ukuphosa itshe esivivaneni sesisombululo ngesifi sonhlangothi, esidume nge-stroke, kumele siye ngqo eqinisweni, singazami ukulungiselela isimo abantu bakithi, bebe bebhubha mihla namalanga. Umsebenzi uJehova angibusisa ngawo wenza ngibalwe nabaningi abasibonayo isifo lesi kaninginingi ukuthi sihlukumeza abafowethu nodadewethu, abazali bethu nabancane imbala. Engosini eyedlule, sikhulume kakhulu ngokwenzekayo uma ushaywa yi-stroke, lapho esingafikanga khona umsusa oyimbangela yawo unhlangothi wansondo!Emuva kwengosi endulela lena ngihlangane nomfowethu ofike ngqo kimi wathi ufisa ukuphendula indawana ebengiyibhale kule ngosi lapho bengikhala ngokuthi abantu bakithi bayakushalazela ukuqala kithi odokotela abalapha ngokwasentshonalanga. Lapha bengikhala ngithi bafika kithi sebeqale ikakhulu kwabomdabu abelaphi, kwesinye isikhathi sebeshaywe ngesesibili nesesithathu i-stroke, isimo sesisibi ukwedlulela. Umfowethu ubephethe iphepha elinale ngosi, lapho ebengigcizelela ukuthi lokhu kwenza kusibeke thina njengabantu abahlulekayo ukuselapha lesi sifo ngoba abaningi bagcina sebeshonela ezandleni zethu, okusishiya nopende othi uma uye kwabasentshonalanga uphethwe ngunhlangothi, ubuya ngebhokisi. Engosini edlule, ngiye ngabuza ukuthi akusikho yini ukusidlala injenje kubelaphi bomdabu lokhu ngoba phela ufika kubo kusanda kwenzeka bese kuthi uma esegula kakhulu, bamkhuthaze ukuthi aye kwabasentshonalanga abelaphi. Iqiniso ukuthi bona bahlale besala bemsulwa kube imitholampilo, odokotela nezibhedlela abasala  nencabhayi. Umbuzo ubuthi abamgcini ngani ogulayo kuze kube sekugcineni? Umfowethu uyavumelana nami kodwa abefisa ukukuveza ukuthi, ngokwakhe yithina odokotela abafundiswe ngokwasentshonalanga ababhebhethekisa ukuthi abantu bakithi bangezi ngokushesha uma beshaywe inyoni ye-stroke, kodwa baqale kwabomdabu. Ulandisa uthi phela thina sigxibha sihlakaze ukusebenza kwabomdabu odokotela bese besaba ukuthi uma bengaqala kithi ngeke sibavumele okanye ngeke sibakhuthaze ukuya kwabomdabu. Uthi ukwelapha komdabu sikubukela phansi kakhulu size sichizele noma yini eyenziwe ngabelaphi abangabanye. Uze angenzele isibonelo sezinhlanga emzimbeni koshaywe i-stroke, uthi odokotela nabahlengikazi baze bakhombisane ngawe, uzizwe ugconeka ubukeleka phansi ikakhulu ngalokhu okusemzimbeni wakho. Umfowethu lona ungikhumbuze ukuthi ukwelapha kwasentshonalanga akuyona impendulo kuzo zonke izifo. Uphinde abuze ukuthi yini eyenza sibukele phansi abanye abelaphi? Abelaphi bomdabu bayabahlonipha abasentshonalanga ekubeni thina singabahloniphi abomdabu. Ubuza kimi ukuthi uma kuzoba nzima ukuya kwabomdabu uma oshaywe uhlangothi ezoqala kowasentshonalanga angicabangi yini ukuthi lokhu kukhuthaza umuntu ohaqwe iy-stroke ukuthi aqale kwabomdabu bese elandelisa? Ngivumile, ngamvumela kupende wabaningi abalolongwe ngokwasentshonalanga ababukela phansi ukwelapha kwakithi komdabu. Yebo, ngisivumile isibhaxu ngokuzithoba. Ekugcineni ngiye ngamqaphelisa ukuthi umuntu oshaywe wunhlangothi isikhathi esiningi usuke enamahlule egazini asuke edinga ukuhlakazwa ngokushesha ngaphambi kokuthi adale umonakalo odlula owokuqala, yingakho ngokubona kwami kubalulekile ukuza ngokushesha kulowo msizi wezempilo ozokwazi ukusiza kula mahlule asuke esegazini. Sehlukane naye kumnandi, saxhawulana kukuhle!Ingqikithi yanamhlanje ithi asikhulume iqiniso, hheyi asiyeke ukuthenga amehlo abantu; iyini imbangela kanhlangothi? Uyini umsusa we-stroke? Impendulo nansi: sekuhlanganiswe konke okuyimixhantela, imbangela ye-stroke ukudla. Hhayi bo, ikuphi lokhu kudla? Impendulo: ushukela. Ushukela? Yebo ushukela! Ushukela lona esiwufaka etiyeni abanye ekhofini unengxenye ewushevu ngokwedlulele, igama layo kuthiwa ngu-fructose. Ushevu uqobo lona.Wenza amafutha esibindini adala ukuxhwala kwesibindi, isibindi sijiye siqinelane sibe phuzi, isibindi sidilingane sibe namafutha.Lo shukelana ushintsha izinhlayiyana okuthiwa yi-insulin, zijiye ziphendukelane nomzimba.I-fructose idala amaswayana emzimbeni agcina edale umfutho ophezulu egazini nobuhlungu emajoyintini bezinyawo namadolo ikakhulu.Yona kanye le fructose esiyithola kushukela ivala ukusebenza kwengxenyana yomzimba okugcina ngokuthi ungazizwa ukuthi ususuthi, kulokhu kuthi yidla into engapheli. Yilesi sizathu esenza ukoma kungapheli uma uphuza lezi ezihlohlozayo iziphuzo.Zingane zakwethu, ushukela wenza ube nesifo esibi okuthiwa yiMetabolic Syndrome. Lesi sifo siyabulala, sidala i-stroke, ukuhlaselwa yinhliziyo, isifo esigulisa umqondo, uvele ukhohlwe izinto zamanje okungaba amagama ezingane, kwabanye bakhumbula okwenzeka kudala, ukhinyabeze umzimba ukhathale ekuseni, ungakaze wenze lutho okungakubeka kuleso simo.Ushukela ugaywa ngendlela efanayo notshwala, kuhluke ngokuthi kutshwala uyadakwa. Yingakho sibona izingane ezincane sezikhukhumalelwa isibindi, izisu zize zicwebezele sekuqhanse nemithambo, isifo esasaziwa njengesiphatha abantu abadala abanenkinga yophuzo kakhulu. Namhlanje sisibona ezinganeni ngenxa yezingane ezincane esizixhinxa ushukela onhlobonhlobo, amakhekhe, iziphuzo ezihlohlozayo, ama-chips afohlozayo, izinkukhu ezingolamthuthu. Izingane zidla ushevu zizincane.Zonke lezi zindlela zokulimala komzimba zigcina zinomthelela ekuvimbeni igazi lingafinyeleli ezindaweni ezibalulekile okanye lidilingane, lenze amahlule kokunye kugqashuke imithanjana emincane yegazi bese liyopha ligxigxize ebuchosheni. Yizindlela lezi eziholela kwisifo sohlangothi. Zonke lezi zindlela zokugula ushukela, nalowo osungaphezu kwezidingo zomzimba yiwona ongungqo-shishilizi ekudaleni nasekubhebhezeleni isifo sohlangothi.Uma ufisa ukuvikela i-stroke kuyacaca ukuthi impendula ithi: Yeka ukudla ushukela, kuhlanganisa noju, iziphuzo ezihlohlozayo, amajusi nalawa okuthiwa ango-100%.Uma ufisa ukwehlisa ukukhahlamezwa yi-stroke, impendulo ithi: Yeka ukudla ushukela nakho konke okunofulawa no-ice creamUma uthi welapha i-stroke kodwa usadla ushukela: usenga ezimithiyoUma uthi uzivikela kusifo sohlangothi kodwa usadla ushukela usabophela inja nogodo.Sizwe sakithi asingazikhohlisi, manje sesinalo ulwazi. Masiwuvikele unhlangothi, singaziqhathanisi nosibanibani, abantu abasoze bafane. Uma uthanda ukuvikela istroke yeka ushukela. Uma ufisa induku yakho ihlale ivukelwa, inganciphi, ingaweli phakathi, ingasheshi ikhafule: yeka ushukela nakho konke okusondelene, nokufuze wona. Uma ungowesifazane ofisa ukuhlale eshisa ocansini, uhlale uhalela, uvukelwa, inanazi ingabi manzi kakhulu, yeka ushukelaMpilonde!UMASIPALA weTheku uthe ushaqekile ngakubone edolobheni ePinetown ngesikhathi uhambele izindawo ezidayisa ukudla okuphekiwe ngoMsombuluko.Ithimba elibhekele ukuhlanzeka kwemvelo liphume inqina liyohlola ngaphansi komkhankaso okuthiwa usazoqhubeka emadolobheni angaphansi kweTheku.Ithimba ebelijutshwe kule ndawo lifike lathola ukuthi enye yezindawo ezidayisa iShwarma isebenza ngokungemthetho kanti nendawo abapheka baphinde badayisele kuyo ukudla ayikho ezingeni elivumelekile, futhi  nemithetho yenhlanzeko abayilandeli njengoba kuphinde kwavela nokuthi badayisa ngaphandle kwemvume.Izithombe ezifakwe ekhasini likamasipala leFacebook zishiye abantu benyanyile futhi bediniwe.Ithimba lithe lithole ukuthi imithetho ayilandelwa, kanti nabasebenzi bathole ukuthi abanazo izimpahla zokusebenza ezifanele.Kuphinde kwayohlolwa nendawo yabadayisi ekuStanfield Avenue khona kuleli dolobha.Okhulumela umasipala weTheku uMnuz Msawakhe Mayisela uthe basazoqhubeka nale mikhankaso.UMayisela uxwayise abamabhizinisi ikakhulukazi awokudla ukuthi abalandele imithetho."Umkhankaso ongenamukhawulo ngoba sinomsebenzi wokuthi wonke amabhizinisi kumele ahwebe ngokuhlonipha umthetho. Siyaziqhenya kakhulu ngomsebenzi omuhle amathimba ethu awenzayo," kusho uMayisela.UMDLAVUZA wesikhumba uyabahlasela nabantu abanebala elimnyama yize ukuba nebala elikhanyayo kukwenza ukuthi ube sengcupheni yokuwuthola.Ucwaningo olwenziwe yi-American Academy of Dermatology, luveza ukuthi u-25% wabantu abanebala elimnyama uma behlaselwe wumdlavuza wesikhumba ababonakali uma umdlavuza usasesigabeni esiphansi, baze babonakale usungene wagxila egazini, okwenza ukuthi abantu baningi bacabange ukuthi  bona bayasinda kulolu hlobo lomdlavuza.INational Cancer Institute ithi umdlavuza wesikhumba wenzeka ngokuthi kukhule ama-cells esikhumba ngendlela engafanele. Kuyenzeka lawo ma-cells ngesikhathi ekhula zingabikhona izigaxa ezibonakalayo okungaba yizimpawu zokuthi unalo mdlavuza.Ama-cells akhula esikhumbeni adala umdlavuza owaziwa ngeBasal Cell Carcinoma, Squamous Cell, Carcinoma ne-Melanoma.I-Melanoma iwona macells ajwayele ukubonakala kubantu abahlaselwe wumdlavuza wesikhumba. La ma-cells ajwayele ukukhula ezingxenyeni zomzimba ezingambozeki uma umuntu egqokile eziye zitholwe yilanga. Kuba ubuso, izindlebe, isifuba, izingalo, imilenze izindebe nesikhumba sasekhanda kodwa kuyenzeka akhule ezindaweni okungavamisile ukuthi zitholwe ilanga.Izingxenye zomzimba i-Melanoma ejwayele ukuzihlasela ingaphakathi lezandla,  izithende.Lokhu kujwayeleke ukubonakala nakubantu abanebala elimnyama.UNGABONA KANJANI UKUTHI UHLASELWE I-MELANOMA?– Lo mdlavuza ujwayele ukuhlasela abantu abaneminyaka ewu-30 kuya phansi, ikakhulukazi abantu besifazane.– Ngokujwayelekile ubonakala ngokuthi kube namabala angamachashazi amnyama noma ansundu esikhumbeni.– Ongoti besikhumba bathi nakuba ukuhlolwa ngongoti ukuthi awunawo yini umdlavuza, kungenye yezinto eziyingxenye yokuhlolwa okwenziwa njalo kodwa kubalulekile ukuthi nawe usibheke isikhumba sakho ukuthi asinalo yini ushintsho, okungaba ngamachashazi noma amabala angafani nesikhumba sakho.– Uma kukhona okubonayo okuyichashazi elimnyama noma elinsundu obungenakho, kuphitshize uzwe ukuthi akuqinile yini – Ukushintsha kombala wesikhumba– Uma ubuvele unamachachazi bheka ukuthi awashintshi umbala wawo noma kube nokuqinile kuleyo ngxenye yesikhumba.– Ukuvumbuka kwezinsumpa ekade ungenazo.– Ukuba nemihuzuko kodwa ungazange ulimale– Ukuba nezinyawo ezimnyama eziqinile ezithendeni naseduze kwezinzipho.UNkk Murray Hewlett ongumphathi omkhulu wakwa-Affinity Health, uthe: "Ushintsho olubonayo esikhumbeni sakho akusho ukuthi seluchaza ukuthi unomdlavuza wesikhumba, udokotela wakho ozokuhlola ngemuva kokuthi umbikele ngoshintsho olubonayo. Uma esola ukuthi unomdlavuza wesikhumba uzokudlulisela kongoti besikhumba abazophinde bakuhlole futhi,"–Uthe kubalulekile ukuthi usheshe usukume uma ubona ushintsho ukuze uma unomdlavuza usheshe utholakale, uqale ukwelashwa ungakagxili kakhulu.Okunye athe abantu bazame ukukwenza ukuthi bangaphumeli elangeni phakathi kuka-10 ekuseni no-4 ntambama, ikakhulukazi ngezikhathi sasehlobo.Uthe uma uzophumela elangeni kumele ugcobe ukhilimu ovikela ilanga ugqoke nezingubo ezivikela ilangaUma uzobhukuda gcoba ukhilimu ovikela isikhumba elangeniGwema ukuthamela ilanga olwandle ngoba kungalimaza isikhumba sakho Gwema ukuhamba nengane enezinyanga esithupha kuya phansi elangeni.Zama ukubonana nodokotela wesikhumba okungenani kanye ngonyaka.ISIKHUNGO esigunyaza ukusetshenziswa kwemithi yokwelapha kuleli iSouth African Health Products Regulatory Authority (SAHPRA), sigunyaze  ukusetshenziswa komgomo weCovid-19, okhiqizwe yiJohnson &Johnson ngaphandle kocwaningo.Njengamanje umgomo okugonywa ngawo abasebenzi bezempilo bekuvumeleke ukuthi usetshenziswe njengengxenye yocwaningo iSisonke Protocol, manje lesi sikhungo sesigunyaze ukuthi usungasetshenziswa ukugoma abantu okungeyona ingxenye yocwaningo kodwa nakho kuzokwenziwa ngaphansi kwemibandela.Isikhulu esiphezulu kwiSAHPRA uDkt Boitumelo Semete-Makokotlela, sithe ukugunyazwa kwalo mgomo kuncike ekutheni uphephile okuvezwa imininingwane ethunyelwe ngabakhiqizi bawo kulesi sikhungo kusukela phakathi kukaDisemba nyakenye noMashi walo nyaka."Omunye wemibandela ukuthi lo mgomo usetshenziswe kulandelwa imigomo nemibandela yoMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli, okungukuthi kumele imiphumela yocwaningo oluqhubekayo ngawo lo mgomo umnyango waziswe ngayo nokuthi kumele abakhiqizi bazise umnyango ngohlelo abanalo lokulawula ubungozi," kusho uDkt Semente Makokotlela.Uthe okwamanje imininingwane yalo mgomo iveza ukuthi awubagulisi kakhulu abantu uma bewusebenzile, kuyenzeka bagule  nje okungatheni okufana nokukhathala, ubuhlungu lapho bejove khona, ubuhlungu bekhanda nokucanuzela kwenhliziyo.Uthe okwamanje lo mgomo ungagcinwa izinyanga ezingu-24 uma ubekwe endaweni enokubanda okungu-minus 25 degrees  kuya ku-15 degrees. Kulezi zinyanga lo mgomo ungakwazi ukugcinwa efrijini elizowenza ube yiqhwa kodwa uma sewuke wancibilikiswa ngeke usakwazi ukuphinde uwenze iqhwa futhi.UNgqongqoshe wezempilo uDkt Zweli Mkhize,  uthe imigomo engu-1 million  ekhiqizwe iJohnson&Johnson izofika kuleli kule nyanga, engu-900 000 yokwengenza izofika ngoMeyi nangoJuni.Uthe izibalo zabagonyelwa iCovid-19 zizoqala ukwenyuka kusukela ngoJulayi.Uthe lo mnyango wawuhlele ukuthi uzothola umgomo ongu-5.5  million okhiqizwe yi-Pfizer, obekuzogonywa ngawo kuze kufike kuJuni kodwa lo mgomo ubambezelekile.Uthe okunye okubambezele uhlelo lokugoma ukuthi i-AstraZeneca eyase ithengiwe kuleli kwatholakala ukuthi ayiliviki igciwane elitholakale kuleli i501Y.V2."Kudingeke ukuthi sishintshele ekusebenziseni iJ&J nayo ebingeningi, besithola leyo ebuya kwamanye amazwe.  Kodwa uhlelo lwethu lona belukulungele ukugoma abantu," kusho uMkhize.Uthe i-AstraZeneca ebithengwe kuleli isidayiselwe i-African Union (AU).Uthe amazwe abelwe lo mgomo yiNigeria, Ghana, Senegal, Guinea, Togo, Sierra Leone, Zimbabwe, Liberia, Mauritania, Gambia, Guinea-Bissau, Malawi, South Sudan, Comoros, Egypt, Seychelles, ne-Uganda.ISIKHUNGO esibhekelele ukugunyazwa kwemithi yokwelapha, iSouth African Health Products Authority (SAHPRA) ,sithi umgomo weCovid-19 okhiqizwa abakwaPfizer uphephile abantu bakuleli abaqhubeke bagome ngawo.Ngeledlule kuputshuke ulwazi okuthiwa belugcinwe yisikhungo esigunyaza imithi yokwelapha e-United States, iFood and Drug Admninistration (FDA) oluthi zingu-1 291 izifo ezingakuphatha ngemuva kokugoma ezidalwa yilo mgomo.Lokhu kuthiwa kuvezwe ucwaningo obelwenziwa ngabantu abangu-7 million bakuleliya lizwe ababike ukuthi babe nokungaphatheki kahle ngemuva kokugoma ngalo mgomo.Abezempilo bathe akuyona into abantu okumele ibakhathaze ngoba ukugula kuba yisikhashana futhi kwabaningi kuyaziphelela ngemuva kosuku begomile , bambalwa abagule kwaze kwafinyelela ekutheni baye ezibhedlela.Isikhulu esiphezulu se-SAHPRA uDkt Boitumelo Semete-Makokotlela, sithe  ulwazi abanalo ngalo mgomo alukhombisi ukuthi kunobungozi obukhulu ngawo, bathole ukuthi ukungaphatheki kahle okwenzayo kuncane yinto eziphelelayo kwabaningi.“Ukungaphatheki kahle esikwaziyo okudalwa yilo mgomo akuyona into engaholela ekutheni impilo yomuntu ibe sengcupheni. Uma sibheka lokho kungaphatheki kahle sikuqhathanisa nokuthi lo mgomo ugwema ukuthi umuntu angashoni uma ethola iCovid-19, sibona ukuthi umgomo   kusamele usetshenziswe,"  kusho uDkt Semete Makokotlela.Uqhube wathi yonke imikhiqizo yezempilo ngaphambi kokuthi igunyazwe iyahlolwa ukuthi iphephile yini nokuthi abakhiqizi bayo bayilandelile yini imigomo ethile.“Ukuphepha yinto yokuqala ebhekwayo emikhiqizweni yezempilo ngaphambi kokuthi igunyazwe. Uma singekho isiqiniseko sokuphepha leyo mithi ayiphasiswa. Abakhiqizi bemithi ngaphambi kokuthi umgomo ugunyazwe basinikeza lonke ulwazi ngomkhiqizo wabo kuhlanganisa nokuthi yini engase ibe wumxhantela mphumela kowusebenzisile,” kusho yena.UKUGOMELA umkhuhlane kubalulekile  ukuze kugwenywe ukuthi kube nabantu abazogula kakhulu badinge ukuthi balaliswe ezibhedlela.Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWord Health Organisation (WHO), ithi u50% wabantu abaphathwa umkhuhlane  kuleli baye badinge ukuthi balaliswe ezibhedlela ngoba baphathwa umkhuhlane onzima,  ngakho kubalulekile ukuthi abantu bawugomele umkhuhlane. Ukuhlasela kobhubhane iCovid-19, sekufake igcindezi ezikhungweni zezempilo, ngakho ukuze kugwenywe ukuthi kube nabantu abaningi abazodinga ukulaliswa ezibhedlela bephethwe umkhuhlane, kubalulekile ukuthi abantu bagomele umkhuhlane.IWHO ithi babalewa ku-3 kuya ku5 million abantu abaphathwa umkhuhlane emhlabeni ngonyaka kubo u1.2 million abantu bakuleli.Ithe yize kunemigomo ebekiwe yokuzama ukunqanda ukusabalala kweCovid-19 okungukuthi abantu kumele baqhelelane , bageze izandla  banciphise nokuhamba behlangana nabantu leyo migomo ingasiza nakuwo umkhuhlane kodwa ithi akusho ukuthi ngeke abantu besaphathwa umkhuhlane uma belandele leyo migomo ngoba igciwane lomkhuhlane likhona emoyeni ngalesi sikhathi.Usolwazi Lucille Blumberg weNational Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD), emqingweni wezempilo okhuluma ngokuphathwa umkhuhlane kuleli, iSouth African Medical Journal (SAMJ), uthe amagciwane omkhuhlane kuleli ahlasela phakathi kukaMeyi noSepthemba.Uthe umkhuhlane usabalala ngokushesha futhi uphatha bonke abantu kungakhathalekile ukuthi baneminyaka emingaki." Umkhuhlane ungaba mubi kakhulu kubantu abanezifo ezenza ukuthi amasosha abe ntekenteke ezifana neHIV, iTB, isifo sikashukela, isifo sezinso, esokungagayeki kahle kokudla nezinye," kugcizelela uSolwazi Blumberg.Uthe abesifazane abakhulelwe nabantu abakhuluphele ngokweqile, izingane ezincane nabantu abadala kunamathuba amaningi okuthi bahlaselwe umkhuhlane futhi kubo ube nzima.Uthe indlela esebenzayo yokuvika umkhuhlane ukuthi  uwugomele yonke iminyakaUthe nakuba umkhuhlane uvgwemeka ngokugoma kodwa abantu abanamasosha antekenteke kungenzeka ukugoma kungabavikeli ngokuphelele kodwa umgomo uyabavikela ekutheni bagule kakhulu badinge ukuya ezibhedlela noma bashone." Ukugomela umkhuhlane kungasiza ekutheni kuvikelgwemeke isimo lapho izikhungo zezempilo zizoba nengcindezi ngenxa yeziguli eziningi ezinomkhuhlane nezineCovid-19.  Okumele sikukhumbule ukuthi umgomo weCovid-19  awuwunqandi umkhuhlane, kanjalo nowomkhuhlane awuyinqandi iCovid-19,“ kusho yena.ONGOTI bezempilo bathi kungakuhle ukuthi nabafana bagonyelwe ukuthi bangasitholi isifo socansi iHuman Papillomavirus (HPV) njengamantombazane.Isikhungo esibhekele ukulawulwa kwezifo e-Africa, i-Africa Centre for Disease Control and Prevention (CDC), sithe iningi labantu abazibandakanya nocansi kuyenzeka bahaqwe ilesi sifo kodwa bangabi nolwazi lokuthi banaso.IHPV kubantu abaningi besifazane uma ingelashwanga iholela ekutheni baphathwe umdlavuza wesibeletho.Ukutheleleka nge-HPV ngokuvamile kudala ukukhula kwesikhumba noma ulwelwesi lwamafinyila (warts). Kunezinhlobo ezingaphezu kuka-100 ze-human papillomavirus (HPV). Ezinye izinhlobo zokutheleleka nge-human papillomavirus (HPV) zibanga izinsumpa, kanti ezinye zingadala izinhlobo ezahlukene zomdlavuza.Izinhlobo eziningi ze-HPV azidali umdlavuza kodwa ezinye zidala umdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho. Ezinye izinhlobo zeHPV  zidala umdlavuza wesitho sangasese sabesilisa, owomlomo wokulahla indle nowomphimbo i-oropharyngeal.Ngokuvamile  iHPV ithelelana ngokuya ocansini nomuntu onayo noma ngokuthintana kwesikhumba. Imithi yokugoma iyasiza ekugwemeni izinhlobo eziningi zeHPV ikakhulukazi ezidala umdlavuza wesibeletho nezinsumpa.ENingizimu Afrika umgomo weHPV unikezwa amantombazane aneminyaka eyisishiyagalolunye kuya phezulu angakazibandakanyi nocansi, okwenziwa ezikoleni ngokubambisana phakathi koMnyango wezeMfundo eyiSisekelo noMnyango wezeMpilo, i-ACDC ithi nabafana kumele banikezwe lo mjovoOdokotela bathi ukumunca isitho sangasese  kunomthelela ekutheni kube nabantu abasha abaphayhwa umdlavuza womphimbo kanti abantu abasha kubukeka sengathi le ndlela yokwenza ucansi bayayithanda.Kule nyanga amakhemisi abakwaDis-chem anomkhankaso wokufundisa ngokubaluleka kokugomela iHPV ikakhulukazi kubafana okuhambisana nokuthi le nyanga eyamadoda.UNkk Lizeth Kruger, isikhulu somtholampilo wakwa-Dis-Chem, uthe: " Akukaze kukhulunywe kakhulu ngokubaluleka kokuthi nabesilisa kumele baligomele leli gciwane. Ukugonywa kwabafana kuzonikeza amantombazane ukuvikeleka okuphindiwe.Yini eyimbangela ye-HPV emadodeni?Igciwane lisabalala kakhulu ngesikhathi kuyiwa  ocansini lwangemuva  noma lwesitho sangasese sowesifazane nokuthintana kwesikhumba nesikhumba ezindaweni zangasese ngesikhathi kuyiwa ocansini.Kunzima ukusho ukuthi leli gciwane likungene nini ngoba  lingaquba emzimbeni wakho iminyaka ngaphambi kokuba kuvele izimpawu.Yiziphi izimpawu ze-HPV?Nakuba iningi lamadoda ane-HPV lingenazo izimpawu kodwa kuyenzeka abanye babe nezinsumpa esithweni sangasese,  ukukhula okungavamile kwenyama kuso isitho sangasese, izimila . Uma ubona noma yikuphi okushiwo ngenhla kumele ubonane nodokotela ngokushesha.Ngenhlonipho, ngingakangeni esihlokweni sanamhlanje ngicela ukuthi jwaphu ngesiguli esingubaba engisibone izolo lokhu. Lo baba wayengakholwa ukuthi ukuqaqamba kwezinyawo kwelapheka ngokushesha, wayesethi hhayi asimelaphe unyawo olulodwa. Nebala senza njalo selapha unyawo lwesokudla kuphela. Simbone esezibuyela yena, esezocela ukwenziwa nakulolu olunye; esesitshela ukuthi usekwazi ukushaya ingoma asine ngalolu olwelwashwayo. Ngivele ngakhumbula nje ukuthi konje abantu besizwe sakithi baze bakholwe ngokubona phela!Namhlanje ngithe ngenyanga yethu osokhaya, izinto eziyizinhloko, ongqongqoshe bamakhaya ake sikhuze umhlume lo ovele wenze induku ithambe ibe imfaba. Ngiyayibongela indoda engakabazi ubuhlungu benduku evele ivuke kancane ibe into ethambile ebhocobele, uthi uyizama wedwa lutho, aze nomlingani wakho ebona usizi azokusiza azokushokisa le nto evele yathamba yangabambeka nasezandleni, nizame nobabili ukuyikhombisa umthombo wensindiso, lutho ngane yakwethu ivele iphelele ezandleni. Yeyi ibuhlungu leyonto! Abantu besilisa engibelaphayo baze bathi kuba ngconywana uma kungumuntu osumjwayele, kubuhlungu kuyezwela uma niqalana, uswela umgodi ozovuleka ungene. Umuntu wesilisa ongakabazi lobu buhlungu, makazi  ukuthi kuyokwenzeka kuye ngelinye ilanga uma engasukumi elaphe umhlume okanye ahlale ezivikele kulo sofasilahlane wesifo esingundabamlonyeni.Induku evuka izithambele inezimbangela cishe eziyisithupha, umhlume ungenye yazo. Induku engaqini evele ilokhu imoyizela ithambile ingadalwa: yigazi elingenele elifinyelela kuyo induku ngenxa yokuvimbeleka emithanjeni, inhliziyo ephundulekile engakwazi ukukhipha igazi elanele, ukushoda kwekhemikhali ethile egazini, izifo ezithinta kakhulu igazi nemithambo njengesifo sikashukela nesifo somfutho ophezulu wokuhambisa igazi emzimbeni, imidlavuza yegazi noma eyezakhi zegazi bese kuba yiwo umhlume.Okugqamayo ukuthi umhlume yiwona ohamba phambili ekuhlukumezeni abesilisa; isimo siyaphindephindeka uma kukhona esinye salezi zifo esesizibale ngenhla.Umhlume kwabesilisa ungena ngomuzwa, lona osuka ngasekupheleni kweqolo uguduze ngaphakathi esinqeni uze uyohlukana kabili ingxenyana iye embhobheni wendle, enye iye ebulilini besilisa. Isifo umhlume senziwa ukuhuzuka noma ukulimala kwalo muzwa omkhulukazi. Lokhu kulimala kungadalwa ukuqunjelwa okungapheli okuzokuphoqa wena oqunjelwe ukuthi ukhanule kakhulu uma uzikhulula. Lokhu kuyacacisa ukuthi akumele sibekezelele ukuqunjelwa, okwenza usuze njalo. Siyabona lapha ukuthi isizathu sokuthi amadoda athande ukuchatha yini? Ukuchatha akulona ichilo, kuyindlela enhle yokukhulula isisu ukuze ungadonsi ukhanule uma uyolahla indle kuze kulimale umuzwa lona ozokudalela umhlume. Okunye okungabangela ukulimala kwalo muzwa izifo ezithinta umzimba wonke, ukulimala emgogodleni nasesinqeni, amakhemikhali awushevu emzimbeni angafika aphihlize aphithanise ukwakheka kwalo muzwa, ukuphuza utshwala, ukubhema ugwayi, ingcindezi engamandla yomqondo, umdlavuza wombhobho wendle nomdlavuza wezicubu zawo umbhobho. Ngiqinisekile ukuthi omunye useyabona ukuthi izimpawu zomhlume kule ndawo: ukuqunjelwa, ukusuza okweqile, iqolo elibuhlungu, ukukhathala komzimba, induku engaqini, induku engavuki nhlobo, induku eshesha ikhafule, induku enciphayo ibe mfishane iphinde ibe ncane ngomzimba, nenduku evuka kodwa ikushiye endleleni enye ize iwele phakathi kumuntu wesifazane.Ngiyethemba ukuthi angiphambuki uma ngithi induku engavuki, esheshe ikhafule, evuka kodwa ivele izicishele endleleni nenduku evele ithambe ize idinge ukushokwa; lesi isimo esibalwa kwezinkulu ezenza owesilisa aphatheke kabi ngendlela eyisimanga. Isifo umhlume singena siguduze silimaze into umuntu wesilisa azizwa ngayo ukuthi uyindoda, uphelele.Umhlume uyakwazi ukudlula lapha bese uya ezindaweni eziningi emzimbeni ufike unombele kuzona. Kuyilapha esiyaye siwunikeze amagama anhlobonhlobo ngokwezindawo ezihlaselwe, kodwa konke kube kungaphansi kwesambulela esiwumhlume.Umhlume uyelapheka nezimpande zawo, esikucelayo ukuthi indoda mayisukume iye kudokotela wayo; asiyeke ukuba ngoFelaphakathi.Amanye amadoda  ayathanda ukuthi sesinazo izingane, umlingani wami‘makakwemukele’ ukuthi ngikulesi simo! Yeyi ayikho leyo nto, indoda nendoda mayiphakamise isandla iphumele emnyango iye kozelapha.Mpilonde!AKEKHO ongaphika ukuthi ukuzingcolisa (ukuzimoshela) umdala, ngenye yezinto ezikuphoxa kakhulu uma yenzeka kunoma ngubani; kungaba sebusuku noma emini.Kunabantu abayaye bacabange ngisho ukuzibulala imbala uma bezithola bephethwe yisifo esibenza bangakuzwa ukuza kwendle okugcina ngokuthi itshe lentaba liziphumele ngaphandle. Usuyozwa ngephunga okanye uzwe ngobumanzi njengengane. Kunzima ukucabanga ukuthi kungakanani ukujivazeka okuhambisana nesimo esinjengalesi, angikhulumi ke uma isehlo senzeka uphakathi kwabantu. Sengihlangane nabantu abaningi abahlushwa yilesi simo. Lokhu kwenzeka kubantu abasha nabadala; abesifazane nabesilisa, awukho umehluko. Okumnandi ukuthi isimo esinjengalesi siyelapheka futhi siphele. Inselelo kuba kubantu bakithi abahlala isikhathi eside bejikileza, bengezi ukuzofuna usizo oluqondile.Umhlume yisifo esinobungozi kakhulu, esidinga ukwelapheka ngokuphelele futhi welaphe umsusa waso. Akusona isifo sokufuhlela imithi nje, ungazi nokuthi iyiphi imbangela oyelaphayo? Sike sachaza ezingosini ezingaphambili ukuthi umhlume yisifo esichamuselwa ukukhuhleka nokulimala kwemizwa, ngenxa yokugangatheka kwemizwa, kugcina kuphunduleka izicubu. Yingakho uthola ukuthi imizwa nezicubu okumele kwenze umhlanganiso wokulawula umbhobho wendle kuvele kuthiphalaze; indle iziphumele nje ngokuthanda kwayo. Umbuzo mhlawumbe uzothi, yini eyenzekayo ngaphambi kokufika ekubeni amabhuleki aphele, indle iziphumele? Asikhumbuzane ukuthi umhlume uyingxenye yokugangatheka kwemizwa nemithambo okuholela ezifeni nasezimeni eziningi ezahlukene. Umhlume wona kusuke kulimele umuzwa omkhulu ovela emgogodleni, empeleni ngasezansi nawo umgogodla. Lo muzwa umkhulu unjalo, uguduza emathanjeni ezinqe uze ufike lapho uhlukana khona kabili, uyolawula imizwa yocansi nezicubu zakhona. Enye ingxenyana ilawula izicubu zombhobho wokukhipha indle. Yingakho uthola ukuthi izimpawu ezilandelayo zivela njengomgodla wevungu:kunembobo embiwe yahlukanisa amathamboUbuhlungu obuba ngaphambili kuba ngathi idolo liyagwaza ezinhlangothini, indawana engaphambili naphakathi nalo Mangiphawule ukuthi umhlume uyabahlasela nabesifazane ebulilini babo, ngoba isikhathi esiningi kuyaye kukhulumeke kube ngathi ngabesilisa ababa nenkinga yokuncishelwa yizinduku zabo ziphinde zingavuki. Kwabesifazane esibabonayo ezikhungweni zokusebenzela esibalaphela umhlume, bonke bakhala ngokungasaluhaleli ucansi futhi bengavukelwa. Abaningi basitshela ukuthi balwenza nje ngoba abalingani babo basuka befisa kanjalo. Siyaye siqhubeke sibabuze ngobhontshisi wabo, ukuthi alukho yini ushintsho abalubonayo? Bonke bayachaza ukuthi ubhontshisi usunciphile abanye baze bathi awusekho mpelampela, sekuyinqudulu nje. Umhlume awukhethi bulili!Ngiyethemba ukuthi lokhu kuyasibeka isithombe sokuthi abesifazane nabo banenkinga enkulu yokungahaleli futhi bengavukelwa. Lokhu okungaholela ekutheni kube nzima ukufika kuvuthondaba. Ngisho lokhu ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi baningi abesilisa abasishayela ucingo nesibabonayo bethi abathandwa babo abafiki kuvuthondaba, lokhu kuyabahlupha kakhulu. Uma kunjalo, kungenzeka isithandwa sakho sinesifo somhlume; impendulo ithi othandiweyo wakho makelaphe umhlume, impilo iqhubeke iye phambili.Namhlanje sikhuluma ngomhlume ogcina ngokuthi iziqhobosho ziphele, indle iziputshukele, kwabanye kuze kuphumele ngaphandle nombhobho wokukhipha indle.Ebesikugcizelela lapha ukuthi lokhu kwenzeka emzimbeni, akukwazi ukuthi kuvele kuzimele kodwa ngokwenzeka, kuningi okunye okwenzekayo okuhambisa nalokhu kugula.Isifo sokuphelelwa ngamabhuleki, ukhiphe umoya kakhulu kuze kuholele ekutheni indle iziputshukele ingabambeki, siyelapheka ngaphandle kokuthi uye kohlinzwa. Hamba uye kudokotela wakho umchazele okwenzekayo, ngisho ngabe wumchamo oziphumelayo; uzoluthola usizo, welapheke ngokuphelele.Mpilonde!KUNETHEMBA lokuthi umjovo ovikela iHIV wezinyanga eziyisithupha ungawavikela amantombazane ukuze angatheleleki ngegciwane.Lokhu kushiwo ngusosayensi oyinhloko eDesmond Tutu HIV Center, engaphansi kweNyuvesi iCape Town, uSolwazi Linda Gail Bekker. I-Desmond Tutu HIV Center, yisikhungo esicwaninga ikhambi okuhloswe ukuthi livikele ukutheleleka kwamantombazane ngegciwane lengculazi.Lolu cwaningo lubheka ezinye izinsiza ezingasiza ekuvikeleni igciwane lengculazi ngaphandle kwamaphilisi aphuzwa zonke izinsuku athithibalisa iHIV, nepre-exposure prophylaxis (PrEP).Lwenziwa ebantwini abangu-5000 okungabaseNingizimu Afrika, nabase-Uganda, ukubheka ukuthi ngabe umjovo onomshanguzo iLenacapavir, neminye emibili ungakwazi yini ukuvikela ukutheleleka kwegciwane leHIV.USolwazi uGail Bekker, uthe ucwaningo beluneminxa emibili, owokuqala ubheke ukuthi umjovo uphephile yini, owesibili wabheka ukuthi ngabe ungawasiza yini amantombazane asemancane okusabonakala eqhubeka ehaqwa yiHIV yize zikhona izindlela zokuvikela igciwane  kuleli amakhondomu, namaphilisi anjengePrep, engamaphilisi nezinye.Kunenkolelo yokuthi amantombazane amancane adinga into azokwazi ukuyisebenzisa ngaphandle kokuthi atshele athandana nabo ngoba ayehluleka ukugcizelela ukuphepha kwathandana nabo."Kulolu cwaningo bekusetshenziswa amakhambi amathathu okuyi Lenacapavir, iTruvada,  neDescovy. Bekusetshenziswa indlela yokuthi abayingxenye yocwaningo nabacwaningi bangabi nalo ulwazi lokuthi ngobani abajova ngamaphi amakhambi,  kuze kube kufike isikhathi sokuthi kubhekwe ukuthi yiliphi ikhambi elenza kangcono. Sithole ukuthi ebantwini abangu-2, 134  abebejova ngeLenacavir akekho otheleleke ngeHIV. Kwabangu-1068 abebejova ngeTruvada abangu-16 batheleleke ngegciwane, ebantwini abangu- 2136 abebejova ngeDescovy babangu-39  batheleleke ngeHIV," kuchaza uSolwazi Gail Bekker.Uqhube wathi ucwaningo luveze ukuthi sikhona isidingo sokuthi kube nenye indlela yokuvikela amantombazane kodwa ingasetshenziswa yodwa njengokuthi abesilisa kumele basoke futhi basebenzise ikhondomu.Uthe ucwaningo aluphelile lusaqhubeka kodwa manje abayingxenye yalo nabacwaningi sebezokwazi ukuthi ngobani abasebenzisa maphi amakhambi. Wathi abayingxenye yocwaningo banikezwe nethuba lokuzikhethela ikhambi abafuna ukujova ngalo.Okwamanje umjovo awukatholakali kuleli, usasetshenziselwa ukwenza ucwaningo kuphela kodwa iGilead Sciences,  ithe izohlinzeka izinkampani ezikhiqiza imithi ngezimvume zokuwukhiqiza ukuze zenze imithi engama-generic engeke ibize kakhulu.UMLOTHA emlonyeni, sasinda ezifweni nasekubulaweni izinso! Lesi kumele kube yisiqubulo sethu sonke thina esisafuna ukuphila isikhathi eside emhlabeni singenankinga yezinso, zonke izifo zihambela kude nathi. Ukube ngangiwumholi wenhlangano yepolitiki, ukube benginamandla okubingelela emisakazweni nakwithelevishini ngabe ngiphoqa wonke umuntu ukuthi aphimisele la mazwi njalo uma eqala okanye ephetha usuku. Awucabange nje zonke izingane zethu ezikoleni sezinesiqubulo esinjenga lesi? Zingancipha ngokuphindiwe izibalo zabanesifo sezinso. Izinga labanemifutho ephezulu lingehla ngokuphindiwe. Uthanda ungathandi, izinkinga zesifuba ziyoya ekushabalaleni. Zingancipha zigcine zishabalele izinhlungu zamadolo namajoyinti nje jikelele.Awucabange nje sesingenazinkinga zamehlo. Nalabo abahlala bekhala ngezinyawo ezibuhlungu sekuyinto eyiphupho. Bangeke basale ngaphandle abahlushwa ngamakhanda angalapheki. Izinkinga zokuqumbelana sekuyiphupho langempela, ngoba ziyobe sezinciphe kakhulu izinkinga zasemathunjini jikelele.Omunye uzothi mhlawumbe udokotela uyaphupha, cha akunjalo ngisezingqondweni, ngiphelele. Konke lokhu ngikusho ngoba ngiyazi ukuthi imbangela yezifo nezimo engizibalayo ziphenjwa wukulimala kokwakheka kwemithambo igcine seyingasakwazi ukuvuleka. Lokhu kudala ukuphunduleka kokukhiqizwa kwekhemikhali ebizwa ngokuthi yi-Nitrogen Oxide. Ukhiye wekhemikhali eyigesi ekhiqizwa yimithambo yethu ukuze ikwazi imithambo ukuvuleka ngokwemvelo. Bafowethu nodadewethu yini esehlula ukuphendula ngeqiniso umbuzo othi esikhathi sakudala, singakazalwa, izifo zezinso zazikuphi? Yayingekho yini le mithambo nenhliziyo namhlanje enyusa ukufutha kwenhliziyo size sidle imishanguzo? I-Heart Attack (ukuhlaselwa kwenhliziyo ngenxa yokushoda kwegazi elinomoya onamandla) yayibayekeleni okhokho bethu? Imidlavuza engaka yayikuphi? Isifuba somoya sona? Amakhanda asesihlakaza ubusuku nemini ayekuphi? Yini eyayenza okhokho bakwazi ukuguqa ngamadolo bagaye etsheni, baphume bayosebenza amasimu, bengakhali ngadolo eligwazayo nelinkenkethayo? Babengakhali yini noma bezwe ubuhlungu bezinyawo? Yini le esenze sahluka kangaka thina?Impendulo ithi babehlanza umlomo namazinyo ngomlotha, ngamalahle, ngesikhonko nangesundu. Yini thina eyasishintsha kulokhu? Impucuzeko! Le mpuncuzeko eyenza singakwazi ukuzicabangela, sihlale silinde kuze kusho abebala bathi, “Yekani-ke manje seningakwenza lokhu”. Nanoma kuzicacela ukuthi siyabhubha, sikhetha ukuvala amehlo. Impucuzeko ize nezifo, sifa ubuthaphuthaphu. Ukubuyela emuva siyoxubha ngomlotha sikubona kuwukuzehlisa, engathi senza okungeyikho ngoba silinde kube abaseMelika abamhlophe abasitshelayo ukuthi masishintshe le nhlanganisela yokuxubha ngoba iyasibulala. Uma kusasho umuntu omnyama njengathi akukabi yikho. Angithi?Babengawusebenzisi ushukela kangaka ngezikhathi zabo, thina konke esikudlayo kunoshukela. Ngisho umuntu esetsheliwe kwathiwa umzimba wakho uyehluleka ukulawula ushukela, wena sekumele ushanguze ngezinto zikashukela. Hhayi thina siyaqhubeka sidle zonke izinto ezinyusa ushukela; kungaba yiziphuzo ezihlohlozayo, ama-pizza, izinkwa, ama-roll, ama-chips, irayisi emhlophe, olamthuthu. Siqoba siyavungula ngoba asinandaba? Ngicela ukuxoxa nansi indatshana eyenzeke kimi uqobo njengoba kade sine-Covid 19, abantu bakithi beshona kakhulu. Abasakhumbula ngabhala kakhulu nami ngiphonsa esivivaneni ngezizathu ezazenza usibhuqabhuqe umkhuhlane, ngangibhala ngesiZulu njengoba ngenza nje. Omunye umlingani wami ongudokotela naye owayesanda kuqeda esikoleni, owayengumlungu, wayesebenza eMseleni esibhedlela; wabhala into eyayifana ncamashi nalena engangiyibhale ngesiZulu, yena wayichaza ngesilungu. Senginqamlela nje, kuthi sikomunye umhlangano omunye engingeke ngimgagule ngegama umholi omkhulu impela nje, waphimisela echaza ukuthi yena le nto uze wayizwa kahle njengoba kade ibhalwe yilo dokotela omhlophe. Ngithi ngakhubeka ngaze ngakhala zehla mi izinyembezi! Umholi phambi kwami uncoma lo mlingani wami ngoba engumlungu, ngento ekade ngiyichaze ncamashi ngesiZulu sakithi kodwa umholi uthi uyizwe wayiqonda ngoba isivela kumlungu, obhale ngesiNgisi! Hheyi ngithi namanje ngeke ngisilibale lesi sahluko. Ozakwethu, ngiyacabanga lokhu kuyenzeka nakweminye imikhakha. Umuntu wakithi omnyama kulula ukukholwa kakhulu alandele into eshiwo owebala, ngisho ngabe ukuphi ngokwamava nangokufunda, lokho kuyenzeka kubonakale kamuva. Uma ungena nje usibuka bese kuthiwa kuwe hamba uyokhuluma nodokotela kukhona owebala, amathuba maningi azothi yiya kulona webala. Baningi abantu bakithi asebahlinzwa ngapha nangapha singekho isidingo kodwa kwasho owebala elithile, bavumela phezulu.Ake sibuyele nje ngesikhathi se-Covid-19, sonke sasazi kamhlophe ukuthi alukho ucwaningo lwesayensi olwalwenziwe, akekho owayenesiqiniseko sezimpawu zayo. Abantu babegula phambi kwethu kodwa kwakuze kukhulunywe ngophawu olubonakalayo lweCovid uma selushiwo abaseMelika, bese uzwa iziphathimandla sezikhuluma ngazo ezweni lethu. Awazi indlela eyayingihlukumeza ngayo le nto? Yini eyayenza singazithatheli izinqumo ngeziguli zethu? Yini salinda kwaze kwaba yiMelika ekhuluma nge-acid okuthiwa yi-Uric Acid kuyi-Covid ngaphambi kokukhuluma ngayo? Yini eyenza kuze kube yiMelika ekhuluma ngokuthi kuyenzeka umuntu one-Covid aguliswe umuminzo, asingabheki amaphaphu nje kuphela? Omunye uyothi udokotela ukhuluma kanje ngoba elwa kanti cha akunjalo. Yingoba umlando uyasitshela ukuthi ukulandela elinye izwe kusidukisile kumanje sibulawa yizifo. Sibulawa ushukela ngenxa yokudukiswa, namhlanje abantu bakithi babulawa amakhemikhali okuxubha ngenxa yokulandela okushiwo nokwenziwa ngelinye izwe. Namuhla sinezinso ezingasebenzi, amakhanda angapheli, sigula ngokomqondo, siyafa ubuthaphuthaphu. Ucwaningo lukhombise alwananaza, lwathi amakhemikhali asenhlanganiseleni yalokhu esixubha ngakho kuyasibulala, kodwa abantu bakithi bakuphakamisela amehlo uma uthi asibuyele emlotheni, yiyona ndlela engasibangeli izifo. Ake sibuyele emuva, lokhu kuyosisiza ekwehliseni isisindo sezifo esizweni.Mpilonde!IQINISO liyakusikhulula! Ubani nobani onenkinga yokungavukelwa kwenduku noma singacikoza sifike kuphi ngokukwazi ukuya ocansini, yena uyojabulela ukuphila kwenduku yakhe, ivuke iqine ngqi, ihlukane nokuwela phakathi. Kwabanye ize inciphe ibe ncanyana, usabe nokuyiveza. Angiphathi lena yokusheshe ikhafule.Kukho konke eyokushesha ikhafule kuziqwaqwada emakhanda ngenxa yokuthi usuke wena usujabulile, usuthe ekugcineni uMdali usewuzwile umthandazo wakho kanti awubuzanga elangeni. Kuzothi usathi nalu uju, ‘khafu' sewuphelile umhlangano olandelayo kawaziwa ukuthi uyoba nini.Usuyominca, uzisongasonge uze ufike lapho ivuma khona! Ozakwethu bazovumelana nami ukuthi lezi zimo ezibhaliwe njengeziyimbangela yenduku ewayo, hhayi sengathi kukhona okungakashiwo! Kuyashiwo phela kubalwe onhliziyo, isifo sikashukela njalo njalo kodwa uyothi usuzibhekele zonke izifo ezibaliwe kodwa induku lutho ukunyakaza.Abanye baze bathandaze izilimi impela, ivele ithi ‘lala lulaza! Akekho ongaphika uma ngithi abafowethu nodadewethu kwezempilo lezi zimo okuthiwa ziyizimbangela sezizanyiwe kodwa umphumela lutho. Kunabesilisa abaqalwa yilesi sifo besebancane, bengenashukela, bengenanhliziyo eyisifo beziphilela nje. Ngikhuluma ngabantu abangenangcindezi ebuchosheni kodwa lutho kwale! Umbuzo uthi pho  inkinga engumsusa ikuphi? Impendulo ilele ekulumbaneni kokusebenza komzimba kuphembelwa wukugula okuphehlwa yisibindi. ‘Uthini udokotela?’, omunye uzosho. Ngisho ngikhumbuza ukuthi isibindi singumakhonya emzimbeni, ukugula kwaso kubhebhethekisa ukugcwala kobuthi egazini, gazi lelo elizogcwala umzimba wonke. Isibindi sithontelanisa amafutha awushevu.Yila mafutha azophehla izifo eziyisishiyagalombili ezivele zigcwale umzimba wonke. Ziyakwazi lezi zifo eziyisishiyagalombili ukwakha amadlangala esibelethweni kowesifazane, bese zidala izigaxa, noma zibe sesidlekeni samaqanda lapho zidala ukungabatholi abantwana. Kowesilisa ziyahlala zihlasele imithanjana ehambisa igazi endukwini, umphumela kube yinduku engavuki, enciphayo nesheshe ikhafule. Kokunye ziyohlala ekhanda kowesilisa nowesifazane, okulandelayo yikhanda elibuhlungu lingayeki iminyakanyaka. Abebe ngazi, yilesi sizathu sokwazi umsusa wamakhanda abuhlungu esenza sikwazi ukwelapha zonke izinhlobo zamakhanda abuhlungu, sikhuluma ngabantu abasuke bekade bephuma bengena bethungatha amakhambi azolapha ikhanda. Engifisa sikubone futhi esikugcizelela kakhulu lapha namhlanje wukuthi umsuka omkhulu oholela endukwini engasebenzi, usuka esibindini.Sithi lezi zifo eziwubuthi zibe seziqonda ngqo ezingxenyeni zobulili besilisa, imiphumela kube yinduku engasebenzi, kokunye kuze kube yinkinga yokungabatholi abantwana.
