Isikhathi esiningi bekulokhu kumangaza ukubona izingane ezincane ezingakabi nazo zonke lezi zifo ezejwayelekile, okuthiwa zinomthelela ezinkingeni zenduku, njengenhliziyo engasenamandla zihlushwa yizinkinga zenduku, kokunye nokungabatholi abantwana.Ucwaniingo seliwukhombile umsusa womhlola. La mafutha esibindini ayinkinga enkulu, uphando lusho njalo. Inselelo odokotela abaningi abafunde lolu cwaningo lungakafiki, ngeke ubezwe bekhuluma ngala mafutha ayingozi kangaka asesibindini. Lesi sisodwa ngesinye sezizathu ezenza lesi sifo sibe yinkinga engaka nabantu babe baningi kangaka abanekinga yenduku, ukuncipha kwayo nokusheshe ikhafule. Enye into engumthelela ngalesi sifo yindlela esingena ngayo. Sizihambela kancane kasijahi ndawo. Wonke umuntu simlimaza ngonyawo lonwabu, elokhu ethi umuntu mahlayeni kusazolunga, kanti yilapha ekuqaleni kwezimpawu okumele ngabe siyangenela selaphe isibindi.Ngicela ukusika elijikayo, ngithi nakwabesifazane isibindi esinamafutha sidala ukwehla kothando locansi, ukungafiki kuvuthondaba, ukungavukelwa ungumuntu wesifazane, nokungabatholi abantwana. Okubuhlungu wukuthi baningi abantu abasaqhubeka benale nkinga ngoba asifuni ukwelapha umsuka okuyila mafutha asesibindini.Ngiyaphinda, abantu bakithi abakathandi ukwelapha isibindi, noma sesichaze kangakanani kule ngosi nalapho sikhuluma umlomo nomlomo. Kwesinye isikhathi ngize ngicabange ukuthi kasifuni ukwelapha isibindi ngoba udokotela ochaza lokhu kugula emnyama ngebala, ukube ngangimhlophe ngabe sikhuluma ngengqwaba yabantu abangabe sebelashiwe. Iqiniso esingasoze silibalekele wukuthi abantu bayagula ngenxa yesibindi, abantu bayaqhubeka bayahamba emhlabeni ngenxa yesibindi esigcwele amafutha. Lokhu kuzokwenzeka sithanda noma singathandi! Uma induku ingasebenzi, uma induku iwela phakathi, induku enciphayo, esheshe ikhafule, konke kungenxa yesibindi esikhiqiza izifo ngenxa yamafutha aqaqele esibindini. Kumele ngabe siyabuza ukuthi la mafutha asesibindini afike kanjani? Seyiphenduke iculo incazelo ethi amafutha asesibindini abangwa ngutshwala, ukudla okuswidi kuhlanganisa ama-roll, isinkwa esimhlophe, ushukela, ukudla okuthengwa sekuphrosesiwe ngikhuluma ngalokhu kudla okunenqwaba yezakhi nawe ongazazi ukuthi ziyini, ukudla okufana nama-pizza, amakhekhe nenyama yenkukhu olamthuthu.Umyalezo wanamuhla uthi: kusisiza kangakanani ukuba nolwazi oludephile ngocansi kodwa lube lungakwazi ukusebenza ithuluzi locansi? Yingakho namhlanje ngikubone kubalulekile ukucoboshisa ngolwazi lomsuka wesifo senduku ewayo, enciphayo nokungabatholi abantwana ungumuntu wesilisa. Siphendula umbuzo othi iyini imbangela yokuphunduleka kwenduku usemncane? Kunesigatshana esingenhla lapho esize sadlula sathi lokhu okwenzeka kowesilisa kuyenzeka nakumuntu wesifazane, athi emncane avele angahaleli ucansi aphinde, angafiki kuvuthondaba, kwabanye aze angavukelwa emncane enjalo. Sichazile sathi imbangela ngamafutha akhela esibindini ebangelwa ikakhulu wushukela nakho konke okunoshukela, ukudla okuphehliwe (processed) njengesinkwa, ama-roll, ama-corn flake, nokuningi okunhlobonhlobo? Uthi bewazi nje ukuthi ushukela owuthola esinkweni esimhlophe ungaphezulu kowuthola esilinganisweni esifanayo sikashukela uqobo? Ngale ndlela ngiyethemba siyabona ubungozi bokudla okuphehliwe ukuthi kubukeka kungenankinga kodwa uma usucubungulisisa ingozi iyazicacisa. Yini okumele siyenze ukuze induku iphile ibe ngumqemane, abangenabantwana bashekelele okonakalayo? Yini esingayeza ukuze mina wesifazane ngifike kuvuthondaba, ngihalele ucansi, ngiyeke ukungavukelwa?sethu sangaphakathilokudla. Ngenxa yamagama anqunyelwe ingosingeke ngikwazi ukuchaza konkeMpilonde!ONGOTI bezempilo bathi umuthi okufuthwa ngawo amakhala okuthiwa uvikela iCovid-19 osetshenziswa kakhulu emazweni ase-Europe, ungaholela ekutheni igciwane libe yingozi.Isikhungo esenza ucwaningo i-Africa Health Research Institute (AHRI) sixwayise ngokusetshenziswa kwalo muthi ofuthwa emakhaleni, okuthiwa uthengwa kakhulu emazweni ase-Europe, iViraleze, ngenhloso yokuthi ulwe negciwane.Lesi sikhungo sithi umphakathi kumele ukugweme ukusebenzisa lo muthi ngoba okwamanje ukugoma kuseyikona kuphela okungasiza ekutheni igciwane lingamgulisi kakhulu ongenwe yilona.Sithe inkinga lo muthi ukuthi njengoba ungewona umgomo abantu bangawuthenga balokhu bewusebenzisa bese bewusebenzisa ngokweqile okungaholela ekutheni ugcine ungasasebenzi.I-AHRI yenze lesi sixwayiso kulandela ukuthi abezindaba basemazweni aphesheya bebike ngawo okuholele ekutheni abantu bawuthenge ubuthaphuthaphu.UKUNGALULANDELI uhlelo lokujova uma ulunywe yinja nokungayi nhlobo esikhungweni sezempilo kungaholela ekutheni olunywe yinja afe.Isifo samarabi esingena kumuntu ngokulunywa yinja enalesi sifo sidla lubi eThekwini nasezindaweni ezigudle ugu.UDkt Minkie Masimege owudokotela wezilwane eMnyangweni wezoLimo KwaZulu-Natal, uthe abantu abaningi bayithatha kancane indaba yamarabi. Abanye bajova kanye esikhundleni sokujova kane, abanye abayi hlobo esikhungweni sezempilo uma belunywe izinja." Ukujova isona sikhali sokuvimbela ukuthi igciwane elingena ngesikhathi ulunywa yinja liye ebuchosheni bese liphenduka liba amarabi. Leli gciwane lingena enxebeni ngesikhathi amathe ehlangana nalo. Lesi sifo aselapheki uma sesize sazinza egazini saba ngamarabi. Esikhungweni sezempilo bakunika imithi yezinhlungu kodwa basuke bengeke besakwelapha uma uze wafinyelela kuleso sigaba,“   kusho uDkt  Masimege.Uthe isifo samarabi isifo esidala, esingena ngaphansi kwezifo ezibizwa ngezoonotic diseases  ezidluliselwa izilwane ebantwini." Lesi sifo selokhu sangena kuleli siningi eThekwini, ucwaningo lusitshela ukuthi izinja ziba ziningi lapho kunabantu abaningi khona. Kule minyaka embalwa edlule sesiyabona ukuthi izindawo ezifana nakuMasipala weLembe,  Ugu noMgungundlovu,  siyanda isibalo sezinja ezikhona," kusho uDkt Masimege.EThekwini kunezinja ezingu-350 000. Kusukela ngoJanuwari nyakenye zingu-233 izigameko zamarabi ezibikiwe KwaZulu-Natal. Kulezi zigameko bangu-17 abantu ababulewe ilesi sifo kubo abangu-10 abaseThekwini.Abashonile izingane ezineminyaka ephakathi kwemibili nengu-13.Uthe izingane zijwayele ukulunywa izinja ngoba zithanda ukuzidlalisa noma ukuzichukuluza. Kuyenzeka zingasho emakhaya ukuthi zilunywe yinja ngoba zisaba ukuthi zizoshaywa ngoba kuzozwakala ukuthi izona ebezichukuluza izinja.UDkt Masimege uthe kuyenzeka emiphakathini yabantu abamnyama amarabi aphambaniswe nobuthakathi ngoba onalesi sifo, uba nolaka enze umsindo ofana nowenja, ahayize, agxize amathe."Inja enamarabi ifa ngemuva kwezinsuku ezimbalwa kanti umuntu olunywe yiyo, uma engelashwanga,  kuyenzeka kuze kuphele iminyaka emibili igciwane liphila kuye kodwa lingakabi amarabi. Kuya ngokuthi inja imlume kuyiphi ingxenye yomzimba  nokuthi amanxeba mangaki,  futhi ajule kangakanani. Uma esonyaweni noma emaqakaleni kuthatha isikhathi ukuthi igciwane lihambe lize liyofika ebuchosheni,  bese liphenduka amarabi. Ngesikhathi kwenzeka lokhu abantu basuke sebekhohliwe ukuthi onezimpawu wake walunywa yinja bese becabanga ukuthi ubuthakathi," kuxwayisa uDkt Masimege.Uthe indlela yokuzivikela kulesi sifo ukuthi abanikazi bezinja bazigomele amarabi. Uma ulunywe yinja uye emtholampilo. NGIYAPHOQELEKA namhlanje ukuthi ngigagule esinye seziguli esisithe thasi sesiyongena ogibeni lomgudu wokuphela kwempilo. Ngabe kukhulunywa okunye ukube asixhunyaniswanga yindodakazi eyayizwe ngosizo esilwenzayo maqede yathatha ucingo yalushaya ngenyanga edlule. Yayinomama owayelashwa esibhedlela esiseduze kwakhe. Umama lo wayesekholelwe isikhathi eside kwinkoleloze ethi isifo sikashukela aselapheki, kumele adle imishanguzo aze ahambe emhlabeni. Okwakumangalisa ngaleya nkathi wayengasakwazi ukunyathela ngezinyawo ngenxa yobuhlungu obabugwaza njengontshumentshu ezansi kweqakala. Noma kunjalo wayengakholelwa ukuthi ushukela ungelapheka ziphele izinhlungu.Ngiyafisa siyisizwe sikuqaphele ukuthi ukwelashwa kwezempilo umsebenzi omuhle oncomekayo futhi wenziwa ngabantu abaqeqeshiwe abenza into elungile. Malingasilahlekeli iqiniso elithi isakhiwo salokhu kwelashwa yibhizinisi. Ebhizinisini okuphambili inzuzo. Abafuna sidle imishanguzo size siye egodini akungoba bengazi ukuthi ushukela uyelapheka uphume uphele emishanguzweni.  Okuphambili kubo yimali eyizigidigidi. Le nzuzo ayizi kithi njengezwekazi ngoba thina siyathenga, kodwa iya emazweni angaphandle. Uma bengafundisa thina odokotela nathi sonke kwezempilo ukuthi isifo sikashukela siyelapheka siphele, ibhizinisi labasunguli liyowa nakanjani emuva kwesikhathi. Abakufuni lokho.Uma owezempilo ethi isifo sikashukela aselapheki usho akufunzwayo. Odokotela ngokwethu bakhuluma iqiniso elimsulwa yingakho sakholwa ukuthi awelapheki ushukela angithi? Izingqondo zethu zawinwa ngokufundisa thina odokotela ukuze sifunze isizwe okungelona iqiniso elimsulwa. Asikwazi  ukungabakholwa  laba esithi ngodokotela. Ngike ngafonelwa esinye seziguli sisho sakuqhosha sithi sihlale esibhedlela saseThekwini izinyanga selulwa ngenxa ye-stroke, umqondo wethu bawuwina.Angithi uzogcina uphazamisekile emqondweni une- dementia ngenxa ye- insulin, i-uric acid egazini lakho elizoya ebuchosheni, imithambo ayisavuleki ngenxa yokuvalwa ukuxubha ngala makhemikhali ayi-flouride ekwi- toothpaste nasemanzini esiwaphuzayo. Lapho ususetshenzwa ngodokotela bengqondo, leyo mali iyaphi? Imali yama-toothpaste iyaphi? Ngubani olimalayo? Uma isayensi ithi hlukanani nala ma-toothpaste nithini? ‘Uyahlanya lona, asithengi i-toothpaste ngemali yakhe, sizoqhubeka thina nezingane zethu, ufuna amazinyo agqwale sinuke umlomo’. Ukuxubha ngomlotha akugqwalisi mazinyo, awunukelwa mlomo.Eqhubeka echaza wathi izinyawo ngaphansi zaziqaqamba kanye nobhozo ubuhlungu, sekwaba impilo yakhe. Wayethi owakwakhe uyamthinta kokunye emthoba akhale kuzwe nongaphandle kwegceke. Izinyawo zase zivuvukele zicwebezela, sezigqunqile ngaphambili. Sitholane nalo mndeni isimo sinjena, ushukela egazini uma bewubheka ezikhungweni zezempilo uphezulu udla amagalane, empeleni wayesezitshelile ukuthi lena kuzoba yindlela yakhe yokuphila njengoba namehlo ayesenqundeka, inkwantshu igcwele emzimbeni. Kwakungelula ukumchazela sithi lena akukwazi ukuthi kube yimpilo yakhe. Saze samnqoba ngokuthi sivume ukuthi eze nobaba wakwakhe bezolala lezi zinsuku eziyisishiyagalombili elashwa. Ngingena wangikhombisa izinyawo, nangempela ngasondeza imijovo yakhona saqala savuselela imizwa eyayisiqubudile nje ingawakhiphi amangwevu afanele ngenxa yokuququdwa ngamakhemikhali asuka esibindini okuthiwa ngamaROS (Reactive Oxygen Species). La makhemikhali awahleki nomuntu uma nje unesibindi esigcwele amafutha, aphuma engena efuna lapho enganamathela khona kuqale izinhlungu; kungaba buhlungu  izinyawo, ikhanda, idolo, ngemuva kwedolo, isikhumba, amehlo, amanyonga, ihlombe nangemuva esiphangeni, empeleni le khemikhali inganamathela noma yikuphi ukuze iqale ukuqaqambisa leyo ndawo. Sathi siqeda ukumfaka imijovo sase sikwazi ukuziphulula izinyawo zakhe. Ekumhloleni umzimba wonke sathola ukuthi nebala isibindi sivuvukele sigcwele amafutha, wayenemithambo nemizwa eyayikhukhumele ingaphakathi eyayingasakwazi ukwenza imisebenzi ngendlela elindelekile. Saphinde sagcizelela ubungozi besibindi sakhe esigadlabeza umzimba wakhe ngezifo eziyisishiyagalombili wonke umzuzu uma nje kusenalamafutha. Lezi zifo esithi zikhiqizwa yisibindi zidala inqwaba yezifo emzimbeni kuhlanganisa isifo sikashukela, umfutho ophezulu, imidlavuza enhlobonhlobo, induku engasavuki nenciphayo isheshe iwe (kwabesilisa). Kowesimame akabe esaluhalela ucansi angabe esafika kalula kuvuthondaba ngenxa yemizwa ethunazekayo, amakhanda axakayo, ukugula ngomqondo, ingcindezi ebuchosheni nasemqondweni, ukuvuvukala kwemilenze, izinkinga zesikhumba ezixakayo ukuzelapha. Emuva kokuba umama esejoviwe, akuphelanga ihora wabe esezihambela ngezinyawo zakhe, ukujabula kwabhalwa ebusweni bakhe nobukababa wakwakhe. Kusukela ngalolo suku luka-Agasti impilo yashintsha njengabo bonke abadlula ezandleni zalomsebenzi kuba njalo. Wahlala, wafakwa imijovo ngedriphu izinsuku zilankanyana. Wehla ushukela wansondo. Mangisho ukuthi ekuqaleni kwaba nzima kuye ukulandela indlela okwakumele adle ngayo, kunezikhathi lapho wayegcina esethatha nokudla kukababa wakwakhe. Kodwa sasheshe sakubamba lokho sakhulumisana naye saphinde samceba endodakazini owayeze ngayo esibhedlela.Lo mama uhambe ushukela ususezingeni elemukelekile, ne-Fasting Insulin yakhe isingaphansi kuka-05. Nangaphakathi ekujuleni kokusebenza komzimba wakhe kwase kunenqubekela phambili enkulu, ingcabha yayisikuye kuphela owayengazenzela phansi. Izifo zakhe owasezijwayele zawohloka. Kumanje uphila impilo yokuqikelela okungena emlonyeni, nendlela yokudla yalolu hlelo kulula ukuyilandela.Noma ngubani angafana naye, ashintshe impilo iqhubekele phambili, ungavumeli izifo ezifana noshukela ziyidlavaze iphele singakafiki isikhathi.Yenza konke okusemandleni ukulwela impilo yakho, akekho omunye oyokulwela ngaphandle kwakho.Mpilonde!NGOKUJWAYELEKILE, isikhathi esiningi, uma kuqala unyaka kuba nezinhlelo abantu abazibekela zona nezinto abazifisayo. Yize lo mkhuba uyinto esingenisile kubantu abaningi, kulo nyaka kubukeka kuzoba wumqansa ekutheni abantu bakwazi ukuzigcina zonke izithembiso abazenzayo emqondweni yabo nabafisa ukuthi bazenze ngenxa yeCovid-19 eguqule isimo sempilo.Ungoti wezengqondo, uMnuz Phumlani Mbatha, weMi Wellness, uthe ukuze abantu bagweme ukuphoxeka nokuzithola benengcindezi abangayidingi empilweni yabo, kumele babheke ukuthi u-2020 ubaphathe kanjani. Uthe ukubhidlika kwezinhlelo abebenazo ngonyaka odlule kumele bakubeke emqondweni uma benza izinhlelo zabo kulo nyaka.“Sibone into ebesingayilindele ukuthi ingase yenzeke empilweni yethu ngonyaka owedlule. Abantu abaningi baphelelwe wumsebenzi, abanye bashabalalelwa ngamabhizinisi abo abebethembele kuwona nabengenisa imali. Yize uvalo lukhona kodwa akumele basabe kuze kweqe ngoba bazogcina bemisa izinhlelo okumele ziyise impilo yabo phambili. Okusemqoka manje wukuthi babe nazo ezinye izinhlelo abazibeka eceleni komgodlagodla walezo abazibeke phambili abafuna kube yizo eziphumelela kakhulu ezinhlelweni abanazo,” kusho uMbatha.Uthe ukuze abantu balekeleleke ekutheni bangazitholi sebenokhwantalala lokungaphumeleli kwezinhlelo zabo ngenxa yemali, ukuphelelwa wumsebenzi nokungahambi kahle kwezinto kulo nyaka, kumele bangalehlisi izinga lokuphupha ngezinto ezinhle nabafisa ukuthi zifezeke empilweni. Uthe ukuxukuzisa umqondo ngokucabanga izinto ezinhle kunomthelela omuhle engqondweni yomuntu noma ngabe wukuthi izinto azihambi ngendlela abefisa ukuthi zihambe ngayo empilweni.“Akumele kulo nyaka sikuvumele ukuthuswa yizinto ezenzekayo njengoba senzile kowedlule. Kumele abantu bavive, balindele noma yini engaphazamisa izinhlelo kulo nyaka. Kulabo abaphelelwa wumsebenzi, kumele uphele lo nyaka sebenalo icebo lokuthi imali yabo bazoyisebenzisa kanjani. Lokhu kuzokwenza ukuthi baqaphele ukuthi abayiququdi ngezinto ezingenamqondo neziholela ekutheni basale bemhlwempu ngokuhamba kwesikhathi uma isiphele yonke imali.” Uqhube wathi abantu kumele bazisondeze ezinkampanini zokutshala imali bese begwema amabhanoyi ashabalala nezimali zabo uma esephahlazekile. Uthe njengoba isizwe sibhekene nesimo seCovid-19, kumele abantu bafunde ubumqoka bokwenza ucwaningo mayelana nezinto eziphathelene nemali ngaphambi kokuthi bathathe izinqumo zokuyisebenzisa.Amathiphu ongakwazi ukuphila ngawo kulo nyaka ukuze ugweme ukhwantalala :Yiba namacebo ongaphuma ngawo otakwini obhekene nalo uma izinhlelo obuzibekele zona zingaphumeleliGqugquzeleka ngaso sonke isikhathi ngamaphupho akho  noma ngabe ubhekene nezinselelo ezingakananiQala ibhizinisi ongakwazi ukwenza ngalo imali ukuze ungabi nokhwantalala lokuswela imali noma ukuba nezikweletuYenza ucwaningo olunzulu uma ufuna ukugcina imali oyithole enkampanini obusebenza kuyoGwema ukudlala amabhanoyi ukuze ungazitholi ususenkingeniMbali KhanyileABE-SOUTH  African Depression and Anxiety Group baxwayisa abantu ngokuthi abagweme ukhwantalala njengoba amaholidi  okuphela konyaka enezinto eziningi eziholela ekutheni bagcine benengcindezi.UNksz Collen O’Day  ongungoti ezifweni zengqondo, uthe  kuningi okungaholela ekutheni abantu bagcine beba nokhwantalala kula maholidi nokuholela ekutheni bagcine bephathwa yizifo ezihambisana nokuphazamiseka kwengqondo.“ Uma kungamaholidi okuphela konyaka kuvamise ukuthi kube nezinhlelo eziningi ezidinga imali nesizenza nabangani nemindeni yethu. Lezi zinhlelo ziba yimbangela yokugula kwabantu okudalwa yingcindezi abazithola sebephila ngaphansi kwayo. Ukuhambela imicimbi nokuba matasa ngokuvakasha ngokunye okuba nomthelela enkingeni yokhwantalala,” kusho uNksz O’Day.Uqhube wathi  nalabo abahlala ngabodwana babhekana nengwadla  yokubulawa umzwangedwa oholela ekutheni babe nokhwantalala.Uthe  kumele abantu  bazinike isikhathi esanele sokuhambela ongoti abeluleka ngokwengqondo uma bezizwa bengekho esimeni esikahle emoyeni. Uthe utshwala akumele bube yisisombululo kubantu abazizwa benokhwantalala.“ Izinkinga zanda kakhulu kubantu abacwila otshwaleni ngenhloso yokuzama  ukukhohlwa yikho konke okusuke kubakhungethe. Ngokwemibiko ye-Anxiety and Depression Association of America abantu abaphathwa wukhwantalala bavame ukucwila ezidakamizweni ngenhloso yokuzama ukugwema ukhwantalala. Lokho akusiwo umkhuba omuhle ngoba uzandisa kakhulu izinkinga,” kusho lo ngoti. Nakhu ongakwenza ukuze ugweme ukhwantalala kula maholidi:– Khuluma uma kukhona okungakuphethe kahle. Zama ukungafihli uma uphatheke kabi. Thola umuntu othembekile nongakhuluma naye ukuze akweluleke enkingeni obhekene nayo.– Gwema umzwangedwa. Uma udliwa umzwangedwa zama ukuzisondeza kubantu abangakwenza uzizwe ujabulile emoyeni.– Thola ezinye izindlela zokuxhumana nomndeni nabangani bakho uma uqhelelene nabo. Zijwayeze ukusebenzisa izinkundla zokuxhumana ukuze ungagcini nokukhuluma nabantu osondelene nabo ngocingo kuphela.– Qikelela ukuthi aweqi emalini  oyihlelele ukuyisebenzisa kula maholidi. Lokhu kungakusiza ekugwemeni ukuphathwa wukhwantalala lokuphelelwa yimali engakapheli amaholidi. Kugweme ukujabulisa abantu ngemali yakho yokugcina.–  Hlela izinto kusenesikhathi ukuze ugweme ukhwantalala lokuhlela  ngomzuzu wokugcina. Zihlelele izinsuku zokuthenga igilosa  yakho ukuze ungazitholi usutatazela ngoba ungagcina umosha imali ngokuthenga izinto ongazidingi ngenxa yamatata.– Qikelela ukuthi uyawunakekela umzimba wakho. Isikhathi esiningi uma kuyilesi sikhathi sonyaka abantu abakubheki  abakudlayo nabakuphuzayo. Zama ukugwema isikalo sokudla okuningi kakhulu. Zijwayeze ukudla okunempilo bese uzama ukugwema ukudla oswidi kakhulu neziphuzo ezihlohlozayo. Zijwayeze ukuzivocavoca.– Hambela kude notshwala  nezidakamizwaKULINDELEKE ukuthi ngoLwesithathu umengameli wezwe uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa asayine umthethosivivinywa womshwalense wezempilo kazwelonke.Lokhu kuvezwe yihhovisi likaMengameli ngoMsombuluko ebusuku ngesitatimende esinamekwe ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.Ngokwesitatimende ngoLwesithathu, mhla ziyi-15 kuMeyi 2024, umengameli uzosayina esidlangalaleni uMthethosivivinywa Womshuwalense Wezempilo Kazwelonke oqondisa ukuguqulwa kohlelo lokunakekelwa kwezempilo lwaseNingizimu Afrika ukuze kufinyelelwe ekuhlinzekeni izinsiza zezempilo emhlabeni wonke futhi, ngalokhu, kunqobe ukungalingani okubucayi kwezenhlalo-mnotho kanye nokungalingani okwedlule.Umcimbi wokusayina uzobe use-Union Buildings, ePitoli, ngo-14h00.UmbuzoNgingowesilisa, ngihlala nomama wengane yize ngingakamloboli kodwa ngiyamthanda futhi sesihlale naye isikhathi eside. Inkinga usenomkhuba engingazi ukuthi uwuthathaphi. Useqala ukungincisha ucansi. Uma ngithi ngiyambuza ukuthi ngoneni, uthi usekhathele ukulala nami mahhala. Uthi ngeke esanginika ucansi kuze kube ngiyovela kubo. Yebo ngiyasebenza futhi ngiyafisa ukumlobola kodwa manje njengoba sihlala ndawonye, izindleko ziningi. Nemali igcina iphela, kwazise yimina ngedwa osebenzayo. Ngicela ungibonise MaGumede ngenzenjani ngoba angifuni ukugcina sengiyofuna ucansi ngaphandle ekubeni ekhona yena. Ngiyamthanda kakhulu.ImpenduloYize ngingasazi isizathu esenza ukuthi nigcine senihlala ndawonye ekubeni ningashadile kodwa angiboni kuwumqondo omuhle ukuthi nihlale ndawonye, ngoba nawe uyathanda ukumlobola inkinga izindleko zonke ziphezu kwakho.Kungakuhle nihlukane ngokuhlala yikhona uzokwazi ukuqongelela imali yokuyovela kubo.Uma engeke akwazi ukuyoziqashela, kungcono ayohlala ekhaya kubo ngoba vele akasebenzi uhleli nje.Uma umthanda ngeke uphume uyofuna ucansi ngaphandle kodwa uzokwenza indlela yokuthi nilungise lento ngoba nakho ukuyofuna ucansi ngaphandle kungenza ukuthi isimo sibe sibi kakhulu. Angaze acabange nokuthi awumloboli nje ngoba vele khona osuthandana naye. Ukhumbule amaphutha awalungiswa ngamaphutha.UMNYANGO wezeMpilo kuleli ucela abazali ukuthi bavumele izingane zamantombazane ukuthi zigomele igciwane elidala umdlavuza wesibeletho, iHuman Papilloma Virus  (HPV).Njalo ngoMashi, abahlengikazi abasebenza emnyangweni bavakashela ezikoleni zamabanga aphansi ngenhloso yokugoma abafundi bamantombazane, abaneminyaka eyisishiyagalolunye kuye kwewu-10, ukuze bavikeleke ekutheni bathole igciwane.Iphini likaNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Sibongiseni Dhlomo, lithe umdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho ungowesibili ohlasela abantu  besifazane abaningi kuleli, ulandela umdlavuza webele.UDkt Dhlomo uthe ebantwini besifazane abangu-70% abanomdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho, kutholakala ukuthi imbangela yawo kusuke kuyiHPV. Wathi yingakho uhulumeni wathatha isinqumo sokuthi ligonyelwe igciwane."Kulo nyaka sigubha iminyaka eyishumi saqala ukugomela leli gciwane kuleli. I-HPV iyigciwane elitholakala ngokuya ocansini nomuntu onalo. Uma lingelashwanga liyahlala esithweni sangasese somuntu wesifazane bese kuthi ngokuhamba kweminyaka liphenduke libe umdlavuza wesibeletho. Kule minyaka eyishumi sigoma amantombazane sibone kunempumelelo enkulu yokuthi abagonyiwe ngeke besahlaselwa wumdlavuza womlomo wesibeletho odalwa yigciwane,"  kuchaza uDkt Dhlomo.Uqhube wathi eminyakeni engaphambili amantombazane abegoma kabili ngoMashi, nangoSeptemba ngoba ososayensi bathi kumele intombazane ithole imijovo emibili ukuze ibe nokuvikeleka okuphelele. Wengeza ngokuthi baqale nonyaka ukuthi basebenzise umjovo owodwa womgomo ngemva kocwaningo lwakamuva luveza ukuthi umjovo owodwa unikeza ukuvikeleka okuphelele."Lokhu sekuzosinikeza ithuba lokuthi sikwazi ukugoma abafundi basezikoleni ezizimele, abafunda ezikoleni zabakhubazekile, nabaneminyaka engu-14 kuya kwengu-15 okungenzeka ukuthi babesilele ngemuva," kuchaza uDkt Dhlomo.UDkt Dholomo uquhube wathi u95% wabazali wabafunda ezikoleni zikahulumeni bayavuma ukuthi izingane zabo zigome ngokuthi basayine amafomu akhishwa yizikole."Kuyasijabulisa lokho kodwa inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithe asikakafiki ezingeni elifanele lokuthi sigome amantombazane ukuze sivikele lesi sifo kodwa siyazama ukuthi sinyuse amasokisi. “Okunye esikukhuthazayo ukuthi abantu besifazane bajwayele ukuya emitholampilo uma kunokuthile abangakuzwa kahle. Umdlavuza wesibeletho phambilini ubuhlasela abantu besifazane asebefike esigabeni sokuthi bengasayi esikhathini kodwa manje akusenjalo nabasebancane sekuyenzeka bahlaselwe yilo mdlavuza,"  kusho iPhini likangqongqoshe wezempilo ezweni.UDkt Dhlomo uqhube wathi uma owesifazane eya esikhungweni sezempilo umdlavuza ungakasabalali kakhulu, kusho ukuthi usuke esesigabeni sokuqala kuya kwesesithathu, kunamathuba amaningi okuthi elapheke kodwa uma sekungaphezulu kwalokho kuba nzima.INQWABA yabantu abasuke bephuze kakhulu ngayizolo, bavuka benebhabhalazi okubenza bavuke baphinde baphuze futhi. Abanye basuke bephuza bengakaze badle lutho, okubenza ukuthi ubathole sebezidakelwe kungakakhweli nemini.Odokotela bathi abantu abenza lokhu bafana nse nabasuke befaka uphoyizeni emizimbeni yabo. Bathi utshwala ekuseni ungakaze udle lutho, bufana nse nophoyizeni ongakubulala ukusheshise.Ungoti wakwa-Affinity Health, uMurray Hewlett, uthe uma uphuza ungadlile, kusuke kunobungozi bokuthi utshwala buye ngqo emigudwini yegazi. Lokho kukodwa kwenza utshwala bungene ngqo egazini ngokushesha okwenza bugeleze buye nasezithweni zomzimba ezibalulekile ezifana nesibindi, izinso nokunye.“Ukuphuza usuke wadla kwenza ukuthi utshwala bugayeke mdibi munye nokudla osuke uke wakudla. Noma udakwa kodwa uma udlile awudakwa kakhulu kanjengoba ubuzodakwa ukube uphuze ungadlanga,” kuchaza uHewlett.Labo ngoti babala nokuthi ukujwayela ukuphuza utshwala ekuseni kungenza nokuthi ugcine usuyisidakwa esingakwazi ukuphila ngaphandle kotshwala. Bathi nokusebenza komqondo kuyaphazamiseka uma usujwayele ukuphuza zonke izinsuku. Ukukhuluphala ngokweqile, izinkinga zenhliziyo nokuphazamiseka komgudu ogaya ukudla ngezinye zezinkinga ongazithola ubhekene nazo uma uthanda lo mkhuba. UHewlet uthe isibindi sisebenza kanzima ukuze sihlunge ubuthi egazini lomuntu, sikhiqize amaprotheni abalulekile sibuye silawule izingxenye ezehlukene zokugayeka kokudla i-metabolism."Isibindi sibuye sigaye utshwala. Ukuphuza ngokweqile nokwenza ekuseni, kungaholela ezifweni zesibindi okungaba isibindi esinamafutha, isifo sokusha kwesibindi, ukufa kwama-cells aso isibindi  i-cirrhosis," kuchaza uHewlett.Uthe nakho nje ukuphuza utshwala obuningi kungaphazamisa ulwelwesi lomgudu wokugaya ukudla, okuholela ekuvuvukaleni kwalo. Lokhu kungadala izimo ezifana nokukhuphuka koketshezi olumuncu okumele ngabe luhlala emgudwini wokudla lukhuphuke luze lufike esifubeni okushisa isifuba nezinye izitho zomzimba ngesikhathi lukhuphuka, i-gastritis.Uthe uma ulwelwesi lwesisu luvuvukala kuba buhlungu esiswini, kucanuzele inhliziyo, uphalaze. Uma i-gastritis ingapheli, umuntu angaba sengcupheni yokuba nezilonda nomdlavuza wesisu.Amanyikwe abalulekile ekusizeni ukugaya nokulawula amazinga kashukela egazini. Ukuphuza ngokweqile kungase kuvuvukalise amanyikwe, kube buhlungu isisu, ube nesicanucanu, uphalaze. Uma kwenzeka umuntu eba nenkinga yamanyikwe engalashwa, angagcina esenesifo esingelapheki samanyikwe.Uqhube wathi ukuphuza utshwala ngokweqile kungaholela nasezinhlotsheni zomdlavuza kuzo okubalwa owomlomo, owomphimbo, owomminzo, isibindi, owamathumbu nowesitho sokulahla indle i-rectum."Ukuphuza ngokweqile kungakhinyabeza nomsebenzi womzimba wokumunca izakhamzimba ekudleni. Utshwala buphazamisa indlela umzimba omunca ngayo ama-vitamin nama-mineral abalulekile, okuhlanganisa  u-vitamini B, C, D, calcium, ne-magnesium. Lokhu kungaholela ekushodeni kwalezi zakhamzimba okungadala izinkinga. Ukuntuleka kwe-calcium kungaholela ekuncipheni kwamathambo, uphathwe yisifo samathambo," kuchaza uHewllet.Izindlela ongazisebenzisa ukuqeda ibhabhalazi:–  Musa ukuphuza utshwala ukukhipha ibhabhalazi, kodwa phuza amanzi kakhulu.– Uma kubheda ngaleyo ndlela, phuza ikhofi elimnyama nakhona hhayi kakhulu, uhhafu wenkomishi encane.– Sebenzisa imithi ezikisa i-acid esiswini ngoba utshwala bunomkhuba wokwenyusa lokhu bese isisu siba buhlungu ugajwe nayisilungulela.– Phuza iziphuzo ezine-electrolyte nazo ziyasiza ukubuyisa amanzi emzimbeni okwenzeka uma uphuza utshwala.– Zinike isikhathi esanele sokulala uma uphuze kwaze kwaba sebusuku noma kwaze kwasa. Ukungaphumuli kungenza ube nolaka olungenasidingo.UMBUZONGINGOWESIFAZANE olotsholwe zaphelela zonke, sekusele ukuthi ngishade kodwa manje ngizwa sekuthi xhifi-nje, akusavumi ngiqhubeke nale nto. Angazi noma ngithi angisamfuni yini lo muntu okanye angisathandi ukuhlala naye kodwa nje kukhona into engasavumi kahle. Okubuhlungu ukuthi sebezidlile izinkomo ekhaya futhi ngiyasaba ukuthi kungenzeka umyeni wami azifune ebese ekhaya bengizonda ngokuthi kungani ngingasavumi ukuqhubeka nomkhwenyana. Ngisenkingeni angazi ukuthi ngenzenjani ngoba angisafuni ngempela ukuqhubeka nomshado.IMPENDULOANGAZI kungani uvume ukulotsholwa kwasekuqaleni. Angazi futhi nokuthi yini edala ungabe usafuna ukushada naye kodwa engingakusho wukuthi kungcono uqale utshele umama wakho kuqala ukuthi uzizwa kanjani ngayo yonke le nto ngaphambi kokuthi ifike kumyeni wakho nabasemzini. Mhlawumbe likhona ikhambi abazali bakho abangaphuma nalo. Okumele ukwazi wukuthi umyeni wakho le nto uma engayizwa ingamhlukumeza kakhulu ngoba njengamanje injabulo iyachichima kuye, ulindele ukuthi uzoshadelwa. Kungakuhle-ke niqale niyilungise nodwa ekhaya, uma futhi kunesidingo sokuya kubantu besintu ningaya ngoba njengamanje kubukeka sengathi inkulu inkingaUDUMO lwakwiTik Tok selumvulele amathuba owaziwa ngelikaSimangaliso "Mr Cash only" Mathenjwa ohlala eqhulula amahlaya ezinkundleni zokuxhumana. UMnyango wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal usufake isikhangiso somcimbi wakusasa eMadressini wokusabalalisa ulwazi ngezinhlelo zempilo, okuzophinde kugujwe kuwo usuku lwabesifazane. Umcimbi wezempilo owaziwa ngokuthi; Isibhedlela Kubantu uvamise ukuhambela izindawo ezahlukene nosaziwayo, ikakhulu abesilisa njengoba kusuke kunohlelo lokubakhuthaza ngokuzinakekele ngezempilo nokuzihlola izifo. Abantu bachazekile ngalezi zindaba, babodwa abafisa sengathi uhlelo  luza ngasemakubo. AbaseMondlo bathembise ukuthi nakanjani bazoya kozibonela usomahlaya."Uzobe ebadonsa ngesithuthuthu amahora awu-90 cash,"kusho uMkhwanazi."Kwamina ngivele ngathi dlengelele, ngingaqedi nokusifunda lesi sikhangiso. Siyabonga ngqongqoshe,"kusho uKwanele Dlamini."Songena ngodli la,"kusho uNkosentsha Buthelezi."Weee senifuna ukubulala iziguli ngensini,"kusho uPalesa Nkosi.ESONTWENI eledlulile ngihlaselwe yisihlobo sesinye seziguli zami ngendlela engahlelekile kodwa ebidinga ukwehla nokwemukela isimo njengoba sinjalo ngokushesha okukhulu. Abake babe esimweni esifanayo bayongivumela ukuthi kuyinselelo kangakanani ukuqhamuka komuntu nje ungazelele, azokwehlisa akwenyuse, ethandabuza umsebenzi wakho oqinisekile ngawo nowujulukele kanzima. Miningi imicabango ekufikelayo, ekugcineni akukho okudlula inhlonipho, inhlonipho ngiphinde futhi inhlonipho uma usumcacisela.Umsebenzi wokwelapha isifo sikashukela, ogulayo aphume emishanguzweni yawo ngiyawazi, ngisho ungangivusa ngilele, ngeke kwenze umehluko; ngiyovuka ngikulaphe uhambe uthokozile njengabo bonke esibasizile ngokubelapha kusukela uqala unyaka. Siyazi ukuthi njengoba senza umsebenzi ongajwayelekile futhi osiza isizwe ngale ndlela ziningi izimbangi, baningi abamangala ngokubabaza okungajwayelekile futhi baningi kakhulu abanomona, abangasifiseli inqubekela phambili. Sike sezwa kukhona nabathi sibakhiphelani abantu ebugqileni bukashukela, bona bazohamba beyosiceba? Ngiyavuma esikwenzayo akujwayelekile, ekugcineni ngumsebenzi okumele ngabe kade waqalwa ukwenziwa lona uma besilulandela uphenyo lwesayensi. Inselelo enkulu yithina basebenzi bezempilo esivilaphayo ukufunda. Iningi lethu ligcina ngolwazi elilufunde encwadini nayo eyayisindala, eyayithi isifo sikashukela kaselapheki, kumele udle imishanguzo unomphela. Selokhu sayibamba lapho! Sesilwa nanoma iyiphi into eqhamukayo ezohluka kuloluya lwazi lwakudala, angiphathi uma izogqanyiswa ngumuntu omnyama, angithi? Hhayi kumele siyomceba enhlanganweni elawula ukusebenza kodokotela! Ngaleso sikhathi asiboni ukuthi sizembula izinqe, sivezela izwe ukuthi sikude kangakanani nokuthubeleza ngophenyo lwesayensi lwanamhlanje. Okubuhlungu kulokhu kusalela emuva ngolwazi lwesayensi, sihambe sikhuluma kubantu abasethembayo bethi sinolwazi olwanele nabo basikholwe bengahlolisisanga esikushoyo. Ekugcineni sekwenziwe kwashiwo konke, ushukela i-Type II Diabetes, iyelapheka iphele! Iyelapheka uphume emishanguzweni yayo ngisho ngabe usuyawujovela. Udinga izinsuku eziyisishiyagalombili ulalisiwe esibhedlela sethu, kwabanye bayelapheka emuva kwezinsuku ezinhlanu belalisiwe, inqobo nje uma uzosilalela usheshe ufike ekuguqulweni kokusebenza komzimba wakho.Ngelinye ilanga ngangixoxa komunye umsakazo omkhulu kuleli lizwe lethu, ngichaza ngithi sikubonile ukulapheka komqondo ophundulekile ngenxa yokukhubazeka ebuchosheni kubantwana abancane nakubantu asebekhulile. Ngalelo langa ngenza isibonelo ngomfanyana owayeneminyaka engu-15, owayesehlonzwe njengomtwana okhubazekile waze wakhishwa esikoleni esijwayelekile wasiwa esikoleni okuthiwa siyisipesheli. Kwasithatha amaviki amabili kuphela ukubuyisela umqondo endaweni yawo. Namhlanje lo mfana wenza kahle esikoleni lesi ayesekhishwe kuso. Wenza kahle ngisho esifundweni sezibalo. Ngathi sengizwa kwakukhuluma omunye kulowo msakazo owathi ungudokotela eqaphelisa umphakathi, ethi makuqashelwe “odokotela mbumbulu”. Le mikhonto iqhamuka nxa zonke, ihlaba iphindelela. Ekugcineni, maluqine ukhakhayi!Ngeke ngiyeke ukusho ngithi abanye abasebenzi bezempilo bayavilapha ukuzinothisa ngolwazi lwesayensi lwanamhlanje, bavele bagcine kuloluya besesesikoleni. Umuntu azihlalele nje bese egcina ngokungcofa ulwazi olusha, angiphathi uma lungaveli ngomuntu webala. Umuntu uze akholwe uma kungumuntu webala, angithi? Ake sibheke nje esifweni somfutho wegazi ongalawuleki ophezulu, angithi sasithi isikhathi esiningi isuke ingaziwa imbangela ngenkathi sifundiswa ezikoleni zobudokotela? Kungabe kusenjalo nanamhlanje? Luthini uphenyo lwamanje lwesayensi kulo munxa? Labo abadla umhlanganiso babetheni ophanyweni lwabo okwaholela ekutheni bahlonishwe ngeNobel Prize ye-Physiology and Medicine ngo-1998? Namhlanje ngikhuluma ngokuthi kuyimanje kunoshicilelo lwesayensi olukhuluma ngeNitric Oxide olangaphezu kwekhulu namashumi ayisikhombisa ezinkulungwane avulelwe kuwonkewonke ongawafunda. Uma besilulandela uphenyo lwesayensi ngabe asikhulumi sithi kunomfutho ophezulu wegazi esingawazi ubangwa yini? Kumele sonke ngabe sikhuluma ngephimbo elilodwa, sithi izincwadi ezifundwayo zobudokotela mazishintshwe ezindaweni ezithile ngoba uphenyo lwamanje lonke lusikhomba kanjalo.Lapha ngenxa yenani lamagama olunikezwe le ngosi ngiphoqeke ukuthi ngikhulume ngalezi zibonelo ezimbalwa okuyisifo sikashukela iType II Diabetes, isifo somfutho ophezulu wenhliziyo, nesifo somqondo ophundulekile. Lokhu sikwenze kwayizibonelo zezifo ezelaphekayo ziphele, ogulayo aphume emishanguzweni yazo ebiyisimbelambela. Ziningi ezinye izifo engeke ngikwazi ukuzibala namhlanje. Sineziguli eziningi esezilashwe ushukela zaphuma emishanguzweni nasebugqileni bezifo ezihambisana nawo, kanjalo esifweni somfutho wenhliziyo ophezulu kanye nesifo esiphundula ukusebenza komqondo. Siwenzile futhi siyaqhubeka siyawenza lo msebenzi ezigulini ezifikayo zicele usizo. Asiphoqe muntu, wena uma usafisa ukuqhubeka nemishanguzo yakho qhubeka nayo, esikujabulelayo ngukuqhubeka kodwa ulwazi usunalo oluthi lezi zifo ziyelapheka ziphele.Isifo sikashukela kuthatha izinsuku eziyisishiyagalombili ukuselapha siphele, umfutho ophezulu wenhliziyo izinsuku ezinhlanu, umqondo ubuyela ekusebenzeni ngendlela yakhona ezinsukwini eziyishumi nane. Esikwenzayo silapha umsusa nembangela yazo, akusizi ukushanguza wehlise isivuvu sezimpawu kuphela isiphethu sesifo singasiphulwanga nezimpande zazo. Abanye baye babuze ukuthi sisuke selaphani kulezi zinsuku esizishoyo esifweni sikashukela okanye seBP nezinye izifo? Yisiphi lesi siphethu esisuka sisisiphula? Umsuka wesifo sikashukela ngamafutha asuke eqhoqhobele isibindi eyizinqwaba khona ngokuphindiwe. Elinye ikhanda esisuke silichoboza kulezi zifo ingaphakathi lemithambo eliphundulekile bese lehluleka ukukhiqiza amakhemikhali afanele isifo esisibiza ngokuthi yi-Endothelial Dysfunction. Isibindi esinamafutha iFatty Liver Disease sikhiqiza izifo eziyisishiyagalombili yonke imizuzwana uthanda ungathandi, uma nje ulokhu unalamafutha kuso isibindi. Kwenye yezingosi kuleli phephandaba ngike ngazibala zonke. Izifo eziyisishiyagalombili ezinye zazo ezidala isifo sikashukela iType II Diabetes kusetshenziswana nosinyaka, i-pancreas. Uma sithi sikulapha ushukela sisuke sisemshikashikeni wokwelapha isibindi nesifo esisemithanjeni ngithe yi-Endothelial Dysfunction. Yingakho sidinga eziyisishiyagalombili ukukwelapha ukuze uphume welapheke ngokuphelele, hhayi nje ukukwehlisela amanani kashukela egazini. Abanye siyaye sithole ukuthi ukulawula kahle kokungena kukashukela ngaphakathi ezakhiweni eziyisisekelo zomzimba kuphundulekile. Laba yilabo uyaye uthole ukuthi ushukela wakhe uma ukalwa awuzinzi, uba phezulu uphinde ube phansi okanye ube kahle nje. Ngizama ukunikeza isimo lapho kunokuhlakanezeka okanye ukuhambela nxaye kwe GLUT4 Signalling. Ngeke siwageqe onke amagula. Ngiyethemba labo abahlale nemibuzo ethi sisuke selaphani ezinsukwini eziyisishiyagalombili okanye ezinhlanu, bayophinde bayithole incazelo.“Yelapha isifo sikashukela, uphume ekuguleni nasemishanguzweni yaso -  lesi makube yisipho sakho siKhakhisimusi nonyaka omusha u-2024!”Mpilonde!BANINGI kakhulu abantu bakithi abahlushwa isigubhukane okanye kube isimbelambela sesiyezi nokukhathala, baphume bengena befuna usizo, abanye bagcine sebelashelwa igazi okuthi  walehlile emzimbeni kodwabagcine bengasizakalanga.Ziningi izimo nezifo ezingabangela isiyezi nokukhathala kodwa namhlanje ngifisa ke sibuke imbangela evumbuka enhliziyweni nalena ephehlwa yindlala esentanyeni, iThyroid. Isiyezi nokukhathala izimo ezikhathaza zithunaze kakhulu umzimba. Uma unenhliziyo enamaxhwala, uzwa esifubeni ubuhlungu obungapheli obukubelesela uzeuvume uNoyana, izinhlungu zakhona zize zinyukele entanyeni nasengalweni yesinxele, iqaqambe kuzwele ngaphakathi ngasekhwapheni.Kwesinye isikhathi uthiuma uyohlola ngomshini wenhliziyo okuthiwa yi-ECG (Electrocardiogram), udokotela akuchazele ukuthi inhliziyo yakho ikhombisa ingcindezi yamaxhwala akhandwe amanxeba asenesikhathi enzeka kodwa elokhu eshaya, inhliziyo iqhubeka nokulokhu ifingqana nje. Ithi ikhipha igazikanti isinyathela nasesishozini bese kusondela izinhlungu ongakwazi ukuzibekezelela.Siyisizwe esiyiso, sikujwayele ukubekezela sithule nje, sibe sibona ukuthi ukugula kuhamba nathi. Ake sibukisane esinye isimo esikhandeka sibe ukukhathala okuhambisana nesiyezi okubangelwa yiyo inhliziyo.Inhliziyo ithi uma ifingqana ikhipha igazi ilisabalalisa, kumele libe ngamalitha amahlanu njalo ukuze  kuhlangatshezwane nezidingo zomzimba. Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi lapho elitheleka khonaigazi lisuka emaphashini, kumele kukwazi ukumumatha ubungako balo.Uma ngandlela thize ummumatho ungaselona inani legazi elilindelekile, nakanjani zizoqala izinkinga zokuphelelwa ngamandla, isiyezi, kwabanye kuhambisane nekhanda, inkwantshu engalapheki namajaqamba emzimbeni azojikeleza aye ngapha nangapha. Esinye sezizathu ezenza inhliziyo ibe nommumatho omncane, ukukhukhumalela ngaphakathi kwayo, endaweni yokuthi inwebekele ibheke ngaphandle yona ishintshe umkhondo. Asisale sesikhuluma nangokuthi inhliziyo uma seyikhukhumele iyasindana ingabe isakwazi ukusukuma ifingqane ngendlela yakhona.Nalokhu kunciphisa igazi elikhishwa yinhliziyo kulokhu kube ngenxa yokusindana ukusukuma kwenhliziyo. Lezi zizathu ziyathungelana okunye kuholele kokunye, ihluleke inhliziyo ize ithelele izinso, induku kwabesilisa, ukungahaleli kwabesifazane, iphele imizi, imindeni ibhekane ngeziqu zamehlo, kube yimbedu mehlwana emphakathini.Zonke lezi zigigaba esisizibalile zilandelisa ngokukhathala nesiyezi okungalawuleki. Ngike ngasho ngathi kuningi okwenza umzimba ukhathale ucobeke. Omunye useze wakujwayela ukukhathala ngale ndlela. Esizolokhu sikugcizelela namhlanje ukubaluleka kokuthola umsusa. Thola ukuthi umhlola uvelaphi. Baningi abantu bakithioyaye uzwe kuthiwe ubike ukukhathala wagcina elala unomphela, akabange esavuka. Uma uzwa umbiko onjena, kumele uzibuze njalo ukuthi usuhambe wafikaphi wena ngokukhuluma wazise abantu bakithi ngezifo ezinhlobonhlobo futhi ezilaphekayo? Uma uzibuza ukuthi yiziphi izifo ezingu-10 ezihamba phambili ekuthatheni impilo yabantu, impendulo ithiizifo eziyisimbelambela futhi ezelaphekayo ziphinde zivikeleke kalula nje. Pho yini eyenza abantu bakithi bahambe emhlabeni kanjena?Yini eyenza singafuni ukungena ohlelweni lokuzivikela ukuze siphephe kule nsindabadala esibhuqabhuqayo? Namhlanje ngithe ake sibuyele kwisiyezi nokukhathaIa, sihlaziye ngobaabaningi babika lezi zimpawo, okulandelayo sebehambile emhlabeni. Abanye baphelelwa amandla banqanyukelwe ngumoya, kungaphefumuleki, ukusuka lapho, nqwambi sebeshonile njalo. Lezi zimo ziyavikeleka! Yini pho sivume ukushiya imindeni yethu isidinga kangaka? Umbuzo othi yini engingayenza ukuthatha igxathu lokwelapha inhliziyo? Impendulo ilele ekwelapheni umsusa wokugula okuwukudla ushukela, ukudlala manandinandi esiwathenga ezitolo ziwukudla okusheshayo (fast foods) nokudla inyama yezinyoni nezilwane ezikhuliswe kusheshiswa. Ngikhuluma ngolamthuthu, inyama yenkomo yasezitolo, eyemvu yakhona neyengulube.Ake sizilinge senze lokhu, sizinike izinsuku ezingu-10 nje kuphela.Nazi lezi zinto:1. Asiyeke ukudlaushukela, nazo zonke izidlo ezinoshukela okungaba iziphuzo ezihlohlozayo, amajusi okuthiwa akhiwe ngemvelo yawo uma besikhohlisa, izinkwa, yizidlo ezinye ezidinga ubisi zasekuseni, iziphuzo okuthiwa azinashukela, uju oluthengwa ezitolo. Sehlukane nokunoshukela nje, zibe ngu-10 izinsuku.2. Asehlukane nokuthenga sidle izidlo ezidayiswa sezivuthiwe, okwethukube ukufudumeza. Lapha ngikhuluma ngo-pizza, hot dog, ice cream, kuningi kakhulu.3. Asisebenzise i-ExtraVirgin Olive Oil, ibe ngu-150mls ngosuku okanye ibenguhhafu enkomishini njalo ngosuku.4. Asiphuze amanzi ngendlela yempilo; okuwukuphuza izingilazi ezimbili uma sivuka; siphinde ezimbili ngaphambi kokulala, bese siphuza ezimbili njalo ngaphambi kokudla5. Asidle amasi okungenanikane ngeviki, okanyei-yoghurt eyi-full cream ekhandwa ngamajikijolo noma ingafakwa zithako. Sidle okuphuma ezihlahleni, kungaba amagwava, ukherothi,..okungenani kube kuhlanu ngosuku. Singakhohlwa amakhowe nokotapheya. Lezi zithelo asisidle kane evikini zona zizodwa.6. Asehlukane nenkukhu ulamthuthu, sehlukane nama-braai pack, inyama ethengwa isivuthiwe yezitolo esizijwayele nezinye ngenxa yamakhemikhali afakwe kuzo ikakhulu uma zichanyiselwa nalapho zikhuliswa. Kanjalo nenyama yezinkomo yasezitolo, amabhusha. Konke kukhuliswe ngamakhemikhali. Asidle inyama yenkukhu ekhuliswe ekhaya, inkomo nemvu okukhuliswe ekhaya ngoba yikhona okunempilo evelele.7. Thola isikhathi sokuphumuza umqondo njalo osukwini, uthandaze ngaleyo ndlela ehambisana nawe, uzivocavoce imizuzu engu-20 ngosuku, zibe zine izinsuku evikini. Ngithi nakhu sizwe sakithi, izinsuku ezilishumi kuphela uzowubona umehluko ozokwenzeka empilweni yakho.Mpilonhle!UNGOTI ocwaninga ngamagciwane adala izifo uSolwazi Abdool Karim Salim uxwayisa ngokuthi kungenzeka igciwane leCorona elizobe likhona ngesiwombe sesihlanu liholele ekutheni izibhedlela zigcwale ngesikhathi esincane.Isiqubu sesihlanu sokuhlasela kwaleli gciwane kulindeleke ukuthi sifike kuleli ngenyanga ezayo. Ososayensi phambilini bebethi kungenzeka igciwane elizobe likhona ngalesi sikhathi lingabi nawo amandla ngenxa yokuthi abantu abaningi kuleli sebeke bahaqwa iCovid-19, abanye bagomile kodwa uSalim, uthe kumele sifike lesi siwombe abantu sebekulungele ukubhekana naso ngoba uma kungenjalo bangazithola belaliswa ezibhedlela ngoba maningi amathuba okuthi leli gciwane lisabalale kakhulu kune-Omicron okuyigciwane lokugcina ebelihaqa abantu kuleli.“Esikwaziyo ngaleli gciwane ukuthi lizosabalala ngokushesha kune-Omicron ngoba igciwane elisha ukuze ligqibe ebelikhona phambilini kumele libe namandla kunalelo elisuke likade likhona. “Leli gciwane ngeke ligcine ngokusabalala masinyane kodwa lizobe lihaqa abantu abaningi ngokushesha okungaholela ekutheni izibhedlela zibe nengcindezi ngesikhathi esincane,” kusho yena.Usolwazi uthe umengameli wenze kahle waxegisa imithetho elawula ukusabalala kwegciwane ngalesi sikhathi njengoba izibalo zabahaqwa yilona zisephansi.“Lesi yisikhathi esikahle sokuthi abantu benze imicimbi yabo ebebeyimisile ngesikhathi igciwane lisasabalala ngamandla.“Abenza imicimbi yokuthwesa iziqu abayenze ngoba ukusabalala kwegciwane akuzuhlala kukuleli zinga okukulo njengamanje kungenzeka isimo sishintshe. Maphakathi noMeyi kungenzeka sibone izibalo zabahaqwa yigciwane zenyuka futhi," kusho yena.Uma kwenzeka izibalo zinyuka kumele abantu bakhumbule ukuthi zikhona izindlela zokunqanda ukusabalala kwalo ezifana nokufaka izifonyo, ukuqhelelana nokugwema imicimbi esendaweni evalekile."Uma zinyuka izibalo zabahaqekayo akusho ukuthi sekumele senze izaba zokunqanda ukusabalala kwegciwane ngesikhathi esisodwa, kumele senze lokho okuvumelena nesimo ngaleso sikhathi.”Isikhungo esenza ucwaningo lwezomnotho iBureau for Economic Research (BER), sithe amasampula amanzi ahambisa indle aseGauteng akhombisa ukuthi seliyenyuka izinga labantu abahaqwe iCovid-19 okusho ukuthi siyeza isiwombe sesihlanu sokuhlasela kwegciwane.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo eBotswana uDkt Christopher Nyanga umemezele ukuthi kunegciwane elisha le-Omicron elitholakale kuleliya lizwe kodwa wathi abantu abangethuki, ososayensi basalihlola.KUNINGI osekwenziwe ngasohlangothini lwesayensi ukuze kutholakale amasu amasha okwelapha noma okulwa nesifo sofuba, iTuberculosis (TB). Kumanje kunezinhlelo eziwu-17 zocwaningo ezenziwayo emazweni ahlukene zokuhlolwa kwabantu. Nyakenye inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), iveze ukuthi ngenxa yocwaningo lwesayensi oluqhubekayo emhlabeni, kunamazwe anjengeSwatini, iKenya, iMozambique, iSouth Sudan, iTogo, i-Uganda, iZambia,  neNingizimu Afrika akwazile ukwehlisa ukusabalala kwegciwane ngokukodwa kokuthathu ngo-2015.Yize kunjalo, iWHO idalule nokuthi amazwe anezinsiza kudingeka ukuthi agxile ekwelapheni abantu abathathwa njengabasengcupheni yokuthola iTB, okungaba abantu abahaqwe yiHIV/Aids.I-WHO ithe inselelo ebhekene namazwe ase-Afrika, ukuqinisekisa ukuthi iziguli ziyayiqeda imithi yazo. Ngokwejwayelekile ukwelashwa kweTB  kuthatha izinyanga eziyisithupha.“Izindlela ezintsha ezisunguliwe zakamuva ngezokuthi kube nabantu basemphakathini abahambisela iziguli imishanguzo emakhaya noma imishanguzo ithunyelwe ezikhungweni eziseduze okungaba izitolo, amahholo nokunye, ukuze abadla imishanguzo bangakhali ngokuthi imitholampilo ikude nalapho behlala khona noma ukuthi abanayo imali yokuya kuyo,” kudalula iWHO esitatimendeni.Ngokwezibalo zakamuva zocwaningo ngesifo sofuba oluphothulwe ngo-2022, lwethulwa emphakathini nyakenye kuvela ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika inesibalo esiphezulu kakhulu sabantu abaneTB, uma iqhathaniswa namanye amazwe emhlabeni. Ngokwezibalo balinganiselwa ku-280 000 abahaqwa yisifo ngonyaka, bangu-54 000 ababulawa yiTB ngonyaka.Isikhulu seTB HIV Care, uSolwazi Harry Hausler, uthe ukuhlolwa kwabantu ngoba benezimpawu kukodwa kungaholela  ukuthi u50%  weziguli ezinaleli gciwane zingahlonzwa.“Ngokuvamile iningi labantu ababi nazo izimpawu, nokuholela ekutheni kulibaziseke ukuhlonzwa kwabo, okuholela ekutheni  iTB isabalale kalula, kugule abantu abaningi. Okudala  izinkinga eziningi eziholela  ekufeni kwabantu abebengasinda ukube bekuhlolwa bonke abantu. "Uhlelo olusha lokuhlolwa kwalesi sifo olwaziwa nge-Targeted Universal Testing for TB (TUTT), lungaqinisekisa ukuthi abantu abasengozini enkulu yokuthola  iTB  bayahlolwa ngomshini okhipha imiphumela ngokushesha i-GeneXpert ngisho bengenazo izimpawu, ” kusho uSolwazi Hausler. Ngo-2010,  iWHO yanikeza  amazwe igunya lokuthi asebenzise  i-GeneXpert  ukuze kuhlolwe isifo.Ngokusho kukaSolwazi uHausle, iTUTT ivumela abasebenzi bezempilo ukuthi bakwazi ukuhlolwa nabantu abangenazo izimpawu.“I-TB HIV Care igqugquzela ukuthi kwandiswe izinhlelo zokuhlolwa kwabantu abaneHIV nabasondelene nabo. Kuphinde kube nemishanguzo ethathwa isikhathi  okuyi-isoniazid ne-rifapentine ephuzwa kanye ngesonto  isikhathi esiyizinyanga ezintathu,”  kusho uSolwazi Hausle. BABALELWA ku-1.6 million abantu abaguliswa ukudla ukudla okungaphephile emhlabeni ngosuku.Lokhu kushiwo yiNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ixwayisa abantu ngokuthi kumele baqaphele ukuthi badla ukudla okuphephile.Lo myalezo uhambisana nosuku olusetshenziselwa ukuxwayisa umphakathi ngezifo ezidalwa ukudla ukudla okungaphelile, iWorld Food Safety, olukusasa.UDkt Maria Niera, weWHO, uthe zibalelwa ku-200 izifo ezidalwa ukudla ukudla okungaphephile, ezinye zazo ziyabulala.Uthe phakathi kwezifo ezidalwa ukudla ukudla okungaphephile kubalwa ityphoid, icholera nelisteriosis."Lezi zifo ngokuvamile ziba nezimpawu ezifana nokukhishwa yisisu, ukuphalaza namajaqamba esiswini," kusho uDkt Neira.Odokotela bathi esimeni esidlulele kuyenzeka ukudla okungaphephile kuholele ekutheni umuntu agcine esenemizwa ephazamisekile, abe nenkinga yokungasebenzi kwezinye izitho zomzimba, umdlavuza kanti  kwesinye isikhathi angagcina ngokufa.UDkt Antonina, we-African Population and Reseach Center, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba, ethi kubalulekile ukuthi uma uzwa ezinye zalezi zimpawu zikuqinisa ngemuva kokudla noma ukuphuza okuthile,  usheshe ubonane nabezempilo abazokuhlola, bathole umsuka wazo bese uyelashwa."Izingane ezineminyaka engaphansi kwemihlanu zisengozini kakhulu yezifo ezitholakala ngokudla. U-40% wabantu abaguliswa yizifo ezitholakala ngokudla kuba yizingane. Amasosha omzimba wengane asathuthuka, awakwazi ukulwa nezifo ngendlela efana neyomuntu omdala," kusho uDkt Mutoro.Uqhube wathi emazweni antulayo nanomnotho ophakathi nendawo ukuvikeleka kwezingane ezifeni kuyancipha ngenxa yokungondleki, ukungahlanzeki nokungahanjiswa kwendle ngendlela efanele, okuhlanganisa ukuswela amanzi aphephile nezindlu zangasese. Uma izingane zigula, zivame ukungakuthandi ukudla. Lokhu kudala ukuthi zidle ukudla okungaphansi kokufanele. Ngaleso sikhathi zilahlekelwa izakhamzimba nemisoco ngenxa yokuhuda nokuphalaza. Lokhu kungaholela ekutheni ingane igcine inesifo sendlala okungaholela ekutheni igule kakhulu noma ife," kusho uDkt Mutoro.UDkt Niera uthe ulwazi olugcinwe kwiWHO lukhombisa ukuthi izingane ezingaphansi kweminyaka emihlanu ezingu-340 emhlabeni zibulawa yizifo ezingagwemeka njalo ngosuku. Kulezo zifo kubalwa nezifo ezidalwa ukudla ukudla okungaphephile.Okunye ukungaphephi kokudla kudalwa ukubakhona kwezinambuzane  namagundane lapho kugcinwa khona ukudla.Okunye kudalwa yizibulali zinambuzane ezisetshenziswa ngesikhathi kutshalwa.Ezinye izinto ezibalwa ngabezimpilo njengezinomthelela ekutheni umuntu agcine edle ukudla okungaphephile ukungazigezi izandla ngaphambi kokudla, uma uphuma endlini encane, uma kade ufinya noma uthimula, ukusebenzisa izitsha ezingahlanzekile uma wenza ukudla nokungazigezi izithelo noma imifino ngaphambi kokuyidla.EMAKHAYA amaningi izingane nabanye abantu abadala badlela ezitsheni zepulastiki ngoba bethi azisheshi ukufa kodwa ongoti bezempilo bayaxwayisa ngalokhu. Bathi uma ungumuntu ohlale ezibheke ukuthi udlani ngoba efuna ukuphila kahle, kumele ukubheke ukuthi udlela esitsheni esakhiwe ngani nokuthi kufakwani uma sakhiwa.Bathi ushevu ongawuthola ngokudla ngesitsha sepulastiki, okusetshenziswe kuso amanye amakhemikhali, ufana nokuthi unesifo sikashukela.UMnuz Priyanka Kheruka, oyiBrand Head, eBorosil, uthe isitsha sepulastiki uma usifudumeza sikhipha ikhemikhali, i-phthalates, eyaziwa nge-plasticers engu-95% , leyo khemikhali igcina ingene ekudleni uma ubufudumeza ukudla ngaleso sitsha."Ukudla okunamafutha okufana nenyama noshizi kunamathuba amaningi, uma kufudunyezwe ngesitsha sepulastiki, okuthi i-phthalates ingene ngqo kukona masinyane. Uma udla lokho kudla, ubeka engcupheni amaphaphu, izinso nesibindi. Ngakolunye uhlangothi, i-bisphenol eyaziwa ngokuthi iBPA ephuma kuzo izitsha zepulastiki yenyusa amathuba okuthi uhlaselwe yisifo senhliziyo nesikashukela," kusho yena.Uthe ingilazi yona ayifani nepulastiki, ayiwukhiphi ushevu uma ufudumeze ngayo futhi aliyilimazi imvelo uma isilahliwe ngoba ayikho ikhemikhali eyikhiphayo ehlukumeza imvelo.“Ukusebenzisa isitsha esiyingilazi esivalwayo kuyasiza ekutheni singabikhona isidingo sokuthi usebenzise ipulastiki yokugoqa ukudla, i-cling wrap. Ukusebenzisa izitsha ezakhiwe ngokusansimbi nakho kungasiza ekutheni ungabi nezinkinga zempilo," kusho yena.“Amabhodwe akhiwe ngokusansimbi (steel) awayikhiphi ikhemikhali  eyingozi uma uphekile kanti ukudla okugcinwe ebhodweni akushintshi indlela okunambitheka ngayo futhi kulula ukuwahlanza. Amabhodlela okugcina ukudla ezitolo maningi, kumele ukhethe lawa avaleka athi ngci futhi izivalo zawo ezingathombi (rust) ukuze ukudla kuhlale kusezingeni elifanele," kusho yena.Uthe izitsha ezakhiwe ngethusi (bronze) zikulungele ukuthi kufudunyezwe ngazo ngoba ziyakugcina ukushisa."Ziningi izinto ongakhetha kuzo ezakhiwe ngethusi. Izintambo zethusi zinhle kakhulu ekufudumaliseni amanzi nokugcina ukushisa," kusho yena.I-BPA sekunesikhathi kukhalwa ngokuthi iyingozi, amabhodlela okuncelisa ingane sekuze kwakhiwa okuthiwa aphephile, ayisetshenziswa le khemikhali uma akhiwa abizwa ngeBPA free.Ucwaningo luveza ukuthi izinsalela zeBPA, uma zidliwa umuntu, zengeza amathuba okuthi abe nezinkinga zesibeletho, zokungabatholi abantwana, umdlavuza webele. Ezinganeni idala inkinga yokungakwazi ukufunda kahle.I-phthalatesnoma ne-plasticers yingxube yamakhemikhali asetshenziselwa ukuncibilikisa imikhiqizo ethile kuyo, okuyiplastiki, uwoyela wokuthambisa izinsimbi, umata i-vinyl, izinsipho zokugeza, ezokugeza izinwele (shampoo) nezigcobo zokuzokunakekela izinwele.KUSAZOTHATHA isikhathi ngaphambi kokuthi kubonakale zehla izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Joe Phaahla, uthe kungenzeka kuphele amasonto amabili ngaphambi kokuthi kubonakale zehla izibalo zabahaqwa yiCorona kuleli.Uthe okwamanje izifundazwe ezihamba phambili ngabantu abaningi abahaqwa yileli gciwane iWestern Cape neKwaZulu-Natal.IWestern Cape seyike yafika esigabeni sokuthi izinombolo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane zingabe zisenyuka kodwa kwaba ngokwesikhashana. Njengamanje seziphinde zenyuka, kanti KwaZulu-Natal khona zisalokhu zenyukile izibalo. "Okwenzeke eWestern Cape akujwayelekile. Esikwaziyo ukuthi uma izibalo sezifike lapho zimi khona ndawonye zibe sezehla, kodwa kunokuthi zehle sezivele zaqala phansi zenyuka. Ngiyazi lokhu kuyethusa kodwa okusempeleni, sinegciwane elisha esingazi nathi ukuthi silindeleni ngalo ngoba lisazishintshashintsha," kusho yena.Uthe kulesi siwombe sesithathu sokuhlasela kweCovid-19 kuleli, babe bancane abasebenzi bezempilo abahlaselwe yiCovid-19 ngenxa yokuthi iningi labo ligomile."Inkinga esibhekene nayo eyokuthi, nakuba bengagulanga kakhulu kulesi siwombe abasebenzi bezempilo kodwa bakhathele, badinga ukuphumula. Sidinga ukuthi senze izinhlelo zokuthi kuqashwe abanye abasebenzi bezempilo abengeziwe ukuze laba abakhona bezokwazi ukuthatha ikhefu, baphumule ukuze bakwazi ukubhekana nesiwombe sesine sokuhlasela kwegciwane okulindeleke ukuthi kufike ngoDisemba," kusho uDkt Phaahla.Izibalo zakamuva zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli ezikhishwe yisikhungo esicubungula izifo ezithathelanayo kuleli, iNational Institute of Communicable Diseases (NICD), zikhomba ukuthi bangu-10 748 abantu  abahaqwe yiCovid-19 emahoreni angu-24, okwenza ukuthi isibalo sabahaqwe yiCovid-19 kuleli, senyukele ku-2 690 973.Abantu bakamuva ababulelwe yizifo ezisondelene neCovid-19 bangu-170 okuholele ekutheni isibalo sababulewe okuhlobene nobhubhane kuleli senyukele ku-79 421.UNkk Sinenhlanhla Jimoh weNICD, uthe izibalo zakamuva zabahaqiwe, zikhomba ukuthi eKZN abantu abahaqwe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 bangu-13%, e-Eastern Cape bangu-16% abase-Western Cape babe ngu-22%. KUGQUGQUZELWE abazali ukuthi banake izingane zabo ezineminyaka ewu-15 kuya ku-19 kwazise ucwaningo luveza ukuthi iningi lazo liyazibulala.Njalo ngoFebhuwari 14 kuya kuFebhuwari 21, iSouth African Depression and Anxiety Group (Sagad) iqwashisa ngokuzibulala kwezingane ezineminyaka ewu-15 kuya ku-19.Ngokocwaningo luka-2020 lweWorld Health Organisation (WHO), kuvela ukuthi izingane ezikule minyaka zisengcupheni yokuzibulala ngenxa yokhwantalala.UDkt Frans Korb onguSihlalo weBhodi leSadag futhi ongudokotela wengqondo, ucele abazali ukuthi bayeke ukuzitshela ukuthi izingane azihlaselwa wukhwantalala ngoba akusilo iqiniso leli.“Izingane ziyaba nokhwantalala ikakhulukazi kulesi sikhathi sokufunda online, ukungayi esikoleni, ukuhlala ngawedwana, ukushonelwa nezinye izimo zempilo. Ucwaningo luthole ukuthi izingane ezineminyaka ewu-15 kuya ku-19 zisengcupheni enkulu yokuzibulala. Sikhumbuza abazali ukuthi ukhwantalala alukhethi bala, minyaka, bulili, inkolo nesimo somnotho. Luphatha noma wubani,” kusho uKorb.Uthe ziningi  izingcingo abazithola kulayini wabo wokugwema ukuzibulala ngakho abazali kubalulekile ukuthi basondele ezinganeni zabo.UNkk Cassey Chambers obhekele ukusebenza kweSadag, uthe abazali othisha nabanakekela izingane abavamisile ukukhuluma ngokuzibulala.“Siyabagqugquzela abazali, abagada izingane nothisha ukuthi bakhulume ngodaba lokuzibulala. Ucwaningo lukhombisa ukuthi izingane okukhulunywa nazo ngalesi sihloko azibi nomqondo wokuzibulala. Ukugwema ukukhuluma ngokuzibulala yikhona okungaholela ekutheni izingane zizibulale ngoba zisuke zingazi ukuthi zizoxoxa nobani ngezingqinamba ezibhekene nazo,” kusho uNkk Chambers.Uthe ngoFebhuwari 24 bazoba ne-webinar yamahhala ezolekelela othisha ukuthi bakhulume ngodaba lokuzibulala, eyabazali izoba ngoFebhuwari 25 ngo-1emini.Uma ingane ibhekene nezingqinamba eziningi ingashayela u-0800 567 567 ukukhuluma nabaluleka ngengqondo, ingathumela ne-sms ku-31393 lapho izoshayelwa khona ozoyiluleka. Zingaya kwi-website ethi:www.sadag.org. SIYAKHULA isibalo sezingane ezihlonzwa ukuthi zine-autism kanti ongoti bathi sekuyisikhathi sokuthi abantu bafunde futhi basiqonde lesi simo.Ungoti obhekele ukuhlonza  nokwelashwa  kwalesi simo ezinganeni,  iNeurodevelopment Paediatrician, osebenza esibhedlela iNetcare St Augustine, uDkt  Nerica Ramsundhar, uthe  eminyakeni emihlanu kuya kweyisithupha eyedlule sibonakale sinyuka isibalo sezingane ezine-autism.Uthe ngokolwazi olukhishwe i-US Center of Control nyakenye ucwaningo beluveza ukuthi ezinganeni ezingu-36 eyodwa ine-autism kanti phambilini beluveza ukuthi ezinganeni ezingu-56 eyodwa ine-autism.UDkt Ramsundhar uthe abantu abane-autism baba nezinselelo zoxhumana ngendlela kwemizwa i-neurodevelopmental okudala ukuthi ihluke indlela  abakhuluma ngayo nendlela abaziphatha ngayo uma kuqhathaniswa neyabanye abantu. Uthe bajwayele ukwenza into bayiphindaphinde."Lokhu kunomthelela endleleni  ulimi oluveza imizwa ngokwejwayelekile, okuyikhono lethu lokukhuluma; ikhono lethu lokuqonda; kanye nokukhuluma  libe lingaphumi izwi okungaba ukukhuluma ngokushintsha ubuso, indlela amehlo abuka ngayo,  ukuthinta komzimba nokunye," kuchaza uDkt Ramsundhar. Uqhube wathi izingane ezine-autism ngokuvamile aziyivezi imizwa ngesimo sobuso bazo, zivamise ukwenza okuthile ngesandla okungaba ukuhebeza, ukugxuma, ukuzigingqa phansi, ukuzisonta umzimba nakho okungabonakala."Izingane ezine-autism ngokuvamile  zihlale zimatasatasa ngezinto ezithile ezenza umqondo wazo uhlale usebenza, njengokuqaqa ithoyizi lemoto esikhundleni sokudlala ngalo, ukucubungula izinkinobho, amatshe noma yini enye. Konke lokhu kwenza ukuthi zingabi naso isikhathi sokudlala nezinye izingane ngoba umqondo wazo ugxila kulokho ezifuna ukukuxazulula," kuchaza udokotela.Wengeze ngokuthi izingane ezine-autism zingase zibe nokuxhumana nomphakathi  okungejwayelekile ngoba ziyakugwema ukuxhumana nabantu kakhulu.“Ukushintshana ngamathoyizi kanye nokudlala ngamathoyizi kungase kuzicasule," kusho uDkt Ramsundhar.Uthe uma behlola izingane bakhuluma nabazali  babheke umlando kamama ngesikhathi ekhulelwe ingane. Babheke ukuthi ingane ibikhula kanjani ngalesi sikhathi ."Sixoxa nomndeni  mayelana nokudlala kwengane, ukuhlalisana kwayo nabanye abantu, ukwenza izinto ngokuphindaphinda noma ukucubungula umehluko entweni eyodwa. Bese kuba khona lapho sibheka ukuthi ingane ixoxa kanjani nabazali bayo. Ukuthi yenzenjani uma icela okuthile, imaphi amagama ekwazi ukuwaphimisa  nokunye,"  kuchaza uDkt Ramsundhar.Uthe lezi zinto azibalile abakhulisa izingane kumele baziqaphele emakhaya ukuze basheshe babone uma kunokungajwayelekile.SELENYUKELE ku-21.1% izinga lokutheleleka kwabantu ngegciwane iCorona kuleli.Izibalo zakamuva ezikhishiwe yisikhungo ezibhekele izifo ezithathelanayo kuleli, iNational Institute of Commnunicable Diseases (NICD), zikhomba ukuthi bangu-6,372 abantu abasha abahaqwe yileli gciwane kuleli. Lokhu  kuholele ekutheni babe ngu-3,776,298 abahaqwe yileli gciwane selokhu lafika kuleli, abashonile ngesikhathi esifanayo bathathu, osekuholele ekutheni isibalo sababulawe yileli gciwane selokhu lafika kuleli senyukele ku-100,351.Ngokombiko okhishwe ngeSonto ntambama, iGauteng ihamba phambili ngesibalo esiphezulu sabantu abangu-1 727 abahaqwe yileli gciwane, ilandelwe yiKwaZulu-Natal ngabantu abangu-818 abahaqwe yigciwane.Amagciwane azalwe yi-Omicron yiBA.4 neBA.5 yiwona ahaqa abantu okwamanje.UDkt Nicholas Crisp, umqondisi woMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli, uthe abakuqaphelayo ngalezi zibalo wukuthi abantu abaningi abahaqwe yigciwane ngabantu abangagomile.Uqhube wathi okwamanje abakabi baningi abantu abalaliswe ezibhedlela ngenxa yegciwane."Esikukhuthaza wukuthi abantu abangakagomi bagome. Abasagome umgomo owodwa okumele ngabe bagome imigomo emibili mabaye ezikhungweni zempilo bayogoma umgomo wesibili; okumele bayojova imijovo enikeza imigomo amandla ama-boosters babuyele bayothatha leyo migomo ukuze sivikele ukuthi abantu bagule kakhulu uma behaqwa yileli gciwane,"  kusho yena.UMA ucabanga impilo yowesifazane yesimanje, uba nesithombe somuntu ovuka ekuseni ageze aziphaqule, angene ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ezehlukene okubalwa uWhatsapp, Facebook, Twitter, Instagram, tik tok nezinye. Lokhu abesifazane bakwenza bephila emazingeni empilo angefani neminyaka engalingani ngoba nasebekhulile abangenazo izinkundla zokuxhumana banolwazi ngazo. Kodwa uma useKranskop, eMakhabeleni esigodini saKwaSenge, kunabesifazane abangazi nokuthi ukhuluma ngani uma ubala zonke lezi zinto futhi abangazihaleli nakancane ngoba abanalwazi ngazo.Leli phephandaba libe nenhlanhla yokukhuluma nabanye besifazane bakule ndawo abaveze ukuthi izinhlelo zethelevishini abahlala befunda ngazo kwiSolezwe, abazi nokuthi kusuke kukhulunywa ngani ngoba abazibuki. Uma bevuka into yokuqala abayenzayo basheshisa imisebenzi yasendlini bahlukane phakathi abanye balibangise ehlathini beyotheza, abanye bayokha amanzi bese kuba khona nabayongena emasimini. Lena yimpilo abathi ibagcina bejabule futhi abaziboni beyohlala emalokishini nasemadolobheni ngoba ngeke besajwayela enye indlela yokuphila. Yize bengathanda ukuba nogesi amanzi, itiyela nezitolo ezinkulu kodwa indlela abaphila ngayo bayayithakasela ngoba ayibafaki ezindlekweni.Owesifazane ozalelwe kule ndawo nongazange asiqede isikole ngoba ethole umendo uthe, yena nabangani bakhe bagaya idokwe bese besheshisa imisebenzi yasendlini balibangise emfuleni ekuseni baze babuye liyoshona nokuyinto ejwayelekile. Yilapho athe bathola khona  ithuba lokuthamunda izindaba zabo zabesifazane nezomendo nokuyinto eyenzeka cishe zonke izinsuku. "Angikaze ngivakashe eThekwini, ngike ngizwe abanye bethi bayovakasha olwandle. Ngeke ngisayijwayela enye impilo ngoba sengijwayele ukuvuka ekuseni ngiyocosha izinkuni zokupheka, ngiyokha amanzi ngihlangane nabanye omama," kusho lo wesifazane.Omunye uveze ukuthi yize esewumakoti omncane kodwa naye uyayijabulela impilo yasemakhaya nokuhlala nomamezala.  Inkonzo yasekamelweni uthi kuyenzeka nayo ayithole kanye noma kabili ngonyaka uma kubuye umyeni futhi akanankinga.  "Umyeni wami kuyenzeka kucishe kuphele unyaka engabuyanga ekhaya kodwa angibi nayo inkinga ngoba ngisuke ngihleli nomamezala. Angisizwa isizungu ngoba senza imisebenzi yasekhaya uma ezovakasha naye ufica konke kulungile ekhaya,"kusho lo wesifazaneOmunye uveze ukuthi selokhu azalwa akakaze asebenzise iziphaqulo futhi nesidingo sazo akasiboni ngoba akuyona into abayisebenzisayo. Into ehamba phambili neyenza isikhumba sowesifazane ikhazimule abe muhle kule ndawo, yibomvu eligcotshwa ekuseni kusaphuma ilanga lize ligezwe seliyoshona. "Isikhathi esiningi sihlala ehlathini nasemfuleni, asibi nesikhathi sokuhlala endlini singenzi lutho. Ngesikhathi sokutshala singena emasimini siligcobile, siyokha amanzi siligcobile noma siyotheza liyasivikela elangeni. Angiboni ukuthi ngingajwayela ukugcoba le zinto ezigcotshwayo,“ kusho lo wesifazane.Izitayela zemfashini yize zikhona futhi zingena zidedelana ezitolo kodwa abaningi besifazane bakule ndawo bakhonze iziketi namaphinifa kulaba asebekhulile nabaganile. Omunye utshele leli phephandaba ukuthi selokhu azalwa akakaze aligqoke ibhulukwe futhi ukhule lingagqokwa nakubo. "Angikakaze ngizibone ngigqoka ibhulukwe, sezikhona izingane ezincane eziswenka ngawo kodwa mina ngeke ngaligqoka noma kungabanda kanjani ngifaka amasokisi okungcono. Into engiyithandayo ukuvunula, ngiyazizwa ngisho ngihamba, nanamhlanje ngiyazisola ukuthi ngigqokeleni kanje bekufanele ngivunule ngoba kunezivakashi," kusho owesifazane.ININGI labantu besilisa alivamile ngokuzikhathaza kakhulu ngezinguquko ezenzeka emzimbeni njengokukhuluphala, ukuzehlisa isisindo somzimba, indlela obukeka ngayo okubalwa nosayizi wezimpahla zokugqoka. Uma kuthuke kwakhona okukhuthalele, kuba namagama ayiziswana njengokuthi wenza izinto zabesimame.Ongoti bezempilo bathi kumele nakanjani nabesilisa bazikhathaze ngezinguquko ezenzeka emzimbeni yabo ngoba zingaba yizimpawu zokunyonyobelwa wukugula okuthize noma izinkinga zezempilo nje jikelele.Kulezo zinkinga kungaba izimpawu zokuhlaselwa okubizwa nge-Andropause efana nse neMenopause ehlasela abesifazane.I-Andropause yisigaba lapho owesilisa ehlelwa khona wumdlandla wezinto eziningi ngesikhathi esisodwa. Lokhu imvamisa kwenza abesilisa abasanda kuhlanganisa iminyaka ewu-30 nangaphezulu. Ongoti baveza ukuthi ngesikhathi kwehla izinga lehomoni elibizwa ngeTestosterone, kuthinteka okunye okubizwa ngeHypothalamus okuyingxenye yezicubu zengqondo ezibhekelele ukulawula ukushisa nokubanda emzimbeni wakho. Kungenza kube nokudideka okuholela ekutheni kungabe kusalawuleka kahle ukushisa nokuphola komzimba wakho. Isikhulu esiphezulu (CEO) kwa-Affinity Health, uMnuz Murray Hewlett uveza ukuthi ezinye zezimpawu zalesi sifo azinakwenza neminyaka yomuntu kodwa kumele uhlobo lwempilo oyiphilayo lukulekelele ukugcina umzimba wakho unempilo. "Ukukhuluphala, ushukela, umphimbo nengcindezi yengqondo ngezinye zezimpawu ezivame kwabesilisa abasuke sebehlaselwa i-Andropause.  Uma kukhona ongakuboni kahle noma okusolayo, zisukumele uyothola usizo lwezempilo," kusho uHewlett.Ongoti bathi ukudla izinto ezinempilo, ukuphuza amanzi, ukuzivocavoca nokuhlala uvakashela odokotela nasemtholampilo kungakusiza ukugwena i-Andropause.Izimpawu ezijwayelekile ongaziqaphela uma usuqalwa yi-Andropause:-Ingcindezi yengqondo ngenye yezinkomba zokuthi ususenkingeni, uhleka manje, udinwe, uphatheke kabi noma kube khona okukudinayo kungonakele lutho.-Ukukhathala yize kuyinto eyenza wonke umuntu kodwa kowesilisa kugadla kuzwele.-Umdlandla wocansi uya ngokuncipha kube nzima ngisho ukululangazelela.-Ukhohlwa kalula, ingqondo yakho ithatha kade noma wenza into ungakwazi ukubhekana nayo ngqo, ugcine ungasazi nokuthi bewuhlele ukwenzani.-Ubuthongo bukubamba isikhashana bese uyaqwasha ebusuku noma kube nzima nokuzumeka uma sekushaye isikhathi sokungena embhedeni.-Ukushisa komzimba esikhaleni ube nesifuthufuthu nokuyinto evame kwabesifazane uma bengena kwi-monopause, nakwabesilisa kuyenzeka kulesi sigaba.-Amalungu omzimba ayakhathala ahlale ebuhlungu yilapho okusuke sekwehle ngamandla itestosterone nokufanele idlale indima enkulu ukugcina amalungu omzimba enempilo.-Indlela okuhluma ngayo izinwele zakho iyashintsha, ziqothuke noma ziphephezele kuvele isikhumba phansi. Uma kungenjalo uzobona sezikhula ngamandla emadlebeni nasemakhaleni.-Izicubu zomzimba ziyazwela zikhathale ngokweqile kube nzima nokwenza izinto ezizodinga ube nomdlandla usebenzise izikhwepha. INHLANGANO yodokotela iSouth African Medical Association (Sama) ithi ngeke kwenze umehluko ezibalweni zeCovid-19 ukubuyisela izwe kuthaqa.UDkt Angelique Coetzee owuSihlalo weSama, uthe kufanele kuhlelwe kahle ukusebenza kwezikhungo zempilo, kugonywe abasebenzi bazo hhayi ukuthi izwe livalwe thaqa.“ICorona vele ikhona njengamanje ibhuqabhuqa abantu, lokhu ukubona ngokunyuka kwezibalo zabahaqekile. Uma uhulumeni ebuyisela izwe kuthaqa kusho ukuthi laba abantu abagulayo ngeke basizwe muntu. Okokuqala kukhona imindeni ezivalele ngayodwana esisizwa yizihlobo. Uma uthi abantu abahlale ezindlini, kuvalwe amabhizinisi amaningi kusho ukuthi isimo sizoba sibi kakhulu kunalokhu esiyikona,” kusho uDkt Coetzee.Uthe uhulumeni kufanele avale izikhala zodokotela ezikhona, andise onesi nabanye abasebenzi bezempilo.“Asisho ukuthi uhulumeni akavule izikhala ezintsha zemisebenzi, sithi akagcwalise lezi ezikhona. Akanike abasebenzi bezempilo impahla yokuzivikela, aqinisekise ukuthi ingqalasizinda nazo zonke izinsiza zisebenza kahle ezibhedlela. Ukuvala izwe akusona isisombululo,” kusho uDkt Coetzee.Uveze ukuthi odokotela babathinta nsukuzonke bebatshela ukuthi basebenza amahora amaningi futhi uma bekhala izikhulu zezibhedlela azibanaki.“Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi isibalo sodokotela abasebenzayo njengamanje sizokwehla kakhulu ngenxa yokuthi abanye bayashona, abanye bakhathele. Noma uhulumeni angavala izwe izikhawu eziningi kodwa uma engalungisi inkinga yabasebenza ezikhungweni zempilo ngeke kube nesixazululo. Kuyimanje izibhedlela zigcwele abantu abaneCorona, abezinye izifo bayaxoshwa,” kusho uDkt Coetzee.Uphethe ngokugcizelela ukuthi abasebenzi bezempilo kufanele bathole umgomo ngokushesha ngoba uma bephuma ezibhedlela baya emindenini okusho ukuthi nayo ingase itheleleke uma bengagonyiwe.BANQUME ukusebenzisa amakhambi esintu ukuze bazivikele kubhubhane lweCovid-19, othisha abamaka amaphepha ka-matric ezikhungweni ezehlukene KwaZulu-Natal.Kuthiwa abanye othisha baqale ukumaka sebevele behaqwe yilolu bhubhane, olubuye ngamandla ngehlandla lesibili. Omunye wothisha abamakela e-Adams College, ngaseManzimtoti uveze ukuthi baxube amakhambi esintu okubalwa namaqabunga kagamthilini, base begquma ukuze bazivikele  kwiCovid-19. Uthe othisha bayazama ngayo yonke indlela ukugxila emsebenzini wokumaka yize bethola imiyalezo ngokushona kwezihlobo nabangani babo ngenxa yeCovid-19. Kwenzeka lokhu nje kuvele ukuthi inqwaba yothisha eLimpopo, ibuyele emakhaya yalaxaza ukumaka ngenxa yalo ubhubhane. UMqondisi jikelele wemfundo kuzwelonke uMnuz Mathanzima Mweli, uthe ukumaka kuqhubeka kahle ezifundazweni zonke, wathi bakwazile ukuvala izikhala zalabo abahoxile emva kokutholakala ukuthi sebehaqekile. Uthe bangu-45 000 othisha abamakayo ezweni lonke. Uhlabe ikhwelo kubo bonke othisha abamakayo wathi baqikelele ukuthi balandela imigomo yokuzivikela, okubalwa ukugqoka izifonyo nokuqhelelana.ODOKOTELA bathi bekuvele kulindelekile ukuthi umgomo i-AstraZeneca ungalwi ngokuphelele negciwane iCovid-19 eselizishintshile elitholakale eNingizimu Afrika.UDkt Angelique Kotze umengameli wenhlangano yodokotela iSouth African Medical Association (SAMA),  uthe imiphumela ekhomba ukuthi lomgomo awuvikeli ngokuphelele awubamangazanga ngoba bebevele bekucabanga ukuthi kungenzeka ungasebenzi ngenxa yokuthi igciwane selizishintshile."Okwenzeke  kuleli kuyenzeka nakwamanye amazwe. Maningi amanye amazwe athenge imigomo engakabi nalo ulwazi lokuthi leyo  migomo izosebenza yini. Ngasohlangothini lwethu akukhona ukuthi umgomo awusebenzi, umgomo uyasebenza kodwa awuyilungele iNingizimu Afrika ngoba igciwane lizishintshile,"  kusho uDkt Koetze.Uqhube wathi uyazi ukuthi abantu abaningi bebejahe ukuthi kugonywe ukuze babuyele empilweni ejwayelekile  okuyinto okungelula ukuthi yenzeke."Noma ngabe abantu bebegomile bebesazoqhubeka bafake izifonyo baqhelelane ngoba igciwane liyashesha ukuzishintsha. Ukugoma okwamanje yikhona okungasisiza ngoba alikabi khona ikhambi nakho ukugoma kumele kube yinto esheshayo igciwane lingakazishintshi,"  kusho yena.Uthe miningi imigomo esahlolwa ezongena emakethe  maduze kuleyo migomo  uthe kungenzeka ube khona olungele iNingizimu Afrika.UDkt Julio Oliviera weNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika isebenzise umgomo ososiza ekutheni kunciphe abantu abazodinga ukulaliswa esibhedlela ngoba inkinga enkulu ukugcwala kwezibhedlela.UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo uDkt Zweli Mkhize ukumisile okwesikhashana ukusatshalaliswa komgomo  obuhlelelwe ukugoma abasebenzi bezempilo abangu-1 million."Ukumiswa komgomo okwesikhashana, kungenxa yokuthi ososayensi bethu basazocwaninga bathole ukuthi singawusebenzisa kanjani lo mgomo. Izinhlelo zokugoma abasebenzi bezempilo zizoqhubeka ngomgomo iJohnson &Johnson nePfizer okulindeleke ukuthi ifike kuleli emasontweni azayo,"  kusho yena.USolwazi Shabir Madhi weWits University  obehola ithimba ebelenza ucwaningo lwe-AstraZeneca ne-Oxford uthe lisekhona ithemba lokuthi nakuba lo mgomo ungamvikeli umuntu ukuthi abe nezimpawu ezincane zeCovid-19 kodwa uyamvikela ekutheni agule kakhulu."Ucwaningo luveza ukuthi nakuba igciwane lizishintshile  kodwa ingxenye enkulu yalo ayishintshile okusho ukuthi usengamvikela umuntu ekutheni agule kakhulu aze adinge ukuya esibhedlela,"  kusho yena.Unobhala weNehawu uMnuz Zola Saphetha uthe: “Ukuzishintshashintsha kwegciwane kusho ukuthi kumele kuhlale kwenziwa ucwaningo olubheka ezinye izindlela ezingenziwa uma kwenzeka igciwane lizishintsha  singazitholi sigidagida ndawonye. Ukugoma yikhona okungasiza ekutheni iCovid-19 ingasabalali ngoba ukuqhelelana akuyona into okulula ukuthi yenzeke kwabanye abantu njengoba behlala abanye besebenza ezindaweni ezingakuvumeli ukuthi baqhelelane ngoba zazingakhelwe ukuthi kuqhelelwane, ”  kusho uSaphetha. I-France izokweseka i-Afrika ngemigomo yeCovid-19 engu-30 million.UMengameli wakuleli uMnz Cyril Ramaphosa ongusihlalo we-African Union, ngoLwesihlanu umemezele ukuthi uhulumeni waseFrance uzibophezele ekutheni unikele ngemigomo engu-30 million, ezofakwa ohlelweni lokuthenga ngokubambisana imigomo iCovax.“Singamazwe ase-Afrika sijabule kakhulu ngalo mnikelo njengoba uhulumeni wakuleliya lizwe ezonikela ngemigomo uphinde unikele  ngemali engu-500 wama-Euro ozofakwa ohlelweni lwamazwe ase-Afrika lokuthenga imigomo,” kusho uRamaphosa.URamaphosa ubekhuluma eNyuvesi iPretoria ngemuva komhlangano noMengameli waseFrance, uMnuz Emmanuel Macron. Uthe bebedingida ngezindlela zokulwa nobhubhane lweCovid-19 , ukushintshashintsha kwesimo sezulu, ukuphepha nokuthi lamazwe angasebenzisana kanjani.“Asikwazi ukulokhu silinde kulayini ukuthi kufike ithuba lethu lokuthi lokuthenga imigomo esinethemba lokuthi yiyo ezohlenga isizwe kulolu bhubhane. Ukulinda kwethu isikhathi eside kusibeka engcupheni yokuthi abantu abaningi bahaqwe yilolu bhubhane ,”  kusho uRamaphosa.Uqhube wathi amazwe ase-Afrika asebenzisana ngokubambisana  kwezempilo ukuze abhekane nalolu bhubhane. Uthe lokhu kwenzelwa ukuthi wonke amazwe akwazi ukuhlonza abaneCovid-19.UMacron uthe bazimisele ngokweseka iNingizimu Afrika ne-Afrika yonkana ukuze izikhiqizela imigomo yeCovid-19 . Uthe kudingeka ukuthi kungabi nezimfihlo mayelana nokuthi imigomo ibiza malini."Okunye okumele kubhekisiswe ukuthi kusetshenziswe isayensi nobuchwepheshe ukuze kukhiqizwe imigomo. Ukuze kwenzeke lokhu sidinga ukuthi sitshale izimali emkhakheni wesayensi. I-Ningizimu Afrika ne-Afrika izothola ukwesekwa ukuze ikwazi ukuzikhiqizela eyayo imigomo,” kusho uMacron.Ephawula ngodaba lwenkampani yezokuxhumana eqashwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo, iDigital Vibes uthe: " Ungqongqoshe ungazisile ngophenyo olwenziwa iSpecial Investigating Unit. “KELLY JANE TURNER noPHILI MJOLIISIKHUNGO esigunyaza ukusetshenziswa kwemithi kuleli, iSouth African Health Products Regulatory Authority (Sahpra), sesikugunyazile  ukusetshenziswa kwamaphilisi abulala amazenze nezikelemu ezilwaneni, i-ivermectin,  ekwelapheni iCovid-19.Lesi sikhungo izolo, sithe ukusetshenziswa kwala maphilisi ezigulini ezineCovid-19  kuzolawulwa. Sithe ukuvumela ukuthi amaphilisi asetshenziswe  sikwenza ngoba sizwelana nomphakathi njengoba leli gciwane liwuhlalise lubhojozi. UDkt Boitumelo Semete-Makokotlela uthe: "Lokhu akusho ukuthi sesishintshile kulokhu ebesikusho phambilini, kokuthi abukho ubufakazi besayensi obukhomba ukuthi la maphilisi ayayelapha iCovid-19. Kepha, njengesikhungo sibe nokubonisana, sabheka ukuthi yini engenziwa njengoba sibhekene naleli gciwane elenza ukuthi singakwazi ukwenza izinto ngendlela ebesingenza ngayo ukube belingekho. Abasebenzi bezempilo basazozifaka izicelo kulesi sikhungo uma kuneziguli abafuna ukuzelapha ngawo.“ Uqhube wathi imininingwane mayelana nohlelo oluzolandelwa izodalulwa ezinsukwini ezizayo. “Sinethemba lokuthi ukuvunyelwa kwalawa maphilisi ukuthi asetshenziswe ngendlela elawulekayo, kuzovala  imakethe ebese ivulwe osomathuba ebese bewadayisa ngendlela engafanele.” Uthe uhlelo lokwelashwa kweziguli ngala maphilisi olusazodalulwa luzovuleleka kuzo zonke iziguli kodwa odokotela nabasebenzi bezempilo kuzoba nemithetho okumele bayilandele. NgoMsombuluko i-AfriForum nabanye odokotela bafake lesi sikhungo noNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli uDkt Zweli Mkhize enkantolo,  befuna ukuthi kugunyazwe ukusetshenziswa kwala maphilisi. Bebekhala nangokuthi abalimi okuyibo abawasebenzisa kakhulu la maphilisi, abasawatholi emakhemisi ezilwane kanti uma bewathola aseyabiza. Odokotela abangaphezulu kuka-500 bakuleli ngeledlule babhalele uMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa noDkt Mkhize, becela ukuthi lusheshiswe uhlelo lokuhlolwa kwalamaphilisi kubantu. Kule ncwadi babalule nokuthi la maphilisi ayasetshenziswa nakwamanye amazwe.PHILI MJOLIINHLANGANO egunyaza ukusetshenziswa  kwamakhambi kuleli, iSouth African Health Products Regulatory Authority (SAHPRA),  inxusa odokotela ukuthi bagweme ukwelapha  abaneCorona  ngamaphilisi asetshenziselwa ukubulala amazenze nezikelemu ezilwaneni  i-Ivermectin, kuze kube ayaqinisekiswa ukuthi aphephile ukusetshenziswa kubantu.Kuleli, i-Ivermectin ibhaliselwe ukuthi ibulala amazenze nezikelemu ezilwaneni , ayigunyaziwe ukuthi isetshenziswe kubantu kodwa muva nje abanye odokotela bayisebenzisela ukwelapha iziguli ezineCovid-19 .I-SAHPRA esitatimendeni sayo esithunyelelwe abezindaba, ithe kuyenzeka ikugunyaze ukuthi  i-Ivermectin isetshenziselwe ukwelapha izintwala notwayi kubantu, uma kufakwe isicelo esichaza ngezizathu.Le nhlangano ithi kuyakhula ukusetshenziswa kwala maphilisi ukwelapha iCovid-19 kanti akuvumelekile. NgoLwesine kubanjwe indoda  ebiphuma Dubai esikhumulweni sezindiza iKing Shaka Airport,  iphethe la maphilisi angabiza uR100 000.NgoLwesihlanu isibhedlela esiseThekwini, i-Ahmed Al-Kadi (AAK), sibekwe icala lokwephula umthetho olawula ukukhishwa kwemithi, iMedicines and Related Substances Act , ngemuva kokuthi kutholakale usokhemisi wakhona enikeza isiguli la maphilisi.Esinye seziguli esinikezwe lawa maphilisi  kulesi sibhedlela sibikele amaphoyisa neSAHPRA ukuthi sinikezwe lamaphilisi, uma sekuphenywa nebala kwatholaka ukuthi lokhu kwenzekile.UMnuz Yuven Gounden okhulumela iSAPRAH,  uthe usokhemisi onikeze isiguli amaphilisi nomphathi wesibhedlela, babekwe icala lokwephula umthetho olawula ukukhishwa kwemithiUMNYANGO wezeMpilo kuleli awunazo izinhlelo zokuwubuyisela emuva umgomo weCovid-19, i-AstraZeneca okuvele ukuthi awulwi ngokuphelele negciwane lakamuva leCorona eselizishintshile elitholakale kuleli.UNgqongqoshe walo Mnyango uDkt Zweli Mkhize, izolo uthe okwamanje ososayensi bakuleli ngokubambisana nabenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation(WHO) basahlola ukuthi lo mgomo ungasetshenziswa kanjani. Kulindeleke ukuthi emasontweni amabili ezayo ososayensi babe naso iseluleko.UDkt Mkhize ubechaza ngokuthi ngabe umnyango usukuphi nohlelo lokuqala ukugoma abasebenzi bezempilo obekuhlelwe ukuthi luqalwe ngesonto elizayo obekubukeka sengathi ngeke lusaqhubeka ngendlela obekuhlelwe ngayo ngoba  umgomo i-AstraZeneca obusuthengiwe  kutholakale ukuthi awulwi ngokuphelele negciwane eselizishintshile, i501Y.V2 elitholakale kuleli. " Sengike ngathintwa ngamanye amazwe ethi afuna ukuthi siwadayisele lo mgomo ngoba wona awanalo igciwane eselizishintshile i501Y.V2. Okwamanje asikathathwa isinqumo sokuthi udayiswe sisafuna ukuqale sibe nesiqiniseko sokuthi ayikho yini indlela yokuthi siwusebenzise.
